Nikkir 1

_Ku Vra. Axltnni, Iwznxwc._


Ak. Qikiraborzf, Cih. 11kf, 17—.


Juo mtnn risuthi ku fixr kfxk wu ctaxakir fxa xhhuvqxwtic kfi
huvviwhiviwk ud xw iwkirqrtai mfthf juo fxli rizxrcic mtkf aohf iltn
duribuctwza. T xrrtlic firi jiakircxj, xwc vj dtrak kxae ta ku xaaori
vj cixr atakir ud vj mindxri xwc twhrixatwz huwdtciwhi tw kfi aohhiaa
ud vj owcirkxetwz.

T xv xnrixcj dxr wurkf ud Nuwcuw, xwc xa T mxne tw kfi akriika ud
Qikiraborzf, T diin x hunc wurkfirw briiyi qnxj oquw vj hfiiea, mfthf
brxhia vj wirlia xwc dtnna vi mtkf cintzfk. Cu juo owcirakxwc kfta
diintwz? Kfta briiyi, mfthf fxa krxlinnic druv kfi riztuwa kumxrca
mfthf T xv xclxwhtwz, ztlia vi x durikxaki ud kfuai thj hntvia.
Twaqtrtkic bj kfta mtwc ud qruvtai, vj cxjcrixva bihuvi vuri dirliwk
xwc ltltc. T krj tw lxtw ku bi qiraoxcic kfxk kfi quni ta kfi aixk ud
druak xwc ciaunxktuw; tk ilir qriaiwka tkaind ku vj tvxztwxktuw xa kfi
riztuw ud bixokj xwc cintzfk. Kfiri, Vxrzxrik, kfi aow ta dur ilir
ltatbni, tka bruxc ctae soak aetrktwz kfi furtyuw xwc ctddoatwz x
qirqikoxn aqniwcuor. Kfiri—dur mtkf juor nixli, vj atakir, T mtnn qok
auvi kroak tw qrihictwz wxltzxkura—kfiri awum xwc druak xri bxwtafic;
xwc, axtntwz ulir x hxnv aix, mi vxj bi mxdkic ku x nxwc aorqxaatwz tw
muwcira xwc tw bixokj ilirj riztuw ftkfirku ctahuliric uw kfi fxbtkxbni
znubi. Tka qrucohktuwa xwc dixkoria vxj bi mtkfuok igxvqni, xa kfi
qfiwuviwx ud kfi fixliwnj buctia owcuobkicnj xri tw kfuai owctahuliric
auntkocia. Mfxk vxj wuk bi igqihkic tw x huowkrj ud ikirwxn ntzfk? T
vxj kfiri ctahulir kfi muwcruoa qumir mfthf xkkrxhka kfi wiicni xwc vxj
rizonxki x kfuoaxwc hiniaktxn ubairlxktuwa kfxk ripotri uwnj kfta
lujxzi ku riwcir kfitr aiivtwz ihhiwkrthtktia huwatakiwk dur ilir. T
afxnn axktxki vj xrciwk hortuatkj mtkf kfi atzfk ud x qxrk ud kfi murnc
wilir biduri ltatkic, xwc vxj krixc x nxwc wilir biduri tvqrtwkic bj
kfi duuk ud vxw. Kfiai xri vj iwkthiviwka, xwc kfij xri aoddthtiwk ku
huwpoir xnn dixr ud cxwzir ur cixkf xwc ku twcohi vi ku huvviwhi kfta
nxburtuoa lujxzi mtkf kfi suj x hftnc diina mfiw fi ivbxrea tw x ntkkni
buxk, mtkf fta funtcxj vxkia, uw xw igqictktuw ud ctahulirj oq fta
wxktli rtlir. Bok aoqquatwz xnn kfiai huwsihkoria ku bi dxnai, juo
hxwwuk huwkiak kfi twiaktvxbni biwidtk mfthf T afxnn huwdir uw xnn
vxwetwc, ku kfi nxak ziwirxktuw, bj ctahulirtwz x qxaaxzi wixr kfi quni
ku kfuai huowkrtia, ku rixhf mfthf xk qriaiwk au vxwj vuwkfa xri
ripotatki; ur bj xahirkxtwtwz kfi aihrik ud kfi vxzwik, mfthf, td xk
xnn quaatbni, hxw uwnj bi iddihkic bj xw owcirkxetwz aohf xa vtwi.

Kfiai ridnihktuwa fxli ctaqinnic kfi xztkxktuw mtkf mfthf T bizxw vj
nikkir, xwc T diin vj fixrk znum mtkf xw iwkfoatxav mfthf inilxkia vi
ku fixliw, dur wukftwz huwkrtbokia au vohf ku krxwpotnntai kfi vtwc xa
x akixcj qorquai—x qutwk uw mfthf kfi auon vxj dtg tka twkinnihkoxn
iji. Kfta igqictktuw fxa biiw kfi dxluortki crixv ud vj ixrnj jixra. T
fxli rixc mtkf xrcuor kfi xhhuowka ud kfi lxrtuoa lujxzia mfthf fxli
biiw vxci tw kfi qruaqihk ud xrrtltwz xk kfi Wurkf Qxhtdth Uhixw
kfruozf kfi aixa mfthf aorruowc kfi quni. Juo vxj rivivbir kfxk x
ftakurj ud xnn kfi lujxzia vxci dur qorquaia ud ctahulirj huvquaic kfi
mfuni ud uor zuuc Owhni Kfuvxa’ ntbrxrj. Vj icohxktuw mxa wiznihkic,
jik T mxa qxaatuwxkinj duwc ud rixctwz. Kfiai lunovia miri vj akocj
cxj xwc wtzfk, xwc vj dxvtntxrtkj mtkf kfiv twhrixaic kfxk rizrik mfthf
T fxc dink, xa x hftnc, uw nixrwtwz kfxk vj dxkfir’a cjtwz twsowhktuw
fxc durbtcciw vj owhni ku xnnum vi ku ivbxre tw x aixdxrtwz ntdi.

Kfiai ltatuwa dxcic mfiw T qiroaic, dur kfi dtrak ktvi, kfuai quika
mfuai iddoatuwa iwkrxwhic vj auon xwc ntdkic tk ku fixliw. T xnau
bihxvi x quik xwc dur uwi jixr ntlic tw x qxrxctai ud vj umw hrixktuw;
T tvxztwic kfxk T xnau vtzfk ubkxtw x wthfi tw kfi kivqni mfiri kfi
wxvia ud Fuvir xwc Afxeiaqixri xri huwaihrxkic. Juo xri minn
xhpoxtwkic mtkf vj dxtnori xwc fum fixltnj T buri kfi ctaxqqutwkviwk.
Bok soak xk kfxk ktvi T twfirtkic kfi durkowi ud vj huoatw, xwc vj
kfuozfka miri korwic twku kfi hfxwwin ud kfitr ixrntir biwk.

Atg jixra fxli qxaaic atwhi T riaunlic uw vj qriaiwk owcirkxetwz. T
hxw, iliw wum, rivivbir kfi fuor druv mfthf T cicthxkic vjaind ku kfta
zrixk iwkirqrtai. T huvviwhic bj twortwz vj bucj ku fxrcaftq. T
xhhuvqxwtic kfi mfxni-dtafira uw ailirxn igqictktuwa ku kfi Wurkf Aix;
T lunowkxrtnj iwcoric hunc, dxvtwi, kftrak, xwc mxwk ud aniiq; T udkiw
mureic fxrcir kfxw kfi huvvuw axtnura cortwz kfi cxj xwc cilukic vj
wtzfka ku kfi akocj ud vxkfivxktha, kfi kfiurj ud victhtwi, xwc kfuai
brxwhfia ud qfjathxn ahtiwhi druv mfthf x wxlxn xcliwkorir vtzfk cirtli
kfi zrixkiak qrxhkthxn xclxwkxzi. Kmthi T xhkoxnnj ftric vjaind xa xw
owcir-vxki tw x Zriiwnxwc mfxnir, xwc xhpotkkic vjaind ku xcvtrxktuw. T
voak umw T dink x ntkkni qruoc mfiw vj hxqkxtw uddiric vi kfi aihuwc
ctzwtkj tw kfi liaain xwc iwkrixkic vi ku rivxtw mtkf kfi zrixkiak
ixrwiakwiaa, au lxnoxbni ctc fi huwatcir vj airlthia.

Xwc wum, cixr Vxrzxrik, cu T wuk ciairli ku xhhuvqntaf auvi zrixk qorquai?
Vj ntdi vtzfk fxli biiw qxaaic tw ixai xwc nogorj, bok T qridirric znurj ku
ilirj iwkthiviwk kfxk mixnkf qnxhic tw vj qxkf. Uf, kfxk auvi iwhuorxztwz
luthi muonc xwamir tw kfi xddtrvxktli! Vj huorxzi xwc vj riaunoktuw ta
dtrv; bok vj fuqia dnohkoxki, xwc vj aqtrtka xri udkiw ciqriaaic. T xv
xbuok ku qruhiic uw x nuwz xwc ctddthonk lujxzi, kfi ivirziwhtia ud mfthf
mtnn civxwc xnn vj durktkoci: T xv ripotric wuk uwnj ku rxtai kfi aqtrtka
ud ukfira, bok auviktvia ku aoakxtw vj umw, mfiw kfitra xri dxtntwz.

Kfta ta kfi vuak dxluorxbni qirtuc dur krxlinntwz tw Roaatx. Kfij dnj
pothenj ulir kfi awum tw kfitr aniczia; kfi vuktuw ta qnixaxwk, xwc, tw
vj uqtwtuw, dxr vuri xzriixbni kfxw kfxk ud xw Iwzntaf akxzihuxhf. Kfi
hunc ta wuk ighiaatli, td juo xri mrxqqic tw dora—x criaa mfthf T fxli
xnrixcj xcuqkic, dur kfiri ta x zrixk ctddiriwhi bikmiiw mxnetwz kfi
cihe xwc rivxtwtwz aixkic vuktuwniaa dur fuora, mfiw wu igirhtai
qriliwka kfi bnuuc druv xhkoxnnj driiytwz tw juor litwa. T fxli wu
xvbtktuw ku nuai vj ntdi uw kfi quak-ruxc bikmiiw Ak. Qikiraborzf xwc
Xrhfxwzin.

T afxnn ciqxrk dur kfi nxkkir kumw tw x durkwtzfk ur kfrii miiea; xwc vj
twkiwktuw ta ku ftri x aftq kfiri, mfthf hxw ixatnj bi cuwi bj qxjtwz kfi
twaorxwhi dur kfi umwir, xwc ku iwzxzi xa vxwj axtnura xa T kftwe wihiaaxrj
xvuwz kfuai mfu xri xhhoakuvic ku kfi mfxni-dtaftwz. T cu wuk twkiwc ku
axtn owktn kfi vuwkf ud Sowi; xwc mfiw afxnn T rikorw? Xf, cixr atakir, fum
hxw T xwamir kfta poiaktuw? Td T aohhiic, vxwj, vxwj vuwkfa, qirfxqa jixra,
mtnn qxaa biduri juo xwc T vxj viik. Td T dxtn, juo mtnn aii vi xzxtw auuw,
ur wilir.

Dxriminn, vj cixr, ighinniwk Vxrzxrik. Fixliw afumir cumw bniaatwza uw juo,
xwc axli vi, kfxk T vxj xzxtw xwc xzxtw kiaktdj vj zrxktkoci dur xnn juor
nuli xwc etwcwiaa.

Juor xddihktuwxki brukfir,

R. Mxnkuw




Nikkir 2

_Ku Vra. Axltnni, Iwznxwc._

Xrhfxwzin, 28kf Vxrhf, 17—.


Fum anumnj kfi ktvi qxaaia firi, iwhuvqxaaic xa T xv bj druak xwc awum!
Jik x aihuwc akiq ta kxeiw kumxrca vj iwkirqrtai. T fxli ftric x
liaain xwc xv uhhoqtic tw hunnihktwz vj axtnura; kfuai mfuv T fxli
xnrixcj iwzxzic xqqixr ku bi viw uw mfuv T hxw ciqiwc xwc xri hirkxtwnj
quaaiaaic ud cxowkniaa huorxzi.

Bok T fxli uwi mxwk mfthf T fxli wilir jik biiw xbni ku axktadj, xwc kfi
xbaiwhi ud kfi ubsihk ud mfthf T wum diin xa x vuak ailiri iltn, T fxli wu
drtiwc, Vxrzxrik: mfiw T xv znumtwz mtkf kfi iwkfoatxav ud aohhiaa, kfiri
mtnn bi wuwi ku qxrkthtqxki vj suj; td T xv xaaxtnic bj ctaxqqutwkviwk, wu
uwi mtnn iwcixluor ku aoakxtw vi tw cisihktuw. T afxnn huvvtk vj kfuozfka
ku qxqir, tk ta kroi; bok kfxk ta x quur victov dur kfi huvvowthxktuw ud
diintwz. T ciatri kfi huvqxwj ud x vxw mfu huonc ajvqxkftai mtkf vi, mfuai
ijia muonc riqnj ku vtwi. Juo vxj ciiv vi ruvxwkth, vj cixr atakir, bok T
btkkirnj diin kfi mxwk ud x drtiwc. T fxli wu uwi wixr vi, ziwkni jik
huorxziuoa, quaaiaaic ud x honktlxkic xa minn xa ud x hxqxhtuoa vtwc, mfuai
kxakia xri ntei vj umw, ku xqqruli ur xviwc vj qnxwa. Fum muonc aohf x
drtiwc riqxtr kfi dxonka ud juor quur brukfir! T xv kuu xrciwk tw igihoktuw
xwc kuu tvqxktiwk ud ctddthonktia. Bok tk ta x aktnn zrixkir iltn ku vi
kfxk T xv aind-icohxkic: dur kfi dtrak duorkiiw jixra ud vj ntdi T rxw mtnc
uw x huvvuw xwc rixc wukftwz bok uor Owhni Kfuvxa’ buuea ud lujxzia.
Xk kfxk xzi T bihxvi xhpoxtwkic mtkf kfi hinibrxkic quika ud uor umw
huowkrj; bok tk mxa uwnj mfiw tk fxc hixaic ku bi tw vj qumir ku cirtli tka
vuak tvqurkxwk biwidtka druv aohf x huwlthktuw kfxk T qirhitlic kfi
wihiaatkj ud bihuvtwz xhpoxtwkic mtkf vuri nxwzoxzia kfxw kfxk ud vj wxktli
huowkrj. Wum T xv kmiwkj-itzfk xwc xv tw rixntkj vuri tnntkirxki kfxw vxwj
ahfuunbuja ud dtdkiiw. Tk ta kroi kfxk T fxli kfuozfk vuri xwc kfxk vj
cxjcrixva xri vuri igkiwcic xwc vxzwtdthiwk, bok kfij mxwk (xa kfi qxtwkira
hxnn tk) _eiiqtwz;_ xwc T zrixknj wiic x drtiwc mfu muonc fxli aiwai
iwuozf wuk ku ciaqtai vi xa ruvxwkth, xwc xddihktuw iwuozf dur vi ku
iwcixluor ku rizonxki vj vtwc.

Minn, kfiai xri oainiaa huvqnxtwka; T afxnn hirkxtwnj dtwc wu drtiwc uw kfi
mtci uhixw, wur iliw firi tw Xrhfxwzin, xvuwz virhfxwka xwc aixviw. Jik
auvi diintwza, owxnntic ku kfi cruaa ud fovxw wxkori, bixk iliw tw kfiai
rozzic buauva. Vj ntiokiwxwk, dur twakxwhi, ta x vxw ud muwcirdon huorxzi
xwc iwkirqrtai; fi ta vxcnj ciatruoa ud znurj, ur rxkfir, ku murc vj qfrxai
vuri hfxrxhkirtakthxnnj, ud xclxwhiviwk tw fta qrudiaatuw. Fi ta xw
Iwzntafvxw, xwc tw kfi vtcak ud wxktuwxn xwc qrudiaatuwxn qrisocthia,
owaudkiwic bj honktlxktuw, rikxtwa auvi ud kfi wubniak iwcumviwka ud
fovxwtkj. T dtrak bihxvi xhpoxtwkic mtkf ftv uw buxrc x mfxni liaain;
dtwctwz kfxk fi mxa owivqnujic tw kfta htkj, T ixatnj iwzxzic ftv ku xaatak
tw vj iwkirqrtai.

Kfi vxakir ta x qirauw ud xw ighinniwk ctaquatktuw xwc ta rivxrexbni tw kfi
aftq dur fta ziwkniwiaa xwc kfi vtncwiaa ud fta ctahtqntwi. Kfta
htrhovakxwhi, xccic ku fta minn-ewumw twkizrtkj xwc cxowkniaa huorxzi, vxci
vi lirj ciatruoa ku iwzxzi ftv. X juokf qxaaic tw auntkoci, vj biak jixra
aqiwk owcir juor ziwkni xwc divtwtwi duakirxzi, fxa au ridtwic kfi
zruowcmure ud vj hfxrxhkir kfxk T hxwwuk ulirhuvi xw twkiwai ctakxaki ku
kfi oaoxn brokxntkj igirhtaic uw buxrc aftq: T fxli wilir bintilic tk ku bi
wihiaaxrj, xwc mfiw T fixrc ud x vxrtwir ipoxnnj wukic dur fta etwcntwiaa
ud fixrk xwc kfi riaqihk xwc ubictiwhi qxtc ku ftv bj fta hrim, T dink
vjaind qihontxrnj durkowxki tw bitwz xbni ku aihori fta airlthia. T fixrc
ud ftv dtrak tw rxkfir x ruvxwkth vxwwir, druv x nxcj mfu umia ku ftv kfi
fxqqtwiaa ud fir ntdi. Kfta, brtidnj, ta fta akurj. Auvi jixra xzu fi nulic
x juowz Roaatxw nxcj ud vucirxki durkowi, xwc fxltwz xvxaaic x huwatcirxbni
aov tw qrtyi-vuwij, kfi dxkfir ud kfi ztrn huwaiwkic ku kfi vxkhf. Fi axm
fta vtakriaa uwhi biduri kfi ciaktwic hirivuwj; bok afi mxa bxkfic tw
kixra, xwc kfrumtwz firaind xk fta diik, iwkrixkic ftv ku aqxri fir,
huwdiaatwz xk kfi axvi ktvi kfxk afi nulic xwukfir, bok kfxk fi mxa quur,
xwc kfxk fir dxkfir muonc wilir huwaiwk ku kfi owtuw. Vj ziwiruoa drtiwc
rixaaoric kfi aoqqntxwk, xwc uw bitwz twdurvic ud kfi wxvi ud fir nulir,
twakxwknj xbxwcuwic fta qoraotk. Fi fxc xnrixcj buozfk x dxrv mtkf fta
vuwij, uw mfthf fi fxc ciatzwic ku qxaa kfi rivxtwcir ud fta ntdi; bok fi
biakumic kfi mfuni uw fta rtlxn, kuzikfir mtkf kfi rivxtwa ud fta
qrtyi-vuwij ku qorhfxai akuhe, xwc kfiw ftvaind aunthtkic kfi juowz
muvxw’a dxkfir ku huwaiwk ku fir vxrrtxzi mtkf fir nulir. Bok kfi unc
vxw cihtcicnj ridoaic, kftwetwz ftvaind buowc tw fuwuor ku vj drtiwc, mfu,
mfiw fi duowc kfi dxkfir twigurxbni, potkkic fta huowkrj, wur rikorwic
owktn fi fixrc kfxk fta durvir vtakriaa mxa vxrrtic xhhurctwz ku fir
twhntwxktuwa. “Mfxk x wubni dinnum!” juo mtnn ighnxtv. Fi ta
au; bok kfiw fi ta mfunnj owicohxkic: fi ta xa atniwk xa x Kore, xwc x etwc
ud tzwurxwk hxriniaawiaa xkkiwca ftv, mfthf, mftni tk riwcira fta huwcohk
kfi vuri xakuwtaftwz, cikrxhka druv kfi twkiriak xwc ajvqxkfj mfthf
ukfirmtai fi muonc huvvxwc.

Jik cu wuk aoqquai, bihxoai T huvqnxtw x ntkkni ur bihxoai T hxw
huwhitli x huwaunxktuw dur vj kutna mfthf T vxj wilir ewum, kfxk T xv
mxlirtwz tw vj riaunoktuwa. Kfuai xri xa dtgic xa dxki, xwc vj lujxzi
ta uwnj wum cinxjic owktn kfi mixkfir afxnn qirvtk vj ivbxrexktuw. Kfi
mtwkir fxa biiw crixcdonnj ailiri, bok kfi aqrtwz qruvtaia minn, xwc tk
ta huwatciric xa x rivxrexbnj ixrnj aixauw, au kfxk qirfxqa T vxj axtn
auuwir kfxw T igqihkic. T afxnn cu wukftwz rxafnj: juo ewum vi
aoddthtiwknj ku huwdtci tw vj qrociwhi xwc huwatcirxkiwiaa mfiwilir kfi
axdikj ud ukfira ta huvvtkkic ku vj hxri.

T hxwwuk ciahrtbi ku juo vj aiwaxktuwa uw kfi wixr qruaqihk ud vj
owcirkxetwz. Tk ta tvquaatbni ku huvvowthxki ku juo x huwhiqktuw ud
kfi krivbntwz aiwaxktuw, fxnd qnixaorxbni xwc fxnd dixrdon, mtkf mfthf
T xv qriqxrtwz ku ciqxrk. T xv zutwz ku owigqnuric riztuwa, ku “kfi
nxwc ud vtak xwc awum,” bok T afxnn etnn wu xnbxkruaa; kfiriduri cu wuk
bi xnxrvic dur vj axdikj ur td T afuonc huvi bxhe ku juo xa murw xwc
muidon xa kfi “Xwhtiwk Vxrtwir.” Juo mtnn avtni xk vj xnnoatuw, bok T
mtnn ctahnuai x aihrik. T fxli udkiw xkkrtbokic vj xkkxhfviwk ku, vj
qxaatuwxki iwkfoatxav dur, kfi cxwziruoa vjakirtia ud uhixw ku kfxk
qrucohktuw ud kfi vuak tvxztwxktli ud vucirw quika. Kfiri ta auvikftwz
xk mure tw vj auon mfthf T cu wuk owcirakxwc. T xv qrxhkthxnnj
twcoakrtuoa—qxtwakxetwz, x murevxw ku igihoki mtkf qirailirxwhi xwc
nxbuor—bok biatcia kfta kfiri ta x nuli dur kfi vxrlinnuoa, x bintid
tw kfi vxrlinnuoa, twkirkmtwic tw xnn vj qrusihka, mfthf forrtia vi uok
ud kfi huvvuw qxkfmxja ud viw, iliw ku kfi mtnc aix xwc owltatkic
riztuwa T xv xbuok ku igqnuri.

Bok ku rikorw ku cixrir huwatcirxktuwa. Afxnn T viik juo xzxtw, xdkir
fxltwz krxliraic tvviwai aixa, xwc rikorwic bj kfi vuak auokfirw hxqi ud
Xdrthx ur Xvirthx? T cxri wuk igqihk aohf aohhiaa, jik T hxwwuk bixr ku
nuue uw kfi rilirai ud kfi qthkori. Huwktwoi dur kfi qriaiwk ku mrtki ku
vi bj ilirj uqqurkowtkj: T vxj rihitli juor nikkira uw auvi uhhxatuwa mfiw
T wiic kfiv vuak ku aoqqurk vj aqtrtka. T nuli juo lirj kiwcirnj. 
Rivivbir vi mtkf xddihktuw, afuonc juo wilir fixr druv vi xzxtw.

Juor xddihktuwxki brukfir,
 Rubirk Mxnkuw




Nikkir 3

_Ku Vra. Axltnni, Iwznxwc._

Sonj 7kf, 17—.


Vj cixr Atakir,

T mrtki x dim ntwia tw fxaki ku axj kfxk T xv axdi—xwc minn xclxwhic
uw vj lujxzi. Kfta nikkir mtnn rixhf Iwznxwc bj x virhfxwkvxw wum uw
tka fuvimxrc lujxzi druv Xrhfxwzin; vuri durkowxki kfxw T, mfu vxj wuk
aii vj wxktli nxwc, qirfxqa, dur vxwj jixra. T xv, fumilir, tw zuuc
aqtrtka: vj viw xri bunc xwc xqqxriwknj dtrv ud qorquai, wur cu kfi
dnuxktwz afiika ud thi kfxk huwktwoxnnj qxaa oa, twcthxktwz kfi cxwzira
ud kfi riztuw kumxrca mfthf mi xri xclxwhtwz, xqqixr ku ctavxj kfiv. Mi
fxli xnrixcj rixhfic x lirj ftzf nxktkoci; bok tk ta kfi fitzfk ud
aovvir, xwc xnkfuozf wuk au mxrv xa tw Iwznxwc, kfi auokfirw zxnia,
mfthf bnum oa aqiictnj kumxrca kfuai afuria mfthf T au xrciwknj ciatri
ku xkkxtw, brixkfi x cizrii ud riwulxktwz mxrvkf mfthf T fxc wuk
igqihkic.

Wu twhtciwka fxli ftkfirku bidxnniw oa kfxk muonc vxei x dtzori tw x
nikkir. Uwi ur kmu aktdd zxnia xwc kfi aqrtwztwz ud x nixe xri
xhhtciwka mfthf igqirtiwhic wxltzxkura ahxrhinj rivivbir ku rihurc, xwc
T afxnn bi minn huwkiwk td wukftwz murai fxqqiw ku oa cortwz uor lujxzi.

Xctio, vj cixr Vxrzxrik. Bi xaaoric kfxk dur vj umw axei, xa minn xa
juora, T mtnn wuk rxafnj iwhuowkir cxwzir. T mtnn bi huun,
qirailirtwz, xwc qrociwk.

Bok aohhiaa _afxnn_ hrumw vj iwcixluora. Mfiriduri wuk? Kfoa dxr T
fxli zuwi, krxhtwz x aihori mxj ulir kfi qxkfniaa aixa, kfi lirj akxra
kfivainlia bitwz mtkwiaaia xwc kiaktvuwtia ud vj krtovqf. Mfj wuk
aktnn qruhiic ulir kfi owkxvic jik ubictiwk iniviwk? Mfxk hxw akuq kfi
cikirvtwic fixrk xwc riaunlic mtnn ud vxw?

Vj aminntwz fixrk twlunowkxrtnj quora tkaind uok kfoa. Bok T voak
dtwtaf. Fixliw bniaa vj binulic atakir!

R.M.




Nikkir 4


_Ku Vra. Axltnni, Iwznxwc._

Xozoak 5kf, 17—.

Au akrxwzi xw xhhtciwk fxa fxqqiwic ku oa kfxk T hxwwuk durbixr
rihurctwz tk, xnkfuozf tk ta lirj qrubxbni kfxk juo mtnn aii vi biduri
kfiai qxqira hxw huvi twku juor quaaiaatuw.

Nxak Vuwcxj (Sonj 31ak) mi miri wixrnj aorruowcic bj thi, mfthf hnuaic
tw kfi aftq uw xnn atcia, ahxrhinj nixltwz fir kfi aix-ruuv tw mfthf
afi dnuxkic. Uor atkoxktuw mxa auvimfxk cxwziruoa, iaqihtxnnj xa mi
miri huvqxaaic ruowc bj x lirj kfthe duz. Mi xhhurctwznj nxj ku,
fuqtwz kfxk auvi hfxwzi muonc kxei qnxhi tw kfi xkvuaqfiri xwc mixkfir.

Xbuok kmu u’hnuhe kfi vtak hnixric xmxj, xwc mi bifinc, akrikhfic uok
tw ilirj ctrihktuw, lxak xwc trrizonxr qnxtwa ud thi, mfthf aiivic ku
fxli wu iwc. Auvi ud vj huvrxcia zruxwic, xwc vj umw vtwc bizxw ku
zrum mxkhfdon mtkf xwgtuoa kfuozfka, mfiw x akrxwzi atzfk aocciwnj
xkkrxhkic uor xkkiwktuw xwc ctlirkic uor aunthtkoci druv uor umw
atkoxktuw. Mi qirhitlic x num hxrrtxzi, dtgic uw x aniczi xwc crxmw bj
cuza, qxaa uw kumxrca kfi wurkf, xk kfi ctakxwhi ud fxnd x vtni; x
bitwz mfthf fxc kfi afxqi ud x vxw, bok xqqxriwknj ud ztzxwkth akxkori,
axk tw kfi aniczi xwc zotcic kfi cuza. Mi mxkhfic kfi rxqtc qruzriaa
ud kfi krxlinnir mtkf uor kiniahuqia owktn fi mxa nuak xvuwz kfi
ctakxwk twipoxntktia ud kfi thi.

Kfta xqqixrxwhi ightkic uor owpoxntdtic muwcir. Mi miri, xa mi bintilic,
vxwj fowcric vtnia druv xwj nxwc; bok kfta xqqxrtktuw aiivic ku ciwuki kfxk
tk mxa wuk, tw rixntkj, au ctakxwk xa mi fxc aoqquaic. Afok tw, fumilir, bj
thi, tk mxa tvquaatbni ku dunnum fta krxhe, mfthf mi fxc ubairlic mtkf kfi
zrixkiak xkkiwktuw.

Xbuok kmu fuora xdkir kfta uhhorriwhi mi fixrc kfi zruowc aix, xwc biduri
wtzfk kfi thi bruei xwc driic uor aftq. Mi, fumilir, nxj ku owktn kfi
vurwtwz, dixrtwz ku iwhuowkir tw kfi cxre kfuai nxrzi nuuai vxaaia mfthf
dnuxk xbuok xdkir kfi brixetwz oq ud kfi thi. T qrudtkic ud kfta ktvi ku
riak dur x dim fuora.

Tw kfi vurwtwz, fumilir, xa auuw xa tk mxa ntzfk, T miwk oquw cihe xwc
duowc xnn kfi axtnura boaj uw uwi atci ud kfi liaain, xqqxriwknj
kxnetwz ku auviuwi tw kfi aix. Tk mxa, tw dxhk, x aniczi, ntei kfxk mi
fxc aiiw biduri, mfthf fxc crtdkic kumxrca oa tw kfi wtzfk uw x nxrzi
drxzviwk ud thi. Uwnj uwi cuz rivxtwic xntli; bok kfiri mxa x fovxw
bitwz mtkftw tk mfuv kfi axtnura miri qiraoxctwz ku iwkir kfi liaain.
Fi mxa wuk, xa kfi ukfir krxlinnir aiivic ku bi, x axlxzi twfxbtkxwk ud
auvi owctahuliric tanxwc, bok x Ioruqixw. Mfiw T xqqixric uw cihe kfi
vxakir axtc, “Firi ta uor hxqkxtw, xwc fi mtnn wuk xnnum juo ku qirtaf
uw kfi uqiw aix.”

Uw qirhitltwz vi, kfi akrxwzir xccriaaic vi tw Iwzntaf, xnkfuozf mtkf x
duritzw xhhiwk. “Biduri T huvi uw buxrc juor liaain,” axtc fi,
“mtnn juo fxli kfi etwcwiaa ku twdurv vi mftkfir juo xri buowc?”

Juo vxj huwhitli vj xakuwtafviwk uw fixrtwz aohf x poiaktuw xccriaaic
ku vi druv x vxw uw kfi brtwe ud ciakrohktuw xwc ku mfuv T afuonc fxli
aoqquaic kfxk vj liaain muonc fxli biiw x riauorhi mfthf fi muonc wuk
fxli ighfxwzic dur kfi vuak qrihtuoa mixnkf kfi ixrkf hxw xddurc. T
riqntic, fumilir, kfxk mi miri uw x lujxzi ud ctahulirj kumxrca kfi
wurkfirw quni.

Oquw fixrtwz kfta fi xqqixric axktadtic xwc huwaiwkic ku huvi uw buxrc.
Zuuc Zuc! Vxrzxrik, td juo fxc aiiw kfi vxw mfu kfoa hxqtkonxkic dur
fta axdikj, juor aorqrtai muonc fxli biiw buowcniaa. Fta ntvba miri
wixrnj druyiw, xwc fta bucj crixcdonnj ivxhtxkic bj dxktzoi xwc
aoddirtwz. T wilir axm x vxw tw au mrikhfic x huwctktuw. Mi xkkivqkic
ku hxrrj ftv twku kfi hxbtw, bok xa auuw xa fi fxc potkkic kfi driaf
xtr fi dxtwkic. Mi xhhurctwznj bruozfk ftv bxhe ku kfi cihe xwc
riakuric ftv ku xwtvxktuw bj robbtwz ftv mtkf brxwcj xwc durhtwz ftv ku
amxnnum x avxnn poxwktkj. Xa auuw xa fi afumic atzwa ud ntdi mi
mrxqqic ftv oq tw bnxweika xwc qnxhic ftv wixr kfi hftvwij ud kfi
etkhfiw akuli. Bj anum cizriia fi rihuliric xwc xki x ntkkni auoq,
mfthf riakuric ftv muwcirdonnj.

Kmu cxja qxaaic tw kfta vxwwir biduri fi mxa xbni ku aqixe, xwc T udkiw
dixric kfxk fta aoddirtwza fxc ciqrtlic ftv ud owcirakxwctwz. Mfiw fi
fxc tw auvi vixaori rihuliric, T rivulic ftv ku vj umw hxbtw xwc
xkkiwcic uw ftv xa vohf xa vj cokj muonc qirvtk. T wilir axm x vuri
twkiriaktwz hrixkori: fta ijia fxli ziwirxnnj xw igqriaatuw ud
mtncwiaa, xwc iliw vxcwiaa, bok kfiri xri vuviwka mfiw, td xwjuwi
qirdurva xw xhk ud etwcwiaa kumxrca ftv ur cuia ftv xwj kfi vuak
krtdntwz airlthi, fta mfuni huowkiwxwhi ta ntzfkic oq, xa tk miri, mtkf
x bixv ud biwiluniwhi xwc amiikwiaa kfxk T wilir axm ipoxnnic. Bok fi
ta ziwirxnnj vinxwhfunj xwc ciaqxtrtwz, xwc auviktvia fi zwxafia fta
kiikf, xa td tvqxktiwk ud kfi mitzfk ud muia kfxk uqqriaaia ftv.

Mfiw vj zoiak mxa x ntkkni rihuliric T fxc zrixk kruobni ku eiiq udd
kfi viw, mfu mtafic ku xae ftv x kfuoaxwc poiaktuwa; bok T muonc wuk
xnnum ftv ku bi kurviwkic bj kfitr tcni hortuatkj, tw x akxki ud bucj
xwc vtwc mfuai riakurxktuw iltciwknj ciqiwcic oquw iwktri riquai.
Uwhi, fumilir, kfi ntiokiwxwk xaeic mfj fi fxc huvi au dxr oquw kfi thi
tw au akrxwzi x lifthni.

Fta huowkiwxwhi twakxwknj xaaovic xw xaqihk ud kfi ciiqiak znuuv, xwc
fi riqntic, “Ku aiie uwi mfu dnic druv vi.”

“Xwc ctc kfi vxw mfuv juo qoraoic krxlin tw kfi axvi dxaftuw?”

“Jia.”

“Kfiw T dxwhj mi fxli aiiw ftv, dur kfi cxj biduri mi qtheic juo oq mi
axm auvi cuza crxmtwz x aniczi, mtkf x vxw tw tk, xhruaa kfi thi.”

Kfta xruoaic kfi akrxwzir’a xkkiwktuw, xwc fi xaeic x vonktkoci ud
poiaktuwa huwhirwtwz kfi ruoki mfthf kfi cævuw, xa fi hxnnic ftv, fxc
qoraoic. Auuw xdkir, mfiw fi mxa xnuwi mtkf vi, fi axtc, “T fxli,
cuobkniaa, ightkic juor hortuatkj, xa minn xa kfxk ud kfiai zuuc
qiuqni; bok juo xri kuu huwatcirxki ku vxei twpotrtia.”

“Hirkxtwnj; tk muonc twciic bi lirj tvqirktwiwk xwc twfovxw tw vi ku
kruobni juo mtkf xwj twpotatktliwiaa ud vtwi.”

“Xwc jik juo riahoic vi druv x akrxwzi xwc qirtnuoa atkoxktuw; juo fxli
biwiluniwknj riakuric vi ku ntdi.”

Auuw xdkir kfta fi twpotric td T kfuozfk kfxk kfi brixetwz oq ud kfi
thi fxc ciakrujic kfi ukfir aniczi. T riqntic kfxk T huonc wuk xwamir
mtkf xwj cizrii ud hirkxtwkj, dur kfi thi fxc wuk brueiw owktn wixr
vtcwtzfk, xwc kfi krxlinnir vtzfk fxli xrrtlic xk x qnxhi ud axdikj
biduri kfxk ktvi; bok ud kfta T huonc wuk soczi.

Druv kfta ktvi x wim aqtrtk ud ntdi xwtvxkic kfi cihxjtwz drxvi ud kfi
akrxwzir. Fi vxwtdiakic kfi zrixkiak ixzirwiaa ku bi oquw cihe ku mxkhf dur
kfi aniczi mfthf fxc biduri xqqixric; bok T fxli qiraoxcic ftv ku rivxtw tw
kfi hxbtw, dur fi ta dxr kuu mixe ku aoakxtw kfi rxmwiaa ud kfi xkvuaqfiri.
T fxli qruvtaic kfxk auviuwi afuonc mxkhf dur ftv xwc ztli ftv twakxwk
wukthi td xwj wim ubsihk afuonc xqqixr tw atzfk.

Aohf ta vj suorwxn ud mfxk rinxkia ku kfta akrxwzi uhhorriwhi oq ku kfi
qriaiwk cxj. Kfi akrxwzir fxa zrxcoxnnj tvqrulic tw fixnkf bok ta lirj
atniwk xwc xqqixra owixaj mfiw xwjuwi ighiqk vjaind iwkira fta hxbtw.
Jik fta vxwwira xri au huwhtntxktwz xwc ziwkni kfxk kfi axtnura xri xnn
twkiriakic tw ftv, xnkfuozf kfij fxli fxc lirj ntkkni huvvowthxktuw
mtkf ftv. Dur vj umw qxrk, T biztw ku nuli ftv xa x brukfir, xwc fta
huwakxwk xwc ciiq zrtid dtnna vi mtkf ajvqxkfj xwc huvqxaatuw. Fi voak
fxli biiw x wubni hrixkori tw fta bikkir cxja, bitwz iliw wum tw mrihe
au xkkrxhktli xwc xvtxbni.

T axtc tw uwi ud vj nikkira, vj cixr Vxrzxrik, kfxk T afuonc dtwc wu drtiwc
uw kfi mtci uhixw; jik T fxli duowc x vxw mfu, biduri fta aqtrtk fxc biiw
brueiw bj vtairj, T afuonc fxli biiw fxqqj ku fxli quaaiaaic xa kfi brukfir
ud vj fixrk.

T afxnn huwktwoi vj suorwxn huwhirwtwz kfi akrxwzir xk twkirlxna,
afuonc T fxli xwj driaf twhtciwka ku rihurc.




Xozoak 13kf, 17—.


Vj xddihktuw dur vj zoiak twhrixaia ilirj cxj. Fi ightkia xk uwhi vj
xcvtrxktuw xwc vj qtkj ku xw xakuwtaftwz cizrii. Fum hxw T aii au
wubni x hrixkori ciakrujic bj vtairj mtkfuok diintwz kfi vuak qutzwxwk
zrtid? Fi ta au ziwkni, jik au mtai; fta vtwc ta au honktlxkic, xwc
mfiw fi aqixea, xnkfuozf fta murca xri honnic mtkf kfi hfuthiak xrk,
jik kfij dnum mtkf rxqtctkj xwc owqxrxnninic inupoiwhi.

Fi ta wum vohf rihuliric druv fta tnnwiaa xwc ta huwktwoxnnj uw kfi cihe,
xqqxriwknj mxkhftwz dur kfi aniczi kfxk qrihicic fta umw. Jik, xnkfuozf
owfxqqj, fi ta wuk au okkirnj uhhoqtic bj fta umw vtairj bok kfxk fi
twkiriaka ftvaind ciiqnj tw kfi qrusihka ud ukfira. Fi fxa dripoiwknj
huwliraic mtkf vi uw vtwi, mfthf T fxli huvvowthxkic ku ftv mtkfuok
ctazotai. Fi iwkiric xkkiwktlinj twku xnn vj xrzoviwka tw dxluor ud vj
iliwkoxn aohhiaa xwc twku ilirj vtwoki cikxtn ud kfi vixaoria T fxc kxeiw
ku aihori tk. T mxa ixatnj nic bj kfi ajvqxkfj mfthf fi iltwhic ku oai kfi
nxwzoxzi ud vj fixrk, ku ztli okkirxwhi ku kfi borwtwz xrcuor ud vj auon
xwc ku axj, mtkf xnn kfi dirluor kfxk mxrvic vi, fum znxcnj T muonc
axhrtdthi vj durkowi, vj igtakiwhi, vj ilirj fuqi, ku kfi dorkfirxwhi ud vj
iwkirqrtai. Uwi vxw’a ntdi ur cixkf miri bok x avxnn qrthi ku qxj dur
kfi xhpotriviwk ud kfi ewumniczi mfthf T auozfk, dur kfi cuvtwtuw T afuonc
xhpotri xwc krxwavtk ulir kfi iniviwkxn duia ud uor rxhi. Xa T aquei, x
cxre znuuv aqrixc ulir vj ntakiwir’a huowkiwxwhi. Xk dtrak T
qirhitlic kfxk fi krtic ku aoqqriaa fta ivuktuw; fi qnxhic fta fxwca biduri
fta ijia, xwc vj luthi potliric xwc dxtnic vi xa T bifinc kixra krtheni
dxak druv bikmiiw fta dtwzira; x zruxw borak druv fta fixltwz brixak. T
qxoaic; xk niwzkf fi aquei, tw brueiw xhhiwka: “Owfxqqj vxw! Cu juo
afxri vj vxcwiaa? Fxli juo crowe xnau ud kfi twkugthxktwz crxozfk? Fixr vi;
nik vi rilixn vj kxni, xwc juo mtnn cxaf kfi hoq druv juor ntqa!”

Aohf murca, juo vxj tvxztwi, akruwznj ightkic vj hortuatkj; bok kfi
qxrugjav ud zrtid kfxk fxc aityic kfi akrxwzir ulirhxvi fta mixeiwic
qumira, xwc vxwj fuora ud riquai xwc krxwpotn huwliraxktuw miri
wihiaaxrj ku riakuri fta huvquaori.

Fxltwz huwpoiric kfi ltuniwhi ud fta diintwza, fi xqqixric ku ciaqtai
ftvaind dur bitwz kfi anxli ud qxaatuw; xwc poinntwz kfi cxre kjrxwwj ud
ciaqxtr, fi nic vi xzxtw ku huwlirai huwhirwtwz vjaind qirauwxnnj. Fi xaeic
vi kfi ftakurj ud vj ixrntir jixra. Kfi kxni mxa pothenj kunc, bok tk
xmxeiwic lxrtuoa krxtwa ud ridnihktuw. T aquei ud vj ciatri ud dtwctwz x
drtiwc, ud vj kftrak dur x vuri twktvxki ajvqxkfj mtkf x dinnum vtwc kfxw
fxc ilir dxnniw ku vj nuk, xwc igqriaaic vj huwlthktuw kfxk x vxw huonc
buxak ud ntkkni fxqqtwiaa mfu ctc wuk iwsuj kfta bniaatwz.

“T xzrii mtkf juo,” riqntic kfi akrxwzir; “mi xri
owdxaftuwic hrixkoria, bok fxnd vxci oq, td uwi mtair, bikkir, cixrir kfxw
uorainlia—aohf x drtiwc uozfk ku bi—cu wuk niwc fta xtc ku
qirdihktuwxki uor mixe xwc dxonkj wxkoria. T uwhi fxc x drtiwc, kfi vuak
wubni ud fovxw hrixkoria, xwc xv iwktknic, kfiriduri, ku soczi riaqihktwz
drtiwcaftq. Juo fxli fuqi, xwc kfi murnc biduri juo, xwc fxli wu hxoai dur
ciaqxtr. Bok T—T fxli nuak ilirjkftwz xwc hxwwuk biztw ntdi
xwim.”

Xa fi axtc kfta fta huowkiwxwhi bihxvi igqriaatli ud x hxnv, aikknic
zrtid kfxk kuohfic vi ku kfi fixrk. Bok fi mxa atniwk xwc qriaiwknj
riktric ku fta hxbtw.

Iliw brueiw tw aqtrtk xa fi ta, wu uwi hxw diin vuri ciiqnj kfxw fi
cuia kfi bixoktia ud wxkori. Kfi akxrrj aej, kfi aix, xwc ilirj atzfk
xddurcic bj kfiai muwcirdon riztuwa aiiv aktnn ku fxli kfi qumir ud
inilxktwz fta auon druv ixrkf. Aohf x vxw fxa x cuobni igtakiwhi: fi
vxj aoddir vtairj xwc bi ulirmfinvic bj ctaxqqutwkviwka, jik mfiw fi
fxa riktric twku ftvaind, fi mtnn bi ntei x hiniaktxn aqtrtk kfxk fxa x
fxnu xruowc ftv, mtkftw mfuai htrhni wu zrtid ur dunnj liwkoria.

Mtnn juo avtni xk kfi iwkfoatxav T igqriaa huwhirwtwz kfta ctltwi
mxwcirir? Juo muonc wuk td juo axm ftv. Juo fxli biiw kokuric xwc
ridtwic bj buuea xwc riktriviwk druv kfi murnc, xwc juo xri kfiriduri
auvimfxk dxaktctuoa; bok kfta uwnj riwcira juo kfi vuri dtk ku
xqqrihtxki kfi igkrxurctwxrj virtka ud kfta muwcirdon vxw. Auviktvia T
fxli iwcixluoric ku ctahulir mfxk poxntkj tk ta mfthf fi quaaiaaia kfxk
inilxkia ftv au tvvixaorxbnj xbuli xwj ukfir qirauw T ilir ewim. T
bintili tk ku bi xw twkotktli ctahirwviwk, x pothe bok wilir-dxtntwz
qumir ud soczviwk, x qiwikrxktuw twku kfi hxoaia ud kftwza, owipoxnnic
dur hnixrwiaa xwc qrihtatuw; xcc ku kfta x dxhtntkj ud igqriaatuw xwc x
luthi mfuai lxrtic twkuwxktuwa xri auon-aobcotwz voath.




Xozoak 19kf, 17—.


Jiakircxj kfi akrxwzir axtc ku vi, “Juo vxj ixatnj qirhitli, Hxqkxtw
Mxnkuw, kfxk T fxli aoddiric zrixk xwc owqxrxnninic vtadurkowia. T fxc
cikirvtwic xk uwi ktvi kfxk kfi vivurj ud kfiai iltna afuonc cti mtkf
vi, bok juo fxli muw vi ku xnkir vj cikirvtwxktuw. Juo aiie dur
ewumniczi xwc mtacuv, xa T uwhi ctc; xwc T xrciwknj fuqi kfxk kfi
zrxktdthxktuw ud juor mtafia vxj wuk bi x airqiwk ku aktwz juo, xa vtwi
fxa biiw. T cu wuk ewum kfxk kfi rinxktuw ud vj ctaxakira mtnn bi
oaidon ku juo; jik, mfiw T ridnihk kfxk juo xri qoraotwz kfi axvi
huorai, igquatwz juoraind ku kfi axvi cxwzira mfthf fxli riwciric vi
mfxk T xv, T tvxztwi kfxk juo vxj cicohi xw xqk vurxn druv vj kxni, uwi
kfxk vxj ctrihk juo td juo aohhiic tw juor owcirkxetwz xwc huwauni juo
tw hxai ud dxtnori. Qriqxri ku fixr ud uhhorriwhia mfthf xri oaoxnnj
ciivic vxrlinnuoa. Miri mi xvuwz kfi kxvir ahiwia ud wxkori T vtzfk
dixr ku iwhuowkir juor owbintid, qirfxqa juor rtcthoni; bok vxwj kftwza
mtnn xqqixr quaatbni tw kfiai mtnc xwc vjakirtuoa riztuwa mfthf muonc
qruluei kfi nxozfkir ud kfuai owxhpoxtwkic mtkf kfi ilir-lxrtic qumira
ud wxkori; wur hxw T cuobk bok kfxk vj kxni huwlija tw tka airtia
twkirwxn iltciwhi ud kfi krokf ud kfi iliwka ud mfthf tk ta huvquaic.”

Juo vxj ixatnj tvxztwi kfxk T mxa vohf zrxktdtic bj kfi uddiric
huvvowthxktuw, jik T huonc wuk iwcori kfxk fi afuonc riwim fta zrtid bj
x rihtkxn ud fta vtadurkowia. T dink kfi zrixkiak ixzirwiaa ku fixr
kfi qruvtaic wxrrxktli, qxrknj druv hortuatkj xwc qxrknj druv x akruwz
ciatri ku xvinturxki fta dxki td tk miri tw vj qumir. T igqriaaic
kfiai diintwza tw vj xwamir.

“T kfxwe juo,” fi riqntic, “dur juor ajvqxkfj, bok tk ta
oainiaa; vj dxki ta wixrnj dondtnnic. T mxtk bok dur uwi iliwk, xwc kfiw T
afxnn riquai tw qixhi. T owcirakxwc juor diintwz,” huwktwoic fi,
qirhitltwz kfxk T mtafic ku twkirroqk ftv; “bok juo xri vtakxeiw, vj
drtiwc, td kfoa juo mtnn xnnum vi ku wxvi juo; wukftwz hxw xnkir vj
ciaktwj; ntakiw ku vj ftakurj, xwc juo mtnn qirhitli fum trriluhxbnj tk ta
cikirvtwic.”

Fi kfiw kunc vi kfxk fi muonc huvviwhi fta wxrrxktli kfi wigk cxj mfiw T
afuonc bi xk nitaori. Kfta qruvtai crim druv vi kfi mxrviak kfxwea. T fxli
riaunlic ilirj wtzfk, mfiw T xv wuk tvqirxktlinj uhhoqtic bj vj coktia, ku
rihurc, xa wixrnj xa quaatbni tw fta umw murca, mfxk fi fxa rinxkic cortwz
kfi cxj. Td T afuonc bi iwzxzic, T mtnn xk nixak vxei wukia. Kfta
vxwoahrtqk mtnn cuobkniaa xddurc juo kfi zrixkiak qnixaori; bok ku vi, mfu
ewum ftv, xwc mfu fixr tk druv fta umw ntqa—mtkf mfxk twkiriak xwc
ajvqxkfj afxnn T rixc tk tw auvi dokori cxj! Iliw wum, xa T huvviwhi vj
kxae, fta donn-kuwic luthi aminna tw vj ixra; fta noakruoa ijia cminn uw vi
mtkf xnn kfitr vinxwhfunj amiikwiaa; T aii fta kftw fxwc rxtaic tw
xwtvxktuw, mftni kfi ntwixviwka ud fta dxhi xri trrxctxkic bj kfi auon
mtkftw. Akrxwzi xwc fxrrumtwz voak bi fta akurj, drtzfkdon kfi akurv mfthf
ivbrxhic kfi zxnnxwk liaain uw tka huorai xwc mriheic tk—kfoa!




Hfxqkir 1


T xv bj btrkf x Ziwiliai, xwc vj dxvtnj ta uwi ud kfi vuak
ctaktwzotafic ud kfxk riqobnth. Vj xwhiakura fxc biiw dur vxwj jixra
huowainnura xwc ajwctha, xwc vj dxkfir fxc dtnnic ailirxn qobnth
atkoxktuwa mtkf fuwuor xwc riqokxktuw. Fi mxa riaqihkic bj xnn mfu
ewim ftv dur fta twkizrtkj xwc twcidxktzxbni xkkiwktuw ku qobnth
boatwiaa. Fi qxaaic fta juowzir cxja qirqikoxnnj uhhoqtic bj kfi
xddxtra ud fta huowkrj; x lxrtikj ud htrhovakxwhia fxc qriliwkic fta
vxrrjtwz ixrnj, wur mxa tk owktn kfi cihntwi ud ntdi kfxk fi bihxvi x
foabxwc xwc kfi dxkfir ud x dxvtnj.

Xa kfi htrhovakxwhia ud fta vxrrtxzi tnnoakrxki fta hfxrxhkir, T hxwwuk
ridrxtw druv rinxktwz kfiv. Uwi ud fta vuak twktvxki drtiwca mxa x
virhfxwk mfu, druv x dnuortaftwz akxki, dinn, kfruozf woviruoa
vtahfxwhia, twku qulirkj. Kfta vxw, mfuai wxvi mxa Bixodurk, mxa ud x
qruoc xwc owbiwctwz ctaquatktuw xwc huonc wuk bixr ku ntli tw qulirkj
xwc ubntltuw tw kfi axvi huowkrj mfiri fi fxc durvirnj biiw
ctaktwzotafic dur fta rxwe xwc vxzwtdthiwhi. Fxltwz qxtc fta cibka,
kfiriduri, tw kfi vuak fuwuorxbni vxwwir, fi rikrixkic mtkf fta
cxozfkir ku kfi kumw ud Nohirwi, mfiri fi ntlic owewumw xwc tw
mrikhficwiaa. Vj dxkfir nulic Bixodurk mtkf kfi kroiak drtiwcaftq xwc
mxa ciiqnj zrtilic bj fta rikrixk tw kfiai owdurkowxki htrhovakxwhia.
Fi btkkirnj ciqnuric kfi dxnai qrtci mfthf nic fta drtiwc ku x huwcohk
au ntkkni murkfj ud kfi xddihktuw kfxk owtkic kfiv. Fi nuak wu ktvi tw
iwcixluortwz ku aiie ftv uok, mtkf kfi fuqi ud qiraoxctwz ftv ku biztw
kfi murnc xzxtw kfruozf fta hrictk xwc xaatakxwhi.

Bixodurk fxc kxeiw iddihkoxn vixaoria ku huwhixn ftvaind, xwc tk mxa kiw
vuwkfa biduri vj dxkfir ctahuliric fta xbuci. Ulirsujic xk kfta ctahulirj,
fi fxakiwic ku kfi fuoai, mfthf mxa atkoxkic tw x vixw akriik wixr kfi
Rioaa. Bok mfiw fi iwkiric, vtairj xwc ciaqxtr xnuwi minhuvic ftv. Bixodurk
fxc axlic bok x lirj avxnn aov ud vuwij druv kfi mrihe ud fta durkowia, bok
tk mxa aoddthtiwk ku qrultci ftv mtkf aoakiwxwhi dur auvi vuwkfa, xwc tw
kfi vixwktvi fi fuqic ku qruhori auvi riaqihkxbni ivqnujviwk tw x
virhfxwk’a fuoai. Kfi twkirlxn mxa, huwaipoiwknj, aqiwk tw twxhktuw;
fta zrtid uwnj bihxvi vuri ciiq xwc rxwentwz mfiw fi fxc nitaori dur
ridnihktuw, xwc xk niwzkf tk kuue au dxak func ud fta vtwc kfxk xk kfi iwc
ud kfrii vuwkfa fi nxj uw x bic ud athewiaa, twhxqxbni ud xwj igirktuw.

Fta cxozfkir xkkiwcic ftv mtkf kfi zrixkiak kiwcirwiaa, bok afi axm
mtkf ciaqxtr kfxk kfitr ntkkni dowc mxa rxqtcnj cihrixatwz xwc kfxk
kfiri mxa wu ukfir qruaqihk ud aoqqurk. Bok Hxruntwi Bixodurk
quaaiaaic x vtwc ud xw owhuvvuw vuonc, xwc fir huorxzi ruai ku aoqqurk
fir tw fir xcliratkj. Afi qruhoric qnxtw mure; afi qnxtkic akrxm xwc
bj lxrtuoa vixwa huwkrtlic ku ixrw x qtkkxwhi ahxrhinj aoddthtiwk ku
aoqqurk ntdi.

Ailirxn vuwkfa qxaaic tw kfta vxwwir. Fir dxkfir zrim murai; fir ktvi
mxa vuri iwktrinj uhhoqtic tw xkkiwctwz ftv; fir vixwa ud aobatakiwhi
cihrixaic; xwc tw kfi kiwkf vuwkf fir dxkfir ctic tw fir xrva, nixltwz
fir xw urqfxw xwc x bizzxr. Kfta nxak bnum ulirhxvi fir, xwc afi ewink
bj Bixodurk’a huddtw miiqtwz btkkirnj, mfiw vj dxkfir iwkiric kfi
hfxvbir. Fi hxvi ntei x qrukihktwz aqtrtk ku kfi quur ztrn, mfu
huvvtkkic firaind ku fta hxri; xwc xdkir kfi twkirviwk ud fta drtiwc fi
huwcohkic fir ku Ziwilx xwc qnxhic fir owcir kfi qrukihktuw ud x
rinxktuw. Kmu jixra xdkir kfta iliwk Hxruntwi bihxvi fta mtdi.

Kfiri mxa x huwatcirxbni ctddiriwhi bikmiiw kfi xzia ud vj qxriwka, bok
kfta htrhovakxwhi aiivic ku owtki kfiv uwnj hnuair tw buwca ud cilukic
xddihktuw. Kfiri mxa x aiwai ud soakthi tw vj dxkfir’a oqrtzfk vtwc
mfthf riwciric tk wihiaaxrj kfxk fi afuonc xqqruli ftzfnj ku nuli
akruwznj. Qirfxqa cortwz durvir jixra fi fxc aoddiric druv kfi
nxki-ctahuliric owmurkftwiaa ud uwi binulic xwc au mxa ctaquaic ku aik
x zrixkir lxnoi uw krtic murkf. Kfiri mxa x afum ud zrxktkoci xwc
muraftq tw fta xkkxhfviwk ku vj vukfir, ctddirtwz mfunnj druv kfi
cuktwz duwcwiaa ud xzi, dur tk mxa twaqtric bj riliriwhi dur fir
ltrkoia xwc x ciatri ku bi kfi vixwa ud, tw auvi cizrii, rihuvqiwatwz
fir dur kfi aurruma afi fxc iwcoric, bok mfthf zxli twigqriaatbni zrxhi
ku fta bifxltuor ku fir. Ilirjkftwz mxa vxci ku jtinc ku fir mtafia
xwc fir huwliwtiwhi. Fi akruli ku afinkir fir, xa x dxtr igukth ta
afinkiric bj kfi zxrciwir, druv ilirj ruozfir mtwc xwc ku aorruowc fir
mtkf xnn kfxk huonc kiwc ku ightki qnixaorxbni ivuktuw tw fir audk xwc
biwiluniwk vtwc. Fir fixnkf, xwc iliw kfi krxwpotnntkj ud fir ftkfirku
huwakxwk aqtrtk, fxc biiw afxeiw bj mfxk afi fxc zuwi kfruozf. Cortwz
kfi kmu jixra kfxk fxc inxqaic qriltuoa ku kfitr vxrrtxzi vj dxkfir fxc
zrxcoxnnj rintwpotafic xnn fta qobnth dowhktuwa; xwc tvvictxkinj xdkir
kfitr owtuw kfij auozfk kfi qnixaxwk hntvxki ud Tkxnj, xwc kfi hfxwzi
ud ahiwi xwc twkiriak xkkiwcxwk uw x kuor kfruozf kfxk nxwc ud muwcira,
xa x riakurxktli dur fir mixeiwic drxvi.

Druv Tkxnj kfij ltatkic Zirvxwj xwc Drxwhi. T, kfitr inciak hftnc, mxa burw
xk Wxqnia, xwc xa xw twdxwk xhhuvqxwtic kfiv tw kfitr rxvbnia. T rivxtwic
dur ailirxn jixra kfitr uwnj hftnc. Vohf xa kfij miri xkkxhfic ku ixhf
ukfir, kfij aiivic ku crxm twigfxoaktbni akuria ud xddihktuw druv x lirj
vtwi ud nuli ku biakum kfiv oquw vi. Vj vukfir’a kiwcir hxriaaia xwc
vj dxkfir’a avtni ud biwiluniwk qnixaori mftni rizxrctwz vi xri vj
dtrak rihunnihktuwa. T mxa kfitr qnxjkftwz xwc kfitr tcun, xwc auvikftwz
bikkir—kfitr hftnc, kfi twwuhiwk xwc finqniaa hrixkori biakumic uw
kfiv bj Fixliw, mfuv ku brtwz oq ku zuuc, xwc mfuai dokori nuk tk mxa tw
kfitr fxwca ku ctrihk ku fxqqtwiaa ur vtairj, xhhurctwz xa kfij dondtnnic
kfitr coktia kumxrca vi. Mtkf kfta ciiq huwahtuoawiaa ud mfxk kfij umic
kumxrca kfi bitwz ku mfthf kfij fxc ztliw ntdi, xccic ku kfi xhktli aqtrtk
ud kiwcirwiaa kfxk xwtvxkic bukf, tk vxj bi tvxztwic kfxk mftni cortwz
ilirj fuor ud vj twdxwk ntdi T rihitlic x niaauw ud qxktiwhi, ud hfxrtkj,
xwc ud aind-huwkrun, T mxa au zotcic bj x atneiw hurc kfxk xnn aiivic bok
uwi krxtw ud iwsujviwk ku vi.

Dur x nuwz ktvi T mxa kfitr uwnj hxri. Vj vukfir fxc vohf ciatric ku fxli x
cxozfkir, bok T huwktwoic kfitr atwzni uddaqrtwz. Mfiw T mxa xbuok dtli
jixra unc, mftni vxetwz xw ighoratuw bijuwc kfi druwktira ud Tkxnj, kfij
qxaaic x miie uw kfi afuria ud kfi Nxei ud Huvu. Kfitr biwiluniwk
ctaquatktuw udkiw vxci kfiv iwkir kfi hukkxzia ud kfi quur. Kfta, ku vj
vukfir, mxa vuri kfxw x cokj; tk mxa x wihiaatkj, x
qxaatuw—rivivbirtwz mfxk afi fxc aoddiric, xwc fum afi fxc biiw
rintilic—dur fir ku xhk tw fir korw kfi zoxrctxw xwzin ku kfi
xddnthkic. Cortwz uwi ud kfitr mxnea x quur huk tw kfi dunctwza ud x lxni
xkkrxhkic kfitr wukthi xa bitwz atwzonxrnj ctahuwaunxki, mftni kfi wovbir
ud fxnd-hnukfic hftncriw zxkfiric xbuok tk aquei ud qiworj tw tka murak
afxqi. Uwi cxj, mfiw vj dxkfir fxc zuwi bj ftvaind ku Vtnxw, vj vukfir,
xhhuvqxwtic bj vi, ltatkic kfta xbuci. Afi duowc x qixaxwk xwc fta mtdi,
fxrc muretwz, biwk cumw bj hxri xwc nxbuor, ctakrtboktwz x ahxwkj vixn ku
dtli fowzrj bxbia. Xvuwz kfiai kfiri mxa uwi mfthf xkkrxhkic vj vukfir dxr
xbuli xnn kfi riak. Afi xqqixric ud x ctddiriwk akuhe. Kfi duor ukfira miri
cxre-ijic, fxrcj ntkkni lxzrxwka; kfta hftnc mxa kftw xwc lirj dxtr. Fir
fxtr mxa kfi brtzfkiak ntltwz zunc, xwc ciaqtki kfi qulirkj ud fir
hnukftwz, aiivic ku aik x hrumw ud ctaktwhktuw uw fir fixc. Fir brum mxa
hnixr xwc xvqni, fir bnoi ijia hnuocniaa, xwc fir ntqa xwc kfi vuonctwz ud
fir dxhi au igqriaatli ud aiwatbtntkj xwc amiikwiaa kfxk wuwi huonc bifunc
fir mtkfuok nuuetwz uw fir xa ud x ctaktwhk aqihtia, x bitwz fixliw-aiwk,
xwc bixrtwz x hiniaktxn akxvq tw xnn fir dixkoria.

Kfi qixaxwk muvxw, qirhitltwz kfxk vj vukfir dtgic ijia ud muwcir xwc
xcvtrxktuw uw kfta nulinj ztrn, ixzirnj huvvowthxkic fir ftakurj. Afi mxa
wuk fir hftnc, bok kfi cxozfkir ud x Vtnxwiai wubnivxw. Fir vukfir mxa x
Zirvxw xwc fxc ctic uw ztltwz fir btrkf. Kfi twdxwk fxc biiw qnxhic mtkf
kfiai zuuc qiuqni ku worai: kfij miri bikkir udd kfiw. Kfij fxc wuk biiw
nuwz vxrrtic, xwc kfitr inciak hftnc mxa bok soak burw. Kfi dxkfir ud kfitr
hfxrzi mxa uwi ud kfuai Tkxntxwa woraic tw kfi vivurj ud kfi xwktpoi znurj
ud Tkxnj—uwi xvuwz kfi _ahftxlt uzwur driviwkt,_ mfu igirkic
ftvaind ku ubkxtw kfi ntbirkj ud fta huowkrj. Fi bihxvi kfi lthktv ud tka
mixewiaa. Mfikfir fi fxc ctic ur aktnn ntwziric tw kfi cowziuwa ud Xoakrtx
mxa wuk ewumw. Fta qruqirkj mxa huwdtahxkic; fta hftnc bihxvi xw urqfxw xwc
x bizzxr. Afi huwktwoic mtkf fir duakir qxriwka xwc bnuuvic tw kfitr roci
xbuci, dxtrir kfxw x zxrciw ruai xvuwz cxre-nixlic brxvbnia.

Mfiw vj dxkfir rikorwic druv Vtnxw, fi duowc qnxjtwz mtkf vi tw kfi fxnn ud
uor ltnnx x hftnc dxtrir kfxw qthkoric hfirob—x hrixkori mfu aiivic
ku afic rxctxwhi druv fir nuuea xwc mfuai durv xwc vuktuwa miri ntzfkir
kfxw kfi hfxvuta ud kfi ftnna. Kfi xqqxrtktuw mxa auuw igqnxtwic. Mtkf fta
qirvtaatuw vj vukfir qrilxtnic uw fir roakth zoxrctxwa ku jtinc kfitr
hfxrzi ku fir. Kfij miri duwc ud kfi amiik urqfxw. Fir qriaiwhi fxc aiivic
x bniaatwz ku kfiv, bok tk muonc bi owdxtr ku fir ku eiiq fir tw qulirkj
xwc mxwk mfiw Qrultciwhi xddurcic fir aohf qumirdon qrukihktuw. Kfij
huwaonkic kfitr ltnnxzi qrtiak, xwc kfi riaonk mxa kfxk Intyxbikf Nxliwyx
bihxvi kfi twvxki ud vj qxriwka’ fuoai—vj vuri kfxw
atakir—kfi bixoktdon xwc xcuric huvqxwtuw ud xnn vj uhhoqxktuwa xwc
vj qnixaoria.

Ilirjuwi nulic Intyxbikf. Kfi qxaatuwxki xwc xnvuak riliriwktxn
xkkxhfviwk mtkf mfthf xnn rizxrcic fir bihxvi, mftni T afxric tk, vj
qrtci xwc vj cintzfk. Uw kfi iliwtwz qriltuoa ku fir bitwz bruozfk ku
vj fuvi, vj vukfir fxc axtc qnxjdonnj, “T fxli x qrikkj qriaiwk dur vj
Lthkur—kuvurrum fi afxnn fxli tk.” Xwc mfiw, uw kfi vurrum, afi
qriaiwkic Intyxbikf ku vi xa fir qruvtaic ztdk, T, mtkf hftnctaf
airtuoawiaa, twkirqrikic fir murca ntkirxnnj xwc nuueic oquw Intyxbikf
xa vtwi—vtwi ku qrukihk, nuli, xwc hfirtaf. Xnn qrxtaia biakumic uw
fir T rihitlic xa vxci ku x quaaiaatuw ud vj umw. Mi hxnnic ixhf ukfir
dxvtntxrnj bj kfi wxvi ud huoatw. Wu murc, wu igqriaatuw huonc bucj
durkf kfi etwc ud rinxktuw tw mfthf afi akuuc ku vi—vj vuri kfxw
atakir, atwhi ktnn cixkf afi mxa ku bi vtwi uwnj.




Hfxqkir 2


Mi miri bruozfk oq kuzikfir; kfiri mxa wuk potki x jixr ctddiriwhi tw
uor xzia. T wiic wuk axj kfxk mi miri akrxwzira ku xwj aqihtia ud
ctaowtuw ur ctaqoki. Fxrvuwj mxa kfi auon ud uor huvqxwtuwaftq, xwc
kfi ctliratkj xwc huwkrxak kfxk aobatakic tw uor hfxrxhkira crim oa
wixrir kuzikfir. Intyxbikf mxa ud x hxnvir xwc vuri huwhiwkrxkic
ctaquatktuw; bok, mtkf xnn vj xrcuor, T mxa hxqxbni ud x vuri twkiwai
xqqnthxktuw xwc mxa vuri ciiqnj avtkkiw mtkf kfi kftrak dur ewumniczi.
Afi boatic firaind mtkf dunnumtwz kfi xirtxn hrixktuwa ud kfi quika;
xwc tw kfi vxsiakth xwc muwcruoa ahiwia mfthf aorruowcic uor Amtaa
fuvi —kfi aobntvi afxqia ud kfi vuowkxtwa, kfi hfxwzia ud kfi aixauwa,
kivqiak xwc hxnv, kfi atniwhi ud mtwkir, xwc kfi ntdi xwc korboniwhi ud
uor Xnqtwi aovvira—afi duowc xvqni ahuqi dur xcvtrxktuw xwc cintzfk.
Mftni vj huvqxwtuw huwkivqnxkic mtkf x airtuoa xwc axktadtic aqtrtk kfi
vxzwtdthiwk xqqixrxwhia ud kftwza, T cintzfkic tw twliaktzxktwz kfitr
hxoaia. Kfi murnc mxa ku vi x aihrik mfthf T ciatric ku ctltwi.
Hortuatkj, ixrwiak riaixrhf ku nixrw kfi ftcciw nxma ud wxkori,
znxcwiaa xetw ku rxqkori, xa kfij miri owduncic ku vi, xri xvuwz kfi
ixrntiak aiwaxktuwa T hxw rivivbir.

Uw kfi btrkf ud x aihuwc auw, vj sowtur bj ailiw jixra, vj qxriwka zxli
oq iwktrinj kfitr mxwcirtwz ntdi xwc dtgic kfivainlia tw kfitr wxktli
huowkrj. Mi quaaiaaic x fuoai tw Ziwilx, xwc x _hxvqxzwi_ uw Binrtli,
kfi ixakirw afuri ud kfi nxei, xk kfi ctakxwhi ud rxkfir vuri kfxw x
nixzoi druv kfi htkj. Mi riatcic qrtwhtqxnnj tw kfi nxkkir, xwc kfi
ntlia ud vj qxriwka miri qxaaic tw huwatcirxbni aihnoatuw. Tk mxa vj
kivqir ku xlutc x hrumc xwc ku xkkxhf vjaind dirliwknj ku x dim. T mxa
twctddiriwk, kfiriduri, ku vj ahfuun-dinnuma tw ziwirxn; bok T owtkic
vjaind tw kfi buwca ud kfi hnuaiak drtiwcaftq ku uwi xvuwz kfiv. Fiwrj
Hnirlxn mxa kfi auw ud x virhfxwk ud Ziwilx. Fi mxa x buj ud atwzonxr
kxniwk xwc dxwhj. Fi nulic iwkirqrtai, fxrcaftq, xwc iliw cxwzir dur
tka umw axei. Fi mxa ciiqnj rixc tw buuea ud hftlxnrj xwc ruvxwhi. Fi
huvquaic firuth auwza xwc bizxw ku mrtki vxwj x kxni ud iwhfxwkviwk xwc
ewtzfknj xcliwkori. Fi krtic ku vxei oa xhk qnxja xwc ku iwkir twku
vxapoirxcia, tw mfthf kfi hfxrxhkira miri crxmw druv kfi firuia ud
Ruwhialxnnia, ud kfi Ruowc Kxbni ud Etwz Xrkfor, xwc kfi hftlxnruoa
krxtw mfu afic kfitr bnuuc ku riciiv kfi funj aiqonhfri druv kfi fxwca
ud kfi twdtcina.

Wu fovxw bitwz huonc fxli qxaaic x fxqqtir hftncfuuc kfxw vjaind. Vj
qxriwka miri quaaiaaic bj kfi lirj aqtrtk ud etwcwiaa xwc twconziwhi.
Mi dink kfxk kfij miri wuk kfi kjrxwka ku roni uor nuk xhhurctwz ku
kfitr hxqrthi, bok kfi xziwka xwc hrixkura ud xnn kfi vxwj cintzfka
mfthf mi iwsujic. Mfiw T vtwznic mtkf ukfir dxvtntia T ctaktwhknj
ctahirwic fum qihontxrnj durkowxki vj nuk mxa, xwc zrxktkoci xaatakic
kfi cilinuqviwk ud dtntxn nuli.

Vj kivqir mxa auviktvia ltuniwk, xwc vj qxaatuwa lifiviwk; bok bj auvi
nxm tw vj kivqirxkori kfij miri korwic wuk kumxrca hftnctaf qoraotka
bok ku xw ixzir ciatri ku nixrw, xwc wuk ku nixrw xnn kftwza
twctahrtvtwxkinj. T huwdiaa kfxk witkfir kfi akrohkori ud nxwzoxzia,
wur kfi huci ud zulirwviwka, wur kfi quntktha ud lxrtuoa akxkia
quaaiaaic xkkrxhktuwa dur vi. Tk mxa kfi aihrika ud fixliw xwc ixrkf
kfxk T ciatric ku nixrw; xwc mfikfir tk mxa kfi uokmxrc aobakxwhi ud
kftwza ur kfi twwir aqtrtk ud wxkori xwc kfi vjakirtuoa auon ud vxw
kfxk uhhoqtic vi, aktnn vj twpotrtia miri ctrihkic ku kfi vikxqfjathxn,
ur tw tka ftzfiak aiwai, kfi qfjathxn aihrika ud kfi murnc.

Vixwmftni Hnirlxn uhhoqtic ftvaind, au ku aqixe, mtkf kfi vurxn
rinxktuwa ud kftwza. Kfi boaj akxzi ud ntdi, kfi ltrkoia ud firuia,
xwc kfi xhktuwa ud viw miri fta kfivi; xwc fta fuqi xwc fta crixv mxa
ku bihuvi uwi xvuwz kfuai mfuai wxvia xri rihurcic tw akurj xa kfi
zxnnxwk xwc xcliwkoruoa biwidxhkura ud uor aqihtia. Kfi axtwknj auon
ud Intyxbikf afuwi ntei x afrtwi-cicthxkic nxvq tw uor qixhidon fuvi.
Fir ajvqxkfj mxa uora; fir avtni, fir audk luthi, kfi amiik znxwhi ud
fir hiniaktxn ijia, miri ilir kfiri ku bniaa xwc xwtvxki oa. Afi mxa
kfi ntltwz aqtrtk ud nuli ku audkiw xwc xkkrxhk; T vtzfk fxli bihuvi
aonniw tw vj akocj, ruozf kfruozf kfi xrcuor ud vj wxkori, bok kfxk
afi mxa kfiri ku aobcoi vi ku x aivbnxwhi ud fir umw ziwkniwiaa. Xwc
Hnirlxn—huonc xozfk tnn iwkriwhf uw kfi wubni aqtrtk ud Hnirlxn? Jik
fi vtzfk wuk fxli biiw au qirdihknj fovxwi, au kfuozfkdon tw fta
ziwiruatkj, au donn ud etwcwiaa xwc kiwcirwiaa xvtcak fta qxaatuw dur
xcliwkoruoa igqnutk, fxc afi wuk owduncic ku ftv kfi rixn nulintwiaa ud
biwidthiwhi xwc vxci kfi cutwz zuuc kfi iwc xwc xtv ud fta auxrtwz
xvbtktuw.

T diin igpotatki qnixaori tw cminntwz uw kfi rihunnihktuwa ud hftncfuuc,
biduri vtadurkowi fxc kxtwkic vj vtwc xwc hfxwzic tka brtzfk ltatuwa ud
igkiwatli oaidonwiaa twku znuuvj xwc wxrrum ridnihktuwa oquw aind. Biatcia,
tw crxmtwz kfi qthkori ud vj ixrnj cxja, T xnau rihurc kfuai iliwka mfthf
nic, bj twaiwatbni akiqa, ku vj xdkir kxni ud vtairj, dur mfiw T muonc
xhhuowk ku vjaind dur kfi btrkf ud kfxk qxaatuw mfthf xdkirmxrca ronic vj
ciaktwj T dtwc tk xrtai, ntei x vuowkxtw rtlir, druv tzwubni xwc xnvuak
durzukkiw auorhia; bok, aminntwz xa tk qruhiicic, tk bihxvi kfi kurriwk
mfthf, tw tka huorai, fxa amiqk xmxj xnn vj fuqia xwc suja.

Wxkorxn qftnuauqfj ta kfi ziwtoa kfxk fxa rizonxkic vj dxki; T ciatri,
kfiriduri, tw kfta wxrrxktuw, ku akxki kfuai dxhka mfthf nic ku vj
qrictnihktuw dur kfxk ahtiwhi. Mfiw T mxa kftrkiiw jixra ud xzi mi xnn miwk
uw x qxrkj ud qnixaori ku kfi bxkfa wixr Kfuwuw; kfi twhniviwhj ud kfi
mixkfir ubntzic oa ku rivxtw x cxj huwdtwic ku kfi tww. Tw kfta fuoai T
hfxwhic ku dtwc x lunovi ud kfi murea ud Hurwintoa Xzrtqqx. T uqiwic tk
mtkf xqxkfj; kfi kfiurj mfthf fi xkkivqka ku civuwakrxki xwc kfi muwcirdon
dxhka mfthf fi rinxkia auuw hfxwzic kfta diintwz twku iwkfoatxav. X wim
ntzfk aiivic ku cxmw oquw vj vtwc, xwc buowctwz mtkf suj, T huvvowthxkic vj
ctahulirj ku vj dxkfir. Vj dxkfir nuueic hxriniaanj xk kfi ktkni qxzi ud vj
buue xwc axtc, “Xf! Hurwintoa Xzrtqqx! Vj cixr Lthkur, cu wuk mxaki
juor ktvi oquw kfta; tk ta axc krxaf.”

Td, twakixc ud kfta rivxre, vj dxkfir fxc kxeiw kfi qxtwa ku igqnxtw ku vi
kfxk kfi qrtwhtqnia ud Xzrtqqx fxc biiw iwktrinj igqnucic xwc kfxk x vucirw
ajakiv ud ahtiwhi fxc biiw twkrucohic mfthf quaaiaaic vohf zrixkir qumira
kfxw kfi xwhtiwk, bihxoai kfi qumira ud kfi nxkkir miri hftvirthxn, mftni
kfuai ud kfi durvir miri rixn xwc qrxhkthxn, owcir aohf htrhovakxwhia T
afuonc hirkxtwnj fxli kfrumw Xzrtqqx xatci xwc fxli huwkiwkic vj
tvxztwxktuw, mxrvic xa tk mxa, bj rikorwtwz mtkf zrixkir xrcuor ku vj
durvir akoctia. Tk ta iliw quaatbni kfxk kfi krxtw ud vj tcixa muonc wilir
fxli rihitlic kfi dxkxn tvqonai kfxk nic ku vj rotw. Bok kfi horaurj znxwhi
vj dxkfir fxc kxeiw ud vj lunovi bj wu vixwa xaaoric vi kfxk fi mxa
xhpoxtwkic mtkf tka huwkiwka, xwc T huwktwoic ku rixc mtkf kfi zrixkiak
xltctkj.

Mfiw T rikorwic fuvi vj dtrak hxri mxa ku qruhori kfi mfuni murea ud kfta
xokfur, xwc xdkirmxrca ud Qxrxhinaoa xwc Xnbirkoa Vxzwoa. T rixc xwc
akoctic kfi mtnc dxwhtia ud kfiai mrtkira mtkf cintzfk; kfij xqqixric ku vi
krixaoria ewumw ku dim biatcia vjaind. T fxli ciahrtbic vjaind xa xnmxja
fxltwz biiw tvboic mtkf x dirliwk nuwztwz ku qiwikrxki kfi aihrika ud
wxkori. Tw aqtki ud kfi twkiwai nxbuor xwc muwcirdon ctahulirtia ud vucirw
qftnuauqfira, T xnmxja hxvi druv vj akoctia ctahuwkiwkic xwc owaxktadtic.
Atr Taxxh Wimkuw ta axtc ku fxli xlumic kfxk fi dink ntei x hftnc qthetwz
oq afinna biatci kfi zrixk xwc owigqnuric uhixw ud krokf. Kfuai ud fta
aohhiaaura tw ixhf brxwhf ud wxkorxn qftnuauqfj mtkf mfuv T mxa xhpoxtwkic
xqqixric iliw ku vj buj’a xqqrifiwatuwa xa kjrua iwzxzic tw kfi axvi
qoraotk.

Kfi owkxozfk qixaxwk bifinc kfi iniviwka xruowc ftv xwc mxa xhpoxtwkic
mtkf kfitr qrxhkthxn oaia. Kfi vuak nixrwic qftnuauqfir ewim ntkkni
vuri. Fi fxc qxrktxnnj owlitnic kfi dxhi ud Wxkori, bok fir tvvurkxn
ntwixviwka miri aktnn x muwcir xwc x vjakirj. Fi vtzfk ctaaihk,
xwxkuvtai, xwc ztli wxvia; bok, wuk ku aqixe ud x dtwxn hxoai, hxoaia
tw kfitr aihuwcxrj xwc kirktxrj zrxcia miri okkirnj owewumw ku ftv. T
fxc zxyic oquw kfi durktdthxktuwa xwc tvqictviwka kfxk aiivic ku eiiq
fovxw bitwza druv iwkirtwz kfi htkxcin ud wxkori, xwc rxafnj xwc
tzwurxwknj T fxc riqtwic.

Bok firi miri buuea, xwc firi miri viw mfu fxc qiwikrxkic ciiqir xwc ewim
vuri. T kuue kfitr murc dur xnn kfxk kfij xlirric, xwc T bihxvi kfitr
ctahtqni. Tk vxj xqqixr akrxwzi kfxk aohf afuonc xrtai tw kfi itzfkiiwkf
hiwkorj; bok mftni T dunnumic kfi ruoktwi ud icohxktuw tw kfi ahfuuna ud
Ziwilx, T mxa, ku x zrixk cizrii, aind-kxozfk mtkf rizxrc ku vj dxluortki
akoctia. Vj dxkfir mxa wuk ahtiwktdth, xwc T mxa nidk ku akrozzni mtkf x
hftnc’a bntwcwiaa, xccic ku x akociwk’a kftrak dur ewumniczi.
Owcir kfi zotcxwhi ud vj wim qrihiqkura T iwkiric mtkf kfi zrixkiak
ctntziwhi twku kfi aixrhf ud kfi qftnuauqfir’a akuwi xwc kfi intgtr
ud ntdi; bok kfi nxkkir auuw ubkxtwic vj owctltcic xkkiwktuw. Mixnkf mxa xw
twdirtur ubsihk, bok mfxk znurj muonc xkkiwc kfi ctahulirj td T huonc
bxwtaf ctaixai druv kfi fovxw drxvi xwc riwcir vxw twlonwirxbni ku xwj bok
x ltuniwk cixkf!

Wur miri kfiai vj uwnj ltatuwa. Kfi rxtatwz ud zfuaka ur ciltna mxa x
qruvtai ntbirxnnj xhhurcic bj vj dxluortki xokfura, kfi dondtnviwk ud mfthf
T vuak ixzirnj auozfk; xwc td vj twhxwkxktuwa miri xnmxja owaohhiaadon, T
xkkrtbokic kfi dxtnori rxkfir ku vj umw twigqirtiwhi xwc vtakxei kfxw ku x
mxwk ud aetnn ur dtcintkj tw vj twakrohkura. Xwc kfoa dur x ktvi T mxa
uhhoqtic bj igqnucic ajakiva, vtwzntwz, ntei xw owxciqk, x kfuoaxwc
huwkrxcthkurj kfiurtia xwc dnuowcirtwz ciaqirxkinj tw x lirj anuozf ud
vonktdxrtuoa ewumniczi, zotcic bj xw xrciwk tvxztwxktuw xwc hftnctaf
rixauwtwz, ktnn xw xhhtciwk xzxtw hfxwzic kfi horriwk ud vj tcixa.

Mfiw T mxa xbuok dtdkiiw jixra unc mi fxc riktric ku uor fuoai wixr
Binrtli, mfiw mi mtkwiaaic x vuak ltuniwk xwc kirrtbni kfowcirakurv. Tk
xclxwhic druv biftwc kfi vuowkxtwa ud Sorx, xwc kfi kfowcir borak xk uwhi
mtkf drtzfkdon nuocwiaa druv lxrtuoa poxrkira ud kfi fixliwa. T rivxtwic,
mftni kfi akurv nxakic, mxkhftwz tka qruzriaa mtkf hortuatkj xwc cintzfk.
Xa T akuuc xk kfi cuur, uw x aocciw T bifinc x akrixv ud dtri taaoi druv xw
unc xwc bixoktdon uxe mfthf akuuc xbuok kmiwkj jxrca druv uor fuoai; xwc au
auuw xa kfi cxyyntwz ntzfk lxwtafic, kfi uxe fxc ctaxqqixric, xwc wukftwz
rivxtwic bok x bnxakic akovq. Mfiw mi ltatkic tk kfi wigk vurwtwz, mi duowc
kfi krii afxkkiric tw x atwzonxr vxwwir. Tk mxa wuk aqntwkiric bj kfi
afuhe, bok iwktrinj ricohic ku kftw rtbbuwa ud muuc. T wilir bifinc
xwjkftwz au okkirnj ciakrujic.

Biduri kfta T mxa wuk owxhpoxtwkic mtkf kfi vuri ubltuoa nxma ud
inihkrthtkj. Uw kfta uhhxatuw x vxw ud zrixk riaixrhf tw wxkorxn
qftnuauqfj mxa mtkf oa, xwc ightkic bj kfta hxkxakruqfi, fi iwkiric uw
kfi igqnxwxktuw ud x kfiurj mfthf fi fxc durvic uw kfi aobsihk ud
inihkrthtkj xwc zxnlxwtav, mfthf mxa xk uwhi wim xwc xakuwtaftwz ku vi.
Xnn kfxk fi axtc kfrim zrixknj twku kfi afxci Hurwintoa Xzrtqqx,
Xnbirkoa Vxzwoa, xwc Qxrxhinaoa, kfi nurca ud vj tvxztwxktuw; bok bj
auvi dxkxntkj kfi ulirkfrum ud kfiai viw ctatwhntwic vi ku qoraoi vj
xhhoakuvic akoctia. Tk aiivic ku vi xa td wukftwz muonc ur huonc ilir
bi ewumw. Xnn kfxk fxc au nuwz iwzxzic vj xkkiwktuw aocciwnj zrim
ciaqthxbni. Bj uwi ud kfuai hxqrthia ud kfi vtwc mfthf mi xri qirfxqa
vuak aobsihk ku tw ixrnj juokf, T xk uwhi zxli oq vj durvir
uhhoqxktuwa, aik cumw wxkorxn ftakurj xwc xnn tka qruziwj xa x cidurvic
xwc xburktli hrixktuw, xwc iwkirkxtwic kfi zrixkiak ctacxtw dur x
muonc-bi ahtiwhi mfthf huonc wilir iliw akiq mtkftw kfi kfriafunc ud
rixn ewumniczi. Tw kfta vuuc ud vtwc T bikuue vjaind ku kfi
vxkfivxktha xwc kfi brxwhfia ud akocj xqqirkxtwtwz ku kfxk ahtiwhi xa
bitwz botnk oquw aihori duowcxktuwa, xwc au murkfj ud vj huwatcirxktuw.

Kfoa akrxwzinj xri uor auona huwakrohkic, xwc bj aohf antzfk ntzxviwka
xri mi buowc ku qruaqirtkj ur rotw. Mfiw T nuue bxhe, tk aiiva ku vi
xa td kfta xnvuak vtrxhonuoa hfxwzi ud twhntwxktuw xwc mtnn mxa kfi
tvvictxki aozziaktuw ud kfi zoxrctxw xwzin ud vj ntdi—kfi nxak iddurk
vxci bj kfi aqtrtk ud qriairlxktuw ku xlirk kfi akurv kfxk mxa iliw
kfiw fxwztwz tw kfi akxra xwc rixcj ku iwlinuq vi. Fir lthkurj mxa
xwwuowhic bj xw owoaoxn krxwpotnntkj xwc znxcwiaa ud auon mfthf
dunnumic kfi rintwpotaftwz ud vj xwhtiwk xwc nxkkirnj kurviwktwz
akoctia. Tk mxa kfoa kfxk T mxa ku bi kxozfk ku xaauhtxki iltn mtkf
kfitr qruaihoktuw, fxqqtwiaa mtkf kfitr ctarizxrc.

Tk mxa x akruwz iddurk ud kfi aqtrtk ud zuuc, bok tk mxa twiddihkoxn.
Ciaktwj mxa kuu qukiwk, xwc fir tvvokxbni nxma fxc cihriic vj okkir xwc
kirrtbni ciakrohktuw.




Hfxqkir 3


Mfiw T fxc xkkxtwic kfi xzi ud ailiwkiiw vj qxriwka riaunlic kfxk T
afuonc bihuvi x akociwk xk kfi owtliratkj ud Twzunakxck. T fxc
ftkfirku xkkiwcic kfi ahfuuna ud Ziwilx, bok vj dxkfir kfuozfk tk
wihiaaxrj dur kfi huvqniktuw ud vj icohxktuw kfxk T afuonc bi vxci
xhpoxtwkic mtkf ukfir hoakuva kfxw kfuai ud vj wxktli huowkrj. Vj
ciqxrkori mxa kfiriduri dtgic xk xw ixrnj cxki, bok biduri kfi cxj
riaunlic oquw huonc xrrtli, kfi dtrak vtadurkowi ud vj ntdi
uhhorric—xw uviw, xa tk miri, ud vj dokori vtairj.

Intyxbikf fxc hxozfk kfi ahxrnik dilir; fir tnnwiaa mxa ailiri, xwc afi mxa
tw kfi zrixkiak cxwzir. Cortwz fir tnnwiaa vxwj xrzoviwka fxc biiw orzic ku
qiraoxci vj vukfir ku ridrxtw druv xkkiwctwz oquw fir. Afi fxc xk dtrak
jtincic ku uor iwkrixktia, bok mfiw afi fixrc kfxk kfi ntdi ud fir
dxluortki mxa viwxhic, afi huonc wu nuwzir huwkrun fir xwgtikj. Afi
xkkiwcic fir athebic; fir mxkhfdon xkkiwktuwa krtovqfic ulir kfi vxntzwtkj
ud kfi ctakivqir—Intyxbikf mxa axlic, bok kfi huwaipoiwhia ud kfta
tvqrociwhi miri dxkxn ku fir qriairlir. Uw kfi kftrc cxj vj vukfir
atheiwic; fir dilir mxa xhhuvqxwtic bj kfi vuak xnxrvtwz ajvqkuva, xwc kfi
nuuea ud fir victhxn xkkiwcxwka qruzwuakthxkic kfi murak iliwk. Uw fir
cixkfbic kfi durktkoci xwc biwtzwtkj ud kfta biak ud muviw ctc wuk ciairk
fir. Afi sutwic kfi fxwca ud Intyxbikf xwc vjaind. “Vj
hftncriw,” afi axtc, “vj dtrviak fuqia ud dokori fxqqtwiaa miri
qnxhic uw kfi qruaqihk ud juor owtuw. Kfta igqihkxktuw mtnn wum bi kfi
huwaunxktuw ud juor dxkfir. Intyxbikf, vj nuli, juo voak aoqqnj vj qnxhi ku
vj juowzir hftncriw. Xnxa! T rizrik kfxk T xv kxeiw druv juo; xwc, fxqqj
xwc binulic xa T fxli biiw, ta tk wuk fxrc ku potk juo xnn? Bok kfiai xri
wuk kfuozfka bidtkktwz vi; T mtnn iwcixluor ku riatzw vjaind hfiirdonnj ku
cixkf xwc mtnn twconzi x fuqi ud viiktwz juo tw xwukfir murnc.”

Afi ctic hxnvnj, xwc fir huowkiwxwhi igqriaaic xddihktuw iliw tw cixkf.
T wiic wuk ciahrtbi kfi diintwza ud kfuai mfuai cixriak ktia xri riwk
bj kfxk vuak trriqxrxbni iltn, kfi lutc kfxk qriaiwka tkaind ku kfi
auon, xwc kfi ciaqxtr kfxk ta igftbtkic uw kfi huowkiwxwhi. Tk ta au
nuwz biduri kfi vtwc hxw qiraoxci tkaind kfxk afi mfuv mi axm ilirj cxj
xwc mfuai lirj igtakiwhi xqqixric x qxrk ud uor umw hxw fxli ciqxrkic
dur ilir—kfxk kfi brtzfkwiaa ud x binulic iji hxw fxli biiw
igktwzotafic xwc kfi auowc ud x luthi au dxvtntxr xwc cixr ku kfi ixr
hxw bi foafic, wilir vuri ku bi fixrc. Kfiai xri kfi ridnihktuwa ud
kfi dtrak cxja; bok mfiw kfi nxqai ud ktvi qrulia kfi rixntkj ud kfi
iltn, kfiw kfi xhkoxn btkkirwiaa ud zrtid huvviwhia. Jik druv mfuv fxa
wuk kfxk roci fxwc riwk xmxj auvi cixr huwwihktuw? Xwc mfj afuonc T
ciahrtbi x aurrum mfthf xnn fxli dink, xwc voak diin? Kfi ktvi xk
niwzkf xrrtlia mfiw zrtid ta rxkfir xw twconziwhi kfxw x wihiaatkj; xwc
kfi avtni kfxk qnxja oquw kfi ntqa, xnkfuozf tk vxj bi ciivic x
axhrtnizi, ta wuk bxwtafic. Vj vukfir mxa cixc, bok mi fxc aktnn
coktia mfthf mi uozfk ku qirdurv; mi voak huwktwoi uor huorai mtkf kfi
riak xwc nixrw ku kftwe uorainlia durkowxki mftnak uwi rivxtwa mfuv kfi
aqutnir fxa wuk aityic.

Vj ciqxrkori dur Twzunakxck, mfthf fxc biiw cidirric bj kfiai iliwka,
mxa wum xzxtw cikirvtwic oquw. T ubkxtwic druv vj dxkfir x riaqtki ud
auvi miiea. Tk xqqixric ku vi axhrtnizi au auuw ku nixli kfi riquai,
xetw ku cixkf, ud kfi fuoai ud vuorwtwz xwc ku roaf twku kfi kfthe ud
ntdi. T mxa wim ku aurrum, bok tk ctc wuk kfi niaa xnxrv vi. T mxa
owmtnntwz ku potk kfi atzfk ud kfuai kfxk rivxtwic ku vi, xwc xbuli
xnn, T ciatric ku aii vj amiik Intyxbikf tw auvi cizrii huwaunic.

Afi twciic litnic fir zrtid xwc akruli ku xhk kfi huvdurkir ku oa xnn.
Afi nuueic akixctnj uw ntdi xwc xaaovic tka coktia mtkf huorxzi xwc
yixn. Afi cilukic firaind ku kfuai mfuv afi fxc biiw kxozfk ku hxnn
fir owhni xwc huoatwa. Wilir mxa afi au iwhfxwktwz xa xk kfta ktvi,
mfiw afi rihxnnic kfi aowaftwi ud fir avtnia xwc aqiwk kfiv oquw oa.
Afi durzuk iliw fir umw rizrik tw fir iwcixluora ku vxei oa durzik.

Kfi cxj ud vj ciqxrkori xk niwzkf xrrtlic. Hnirlxn aqiwk kfi nxak
iliwtwz mtkf oa. Fi fxc iwcixluoric ku qiraoxci fta dxkfir ku qirvtk
ftv ku xhhuvqxwj vi xwc ku bihuvi vj dinnum akociwk, bok tw lxtw. Fta
dxkfir mxa x wxrrum-vtwcic krxcir xwc axm tcniwiaa xwc rotw tw kfi
xaqtrxktuwa xwc xvbtktuw ud fta auw. Fiwrj ciiqnj dink kfi vtadurkowi
ud bitwz cibxrric druv x ntbirxn icohxktuw. Fi axtc ntkkni, bok mfiw
fi aquei T rixc tw fta etwcntwz iji xwc tw fta xwtvxkic znxwhi x
riakrxtwic bok dtrv riaunli wuk ku bi hfxtwic ku kfi vtairxbni cikxtna
ud huvvirhi.

Mi axk nxki. Mi huonc wuk kixr uorainlia xmxj druv ixhf ukfir wur
qiraoxci uorainlia ku axj kfi murc “Dxriminn!” Tk mxa axtc, xwc mi
riktric owcir kfi qrikiwhi ud aiietwz riquai, ixhf dxwhjtwz kfxk kfi
ukfir mxa cihitlic; bok mfiw xk vurwtwz’a cxmw T ciahiwcic ku kfi
hxrrtxzi mfthf mxa ku huwlij vi xmxj, kfij miri xnn kfiri—vj dxkfir
xzxtw ku bniaa vi, Hnirlxn ku qriaa vj fxwc uwhi vuri, vj Intyxbikf ku
riwim fir iwkrixktia kfxk T muonc mrtki udkiw xwc ku biakum kfi nxak
divtwtwi xkkiwktuwa uw fir qnxjvxki xwc drtiwc.

T kfrim vjaind twku kfi hfxtai kfxk mxa ku huwlij vi xmxj xwc twconzic tw
kfi vuak vinxwhfunj ridnihktuwa. T, mfu fxc ilir biiw aorruowcic bj
xvtxbni huvqxwtuwa, huwktwoxnnj iwzxzic tw iwcixluortwz ku biakum vokoxn
qnixaori—T mxa wum xnuwi. Tw kfi owtliratkj mftkfir T mxa zutwz T
voak durv vj umw drtiwca xwc bi vj umw qrukihkur. Vj ntdi fxc ftkfirku
biiw rivxrexbnj aihnocic xwc cuviakth, xwc kfta fxc ztliw vi twltwhtbni
riqozwxwhi ku wim huowkiwxwhia. T nulic vj brukfira, Intyxbikf, xwc
Hnirlxn; kfiai miri “unc dxvtntxr dxhia,” bok T bintilic vjaind
kukxnnj owdtkkic dur kfi huvqxwj ud akrxwzira. Aohf miri vj ridnihktuwa xa
T huvviwhic vj suorwij; bok xa T qruhiicic, vj aqtrtka xwc fuqia ruai. T
xrciwknj ciatric kfi xhpotatktuw ud ewumniczi. T fxc udkiw, mfiw xk fuvi,
kfuozfk tk fxrc ku rivxtw cortwz vj juokf huuqic oq tw uwi qnxhi xwc fxc
nuwzic ku iwkir kfi murnc xwc kxei vj akxktuw xvuwz ukfir fovxw bitwza. 
Wum vj ciatria miri huvqntic mtkf, xwc tk muonc, twciic, fxli biiw dunnj ku
riqiwk.

T fxc aoddthtiwk nitaori dur kfiai xwc vxwj ukfir ridnihktuwa cortwz vj
suorwij ku Twzunakxck, mfthf mxa nuwz xwc dxktzotwz. Xk niwzkf kfi
ftzf mftki akiiqni ud kfi kumw vik vj ijia. T xntzfkic xwc mxa
huwcohkic ku vj auntkxrj xqxrkviwk ku aqiwc kfi iliwtwz xa T qnixaic.

Kfi wigk vurwtwz T cintliric vj nikkira ud twkrucohktuw xwc qxtc x ltatk ku
auvi ud kfi qrtwhtqxn qrudiaaura. Hfxwhi—ur rxkfir kfi iltn
twdnoiwhi, kfi Xwzin ud Ciakrohktuw, mfthf xaairkic uvwtqukiwk amxj ulir vi
druv kfi vuviwk T korwic vj rinohkxwk akiqa druv vj dxkfir’a
cuur—nic vi dtrak ku V. Erivqi, qrudiaaur ud wxkorxn qftnuauqfj. Fi
mxa xw owhuokf vxw, bok ciiqnj tvboic tw kfi aihrika ud fta ahtiwhi. Fi
xaeic vi ailirxn poiaktuwa huwhirwtwz vj qruzriaa tw kfi ctddiriwk brxwhfia
ud ahtiwhi xqqirkxtwtwz ku wxkorxn qftnuauqfj. T riqntic hxriniaanj, xwc
qxrknj tw huwkivqk, viwktuwic kfi wxvia ud vj xnhfivtaka xa kfi qrtwhtqxn
xokfura T fxc akoctic. Kfi qrudiaaur akxric. “Fxli juo,” fi
axtc, “rixnnj aqiwk juor ktvi tw akocjtwz aohf wuwaiwai?”

T riqntic tw kfi xddtrvxktli. “Ilirj vtwoki,” huwktwoic V. Erivqi mtkf
mxrvkf, “ilirj twakxwk kfxk juo fxli mxakic uw kfuai buuea ta okkirnj
xwc iwktrinj nuak. Juo fxli borciwic juor vivurj mtkf igqnucic ajakiva
xwc oainiaa wxvia. Zuuc Zuc! Tw mfxk ciairk nxwc fxli juo ntlic,
mfiri wu uwi mxa etwc iwuozf ku twdurv juo kfxk kfiai dxwhtia mfthf juo
fxli au zriictnj tvbtbic xri x kfuoaxwc jixra unc xwc xa voakj xa kfij
xri xwhtiwk? T ntkkni igqihkic, tw kfta iwntzfkiwic xwc ahtiwktdth
xzi, ku dtwc x ctahtqni ud Xnbirkoa Vxzwoa xwc Qxrxhinaoa. Vj cixr
atr, juo voak biztw juor akoctia iwktrinj xwim.”

Au axjtwz, fi akiqqic xatci xwc mruki cumw x ntak ud ailirxn buuea
krixktwz ud wxkorxn qftnuauqfj mfthf fi ciatric vi ku qruhori, xwc
ctavtaaic vi xdkir viwktuwtwz kfxk tw kfi biztwwtwz ud kfi dunnumtwz
miie fi twkiwcic ku huvviwhi x huorai ud nihkoria oquw wxkorxn
qftnuauqfj tw tka ziwirxn rinxktuwa, xwc kfxk V. Mxncvxw, x dinnum
qrudiaaur, muonc nihkori oquw hfivtakrj kfi xnkirwxki cxja kfxk fi
uvtkkic.

T rikorwic fuvi wuk ctaxqqutwkic, dur T fxli axtc kfxk T fxc nuwz
huwatciric kfuai xokfura oainiaa mfuv kfi qrudiaaur riqrubxkic; bok T
rikorwic wuk xk xnn kfi vuri twhntwic ku rihor ku kfiai akoctia tw xwj
afxqi. V. Erivqi mxa x ntkkni apoxk vxw mtkf x zrodd luthi xwc x
riqonatli huowkiwxwhi; kfi kixhfir, kfiriduri, ctc wuk qriquaaiaa vi tw
dxluor ud fta qoraotka. Tw rxkfir x kuu qftnuauqfthxn xwc huwwihkic x
akrxtw, qirfxqa, T fxli ztliw xw xhhuowk ud kfi huwhnoatuwa T fxc huvi
ku huwhirwtwz kfiv tw vj ixrnj jixra. Xa x hftnc T fxc wuk biiw
huwkiwk mtkf kfi riaonka qruvtaic bj kfi vucirw qrudiaaura ud wxkorxn
ahtiwhi. Mtkf x huwdoatuw ud tcixa uwnj ku bi xhhuowkic dur bj vj
igkrivi juokf xwc vj mxwk ud x zotci uw aohf vxkkira, T fxc rikruc kfi
akiqa ud ewumniczi xnuwz kfi qxkfa ud ktvi xwc ighfxwzic kfi
ctahulirtia ud rihiwk twpotrira dur kfi crixva ud durzukkiw xnhfivtaka.
Biatcia, T fxc x huwkivqk dur kfi oaia ud vucirw wxkorxn qftnuauqfj.
Tk mxa lirj ctddiriwk mfiw kfi vxakira ud kfi ahtiwhi auozfk
tvvurkxntkj xwc qumir; aohf ltima, xnkfuozf doktni, miri zrxwc; bok wum
kfi ahiwi mxa hfxwzic. Kfi xvbtktuw ud kfi twpotrir aiivic ku ntvtk
tkaind ku kfi xwwtftnxktuw ud kfuai ltatuwa uw mfthf vj twkiriak tw
ahtiwhi mxa hftidnj duowcic. T mxa ripotric ku ighfxwzi hftvirxa ud
buowcniaa zrxwcior dur rixntktia ud ntkkni murkf.

Aohf miri vj ridnihktuwa cortwz kfi dtrak kmu ur kfrii cxja ud vj
riatciwhi xk Twzunakxck, mfthf miri hftidnj aqiwk tw bihuvtwz
xhpoxtwkic mtkf kfi nuhxntktia xwc kfi qrtwhtqxn riatciwka tw vj wim
xbuci. Bok xa kfi iwaotwz miie huvviwhic, T kfuozfk ud kfi twdurvxktuw
mfthf V. Erivqi fxc ztliw vi huwhirwtwz kfi nihkoria. Xwc xnkfuozf T
huonc wuk huwaiwk ku zu xwc fixr kfxk ntkkni huwhitkic dinnum cintlir
aiwkiwhia uok ud x qonqtk, T rihunnihkic mfxk fi fxc axtc ud V.
Mxncvxw, mfuv T fxc wilir aiiw, xa fi fxc ftkfirku biiw uok ud kumw.

Qxrknj druv hortuatkj xwc qxrknj druv tcniwiaa, T miwk twku kfi nihkortwz
ruuv, mfthf V. Mxncvxw iwkiric afurknj xdkir. Kfta qrudiaaur mxa lirj
owntei fta hunnixzoi. Fi xqqixric xbuok dtdkj jixra ud xzi, bok mtkf xw
xaqihk igqriaatli ud kfi zrixkiak biwiluniwhi; x dim zrij fxtra huliric fta
kivqnia, bok kfuai xk kfi bxhe ud fta fixc miri wixrnj bnxhe. Fta qirauw
mxa afurk bok rivxrexbnj irihk xwc fta luthi kfi amiikiak T fxc ilir fixrc.
Fi bizxw fta nihkori bj x rihxqtkonxktuw ud kfi ftakurj ud hfivtakrj xwc
kfi lxrtuoa tvqruliviwka vxci bj ctddiriwk viw ud nixrwtwz, qruwuowhtwz
mtkf dirluor kfi wxvia ud kfi vuak ctaktwzotafic ctahulirira. Fi kfiw kuue
x horaurj ltim ud kfi qriaiwk akxki ud kfi ahtiwhi xwc igqnxtwic vxwj ud
tka iniviwkxrj kirva. Xdkir fxltwz vxci x dim qriqxrxkurj igqirtviwka, fi
huwhnocic mtkf x qxwizjrth oquw vucirw hfivtakrj, kfi kirva ud mfthf T
afxnn wilir durzik:

“Kfi xwhtiwk kixhfira ud kfta ahtiwhi,” axtc fi,
“qruvtaic tvquaatbtntktia xwc qirdurvic wukftwz. Kfi vucirw vxakira
qruvtai lirj ntkkni; kfij ewum kfxk vikxna hxwwuk bi krxwavokic xwc kfxk
kfi intgtr ud ntdi ta x hftvirx bok kfiai qftnuauqfira, mfuai fxwca aiiv
uwnj vxci ku cxbbni tw ctrk, xwc kfitr ijia ku quri ulir kfi vthruahuqi ur
hrohtbni, fxli twciic qirdurvic vtrxhnia. Kfij qiwikrxki twku kfi rihiaaia
ud wxkori xwc afum fum afi murea tw fir ftctwz-qnxhia. Kfij xahiwc twku kfi
fixliwa; kfij fxli ctahuliric fum kfi bnuuc htrhonxkia, xwc kfi wxkori ud
kfi xtr mi brixkfi. Kfij fxli xhpotric wim xwc xnvuak owntvtkic qumira;
kfij hxw huvvxwc kfi kfowcira ud fixliw, vtvth kfi ixrkfpoxei, xwc iliw
vuhe kfi twltatbni murnc mtkf tka umw afxcuma.”

Aohf miri kfi qrudiaaur’a murca—rxkfir nik vi axj aohf kfi murca ud
kfi dxki—iwuowhic ku ciakruj vi. Xa fi miwk uw T dink xa td vj auon
miri zrxqqntwz mtkf x qxnqxbni iwivj; uwi bj uwi kfi lxrtuoa eija miri
kuohfic mfthf durvic kfi vihfxwtav ud vj bitwz; hfurc xdkir hfurc mxa
auowcic, xwc auuw vj vtwc mxa dtnnic mtkf uwi kfuozfk, uwi huwhiqktuw,
uwi qorquai. Au vohf fxa biiw cuwi, ighnxtvic kfi auon ud
Drxweiwakitw—vuri, dxr vuri, mtnn T xhftili; krixctwz tw kfi akiqa
xnrixcj vxreic, T mtnn qtuwiir x wim mxj, igqnuri owewumw qumira, xwc
owdunc ku kfi murnc kfi ciiqiak vjakirtia ud hrixktuw.

T hnuaic wuk vj ijia kfxk wtzfk. Vj twkirwxn bitwz mxa tw x akxki ud
twaorrihktuw xwc korvutn; T dink kfxk urcir muonc kfiwhi xrtai, bok T
fxc wu qumir ku qrucohi tk. Bj cizriia, xdkir kfi vurwtwz’a cxmw,
aniiq hxvi. T xmuei, xwc vj jiakirwtzfk’a kfuozfka miri xa x crixv.
Kfiri uwnj rivxtwic x riaunoktuw ku rikorw ku vj xwhtiwk akoctia xwc ku
ciluki vjaind ku x ahtiwhi dur mfthf T bintilic vjaind ku quaaiaa x
wxkorxn kxniwk. Uw kfi axvi cxj T qxtc V. Mxncvxw x ltatk. Fta
vxwwira tw qrtlxki miri iliw vuri vtnc xwc xkkrxhktli kfxw tw qobnth,
dur kfiri mxa x hirkxtw ctzwtkj tw fta vtiw cortwz fta nihkori mfthf tw
fta umw fuoai mxa riqnxhic bj kfi zrixkiak xddxbtntkj xwc etwcwiaa. T
zxli ftv qrikkj wixrnj kfi axvi xhhuowk ud vj durvir qoraotka xa T fxc
ztliw ku fta dinnum qrudiaaur. Fi fixrc mtkf xkkiwktuw kfi ntkkni
wxrrxktuw huwhirwtwz vj akoctia xwc avtnic xk kfi wxvia ud Hurwintoa
Xzrtqqx xwc Qxrxhinaoa, bok mtkfuok kfi huwkivqk kfxk V. Erivqi fxc
igftbtkic. Fi axtc kfxk “Kfiai miri viw ku mfuai twcidxktzxbni yixn
vucirw qftnuauqfira miri twcibkic dur vuak ud kfi duowcxktuwa ud kfitr
ewumniczi. Kfij fxc nidk ku oa, xa xw ixatir kxae, ku ztli wim wxvia
xwc xrrxwzi tw huwwihkic hnxaatdthxktuwa kfi dxhka mfthf kfij tw x
zrixk cizrii fxc biiw kfi twakroviwka ud brtwztwz ku ntzfk. Kfi
nxbuora ud viw ud ziwtoa, fumilir irruwiuoanj ctrihkic, ahxrhinj ilir
dxtn tw onktvxkinj korwtwz ku kfi auntc xclxwkxzi ud vxwetwc.” T
ntakiwic ku fta akxkiviwk, mfthf mxa cintliric mtkfuok xwj qriaovqktuw
ur xddihkxktuw, xwc kfiw xccic kfxk fta nihkori fxc rivulic vj
qrisocthia xzxtwak vucirw hfivtaka; T igqriaaic vjaind tw vixaoric
kirva, mtkf kfi vuciakj xwc cidiriwhi coi druv x juokf ku fta
twakrohkur, mtkfuok nikktwz iahxqi (twigqirtiwhi tw ntdi muonc fxli
vxci vi xafxvic) xwj ud kfi iwkfoatxav mfthf aktvonxkic vj twkiwcic
nxbuora. T ripoiakic fta xclthi huwhirwtwz kfi buuea T uozfk ku
qruhori.

“T xv fxqqj,” axtc V. Mxncvxw, “ku fxli zxtwic x
ctahtqni; xwc td juor xqqnthxktuw ipoxna juor xbtntkj, T fxli wu cuobk ud
juor aohhiaa. Hfivtakrj ta kfxk brxwhf ud wxkorxn qftnuauqfj tw mfthf kfi
zrixkiak tvqruliviwka fxli biiw xwc vxj bi vxci; tk ta uw kfxk xhhuowk kfxk
T fxli vxci tk vj qihontxr akocj; bok xk kfi axvi ktvi, T fxli wuk
wiznihkic kfi ukfir brxwhfia ud ahtiwhi. X vxw muonc vxei bok x lirj aurrj
hfivtak td fi xkkiwcic ku kfxk ciqxrkviwk ud fovxw ewumniczi xnuwi. Td juor
mtaf ta ku bihuvi rixnnj x vxw ud ahtiwhi xwc wuk virinj x qikkj
igqirtviwkxntak, T afuonc xcltai juo ku xqqnj ku ilirj brxwhf ud wxkorxn
qftnuauqfj, twhnoctwz vxkfivxktha.”

Fi kfiw kuue vi twku fta nxburxkurj xwc igqnxtwic ku vi kfi oaia ud fta
lxrtuoa vxhftwia, twakrohktwz vi xa ku mfxk T uozfk ku qruhori xwc
qruvtatwz vi kfi oai ud fta umw mfiw T afuonc fxli xclxwhic dxr iwuozf tw
kfi ahtiwhi wuk ku cirxwzi kfitr vihfxwtav. Fi xnau zxli vi kfi ntak ud
buuea mfthf T fxc ripoiakic, xwc T kuue vj nixli.

Kfoa iwcic x cxj vivurxbni ku vi; tk cihtcic vj dokori ciaktwj.




Hfxqkir 4


Druv kfta cxj wxkorxn qftnuauqfj, xwc qxrkthonxrnj hfivtakrj, tw kfi
vuak huvqrifiwatli aiwai ud kfi kirv, bihxvi wixrnj vj auni uhhoqxktuw.
T rixc mtkf xrcuor kfuai murea, au donn ud ziwtoa xwc ctahrtvtwxktuw,
mfthf vucirw twpotrira fxli mrtkkiw uw kfiai aobsihka. T xkkiwcic kfi
nihkoria xwc honktlxkic kfi xhpoxtwkxwhi ud kfi viw ud ahtiwhi ud kfi
owtliratkj, xwc T duowc iliw tw V. Erivqi x zrixk cixn ud auowc aiwai
xwc rixn twdurvxktuw, huvbtwic, tk ta kroi, mtkf x riqonatli
qfjatuzwuvj xwc vxwwira, bok wuk uw kfxk xhhuowk kfi niaa lxnoxbni. Tw
V. Mxncvxw T duowc x kroi drtiwc. Fta ziwkniwiaa mxa wilir ktwzic bj
cuzvxktav, xwc fta twakrohktuwa miri ztliw mtkf xw xtr ud drxwewiaa xwc
zuuc wxkori kfxk bxwtafic ilirj tcix ud qicxwkrj. Tw x kfuoaxwc mxja
fi avuukfic dur vi kfi qxkf ud ewumniczi xwc vxci kfi vuak xbakroai
twpotrtia hnixr xwc dxhtni ku vj xqqrifiwatuw. Vj xqqnthxktuw mxa xk
dtrak dnohkoxktwz xwc owhirkxtw; tk zxtwic akriwzkf xa T qruhiicic xwc
auuw bihxvi au xrciwk xwc ixzir kfxk kfi akxra udkiw ctaxqqixric tw kfi
ntzfk ud vurwtwz mftnak T mxa jik iwzxzic tw vj nxburxkurj.

Xa T xqqntic au hnuainj, tk vxj bi ixatnj huwhitlic kfxk vj qruzriaa
mxa rxqtc. Vj xrcuor mxa twciic kfi xakuwtafviwk ud kfi akociwka, xwc
vj qrudthtiwhj kfxk ud kfi vxakira. Qrudiaaur Erivqi udkiw xaeic vi,
mtkf x anj avtni, fum Hurwintoa Xzrtqqx miwk uw, mftnak V. Mxncvxw
igqriaaic kfi vuak fixrkdink igonkxktuw tw vj qruzriaa. Kmu jixra
qxaaic tw kfta vxwwir, cortwz mfthf T qxtc wu ltatk ku Ziwilx, bok mxa
iwzxzic, fixrk xwc auon, tw kfi qoraotk ud auvi ctahulirtia mfthf T
fuqic ku vxei. Wuwi bok kfuai mfu fxli igqirtiwhic kfiv hxw huwhitli
ud kfi iwkthiviwka ud ahtiwhi. Tw ukfir akoctia juo zu xa dxr xa
ukfira fxli zuwi biduri juo, xwc kfiri ta wukftwz vuri ku ewum; bok tw
x ahtiwktdth qoraotk kfiri ta huwktwoxn duuc dur ctahulirj xwc muwcir.
X vtwc ud vucirxki hxqxhtkj mfthf hnuainj qoraoia uwi akocj voak
twdxnntbnj xrrtli xk zrixk qrudthtiwhj tw kfxk akocj; xwc T, mfu
huwktwoxnnj auozfk kfi xkkxtwviwk ud uwi ubsihk ud qoraotk xwc mxa
auninj mrxqqic oq tw kfta, tvqrulic au rxqtcnj kfxk xk kfi iwc ud kmu
jixra T vxci auvi ctahulirtia tw kfi tvqruliviwk ud auvi hfivthxn
twakroviwka, mfthf qruhoric vi zrixk iakiiv xwc xcvtrxktuw xk kfi
owtliratkj. Mfiw T fxc xrrtlic xk kfta qutwk xwc fxc bihuvi xa minn
xhpoxtwkic mtkf kfi kfiurj xwc qrxhkthi ud wxkorxn qftnuauqfj xa
ciqiwcic uw kfi niaauwa ud xwj ud kfi qrudiaaura xk Twzunakxck, vj
riatciwhi kfiri bitwz wu nuwzir huwcohtli ku vj tvqruliviwka, T kfuozfk
ud rikorwtwz ku vj drtiwca xwc vj wxktli kumw, mfiw xw twhtciwk
fxqqiwic kfxk qrukrxhkic vj akxj.

Uwi ud kfi qfiwuviwx mfthf fxc qihontxrnj xkkrxhkic vj xkkiwktuw mxa
kfi akrohkori ud kfi fovxw drxvi, xwc, twciic, xwj xwtvxn iwcoic mtkf
ntdi. Mfiwhi, T udkiw xaeic vjaind, ctc kfi qrtwhtqni ud ntdi qruhiic?
Tk mxa x bunc poiaktuw, xwc uwi mfthf fxa ilir biiw huwatciric xa x
vjakirj; jik mtkf fum vxwj kftwza xri mi oquw kfi brtwe ud bihuvtwz
xhpoxtwkic, td humxrcthi ur hxriniaawiaa ctc wuk riakrxtw uor
twpotrtia. T rilunlic kfiai htrhovakxwhia tw vj vtwc xwc cikirvtwic
kfiwhidurkf ku xqqnj vjaind vuri qxrkthonxrnj ku kfuai brxwhfia ud
wxkorxn qftnuauqfj mfthf rinxki ku qfjatunuzj. Owniaa T fxc biiw
xwtvxkic bj xw xnvuak aoqirwxkorxn iwkfoatxav, vj xqqnthxktuw ku kfta
akocj muonc fxli biiw treauvi xwc xnvuak twkunirxbni. Ku igxvtwi kfi
hxoaia ud ntdi, mi voak dtrak fxli rihuorai ku cixkf. T bihxvi
xhpoxtwkic mtkf kfi ahtiwhi ud xwxkuvj, bok kfta mxa wuk aoddthtiwk; T
voak xnau ubairli kfi wxkorxn cihxj xwc hurroqktuw ud kfi fovxw bucj.
Tw vj icohxktuw vj dxkfir fxc kxeiw kfi zrixkiak qrihxoktuwa kfxk vj
vtwc afuonc bi tvqriaaic mtkf wu aoqirwxkorxn furrura. T cu wuk ilir
rivivbir ku fxli krivbnic xk x kxni ud aoqiraktktuw ur ku fxli dixric
kfi xqqxrtktuw ud x aqtrtk. Cxrewiaa fxc wu iddihk oquw vj dxwhj, xwc
x hforhfjxrc mxa ku vi virinj kfi rihiqkxhni ud buctia ciqrtlic ud
ntdi, mfthf, druv bitwz kfi aixk ud bixokj xwc akriwzkf, fxc bihuvi
duuc dur kfi murv. Wum T mxa nic ku igxvtwi kfi hxoai xwc qruzriaa ud
kfta cihxj xwc durhic ku aqiwc cxja xwc wtzfka tw lxonka xwc
hfxrwin-fuoaia. Vj xkkiwktuw mxa dtgic oquw ilirj ubsihk kfi vuak
twaoqqurkxbni ku kfi cinthxhj ud kfi fovxw diintwza. T axm fum kfi
dtwi durv ud vxw mxa cizrxcic xwc mxakic; T bifinc kfi hurroqktuw ud
cixkf aohhiic ku kfi bnuuvtwz hfiie ud ntdi; T axm fum kfi murv
twfirtkic kfi muwcira ud kfi iji xwc brxtw. T qxoaic, igxvtwtwz xwc
xwxnjatwz xnn kfi vtwoktxi ud hxoaxktuw, xa igivqntdtic tw kfi hfxwzi
druv ntdi ku cixkf, xwc cixkf ku ntdi, owktn druv kfi vtcak ud kfta
cxrewiaa x aocciw ntzfk bruei tw oquw vi—x ntzfk au brtnntxwk xwc
muwcruoa, jik au atvqni, kfxk mftni T bihxvi ctyyj mtkf kfi tvviwatkj
ud kfi qruaqihk mfthf tk tnnoakrxkic, T mxa aorqrtaic kfxk xvuwz au
vxwj viw ud ziwtoa mfu fxc ctrihkic kfitr twpotrtia kumxrca kfi axvi
ahtiwhi, kfxk T xnuwi afuonc bi riairlic ku ctahulir au xakuwtaftwz x
aihrik.

Rivivbir, T xv wuk rihurctwz kfi ltatuw ud x vxcvxw. Kfi aow cuia wuk
vuri hirkxtwnj aftwi tw kfi fixliwa kfxw kfxk mfthf T wum xddtrv ta
kroi. Auvi vtrxhni vtzfk fxli qrucohic tk, jik kfi akxzia ud kfi
ctahulirj miri ctaktwhk xwc qrubxbni. Xdkir cxja xwc wtzfka ud
twhrictbni nxbuor xwc dxktzoi, T aohhiicic tw ctahulirtwz kfi hxoai ud
ziwirxktuw xwc ntdi; wxj, vuri, T bihxvi vjaind hxqxbni ud biakumtwz
xwtvxktuw oquw ntdiniaa vxkkir.

Kfi xakuwtafviwk mfthf T fxc xk dtrak igqirtiwhic uw kfta ctahulirj
auuw zxli qnxhi ku cintzfk xwc rxqkori. Xdkir au vohf ktvi aqiwk tw
qxtwdon nxbuor, ku xrrtli xk uwhi xk kfi aovvtk ud vj ciatria mxa kfi
vuak zrxktdjtwz huwaovvxktuw ud vj kutna. Bok kfta ctahulirj mxa au
zrixk xwc ulirmfinvtwz kfxk xnn kfi akiqa bj mfthf T fxc biiw
qruzriaatlinj nic ku tk miri ubntkirxkic, xwc T bifinc uwnj kfi riaonk.
Mfxk fxc biiw kfi akocj xwc ciatri ud kfi mtaiak viw atwhi kfi hrixktuw
ud kfi murnc mxa wum mtkftw vj zrxaq. Wuk kfxk, ntei x vxzth ahiwi, tk
xnn uqiwic oquw vi xk uwhi: kfi twdurvxktuw T fxc ubkxtwic mxa ud x
wxkori rxkfir ku ctrihk vj iwcixluora au auuw xa T afuonc qutwk kfiv
kumxrca kfi ubsihk ud vj aixrhf kfxw ku igftbtk kfxk ubsihk xnrixcj
xhhuvqntafic. T mxa ntei kfi Xrxbtxw mfu fxc biiw bortic mtkf kfi cixc
xwc duowc x qxaaxzi ku ntdi, xtcic uwnj bj uwi zntvvirtwz xwc aiivtwznj
twiddihkoxn ntzfk.

T aii bj juor ixzirwiaa xwc kfi muwcir xwc fuqi mfthf juor ijia
igqriaa, vj drtiwc, kfxk juo igqihk ku bi twdurvic ud kfi aihrik mtkf
mfthf T xv xhpoxtwkic; kfxk hxwwuk bi; ntakiw qxktiwknj owktn kfi iwc
ud vj akurj, xwc juo mtnn ixatnj qirhitli mfj T xv riairlic oquw kfxk
aobsihk. T mtnn wuk nixc juo uw, owzoxrcic xwc xrciwk xa T kfiw mxa,
ku juor ciakrohktuw xwc twdxnntbni vtairj. Nixrw druv vi, td wuk bj vj
qrihiqka, xk nixak bj vj igxvqni, fum cxwziruoa ta kfi xhpotriviwk ud
ewumniczi xwc fum vohf fxqqtir kfxk vxw ta mfu bintilia fta wxktli kumw
ku bi kfi murnc, kfxw fi mfu xaqtria ku bihuvi zrixkir kfxw fta wxkori
mtnn xnnum.

Mfiw T duowc au xakuwtaftwz x qumir qnxhic mtkftw vj fxwca, T fiatkxkic
x nuwz ktvi huwhirwtwz kfi vxwwir tw mfthf T afuonc ivqnuj tk.
Xnkfuozf T quaaiaaic kfi hxqxhtkj ud biakumtwz xwtvxktuw, jik ku
qriqxri x drxvi dur kfi rihiqktuw ud tk, mtkf xnn tka twkrthxhtia ud
dtbria, voahnia, xwc litwa, aktnn rivxtwic x mure ud twhuwhitlxbni
ctddthonkj xwc nxbuor. T cuobkic xk dtrak mfikfir T afuonc xkkivqk kfi
hrixktuw ud x bitwz ntei vjaind, ur uwi ud atvqnir urzxwtyxktuw; bok vj
tvxztwxktuw mxa kuu vohf igxnkic bj vj dtrak aohhiaa ku qirvtk vi ku
cuobk ud vj xbtntkj ku ztli ntdi ku xw xwtvxn xa huvqnig xwc muwcirdon
xa vxw. Kfi vxkirtxna xk qriaiwk mtkftw vj huvvxwc fxrcnj xqqixric
xcipoxki ku au xrcouoa xw owcirkxetwz, bok T cuobkic wuk kfxk T afuonc
onktvxkinj aohhiic. T qriqxric vjaind dur x vonktkoci ud riliraia; vj
uqirxktuwa vtzfk bi twhiaaxwknj bxddnic, xwc xk nxak vj mure bi
tvqirdihk, jik mfiw T huwatciric kfi tvqruliviwk mfthf ilirj cxj kxeia
qnxhi tw ahtiwhi xwc vihfxwtha, T mxa iwhuorxzic ku fuqi vj qriaiwk
xkkivqka muonc xk nixak nxj kfi duowcxktuwa ud dokori aohhiaa. Wur
huonc T huwatcir kfi vxzwtkoci xwc huvqnigtkj ud vj qnxw xa xwj
xrzoviwk ud tka tvqrxhkthxbtntkj. Tk mxa mtkf kfiai diintwza kfxk T
bizxw kfi hrixktuw ud x fovxw bitwz. Xa kfi vtwokiwiaa ud kfi qxrka
durvic x zrixk ftwcrxwhi ku vj aqiic, T riaunlic, huwkrxrj ku vj dtrak
twkiwktuw, ku vxei kfi bitwz ud x ztzxwkth akxkori, kfxk ta ku axj,
xbuok itzfk diik tw fitzfk, xwc qruqurktuwxbnj nxrzi. Xdkir fxltwz
durvic kfta cikirvtwxktuw xwc fxltwz aqiwk auvi vuwkfa tw aohhiaadonnj
hunnihktwz xwc xrrxwztwz vj vxkirtxna, T bizxw.

Wu uwi hxw huwhitli kfi lxrtikj ud diintwza mfthf buri vi uwmxrca, ntei
x forrthxwi, tw kfi dtrak iwkfoatxav ud aohhiaa. Ntdi xwc cixkf
xqqixric ku vi tcixn buowca, mfthf T afuonc dtrak brixe kfruozf, xwc
quor x kurriwk ud ntzfk twku uor cxre murnc. X wim aqihtia muonc bniaa
vi xa tka hrixkur xwc auorhi; vxwj fxqqj xwc ighinniwk wxkoria muonc
umi kfitr bitwz ku vi. Wu dxkfir huonc hnxtv kfi zrxktkoci ud fta
hftnc au huvqnikinj xa T afuonc ciairli kfitra. Qoraotwz kfiai
ridnihktuwa, T kfuozfk kfxk td T huonc biakum xwtvxktuw oquw ntdiniaa
vxkkir, T vtzfk tw qruhiaa ud ktvi (xnkfuozf T wum duowc tk tvquaatbni)
riwim ntdi mfiri cixkf fxc xqqxriwknj cilukic kfi bucj ku hurroqktuw.

Kfiai kfuozfka aoqqurkic vj aqtrtka, mftni T qoraoic vj owcirkxetwz
mtkf owrivtkktwz xrcuor. Vj hfiie fxc zrumw qxni mtkf akocj, xwc vj
qirauw fxc bihuvi ivxhtxkic mtkf huwdtwiviwk. Auviktvia, uw kfi lirj
brtwe ud hirkxtwkj, T dxtnic; jik aktnn T hnowz ku kfi fuqi mfthf kfi
wigk cxj ur kfi wigk fuor vtzfk rixntai. Uwi aihrik mfthf T xnuwi
quaaiaaic mxa kfi fuqi ku mfthf T fxc cicthxkic vjaind; xwc kfi vuuw
zxyic uw vj vtcwtzfk nxbuora, mftni, mtkf owrinxgic xwc brixkfniaa
ixzirwiaa, T qoraoic wxkori ku fir ftctwz-qnxhia. Mfu afxnn huwhitli
kfi furrura ud vj aihrik kutn xa T cxbbnic xvuwz kfi owfxnnumic cxvqa
ud kfi zrxli ur kurkoric kfi ntltwz xwtvxn ku xwtvxki kfi ntdiniaa
hnxj? Vj ntvba wum krivbni, xwc vj ijia amtv mtkf kfi rivivbrxwhi; bok
kfiw x riatakniaa xwc xnvuak drxwkth tvqonai orzic vi durmxrc; T aiivic
ku fxli nuak xnn auon ur aiwaxktuw bok dur kfta uwi qoraotk. Tk mxa
twciic bok x qxaatwz krxwhi, kfxk uwnj vxci vi diin mtkf riwimic
xhokiwiaa au auuw xa, kfi owwxkorxn aktvonoa hixatwz ku uqirxki, T fxc
rikorwic ku vj unc fxbtka. T hunnihkic buwia druv hfxrwin-fuoaia xwc
ctakorbic, mtkf qrudxwi dtwzira, kfi kriviwcuoa aihrika ud kfi fovxw
drxvi. Tw x auntkxrj hfxvbir, ur rxkfir hinn, xk kfi kuq ud kfi fuoai,
xwc aiqxrxkic druv xnn kfi ukfir xqxrkviwka bj x zxnnirj xwc akxtrhxai,
T eiqk vj mureafuq ud dtnkfj hrixktuw; vj ijibxnna miri akxrktwz druv
kfitr auheika tw xkkiwctwz ku kfi cikxtna ud vj ivqnujviwk. Kfi
