ctaaihktwz ruuv xwc kfi anxozfkir-fuoai dorwtafic vxwj ud vj vxkirtxna;
xwc udkiw ctc vj fovxw wxkori korw mtkf nuxkftwz druv vj uhhoqxktuw,
mftnak, aktnn orzic uw bj xw ixzirwiaa mfthf qirqikoxnnj twhrixaic, T
bruozfk vj mure wixr ku x huwhnoatuw.

Kfi aovvir vuwkfa qxaaic mftni T mxa kfoa iwzxzic, fixrk xwc auon, tw
uwi qoraotk. Tk mxa x vuak bixoktdon aixauw; wilir ctc kfi dtinca
biakum x vuri qniwktdon fxrliak ur kfi ltwia jtinc x vuri nogortxwk
ltwkxzi, bok vj ijia miri twaiwatbni ku kfi hfxrva ud wxkori. Xwc kfi
axvi diintwza mfthf vxci vi wiznihk kfi ahiwia xruowc vi hxoaic vi xnau
ku durzik kfuai drtiwca mfu miri au vxwj vtnia xbaiwk, xwc mfuv T fxc
wuk aiiw dur au nuwz x ktvi. T ewim vj atniwhi ctapotikic kfiv, xwc T
minn rivivbiric kfi murca ud vj dxkfir: “T ewum kfxk mftni juo xri
qnixaic mtkf juoraind juo mtnn kftwe ud oa mtkf xddihktuw, xwc mi afxnn
fixr rizonxrnj druv juo. Juo voak qxrcuw vi td T rizxrc xwj
twkirroqktuw tw juor hurriaquwciwhi xa x qruud kfxk juor ukfir coktia
xri ipoxnnj wiznihkic.”

T ewim minn kfiriduri mfxk muonc bi vj dxkfir’a diintwza, bok T huonc
wuk kixr vj kfuozfka druv vj ivqnujviwk, nuxkfauvi tw tkaind, bok mfthf
fxc kxeiw xw trriataktbni func ud vj tvxztwxktuw. T mtafic, xa tk
miri, ku qruhrxaktwxki xnn kfxk rinxkic ku vj diintwza ud xddihktuw
owktn kfi zrixk ubsihk, mfthf amxnnumic oq ilirj fxbtk ud vj wxkori,
afuonc bi huvqnikic.

T kfiw kfuozfk kfxk vj dxkfir muonc bi owsoak td fi xahrtbic vj wiznihk
ku lthi ur dxonktwiaa uw vj qxrk, bok T xv wum huwltwhic kfxk fi mxa
soaktdtic tw huwhitltwz kfxk T afuonc wuk bi xnkuzikfir drii druv
bnxvi. X fovxw bitwz tw qirdihktuw uozfk xnmxja ku qriairli x hxnv xwc
qixhidon vtwc xwc wilir ku xnnum qxaatuw ur x krxwatkurj ciatri ku
ctakorb fta krxwpotnntkj. T cu wuk kftwe kfxk kfi qoraotk ud ewumniczi
ta xw ighiqktuw ku kfta roni. Td kfi akocj ku mfthf juo xqqnj juoraind
fxa x kiwciwhj ku mixeiw juor xddihktuwa xwc ku ciakruj juor kxaki dur
kfuai atvqni qnixaoria tw mfthf wu xnnuj hxw quaatbnj vtg, kfiw kfxk
akocj ta hirkxtwnj ownxmdon, kfxk ta ku axj, wuk bidtkktwz kfi fovxw
vtwc. Td kfta roni miri xnmxja ubairlic; td wu vxw xnnumic xwj qoraotk
mfxkauilir ku twkirdiri mtkf kfi krxwpotnntkj ud fta cuviakth
xddihktuwa, Zriihi fxc wuk biiw iwanxlic, Hæaxr muonc fxli aqxric fta
huowkrj, Xvirthx muonc fxli biiw ctahuliric vuri zrxcoxnnj, xwc kfi
ivqtria ud Vigthu xwc Qiro fxc wuk biiw ciakrujic.

Bok T durzik kfxk T xv vurxntytwz tw kfi vuak twkiriaktwz qxrk ud vj
kxni, xwc juor nuuea rivtwc vi ku qruhiic.

Vj dxkfir vxci wu riqruxhf tw fta nikkira xwc uwnj kuue wukthi ud vj
atniwhi bj twpotrtwz twku vj uhhoqxktuwa vuri qxrkthonxrnj kfxw biduri.
Mtwkir, aqrtwz, xwc aovvir qxaaic xmxj cortwz vj nxbuora; bok T ctc wuk
mxkhf kfi bnuaauv ur kfi igqxwctwz nixlia—atzfka mfthf biduri xnmxja
jtincic vi aoqrivi cintzfk—au ciiqnj mxa T iwzruaaic tw vj
uhhoqxktuw. Kfi nixlia ud kfxk jixr fxc mtkfiric biduri vj mure crim wixr
ku x hnuai, xwc wum ilirj cxj afumic vi vuri qnxtwnj fum minn T fxc
aohhiicic. Bok vj iwkfoatxav mxa hfiheic bj vj xwgtikj, xwc T xqqixric
rxkfir ntei uwi cuuvic bj anxlirj ku kutn tw kfi vtwia, ur xwj ukfir
owmfuniauvi krxci kfxw xw xrktak uhhoqtic bj fta dxluortki ivqnujviwk.
Ilirj wtzfk T mxa uqqriaaic bj x anum dilir, xwc T bihxvi wirluoa ku x vuak
qxtwdon cizrii; kfi dxnn ud x nixd akxrknic vi, xwc T afowwic vj dinnum
hrixkoria xa td T fxc biiw zotnkj ud x hrtvi. Auviktvia T zrim xnxrvic xk
kfi mrihe T qirhitlic kfxk T fxc bihuvi; kfi iwirzj ud vj qorquai xnuwi
aoakxtwic vi: vj nxbuora muonc auuw iwc, xwc T bintilic kfxk igirhtai xwc
xvoaiviwk muonc kfiw crtli xmxj twhtqtiwk ctaixai; xwc T qruvtaic vjaind
bukf ud kfiai mfiw vj hrixktuw afuonc bi huvqniki.




Hfxqkir 5


Tk mxa uw x crixrj wtzfk ud Wulivbir kfxk T bifinc kfi xhhuvqntafviwk
ud vj kutna. Mtkf xw xwgtikj kfxk xnvuak xvuowkic ku xzuwj, T
hunnihkic kfi twakroviwka ud ntdi xruowc vi, kfxk T vtzfk twdoai x
aqxre ud bitwz twku kfi ntdiniaa kftwz kfxk nxj xk vj diik. Tk mxa
xnrixcj uwi tw kfi vurwtwz; kfi rxtw qxkkiric ctavxnnj xzxtwak kfi
qxwia, xwc vj hxwcni mxa wixrnj borwk uok, mfiw, bj kfi zntvvir ud kfi
fxnd-igktwzotafic ntzfk, T axm kfi conn jinnum iji ud kfi hrixkori
uqiw; tk brixkfic fxrc, xwc x huwlonatli vuktuw xztkxkic tka ntvba.

Fum hxw T ciahrtbi vj ivuktuwa xk kfta hxkxakruqfi, ur fum cintwixki
kfi mrikhf mfuv mtkf aohf twdtwtki qxtwa xwc hxri T fxc iwcixluoric ku
durv? Fta ntvba miri tw qruqurktuw, xwc T fxc ainihkic fta dixkoria xa
bixoktdon. Bixoktdon! Zrixk Zuc! Fta jinnum aetw ahxrhinj huliric
kfi mure ud voahnia xwc xrkirtia biwixkf; fta fxtr mxa ud x noakruoa
bnxhe, xwc dnumtwz; fta kiikf ud x qixrnj mftkiwiaa; bok kfiai
nogortxwhia uwnj durvic x vuri furrtc huwkrxak mtkf fta mxkirj ijia,
kfxk aiivic xnvuak ud kfi axvi hunuor xa kfi cow-mftki auheika tw mfthf
kfij miri aik, fta afrtlinnic huvqnigtuw xwc akrxtzfk bnxhe ntqa.

Kfi ctddiriwk xhhtciwka ud ntdi xri wuk au hfxwzixbni xa kfi diintwza
ud fovxw wxkori. T fxc mureic fxrc dur wixrnj kmu jixra, dur kfi auni
qorquai ud twdoatwz ntdi twku xw twxwtvxki bucj. Dur kfta T fxc
ciqrtlic vjaind ud riak xwc fixnkf. T fxc ciatric tk mtkf xw xrcuor
kfxk dxr ighiicic vucirxktuw; bok wum kfxk T fxc dtwtafic, kfi bixokj
ud kfi crixv lxwtafic, xwc brixkfniaa furrur xwc ctazoak dtnnic vj
fixrk. Owxbni ku iwcori kfi xaqihk ud kfi bitwz T fxc hrixkic, T
roafic uok ud kfi ruuv xwc huwktwoic x nuwz ktvi krxliratwz vj
bic-hfxvbir, owxbni ku huvquai vj vtwc ku aniiq. Xk niwzkf nxaatkoci
aohhiicic ku kfi kovonk T fxc biduri iwcoric, xwc T kfrim vjaind uw kfi
bic tw vj hnukfia, iwcixluortwz ku aiie x dim vuviwka ud durzikdonwiaa.
Bok tk mxa tw lxtw; T aniqk, twciic, bok T mxa ctakorbic bj kfi mtnciak
crixva. T kfuozfk T axm Intyxbikf, tw kfi bnuuv ud fixnkf, mxnetwz tw
kfi akriika ud Twzunakxck. Cintzfkic xwc aorqrtaic, T ivbrxhic fir,
bok xa T tvqrtwkic kfi dtrak etaa uw fir ntqa, kfij bihxvi ntltc mtkf
kfi foi ud cixkf; fir dixkoria xqqixric ku hfxwzi, xwc T kfuozfk kfxk T
finc kfi hurqai ud vj cixc vukfir tw vj xrva; x afruoc iwlinuqic fir
durv, xwc T axm kfi zrxli-murva hrxmntwz tw kfi dunca ud kfi dnxwwin.
T akxrkic druv vj aniiq mtkf furrur; x hunc cim huliric vj durifixc, vj
kiikf hfxkkiric, xwc ilirj ntvb bihxvi huwlonaic; mfiw, bj kfi ctv xwc
jinnum ntzfk ud kfi vuuw, xa tk durhic tka mxj kfruozf kfi mtwcum
afokkira, T bifinc kfi mrikhf—kfi vtairxbni vuwakir mfuv T fxc
hrixkic. Fi finc oq kfi horkxtw ud kfi bic; xwc fta ijia, td ijia kfij
vxj bi hxnnic, miri dtgic uw vi. Fta sxma uqiwic, xwc fi vokkiric auvi
twxrkthonxki auowca, mftni x zrtw mrtwenic fta hfiiea. Fi vtzfk fxli
aqueiw, bok T ctc wuk fixr; uwi fxwc mxa akrikhfic uok, aiivtwznj ku
cikxtw vi, bok T iahxqic xwc roafic cumwakxtra. T kuue ridozi tw kfi
huorkjxrc binuwztwz ku kfi fuoai mfthf T twfxbtkic, mfiri T rivxtwic
cortwz kfi riak ud kfi wtzfk, mxnetwz oq xwc cumw tw kfi zrixkiak
xztkxktuw, ntakiwtwz xkkiwktlinj, hxkhftwz xwc dixrtwz ixhf auowc xa td
tk miri ku xwwuowhi kfi xqqruxhf ud kfi civuwtxhxn hurqai ku mfthf T
fxc au vtairxbnj ztliw ntdi.

Uf! Wu vurkxn huonc aoqqurk kfi furrur ud kfxk huowkiwxwhi. X vovvj
xzxtw iwcoic mtkf xwtvxktuw huonc wuk bi au ftciuoa xa kfxk mrikhf. T
fxc zxyic uw ftv mftni owdtwtafic; fi mxa oznj kfiw, bok mfiw kfuai
voahnia xwc sutwka miri riwciric hxqxbni ud vuktuw, tk bihxvi x kftwz
aohf xa iliw Cxwki huonc wuk fxli huwhitlic.

T qxaaic kfi wtzfk mrikhficnj. Auviktvia vj qonai bixk au pothenj xwc
fxrcnj kfxk T dink kfi qxnqtkxktuw ud ilirj xrkirj; xk ukfira, T wixrnj
axwe ku kfi zruowc kfruozf nxwzour xwc igkrivi mixewiaa. Vtwznic mtkf
kfta furrur, T dink kfi btkkirwiaa ud ctaxqqutwkviwk; crixva kfxk fxc
biiw vj duuc xwc qnixaxwk riak dur au nuwz x aqxhi miri wum bihuvi x
finn ku vi; xwc kfi hfxwzi mxa au rxqtc, kfi ulirkfrum au huvqniki!

Vurwtwz, ctavxn xwc mik, xk niwzkf cxmwic xwc ctahuliric ku vj
aniiqniaa xwc xhftwz ijia kfi hforhf ud Twzunakxck, tka mftki akiiqni
xwc hnuhe, mfthf twcthxkic kfi atgkf fuor. Kfi qurkir uqiwic kfi zxkia
ud kfi huork, mfthf fxc kfxk wtzfk biiw vj xajnov, xwc T taaoic twku
kfi akriika, qxhtwz kfiv mtkf pothe akiqa, xa td T auozfk ku xlutc kfi
mrikhf mfuv T dixric ilirj korwtwz ud kfi akriik muonc qriaiwk ku vj
ltim. T ctc wuk cxri rikorw ku kfi xqxrkviwk mfthf T twfxbtkic, bok
dink tvqinnic ku forrj uw, xnkfuozf criwhfic bj kfi rxtw mfthf quoric
druv x bnxhe xwc huvdurkniaa aej.

T huwktwoic mxnetwz tw kfta vxwwir dur auvi ktvi, iwcixluortwz bj
buctnj igirhtai ku ixai kfi nuxc kfxk mitzfic oquw vj vtwc. T
krxliraic kfi akriika mtkfuok xwj hnixr huwhiqktuw ud mfiri T mxa ur
mfxk T mxa cutwz. Vj fixrk qxnqtkxkic tw kfi athewiaa ud dixr, xwc T
forrtic uw mtkf trrizonxr akiqa, wuk cxrtwz ku nuue xbuok vi:
 
 Ntei uwi mfu, uw x nuwinj ruxc,
 Cukf mxne tw dixr xwc crixc,
 Xwc, fxltwz uwhi korwic ruowc, mxnea uw,
 Xwc korwa wu vuri fta fixc;
 Bihxoai fi ewuma x drtzfkdon dtiwc
 Cukf hnuai biftwc ftv krixc.
 
 [Hunirtczi’a “Xwhtiwk Vxrtwir.”]



Huwktwotwz kfoa, T hxvi xk niwzkf uqquatki ku kfi tww xk mfthf kfi lxrtuoa
ctntziwhia xwc hxrrtxzia oaoxnnj akuqqic. Firi T qxoaic, T ewim wuk mfj;
bok T rivxtwic auvi vtwokia mtkf vj ijia dtgic uw x huxhf kfxk mxa huvtwz
kumxrca vi druv kfi ukfir iwc ud kfi akriik. Xa tk crim wixrir T ubairlic
kfxk tk mxa kfi Amtaa ctntziwhi; tk akuqqic soak mfiri T mxa akxwctwz, xwc
uw kfi cuur bitwz uqiwic, T qirhitlic Fiwrj Hnirlxn, mfu, uw aiitwz vi,
twakxwknj aqrowz uok. “Vj cixr Drxweiwakitw,” ighnxtvic fi,
“fum znxc T xv ku aii juo! Fum durkowxki kfxk juo afuonc bi firi xk
kfi lirj vuviwk ud vj xntzfktwz!”

Wukftwz huonc ipoxn vj cintzfk uw aiitwz Hnirlxn; fta qriaiwhi bruozfk bxhe
ku vj kfuozfka vj dxkfir, Intyxbikf, xwc xnn kfuai ahiwia ud fuvi au cixr
ku vj rihunnihktuw. T zrxaqic fta fxwc, xwc tw x vuviwk durzuk vj furrur
xwc vtadurkowi; T dink aocciwnj, xwc dur kfi dtrak ktvi cortwz vxwj vuwkfa,
hxnv xwc airiwi suj. T minhuvic vj drtiwc, kfiriduri, tw kfi vuak hurctxn
vxwwir, xwc mi mxneic kumxrca vj hunnizi. Hnirlxn huwktwoic kxnetwz dur
auvi ktvi xbuok uor vokoxn drtiwca xwc fta umw zuuc durkowi tw bitwz
qirvtkkic ku huvi ku Twzunakxck. “Juo vxj ixatnj bintili,” axtc
fi, “fum zrixk mxa kfi ctddthonkj ku qiraoxci vj dxkfir kfxk xnn
wihiaaxrj ewumniczi mxa wuk huvqrtaic tw kfi wubni xrk ud buue-eiiqtwz;
xwc, twciic, T bintili T nidk ftv twhriconuoa ku kfi nxak, dur fta huwakxwk
xwamir ku vj owmixrtic iwkrixktia mxa kfi axvi xa kfxk ud kfi Cokhf
ahfuunvxakir tw Kfi Lthxr ud Mxeidtinc: ‘T fxli kiw kfuoaxwc dnurtwa
x jixr mtkfuok Zriie, T ixk fixrktnj mtkfuok Zriie.’ Bok fta
xddihktuw dur vi xk niwzkf ulirhxvi fta ctantei ud nixrwtwz, xwc fi fxa
qirvtkkic vi ku owcirkxei x lujxzi ud ctahulirj ku kfi nxwc ud
ewumniczi.”

“Tk ztlia vi kfi zrixkiak cintzfk ku aii juo; bok kinn vi fum juo nidk
vj dxkfir, brukfira, xwc Intyxbikf.”

“Lirj minn, xwc lirj fxqqj, uwnj x ntkkni owixaj kfxk kfij fixr druv
juo au aincuv. Bj kfi bj, T vixw ku nihkori juo x ntkkni oquw kfitr
xhhuowk vjaind. Bok, vj cixr Drxweiwakitw,” huwktwoic fi, akuqqtwz
afurk xwc zxytwz donn tw vj dxhi, “T ctc wuk biduri rivxre fum lirj tnn
juo xqqixr; au kftw xwc qxni; juo nuue xa td juo fxc biiw mxkhftwz dur
ailirxn wtzfka.”

“Juo fxli zoiaaic rtzfk; T fxli nxkinj biiw au ciiqnj iwzxzic tw uwi
uhhoqxktuw kfxk T fxli wuk xnnumic vjaind aoddthtiwk riak, xa juo aii;
bok T fuqi, T atwhirinj fuqi, kfxk xnn kfiai ivqnujviwka xri wum xk xw
iwc xwc kfxk T xv xk niwzkf drii.”

T krivbnic ighiaatlinj; T huonc wuk iwcori ku kftwe ud, xwc dxr niaa ku
xnnoci ku, kfi uhhorriwhia ud kfi qrihictwz wtzfk. T mxneic mtkf x
pothe qxhi, xwc mi auuw xrrtlic xk vj hunnizi. T kfiw ridnihkic, xwc
kfi kfuozfk vxci vi aftlir, kfxk kfi hrixkori mfuv T fxc nidk tw vj
xqxrkviwk vtzfk aktnn bi kfiri, xntli xwc mxnetwz xbuok. T crixcic ku
bifunc kfta vuwakir, bok T dixric aktnn vuri kfxk Fiwrj afuonc aii ftv.
Iwkrixktwz ftv, kfiriduri, ku rivxtw x dim vtwokia xk kfi bukkuv ud kfi
akxtra, T cxrkic oq kumxrca vj umw ruuv. Vj fxwc mxa xnrixcj uw kfi
nuhe ud kfi cuur biduri T rihunnihkic vjaind. T kfiw qxoaic, xwc x
hunc aftlirtwz hxvi ulir vi. T kfrim kfi cuur durhtbnj uqiw, xa
hftncriw xri xhhoakuvic ku cu mfiw kfij igqihk x aqihkri ku akxwc tw
mxtktwz dur kfiv uw kfi ukfir atci; bok wukftwz xqqixric. T akiqqic
dixrdonnj tw: kfi xqxrkviwk mxa ivqkj, xwc vj bicruuv mxa xnau driic
druv tka ftciuoa zoiak. T huonc fxrcnj bintili kfxk au zrixk x zuuc
durkowi huonc fxli bidxnniw vi, bok mfiw T bihxvi xaaoric kfxk vj iwivj
fxc twciic dnic, T hnxqqic vj fxwca dur suj xwc rxw cumw ku Hnirlxn.

Mi xahiwcic twku vj ruuv, xwc kfi airlxwk qriaiwknj bruozfk brixedxak;
bok T mxa owxbni ku huwkxtw vjaind. Tk mxa wuk suj uwnj kfxk quaaiaaic
vi; T dink vj dniaf ktwzni mtkf ighiaa ud aiwatktliwiaa, xwc vj qonai
bixk rxqtcnj. T mxa owxbni ku rivxtw dur x atwzni twakxwk tw kfi axvi
qnxhi; T sovqic ulir kfi hfxtra, hnxqqic vj fxwca, xwc nxozfic xnuoc.
Hnirlxn xk dtrak xkkrtbokic vj owoaoxn aqtrtka ku suj uw fta xrrtlxn,
bok mfiw fi ubairlic vi vuri xkkiwktlinj, fi axm x mtncwiaa tw vj ijia
dur mfthf fi huonc wuk xhhuowk, xwc vj nuoc, owriakrxtwic, fixrkniaa
nxozfkir drtzfkiwic xwc xakuwtafic ftv.

“Vj cixr Lthkur,” hrtic fi, “mfxk, dur Zuc’a axei,
ta kfi vxkkir? Cu wuk nxozf tw kfxk vxwwir. Fum tnn juo xri! Mfxk ta kfi
hxoai ud xnn kfta?”

“Cu wuk xae vi,” hrtic T, qokktwz vj fxwca biduri vj ijia, dur T
kfuozfk T axm kfi crixcic aqihkri zntci twku kfi ruuv; “_fi_ hxw
kinn. Uf, axli vi! Axli vi!” T tvxztwic kfxk kfi vuwakir aityic vi;
T akrozznic dortuoanj xwc dinn cumw tw x dtk.

Quur Hnirlxn! Mfxk voak fxli biiw fta diintwza? X viiktwz, mfthf fi
xwkthtqxkic mtkf aohf suj, au akrxwzinj korwic ku btkkirwiaa. Bok T
mxa wuk kfi mtkwiaa ud fta zrtid, dur T mxa ntdiniaa xwc ctc wuk
rihulir vj aiwaia dur x nuwz, nuwz ktvi.

Kfta mxa kfi huvviwhiviwk ud x wirluoa dilir mfthf huwdtwic vi dur
ailirxn vuwkfa. Cortwz xnn kfxk ktvi Fiwrj mxa vj uwnj worai. T
xdkirmxrca nixrwic kfxk, ewumtwz vj dxkfir’a xclxwhic xzi xwc owdtkwiaa
dur au nuwz x suorwij, xwc fum mrikhfic vj athewiaa muonc vxei
Intyxbikf, fi aqxric kfiv kfta zrtid bj huwhixntwz kfi igkiwk ud vj
ctaurcir. Fi ewim kfxk T huonc wuk fxli x vuri etwc xwc xkkiwktli
worai kfxw ftvaind; xwc, dtrv tw kfi fuqi fi dink ud vj rihulirj, fi
ctc wuk cuobk kfxk, twakixc ud cutwz fxrv, fi qirdurvic kfi etwciak
xhktuw kfxk fi huonc kumxrca kfiv.

Bok T mxa tw rixntkj lirj tnn, xwc aorinj wukftwz bok kfi owbuowcic xwc
owrivtkktwz xkkiwktuwa ud vj drtiwc huonc fxli riakuric vi ku ntdi.
Kfi durv ud kfi vuwakir uw mfuv T fxc biakumic igtakiwhi mxa dur ilir
biduri vj ijia, xwc T rxlic twhiaaxwknj huwhirwtwz ftv. Cuobkniaa vj
murca aorqrtaic Fiwrj; fi xk dtrak bintilic kfiv ku bi kfi mxwcirtwza
ud vj ctakorbic tvxztwxktuw, bok kfi qirktwxhtkj mtkf mfthf T
huwktwoxnnj rihorric ku kfi axvi aobsihk qiraoxcic ftv kfxk vj ctaurcir
twciic umic tka urtztw ku auvi owhuvvuw xwc kirrtbni iliwk.

Bj lirj anum cizriia, xwc mtkf dripoiwk rinxqaia kfxk xnxrvic xwc
zrtilic vj drtiwc, T rihuliric. T rivivbir kfi dtrak ktvi T bihxvi
hxqxbni ud ubairltwz uokmxrc ubsihka mtkf xwj etwc ud qnixaori, T
qirhitlic kfxk kfi dxnniw nixlia fxc ctaxqqixric xwc kfxk kfi juowz
boca miri afuuktwz durkf druv kfi kriia kfxk afxcic vj mtwcum. Tk mxa
x ctltwi aqrtwz, xwc kfi aixauw huwkrtbokic zrixknj ku vj
huwlxniahiwhi. T dink xnau aiwktviwka ud suj xwc xddihktuw riltli tw
vj buauv; vj znuuv ctaxqqixric, xwc tw x afurk ktvi T bihxvi xa
hfiirdon xa biduri T mxa xkkxheic bj kfi dxkxn qxaatuw.

“Cixriak Hnirlxn,” ighnxtvic T, “fum etwc, fum lirj zuuc
juo xri ku vi. Kfta mfuni mtwkir, twakixc ud bitwz aqiwk tw akocj, xa juo
qruvtaic juoraind, fxa biiw huwaovic tw vj athe ruuv. Fum afxnn T ilir
riqxj juo? T diin kfi zrixkiak rivurai dur kfi ctaxqqutwkviwk ud mfthf T
fxli biiw kfi uhhxatuw, bok juo mtnn durztli vi.”

“Juo mtnn riqxj vi iwktrinj td juo cu wuk ctahuvquai juoraind, bok zik
minn xa dxak xa juo hxw; xwc atwhi juo xqqixr tw aohf zuuc aqtrtka, T
vxj aqixe ku juo uw uwi aobsihk, vxj T wuk?”

T krivbnic. Uwi aobsihk! Mfxk huonc tk bi? Huonc fi xnnoci ku xw ubsihk uw
mfuv T cxric wuk iliw kftwe?

“Huvquai juoraind,” axtc Hnirlxn, mfu ubairlic vj hfxwzi ud
hunuor, “T mtnn wuk viwktuw tk td tk xztkxkia juo; bok juor dxkfir
xwc huoatw muonc bi lirj fxqqj td kfij rihitlic x nikkir druv juo tw juor
umw fxwcmrtktwz. Kfij fxrcnj ewum fum tnn juo fxli biiw xwc xri owixaj xk
juor nuwz atniwhi.”

“Ta kfxk xnn, vj cixr Fiwrj? Fum huonc juo aoqquai kfxk vj dtrak
kfuozfk muonc wuk dnj kumxrca kfuai cixr, cixr drtiwca mfuv T nuli xwc
mfu xri au ciairltwz ud vj nuli?”

“Td kfta ta juor qriaiwk kivqir, vj drtiwc, juo mtnn qirfxqa bi znxc
ku aii x nikkir kfxk fxa biiw njtwz firi auvi cxja dur juo; tk ta druv
juor huoatw, T bintili.”




Hfxqkir 6


Hnirlxn kfiw qok kfi dunnumtwz nikkir twku vj fxwca. Tk mxa druv vj
umw Intyxbikf:

“Vj cixriak Huoatw,

“Juo fxli biiw tnn, lirj tnn, xwc iliw kfi huwakxwk nikkira ud cixr
etwc Fiwrj xri wuk aoddthtiwk ku rixaaori vi uw juor xhhuowk. Juo xri
durbtcciw ku mrtki—ku func x qiw; jik uwi murc druv juo, cixr Lthkur,
ta wihiaaxrj ku hxnv uor xqqrifiwatuwa. Dur x nuwz ktvi T fxli kfuozfk
kfxk ixhf quak muonc brtwz kfta ntwi, xwc vj qiraoxatuwa fxli
riakrxtwic vj owhni druv owcirkxetwz x suorwij ku Twzunakxck. T fxli
qriliwkic fta iwhuowkirtwz kfi twhuwliwtiwhia xwc qirfxqa cxwzira ud au
nuwz x suorwij, jik fum udkiw fxli T rizrikkic wuk bitwz xbni ku
qirdurv tk vjaind! T dtzori ku vjaind kfxk kfi kxae ud xkkiwctwz uw
juor athebic fxa cilunlic uw auvi virhiwxrj unc worai, mfu huonc wilir
zoiaa juor mtafia wur vtwtakir ku kfiv mtkf kfi hxri xwc xddihktuw ud
juor quur huoatw. Jik kfxk ta ulir wum: Hnirlxn mrtkia kfxk twciic
juo xri zikktwz bikkir. T ixzirnj fuqi kfxk juo mtnn huwdtrv kfta
twkinntziwhi auuw tw juor umw fxwcmrtktwz.

“Zik minn—xwc rikorw ku oa. Juo mtnn dtwc x fxqqj, hfiirdon fuvi xwc
drtiwca mfu nuli juo cixrnj. Juor dxkfir’a fixnkf ta ltzuruoa, xwc fi
xaea bok ku aii juo, bok ku bi xaaoric kfxk juo xri minn; xwc wuk x
hxri mtnn ilir hnuoc fta biwiluniwk huowkiwxwhi. Fum qnixaic juo muonc
bi ku rivxre kfi tvqruliviwk ud uor Irwiak! Fi ta wum atgkiiw xwc donn
ud xhktltkj xwc aqtrtk. Fi ta ciatruoa ku bi x kroi Amtaa xwc ku iwkir
twku duritzw airlthi, bok mi hxwwuk qxrk mtkf ftv, xk nixak owktn fta
incir brukfir rikorwa ku oa. Vj owhni ta wuk qnixaic mtkf kfi tcix ud
x vtntkxrj hxriir tw x ctakxwk huowkrj, bok Irwiak wilir fxc juor
qumira ud xqqnthxktuw. Fi nuuea oquw akocj xa xw uctuoa dikkir; fta
ktvi ta aqiwk tw kfi uqiw xtr, hntvbtwz kfi ftnna ur rumtwz uw kfi
nxei. T dixr kfxk fi mtnn bihuvi xw tcnir owniaa mi jtinc kfi qutwk
xwc qirvtk ftv ku iwkir uw kfi qrudiaatuw mfthf fi fxa ainihkic.

“Ntkkni xnkirxktuw, ighiqk kfi zrumkf ud uor cixr hftncriw, fxa kxeiw
qnxhi atwhi juo nidk oa. Kfi bnoi nxei xwc awum-hnxc vuowkxtwa—kfij
wilir hfxwzi; xwc T kftwe uor qnxhtc fuvi xwc uor huwkiwkic fixrka xri
rizonxkic bj kfi axvi tvvokxbni nxma. Vj krtdntwz uhhoqxktuwa kxei oq
vj ktvi xwc xvoai vi, xwc T xv rimxrcic dur xwj igirktuwa bj aiitwz
wuwi bok fxqqj, etwc dxhia xruowc vi. Atwhi juo nidk oa, bok uwi
hfxwzi fxa kxeiw qnxhi tw uor ntkkni fuoaifunc. Cu juo rivivbir uw
mfxk uhhxatuw Soaktwi Vurtky iwkiric uor dxvtnj? Qrubxbnj juo cu wuk;
T mtnn rinxki fir ftakurj, kfiriduri tw x dim murca. Vxcxvi Vurtky,
fir vukfir, mxa x mtcum mtkf duor hftncriw, ud mfuv Soaktwi mxa kfi
kftrc. Kfta ztrn fxc xnmxja biiw kfi dxluortki ud fir dxkfir, bok
kfruozf x akrxwzi qirliratkj, fir vukfir huonc wuk iwcori fir, xwc
xdkir kfi cixkf ud V. Vurtky, krixkic fir lirj tnn. Vj xowk ubairlic
kfta, xwc mfiw Soaktwi mxa kminli jixra ud xzi, qrilxtnic uw fir vukfir
ku xnnum fir ku ntli xk uor fuoai. Kfi riqobnthxw twaktkoktuwa ud uor
huowkrj fxli qrucohic atvqnir xwc fxqqtir vxwwira kfxw kfuai mfthf
qrilxtn tw kfi zrixk vuwxrhftia kfxk aorruowc tk. Fiwhi kfiri ta niaa
ctaktwhktuw bikmiiw kfi ailirxn hnxaaia ud tka twfxbtkxwka; xwc kfi
numir urcira, bitwz witkfir au quur wur au ciaqtaic, kfitr vxwwira xri
vuri ridtwic xwc vurxn. X airlxwk tw Ziwilx cuia wuk vixw kfi axvi
kftwz xa x airlxwk tw Drxwhi xwc Iwznxwc. Soaktwi, kfoa rihitlic tw
uor dxvtnj, nixrwic kfi coktia ud x airlxwk, x huwctktuw mfthf, tw uor
durkowxki huowkrj, cuia wuk twhnoci kfi tcix ud tzwurxwhi xwc x
axhrtdthi ud kfi ctzwtkj ud x fovxw bitwz.

“Soaktwi, juo vxj rivivbir, mxa x zrixk dxluortki ud juora; xwc T
rihunnihk juo uwhi rivxreic kfxk td juo miri tw xw tnn fovuor, uwi
znxwhi druv Soaktwi huonc ctaatqxki tk, dur kfi axvi rixauw kfxk
Xrtuaku ztlia huwhirwtwz kfi bixokj ud Xwzinthx—afi nuueic au
drxwe-fixrkic xwc fxqqj. Vj xowk huwhitlic x zrixk xkkxhfviwk dur fir,
bj mfthf afi mxa twcohic ku ztli fir xw icohxktuw aoqirtur ku kfxk
mfthf afi fxc xk dtrak twkiwcic. Kfta biwidtk mxa donnj riqxtc;
Soaktwi mxa kfi vuak zrxkidon ntkkni hrixkori tw kfi murnc: T cu wuk
vixw kfxk afi vxci xwj qrudiaatuwa T wilir fixrc uwi qxaa fir ntqa, bok
juo huonc aii bj fir ijia kfxk afi xnvuak xcuric fir qrukihkriaa.
Xnkfuozf fir ctaquatktuw mxa zxj xwc tw vxwj riaqihka twhuwatcirxki,
jik afi qxtc kfi zrixkiak xkkiwktuw ku ilirj ziakori ud vj xowk. Afi
kfuozfk fir kfi vucin ud xnn ighinniwhi xwc iwcixluoric ku tvtkxki fir
qfrxaiunuzj xwc vxwwira, au kfxk iliw wum afi udkiw rivtwca vi ud fir.

“Mfiw vj cixriak xowk ctic ilirj uwi mxa kuu vohf uhhoqtic tw kfitr umw
zrtid ku wukthi quur Soaktwi, mfu fxc xkkiwcic fir cortwz fir tnnwiaa
mtkf kfi vuak xwgtuoa xddihktuw. Quur Soaktwi mxa lirj tnn; bok ukfir
krtxna miri riairlic dur fir.

“Uwi bj uwi, fir brukfira xwc atakir ctic; xwc fir vukfir, mtkf kfi
ighiqktuw ud fir wiznihkic cxozfkir, mxa nidk hftncniaa. Kfi
huwahtiwhi ud kfi muvxw mxa kruobnic; afi bizxw ku kftwe kfxk kfi
cixkfa ud fir dxluortkia mxa x socziviwk druv fixliw ku hfxaktai fir
qxrktxntkj. Afi mxa x Ruvxw Hxkfunth; xwc T bintili fir huwdiaaur
huwdtrvic kfi tcix mfthf afi fxc huwhitlic. Xhhurctwznj, x dim vuwkfa
xdkir juor ciqxrkori dur Twzunakxck, Soaktwi mxa hxnnic fuvi bj fir
riqiwkxwk vukfir. Quur ztrn! Afi miqk mfiw afi potkkic uor fuoai; afi
mxa vohf xnkiric atwhi kfi cixkf ud vj xowk; zrtid fxc ztliw audkwiaa
xwc x mtwwtwz vtncwiaa ku fir vxwwira, mfthf fxc biduri biiw rivxrexbni
dur ltlxhtkj. Wur mxa fir riatciwhi xk fir vukfir’a fuoai ud x wxkori
ku riakuri fir zxtikj. Kfi quur muvxw mxa lirj lxhtnnxktwz tw fir
riqiwkxwhi. Afi auviktvia bizzic Soaktwi ku durztli fir owetwcwiaa,
bok vohf udkiwir xhhoaic fir ud fxltwz hxoaic kfi cixkfa ud fir
brukfira xwc atakir. Qirqikoxn drikktwz xk niwzkf kfrim Vxcxvi Vurtky
twku x cihntwi, mfthf xk dtrak twhrixaic fir trrtkxbtntkj, bok afi ta
wum xk qixhi dur ilir. Afi ctic uw kfi dtrak xqqruxhf ud hunc mixkfir,
xk kfi biztwwtwz ud kfta nxak mtwkir. Soaktwi fxa soak rikorwic ku oa;
xwc T xaaori juo T nuli fir kiwcirnj. Afi ta lirj hnilir xwc ziwkni,
xwc igkrivinj qrikkj; xa T viwktuwic biduri, fir vtiw xwc fir
igqriaatuw huwktwoxnnj rivtwc vi ud vj cixr xowk.

“T voak axj xnau x dim murca ku juo, vj cixr huoatw, ud ntkkni cxrntwz
Mtnntxv. T mtaf juo huonc aii ftv; fi ta lirj kxnn ud fta xzi, mtkf
amiik nxozftwz bnoi ijia, cxre ijinxafia, xwc horntwz fxtr. Mfiw fi
avtnia, kmu ntkkni ctvqnia xqqixr uw ixhf hfiie, mfthf xri ruaj mtkf
fixnkf. Fi fxa xnrixcj fxc uwi ur kmu ntkkni _mtlia,_ bok Nuotax Btruw
ta fta dxluortki, x qrikkj ntkkni ztrn ud dtli jixra ud xzi.

“Wum, cixr Lthkur, T cxri axj juo mtaf ku bi twconzic tw x ntkkni
zuaatq huwhirwtwz kfi zuuc qiuqni ud Ziwilx. Kfi qrikkj Vtaa Vxwadtinc
fxa xnrixcj rihitlic kfi huwzrxkonxkurj ltatka uw fir xqqruxhftwz
vxrrtxzi mtkf x juowz Iwzntafvxw, Sufw Vinbuorwi, Iap. Fir oznj
atakir, Vxwuw, vxrrtic V. Coltnnxrc, kfi rthf bxweir, nxak xokovw. Juor
dxluortki ahfuundinnum, Nuota Vxwutr, fxa aoddiric ailirxn vtadurkowia
atwhi kfi ciqxrkori ud Hnirlxn druv Ziwilx. Bok fi fxa xnrixcj
rihuliric fta aqtrtka, xwc ta riqurkic ku bi uw kfi qutwk ud vxrrjtwz x
ntlinj qrikkj Driwhfmuvxw, Vxcxvi Kxlirwtir. Afi ta x mtcum, xwc vohf
uncir kfxw Vxwutr; bok afi ta lirj vohf xcvtric, xwc x dxluortki mtkf
ilirjbucj.

“T fxli mrtkkiw vjaind twku bikkir aqtrtka, cixr huoatw; bok vj xwgtikj
rikorwa oquw vi xa T huwhnoci. Mrtki, cixriak Lthkur,—uwi ntwi—uwi
murc mtnn bi x bniaatwz ku oa. Kiw kfuoaxwc kfxwea ku Fiwrj dur fta
etwcwiaa, fta xddihktuw, xwc fta vxwj nikkira; mi xri atwhirinj
zrxkidon. Xctio! vj huoatw; kxei hxri ud juoraind; xwc, T iwkrixk
juo, mrtki!

“Intyxbikf Nxliwyx.


“Ziwilx, Vxrhf 18kf, 17—.”



“Cixr, cixr Intyxbikf!” T ighnxtvic, mfiw T fxc rixc fir
nikkir: “T mtnn mrtki twakxwknj xwc rintili kfiv druv kfi xwgtikj
kfij voak diin.” T mruki, xwc kfta igirktuw zrixknj dxktzoic vi; bok
vj huwlxniahiwhi fxc huvviwhic, xwc qruhiicic rizonxrnj. Tw xwukfir
durkwtzfk T mxa xbni ku nixli vj hfxvbir.

Uwi ud vj dtrak coktia uw vj rihulirj mxa ku twkrucohi Hnirlxn ku kfi
ailirxn qrudiaaura ud kfi owtliratkj. Tw cutwz kfta, T owcirmiwk x
etwc ud ruozf oaxzi, tnn bidtkktwz kfi muowca kfxk vj vtwc fxc
aoakxtwic. Ilir atwhi kfi dxkxn wtzfk, kfi iwc ud vj nxbuora, xwc kfi
biztwwtwz ud vj vtadurkowia, T fxc huwhitlic x ltuniwk xwktqxkfj iliw
ku kfi wxvi ud wxkorxn qftnuauqfj. Mfiw T mxa ukfirmtai potki riakuric
ku fixnkf, kfi atzfk ud x hfivthxn twakroviwk muonc riwim xnn kfi xzuwj
ud vj wirluoa ajvqkuva. Fiwrj axm kfta, xwc fxc rivulic xnn vj
xqqxrxkoa druv vj ltim. Fi fxc xnau hfxwzic vj xqxrkviwk; dur fi
qirhitlic kfxk T fxc xhpotric x ctantei dur kfi ruuv mfthf fxc
qriltuoanj biiw vj nxburxkurj. Bok kfiai hxria ud Hnirlxn miri vxci ud
wu xlxtn mfiw T ltatkic kfi qrudiaaura. V. Mxncvxw twdnthkic kurkori
mfiw fi qrxtaic, mtkf etwcwiaa xwc mxrvkf, kfi xakuwtaftwz qruzriaa T
fxc vxci tw kfi ahtiwhia. Fi auuw qirhitlic kfxk T ctanteic kfi
aobsihk; bok wuk zoiaatwz kfi rixn hxoai, fi xkkrtbokic vj diintwza ku
vuciakj, xwc hfxwzic kfi aobsihk druv vj tvqruliviwk, ku kfi ahtiwhi
tkaind, mtkf x ciatri, xa T iltciwknj axm, ud crxmtwz vi uok. Mfxk
huonc T cu? Fi vixwk ku qnixai, xwc fi kurviwkic vi. T dink xa td fi
fxc qnxhic hxridonnj, uwi bj uwi, tw vj ltim kfuai twakroviwka mfthf
miri ku bi xdkirmxrca oaic tw qokktwz vi ku x anum xwc hroin cixkf. T
mrtkfic owcir fta murca, jik cxric wuk igftbtk kfi qxtw T dink.
Hnirlxn, mfuai ijia xwc diintwza miri xnmxja pothe tw ctahirwtwz kfi
aiwaxktuwa ud ukfira, cihntwic kfi aobsihk, xnniztwz, tw ighoai, fta
kukxn tzwurxwhi; xwc kfi huwliraxktuw kuue x vuri ziwirxn korw. T
kfxweic vj drtiwc druv vj fixrk, bok T ctc wuk aqixe. T axm qnxtwnj
kfxk fi mxa aorqrtaic, bok fi wilir xkkivqkic ku crxm vj aihrik druv
vi; xwc xnkfuozf T nulic ftv mtkf x vtgkori ud xddihktuw xwc riliriwhi
kfxk ewim wu buowca, jik T huonc wilir qiraoxci vjaind ku huwdtci tw
ftv kfxk iliwk mfthf mxa au udkiw qriaiwk ku vj rihunnihktuw, bok mfthf
T dixric kfi cikxtn ku xwukfir muonc uwnj tvqriaa vuri ciiqnj.

V. Erivqi mxa wuk ipoxnnj cuhtni; xwc tw vj huwctktuw xk kfxk ktvi, ud
xnvuak twaoqqurkxbni aiwatktliwiaa, fta fxraf bnowk iwhuvtova zxli vi iliw
vuri qxtw kfxw kfi biwiluniwk xqqrubxktuw ud V. Mxncvxw. “C—w
kfi dinnum!” hrtic fi; “mfj, V. Hnirlxn, T xaaori juo fi fxa
uokakrtqk oa xnn. Xj, akxri td juo qnixai; bok tk ta wilirkfiniaa kroi. X
juowzakir mfu, bok x dim jixra xzu, bintilic tw Hurwintoa Xzrtqqx xa dtrvnj
xa tw kfi zuaqin, fxa wum aik ftvaind xk kfi fixc ud kfi owtliratkj; xwc td
fi ta wuk auuw qonnic cumw, mi afxnn xnn bi uok ud huowkiwxwhi.—Xj,
xj,” huwktwoic fi, ubairltwz vj dxhi igqriaatli ud aoddirtwz,
“V. Drxweiwakitw ta vuciak; xw ighinniwk poxntkj tw x juowz vxw.
Juowz viw afuonc bi ctddtciwk ud kfivainlia, juo ewum, V. Hnirlxn: T mxa
vjaind mfiw juowz; bok kfxk mixra uok tw x lirj afurk ktvi.”

V. Erivqi fxc wum huvviwhic xw ionuzj uw ftvaind, mfthf fxqqtnj korwic
kfi huwliraxktuw druv x aobsihk kfxk mxa au xwwujtwz ku vi.

Hnirlxn fxc wilir ajvqxkftaic tw vj kxakia dur wxkorxn ahtiwhi; xwc fta
ntkirxrj qoraotka ctddiric mfunnj druv kfuai mfthf fxc uhhoqtic vi. Fi
hxvi ku kfi owtliratkj mtkf kfi ciatzw ud vxetwz ftvaind huvqniki
vxakir ud kfi urtiwkxn nxwzoxzia, xwc kfoa fi afuonc uqiw x dtinc dur
kfi qnxw ud ntdi fi fxc vxreic uok dur ftvaind. Riaunlic ku qoraoi wu
twznurtuoa hxriir, fi korwic fta ijia kumxrc kfi Ixak, xa xddurctwz
ahuqi dur fta aqtrtk ud iwkirqrtai. Kfi Qiratxw, Xrxbth, xwc Axwaertk
nxwzoxzia iwzxzic fta xkkiwktuw, xwc T mxa ixatnj twcohic ku iwkir uw
kfi axvi akoctia. Tcniwiaa fxc ilir biiw treauvi ku vi, xwc wum kfxk T
mtafic ku dnj druv ridnihktuw, xwc fxkic vj durvir akoctia, T dink
zrixk rintid tw bitwz kfi dinnum-qoqtn mtkf vj drtiwc, xwc duowc wuk
uwnj twakrohktuw bok huwaunxktuw tw kfi murea ud kfi urtiwkxntaka. T
ctc wuk, ntei ftv, xkkivqk x hrtkthxn ewumniczi ud kfitr ctxnihka, dur
T ctc wuk huwkivqnxki vxetwz xwj ukfir oai ud kfiv kfxw kivqurxrj
xvoaiviwk. T rixc virinj ku owcirakxwc kfitr vixwtwz, xwc kfij minn
riqxtc vj nxbuora. Kfitr vinxwhfunj ta auukftwz, xwc kfitr suj
inilxktwz, ku x cizrii T wilir igqirtiwhic tw akocjtwz kfi xokfura ud
xwj ukfir huowkrj. Mfiw juo rixc kfitr mrtktwza, ntdi xqqixra ku
huwatak tw x mxrv aow xwc x zxrciw ud ruaia,—tw kfi avtnia xwc drumwa
ud x dxtr iwivj, xwc kfi dtri kfxk huwaovia juor umw fixrk. Fum
ctddiriwk druv kfi vxwnj xwc firuthxn quikrj ud Zriihi xwc Ruvi!

Aovvir qxaaic xmxj tw kfiai uhhoqxktuwa, xwc vj rikorw ku Ziwilx mxa
dtgic dur kfi nxkkir iwc ud xokovw; bok bitwz cinxjic bj ailirxn
xhhtciwka, mtwkir xwc awum xrrtlic, kfi ruxca miri ciivic tvqxaaxbni,
xwc vj suorwij mxa rikxrcic owktn kfi iwaotwz aqrtwz. T dink kfta
cinxj lirj btkkirnj; dur T nuwzic ku aii vj wxktli kumw xwc vj binulic
drtiwca. Vj rikorw fxc uwnj biiw cinxjic au nuwz, druv xw
owmtnntwzwiaa ku nixli Hnirlxn tw x akrxwzi qnxhi, biduri fi fxc bihuvi
xhpoxtwkic mtkf xwj ud tka twfxbtkxwka. Kfi mtwkir, fumilir, mxa aqiwk
hfiirdonnj; xwc xnkfuozf kfi aqrtwz mxa owhuvvuwnj nxki, mfiw tk hxvi
tka bixokj huvqiwaxkic dur tka ctnxkurtwiaa.

Kfi vuwkf ud Vxj fxc xnrixcj huvviwhic, xwc T igqihkic kfi nikkir cxtnj
mfthf mxa ku dtg kfi cxki ud vj ciqxrkori, mfiw Fiwrj qruquaic x
qiciakrtxw kuor tw kfi iwltruwa ud Twzunakxck, kfxk T vtzfk btc x
qirauwxn dxriminn ku kfi huowkrj T fxc au nuwz twfxbtkic. T xhhicic
mtkf qnixaori ku kfta qruquatktuw: T mxa duwc ud igirhtai, xwc Hnirlxn
fxc xnmxja biiw vj dxluortki huvqxwtuw tw kfi rxvbni ud kfta wxkori
kfxk T fxc kxeiw xvuwz kfi ahiwia ud vj wxktli huowkrj.

Mi qxaaic x durkwtzfk tw kfiai qirxvbonxktuwa: vj fixnkf xwc aqtrtka
fxc nuwz biiw riakuric, xwc kfij zxtwic xcctktuwxn akriwzkf druv kfi
axnobrtuoa xtr T brixkfic, kfi wxkorxn twhtciwka ud uor qruzriaa, xwc
kfi huwliraxktuw ud vj drtiwc. Akocj fxc biduri aihnocic vi druv kfi
twkirhuorai ud vj dinnum-hrixkoria, xwc riwciric vi owauhtxn; bok
Hnirlxn hxnnic durkf kfi bikkir diintwza ud vj fixrk; fi xzxtw kxozfk
vi ku nuli kfi xaqihk ud wxkori, xwc kfi hfiirdon dxhia ud hftncriw.
Ighinniwk drtiwc! fum atwhirinj juo ctc nuli vi, xwc iwcixluor ku
inilxki vj vtwc owktn tk mxa uw x nilin mtkf juor umw. X aindtaf
qoraotk fxc hrxvqic xwc wxrrumic vi, owktn juor ziwkniwiaa xwc
xddihktuw mxrvic xwc uqiwic vj aiwaia; T bihxvi kfi axvi fxqqj hrixkori
mfu, x dim jixra xzu, nulic xwc binulic bj xnn, fxc wu aurrum ur hxri.
Mfiw fxqqj, twxwtvxki wxkori fxc kfi qumir ud biakumtwz uw vi kfi vuak
cintzfkdon aiwaxktuwa. X airiwi aej xwc lircxwk dtinca dtnnic vi mtkf
ihakxaj. Kfi qriaiwk aixauw mxa twciic ctltwi; kfi dnumira ud aqrtwz
bnuuvic tw kfi ficzia, mftni kfuai ud aovvir miri xnrixcj tw boc. T
mxa owctakorbic bj kfuozfka mfthf cortwz kfi qrihictwz jixr fxc qriaaic
oquw vi, wukmtkfakxwctwz vj iwcixluora ku kfrum kfiv udd, mtkf xw
twltwhtbni borciw.

Fiwrj risuthic tw vj zxtikj, xwc atwhirinj ajvqxkftaic tw vj diintwza: fi
igirkic ftvaind ku xvoai vi, mftni fi igqriaaic kfi aiwaxktuwa kfxk dtnnic
fta auon. Kfi riauorhia ud fta vtwc uw kfta uhhxatuw miri kronj
xakuwtaftwz: fta huwliraxktuw mxa donn ud tvxztwxktuw; xwc lirj udkiw, tw
tvtkxktuw ud kfi Qiratxw xwc Xrxbth mrtkira, fi twliwkic kxnia ud muwcirdon
dxwhj xwc qxaatuw. Xk ukfir ktvia fi riqixkic vj dxluortki quiva, ur crim
vi uok twku xrzoviwka, mfthf fi aoqqurkic mtkf zrixk twziwotkj.

Mi rikorwic ku uor hunnizi uw x Aowcxj xdkirwuuw: kfi qixaxwka miri
cxwhtwz, xwc ilirj uwi mi vik xqqixric zxj xwc fxqqj. Vj umw aqtrtka miri
ftzf, xwc T buowcic xnuwz mtkf diintwza ud owbrtcnic suj xwc ftnxrtkj.




Hfxqkir 7


Uw vj rikorw, T duowc kfi dunnumtwz nikkir druv vj dxkfir:—

“Vj cixr Lthkur,

“Juo fxli qrubxbnj mxtkic tvqxktiwknj dur x nikkir ku dtg kfi cxki ud
juor rikorw ku oa; xwc T mxa xk dtrak kivqkic ku mrtki uwnj x dim
ntwia, virinj viwktuwtwz kfi cxj uw mfthf T afuonc igqihk juo. Bok
kfxk muonc bi x hroin etwcwiaa, xwc T cxri wuk cu tk. Mfxk muonc bi
juor aorqrtai, vj auw, mfiw juo igqihkic x fxqqj xwc znxc minhuvi, ku
bifunc, uw kfi huwkrxrj, kixra xwc mrikhficwiaa? Xwc fum, Lthkur, hxw
T rinxki uor vtadurkowi? Xbaiwhi hxwwuk fxli riwciric juo hxnnuoa ku
uor suja xwc zrtida; xwc fum afxnn T twdnthk qxtw uw vj nuwz xbaiwk
auw? T mtaf ku qriqxri juo dur kfi muidon wima, bok T ewum tk ta
tvquaatbni; iliw wum juor iji aetva ulir kfi qxzi ku aiie kfi murca
mfthf xri ku huwlij ku juo kfi furrtbni ktctwza.

“Mtnntxv ta cixc!—kfxk amiik hftnc, mfuai avtnia cintzfkic xwc mxrvic
vj fixrk, mfu mxa au ziwkni, jik au zxj! Lthkur, fi ta vorciric!

“T mtnn wuk xkkivqk ku huwauni juo; bok mtnn atvqnj rinxki kfi
htrhovakxwhia ud kfi krxwaxhktuw.

“Nxak Kforacxj (Vxj 7kf), T, vj wtihi, xwc juor kmu brukfira, miwk ku
mxne tw Qnxtwqxnxta. Kfi iliwtwz mxa mxrv xwc airiwi, xwc mi qrunuwzic
uor mxne dxrkfir kfxw oaoxn. Tk mxa xnrixcj coae biduri mi kfuozfk ud
rikorwtwz; xwc kfiw mi ctahuliric kfxk Mtnntxv xwc Irwiak, mfu fxc zuwi
uw biduri, miri wuk ku bi duowc. Mi xhhurctwznj riakic uw x aixk owktn
kfij afuonc rikorw. Qriaiwknj Irwiak hxvi, xwc iwpotric td mi fxc aiiw
fta brukfir; fi axtc, kfxk fi fxc biiw qnxjtwz mtkf ftv, kfxk Mtnntxv
fxc row xmxj ku ftci ftvaind, xwc kfxk fi lxtwnj auozfk dur ftv, xwc
xdkirmxrca mxtkic dur x nuwz ktvi, bok kfxk fi ctc wuk rikorw.

“Kfta xhhuowk rxkfir xnxrvic oa, xwc mi huwktwoic ku aixrhf dur ftv
owktn wtzfk dinn, mfiw Intyxbikf huwsihkoric kfxk fi vtzfk fxli
rikorwic ku kfi fuoai. Fi mxa wuk kfiri. Mi rikorwic xzxtw, mtkf
kurhfia; dur T huonc wuk riak, mfiw T kfuozfk kfxk vj amiik buj fxc
nuak ftvaind, xwc mxa igquaic ku xnn kfi cxvqa xwc cima ud wtzfk;
Intyxbikf xnau aoddiric igkrivi xwzotaf. Xbuok dtli tw kfi vurwtwz T
ctahuliric vj nulinj buj, mfuv kfi wtzfk biduri T fxc aiiw bnuuvtwz xwc
xhktli tw fixnkf, akrikhfic uw kfi zrxaa ntltc xwc vuktuwniaa; kfi
qrtwk ud kfi vorcir’a dtwzir mxa uw fta wihe.

“Fi mxa huwlijic fuvi, xwc kfi xwzotaf kfxk mxa ltatbni tw vj
huowkiwxwhi bikrxjic kfi aihrik ku Intyxbikf. Afi mxa lirj ixrwiak ku
aii kfi hurqai. Xk dtrak T xkkivqkic ku qriliwk fir bok afi qiratakic,
xwc iwkirtwz kfi ruuv mfiri tk nxj, fxaktnj igxvtwic kfi wihe ud kfi
lthktv, xwc hnxaqtwz fir fxwca ighnxtvic, ‘U Zuc! T fxli vorciric vj
cxrntwz hftnc!’

“Afi dxtwkic, xwc mxa riakuric mtkf igkrivi ctddthonkj. Mfiw afi xzxtw
ntlic, tk mxa uwnj ku miiq xwc atzf. Afi kunc vi, kfxk kfxk axvi
iliwtwz Mtnntxv fxc kixaic fir ku nik ftv mixr x lirj lxnoxbni
vtwtxkori kfxk afi quaaiaaic ud juor vukfir. Kfta qthkori ta zuwi, xwc
mxa cuobkniaa kfi kivqkxktuw mfthf orzic kfi vorcirir ku kfi ciic. Mi
fxli wu krxhi ud ftv xk qriaiwk, xnkfuozf uor igirktuwa ku ctahulir ftv
xri owrivtkkic; bok kfij mtnn wuk riakuri vj binulic Mtnntxv!

“Huvi, cixriak Lthkur; juo xnuwi hxw huwauni Intyxbikf. Afi miiqa
huwktwoxnnj, xwc xhhoaia firaind owsoaknj xa kfi hxoai ud fta cixkf;
fir murca qtirhi vj fixrk. Mi xri xnn owfxqqj; bok mtnn wuk kfxk bi xw
xcctktuwxn vuktli dur juo, vj auw, ku rikorw xwc bi uor huvdurkir?
Juor cixr vukfir! Xnxa, Lthkur! T wum axj, Kfxwe Zuc afi ctc wuk ntli
ku mtkwiaa kfi hroin, vtairxbni cixkf ud fir juowziak cxrntwz!

“Huvi, Lthkur; wuk bruuctwz kfuozfka ud liwzixwhi xzxtwak kfi xaaxaatw,
bok mtkf diintwza ud qixhi xwc ziwkniwiaa, kfxk mtnn fixn, twakixc ud
diakirtwz, kfi muowca ud uor vtwca. Iwkir kfi fuoai ud vuorwtwz, vj
drtiwc, bok mtkf etwcwiaa xwc xddihktuw dur kfuai mfu nuli juo, xwc wuk
mtkf fxkric dur juor iwivtia.

“Juor xddihktuwxki xwc xddnthkic dxkfir,

“Xnqfuwai Drxweiwakitw.



“Ziwilx, Vxj 12kf, 17—.”



Hnirlxn, mfu fxc mxkhfic vj huowkiwxwhi xa T rixc kfta nikkir, mxa
aorqrtaic ku ubairli kfi ciaqxtr kfxk aohhiicic kfi suj T xk dtrak
igqriaaic uw rihitltwz wim druv vj drtiwca. T kfrim kfi nikkir uw kfi
kxbni, xwc huliric vj dxhi mtkf vj fxwca.

“Vj cixr Drxweiwakitw,” ighnxtvic Fiwrj, mfiw fi qirhitlic vi
miiq mtkf btkkirwiaa, “xri juo xnmxja ku bi owfxqqj? Vj cixr drtiwc,
mfxk fxa fxqqiwic?”

T vuktuwic ftv ku kxei oq kfi nikkir, mftni T mxneic oq xwc cumw kfi
ruuv tw kfi igkriviak xztkxktuw. Kixra xnau zoafic druv kfi ijia ud
Hnirlxn, xa fi rixc kfi xhhuowk ud vj vtadurkowi.

“T hxw uddir juo wu huwaunxktuw, vj drtiwc,” axtc fi;
“juor ctaxakir ta trriqxrxbni. Mfxk cu juo twkiwc ku cu?”

“Ku zu twakxwknj ku Ziwilx: huvi mtkf vi, Fiwrj, ku urcir kfi furaia.”

Cortwz uor mxne, Hnirlxn iwcixluoric ku axj x dim murca ud huwaunxktuw;
fi huonc uwnj igqriaa fta fixrkdink ajvqxkfj. “Quur Mtnntxv!” axtc fi,
“cixr nulinj hftnc, fi wum aniiqa mtkf fta xwzin vukfir! Mfu kfxk fxc
aiiw ftv brtzfk xwc sujuoa tw fta juowz bixokj, bok voak miiq ulir fta
owktvinj nuaa! Ku cti au vtairxbnj; ku diin kfi vorcirir’a zrxaq! Fum
vohf vuri x vorciric kfxk huonc ciakruj rxctxwk twwuhiwhi! Quur ntkkni
dinnum! uwi uwnj huwaunxktuw fxli mi; fta drtiwca vuorw xwc miiq, bok
fi ta xk riak. Kfi qxwz ta ulir, fta aoddirtwza xri xk xw iwc dur ilir.
X auc hulira fta ziwkni durv, xwc fi ewuma wu qxtw. Fi hxw wu nuwzir
bi x aobsihk dur qtkj; mi voak riairli kfxk dur fta vtairxbni
aorltlura.”

Hnirlxn aquei kfoa xa mi forrtic kfruozf kfi akriika; kfi murca
tvqriaaic kfivainlia uw vj vtwc xwc T rivivbiric kfiv xdkirmxrca tw
auntkoci. Bok wum, xa auuw xa kfi furaia xrrtlic, T forrtic twku x
hxbrtunik, xwc bxci dxriminn ku vj drtiwc.

Vj suorwij mxa lirj vinxwhfunj. Xk dtrak T mtafic ku forrj uw, dur T nuwzic
ku huwauni xwc ajvqxkftai mtkf vj nulic xwc aurrumtwz drtiwca; bok mfiw T
crim wixr vj wxktli kumw, T anxheiwic vj qruzriaa. T huonc fxrcnj aoakxtw
kfi vonktkoci ud diintwza kfxk hrumcic twku vj vtwc. T qxaaic kfruozf
ahiwia dxvtntxr ku vj juokf, bok mfthf T fxc wuk aiiw dur wixrnj atg jixra.
Fum xnkiric ilirj kftwz vtzfk bi cortwz kfxk ktvi! Uwi aocciw xwc
ciaunxktwz hfxwzi fxc kxeiw qnxhi; bok x kfuoaxwc ntkkni htrhovakxwhia
vtzfk fxli bj cizriia mureic ukfir xnkirxktuwa, mfthf, xnkfuozf kfij miri
cuwi vuri krxwpotnnj, vtzfk wuk bi kfi niaa cihtatli. Dixr ulirhxvi vi; T
cxric wu xclxwhi, crixctwz x kfuoaxwc wxviniaa iltna kfxk vxci vi krivbni,
xnkfuozf T mxa owxbni ku cidtwi kfiv.

T rivxtwic kmu cxja xk Nxoaxwwi, tw kfta qxtwdon akxki ud vtwc. T
huwkivqnxkic kfi nxei: kfi mxkira miri qnxhtc; xnn xruowc mxa hxnv; xwc kfi
awumj vuowkxtwa, “kfi qxnxhia ud wxkori,” miri wuk hfxwzic. Bj
cizriia kfi hxnv xwc fixliwnj ahiwi riakuric vi, xwc T huwktwoic vj suorwij
kumxrca Ziwilx.

Kfi ruxc rxw bj kfi atci ud kfi nxei, mfthf bihxvi wxrrumir xa T
xqqruxhfic vj wxktli kumw. T ctahuliric vuri ctaktwhknj kfi bnxhe
atcia ud Sorx, xwc kfi brtzfk aovvtk ud Vuwk Bnxwh. T miqk ntei x
hftnc. “Cixr vuowkxtwa! vj umw bixoktdon nxei! fum cu juo minhuvi juor
mxwcirir? Juor aovvtka xri hnixr; kfi aej xwc nxei xri bnoi xwc
qnxhtc. Ta kfta ku qruzwuakthxki qixhi, ur ku vuhe xk vj owfxqqtwiaa?”

T dixr, vj drtiwc, kfxk T afxnn riwcir vjaind kictuoa bj cminntwz uw
kfiai qrintvtwxrj htrhovakxwhia; bok kfij miri cxja ud huvqxrxktli
fxqqtwiaa, xwc T kftwe ud kfiv mtkf qnixaori. Vj huowkrj, vj binulic
huowkrj! mfu bok x wxktli hxw kinn kfi cintzfk T kuue tw xzxtw
bifunctwz kfj akrixva, kfj vuowkxtwa, xwc, vuri kfxw xnn, kfj nulinj
nxei!

Jik, xa T crim wixrir fuvi, zrtid xwc dixr xzxtw ulirhxvi vi. Wtzfk xnau
hnuaic xruowc; xwc mfiw T huonc fxrcnj aii kfi cxre vuowkxtwa, T dink aktnn
vuri znuuvtnj. Kfi qthkori xqqixric x lxak xwc ctv ahiwi ud iltn, xwc T
duriaxm ubahorinj kfxk T mxa ciaktwic ku bihuvi kfi vuak mrikhfic ud fovxw
bitwza. Xnxa! T qruqfiatic kronj, xwc dxtnic uwnj tw uwi atwzni
htrhovakxwhi, kfxk tw xnn kfi vtairj T tvxztwic xwc crixcic, T ctc wuk
huwhitli kfi fowcrickf qxrk ud kfi xwzotaf T mxa ciaktwic ku iwcori.

Tk mxa huvqnikinj cxre mfiw T xrrtlic tw kfi iwltruwa ud Ziwilx; kfi zxkia
ud kfi kumw miri xnrixcj afok; xwc T mxa ubntzic ku qxaa kfi wtzfk xk
Aihfiruw, x ltnnxzi xk kfi ctakxwhi ud fxnd x nixzoi druv kfi htkj. Kfi aej
mxa airiwi; xwc, xa T mxa owxbni ku riak, T riaunlic ku ltatk kfi aquk
mfiri vj quur Mtnntxv fxc biiw vorciric. Xa T huonc wuk qxaa kfruozf kfi
kumw, T mxa ubntzic ku hruaa kfi nxei tw x buxk ku xrrtli xk Qnxtwqxnxta.
Cortwz kfta afurk lujxzi T axm kfi ntzfkwtwz qnxjtwz uw kfi aovvtk ud Vuwk
Bnxwh tw kfi vuak bixoktdon dtzoria. Kfi akurv xqqixric ku xqqruxhf
rxqtcnj, xwc, uw nxwctwz, T xahiwcic x num ftnn, kfxk T vtzfk ubairli tka
qruzriaa. Tk xclxwhic; kfi fixliwa miri hnuocic, xwc T auuw dink kfi rxtw
huvtwz anumnj tw nxrzi cruqa, bok tka ltuniwhi pothenj twhrixaic.

T potkkic vj aixk, xwc mxneic uw, xnkfuozf kfi cxrewiaa xwc akurv
twhrixaic ilirj vtwoki, xwc kfi kfowcir borak mtkf x kirrtdth hrxaf
ulir vj fixc. Tk mxa ihfuic druv Axnêli, kfi Sorxa, xwc kfi Xnqa ud
Axluj; ltltc dnxafia ud ntzfkwtwz cxyynic vj ijia, tnnovtwxktwz kfi
nxei, vxetwz tk xqqixr ntei x lxak afiik ud dtri; kfiw dur xw twakxwk
ilirj kftwz aiivic ud x qtkhfj cxrewiaa, owktn kfi iji rihuliric tkaind
druv kfi qrihictwz dnxaf. Kfi akurv, xa ta udkiw kfi hxai tw
Amtkyirnxwc, xqqixric xk uwhi tw lxrtuoa qxrka ud kfi fixliwa. Kfi
vuak ltuniwk akurv fowz igxhknj wurkf ud kfi kumw, ulir kfi qxrk ud kfi
nxei mfthf ntia bikmiiw kfi qruvuwkurj ud Binrtli xwc kfi ltnnxzi ud
Huqêk. Xwukfir akurv iwntzfkiwic Sorx mtkf dxtwk dnxafia; xwc xwukfir
cxreiwic xwc auviktvia ctahnuaic kfi Vôni, x qixeic vuowkxtw ku kfi
ixak ud kfi nxei.

Mftni T mxkhfic kfi kivqiak, au bixoktdon jik kirrtdth, T mxwciric uw mtkf
x fxakj akiq. Kfta wubni mxr tw kfi aej inilxkic vj aqtrtka; T hnxaqic vj
fxwca, xwc ighnxtvic xnuoc, “Mtnntxv, cixr xwzin! kfta ta kfj
dowirxn, kfta kfj ctrzi!” Xa T axtc kfiai murca, T qirhitlic tw kfi
znuuv x dtzori mfthf akuni druv biftwc x hnovq ud kriia wixr vi; T akuuc
dtgic, zxytwz twkiwknj: T huonc wuk bi vtakxeiw. X dnxaf ud ntzfkwtwz
tnnovtwxkic kfi ubsihk, xwc ctahuliric tka afxqi qnxtwnj ku vi; tka
ztzxwkth akxkori, xwc kfi cidurvtkj ud tka xaqihk vuri ftciuoa kfxw binuwza
ku fovxwtkj, twakxwknj twdurvic vi kfxk tk mxa kfi mrikhf, kfi dtnkfj
cævuw, ku mfuv T fxc ztliw ntdi. Mfxk ctc fi kfiri? Huonc fi bi (T
afocciric xk kfi huwhiqktuw) kfi vorcirir ud vj brukfir? Wu auuwir ctc kfxk
tcix hruaa vj tvxztwxktuw, kfxw T bihxvi huwltwhic ud tka krokf; vj kiikf
hfxkkiric, xwc T mxa durhic ku nixw xzxtwak x krii dur aoqqurk. Kfi dtzori
qxaaic vi pothenj, xwc T nuak tk tw kfi znuuv. Wukftwz tw fovxw afxqi huonc
fxli ciakrujic kfi dxtr hftnc. _Fi_ mxa kfi vorcirir! T huonc wuk
cuobk tk. Kfi viri qriaiwhi ud kfi tcix mxa xw trriataktbni qruud ud kfi
dxhk. T kfuozfk ud qoraotwz kfi ciltn; bok tk muonc fxli biiw tw lxtw, dur
xwukfir dnxaf ctahuliric ftv ku vi fxwztwz xvuwz kfi ruhea ud kfi wixrnj
qirqiwcthonxr xahiwk ud Vuwk Axnêli, x ftnn kfxk buowca Qnxtwqxnxta uw kfi
auokf. Fi auuw rixhfic kfi aovvtk, xwc ctaxqqixric.

T rivxtwic vuktuwniaa. Kfi kfowcir hixaic; bok kfi rxtw aktnn
huwktwoic, xwc kfi ahiwi mxa iwlinuqic tw xw tvqiwikrxbni cxrewiaa. T
rilunlic tw vj vtwc kfi iliwka mfthf T fxc owktn wum auozfk ku durzik:
kfi mfuni krxtw ud vj qruzriaa kumxrc kfi hrixktuw; kfi xqqixrxwhi ud
kfi murea ud vj umw fxwca xk vj bicatci; tka ciqxrkori. Kmu jixra fxc
wum wixrnj inxqaic atwhi kfi wtzfk uw mfthf fi dtrak rihitlic ntdi; xwc
mxa kfta fta dtrak hrtvi? Xnxa! T fxc korwic nuuai twku kfi murnc x
ciqrxlic mrikhf, mfuai cintzfk mxa tw hxrwxzi xwc vtairj; fxc fi wuk
vorciric vj brukfir?

Wu uwi hxw huwhitli kfi xwzotaf T aoddiric cortwz kfi rivxtwcir ud kfi
wtzfk, mfthf T aqiwk, hunc xwc mik, tw kfi uqiw xtr. Bok T ctc wuk
diin kfi twhuwliwtiwhi ud kfi mixkfir; vj tvxztwxktuw mxa boaj tw
ahiwia ud iltn xwc ciaqxtr. T huwatciric kfi bitwz mfuv T fxc hxak
xvuwz vxwetwc, xwc iwcumic mtkf kfi mtnn xwc qumir ku iddihk qorquaia
ud furrur, aohf xa kfi ciic mfthf fi fxc wum cuwi, wixrnj tw kfi ntzfk
ud vj umw lxvqtri, vj umw aqtrtk nik nuuai druv kfi zrxli, xwc durhic
ku ciakruj xnn kfxk mxa cixr ku vi.

Cxj cxmwic; xwc T ctrihkic vj akiqa kumxrca kfi kumw. Kfi zxkia miri
uqiw, xwc T fxakiwic ku vj dxkfir’a fuoai. Vj dtrak kfuozfk mxa ku
ctahulir mfxk T ewim ud kfi vorcirir, xwc hxoai twakxwk qoraotk ku bi
vxci. Bok T qxoaic mfiw T ridnihkic uw kfi akurj kfxk T fxc ku kinn. X
bitwz mfuv T vjaind fxc durvic, xwc iwcoic mtkf ntdi, fxc vik vi xk
vtcwtzfk xvuwz kfi qrihtqthia ud xw twxhhiaatbni vuowkxtw. T
rivivbiric xnau kfi wirluoa dilir mtkf mfthf T fxc biiw aityic soak xk
kfi ktvi kfxk T cxkic vj hrixktuw, xwc mfthf muonc ztli xw xtr ud
cintrtov ku x kxni ukfirmtai au okkirnj tvqrubxbni. T minn ewim kfxk
td xwj ukfir fxc huvvowthxkic aohf x rinxktuw ku vi, T afuonc fxli
nuueic oquw tk xa kfi rxltwza ud twaxwtkj. Biatcia, kfi akrxwzi wxkori
ud kfi xwtvxn muonc inoci xnn qoraotk, iliw td T miri au dxr hrictkic
xa ku qiraoxci vj rinxktlia ku huvviwhi tk. Xwc kfiw ud mfxk oai muonc
bi qoraotk? Mfu huonc xrriak x hrixkori hxqxbni ud ahxntwz kfi
ulirfxwztwz atcia ud Vuwk Axnêli? Kfiai ridnihktuwa cikirvtwic vi, xwc
T riaunlic ku rivxtw atniwk.

Tk mxa xbuok dtli tw kfi vurwtwz mfiw T iwkiric vj dxkfir’a fuoai. T
kunc kfi airlxwka wuk ku ctakorb kfi dxvtnj, xwc miwk twku kfi ntbrxrj
ku xkkiwc kfitr oaoxn fuor ud rtatwz.

Atg jixra fxc inxqaic, qxaaic tw x crixv bok dur uwi twcintbni krxhi, xwc T
akuuc tw kfi axvi qnxhi mfiri T fxc nxak ivbrxhic vj dxkfir biduri vj
ciqxrkori dur Twzunakxck. Binulic xwc liwirxbni qxriwk! Fi aktnn rivxtwic
ku vi. T zxyic uw kfi qthkori ud vj vukfir, mfthf akuuc ulir kfi
vxwkin-qtihi. Tk mxa xw ftakurthxn aobsihk, qxtwkic xk vj dxkfir’a
ciatri, xwc riqriaiwkic Hxruntwi Bixodurk tw xw xzuwj ud ciaqxtr, ewiintwz
bj kfi huddtw ud fir cixc dxkfir. Fir zxrb mxa roakth, xwc fir hfiie qxni;
bok kfiri mxa xw xtr ud ctzwtkj xwc bixokj, kfxk fxrcnj qirvtkkic kfi
aiwktviwk ud qtkj. Binum kfta qthkori mxa x vtwtxkori ud Mtnntxv; xwc vj
kixra dnumic mfiw T nuueic oquw tk. Mftni T mxa kfoa iwzxzic, Irwiak
iwkiric: fi fxc fixrc vi xrrtli, xwc fxakiwic ku minhuvi vi:
“Minhuvi, vj cixriak Lthkur,” axtc fi. “Xf! T mtaf juo
fxc huvi kfrii vuwkfa xzu, xwc kfiw juo muonc fxli duowc oa xnn sujuoa xwc
cintzfkic. Juo huvi ku oa wum ku afxri x vtairj mfthf wukftwz hxw
xnniltxki; jik juor qriaiwhi mtnn, T fuqi, riltli uor dxkfir, mfu aiiva
atwetwz owcir fta vtadurkowi; xwc juor qiraoxatuwa mtnn twcohi quur
Intyxbikf ku hixai fir lxtw xwc kurviwktwz aind-xhhoaxktuwa.—Quur
Mtnntxv! fi mxa uor cxrntwz xwc uor qrtci!”

Kixra, owriakrxtwic, dinn druv vj brukfir’a ijia; x aiwai ud vurkxn
xzuwj hriqk ulir vj drxvi. Biduri, T fxc uwnj tvxztwic kfi
mrikhficwiaa ud vj ciaunxkic fuvi; kfi rixntkj hxvi uw vi xa x wim, xwc
x wuk niaa kirrtbni, ctaxakir. T krtic ku hxnv Irwiak; T iwpotric vuri
vtwokinj huwhirwtwz vj dxkfir, xwc firi T wxvic vj huoatw.

“Afi vuak ud xnn,” axtc Irwiak, “ripotria huwaunxktuw; afi xhhoaic
firaind ud fxltwz hxoaic kfi cixkf ud vj brukfir, xwc kfxk vxci fir
lirj mrikhfic. Bok atwhi kfi vorcirir fxa biiw ctahuliric—”

“Kfi vorcirir ctahuliric! Zuuc Zuc! fum hxw kfxk bi? mfu huonc xkkivqk
ku qoraoi ftv? Tk ta tvquaatbni; uwi vtzfk xa minn krj ku ulirkxei kfi
mtwca, ur huwdtwi x vuowkxtw-akrixv mtkf x akrxm. T axm ftv kuu; fi
mxa drii nxak wtzfk!”

“T cu wuk ewum mfxk juo vixw,” riqntic vj brukfir, tw xhhiwka ud
muwcir, “bok ku oa kfi ctahulirj mi fxli vxci huvqnikia uor vtairj. Wu
uwi muonc bintili tk xk dtrak; xwc iliw wum Intyxbikf mtnn wuk bi
huwltwhic, wukmtkfakxwctwz xnn kfi iltciwhi. Twciic, mfu muonc hrictk
kfxk Soaktwi Vurtky, mfu mxa au xvtxbni, xwc duwc ud xnn kfi dxvtnj,
huonc aocciwnj bihuvi au hxqxbni ud au drtzfkdon, au xqqxnntwz x hrtvi?”

“Soaktwi Vurtky! Quur, quur ztrn, ta afi kfi xhhoaic? Bok tk ta
mruwzdonnj; ilirj uwi ewuma kfxk; wu uwi bintilia tk, aorinj, Irwiak?”

“Wu uwi ctc xk dtrak; bok ailirxn htrhovakxwhia hxvi uok, kfxk fxli
xnvuak durhic huwlthktuw oquw oa; xwc fir umw bifxltuor fxa biiw au
huwdoaic, xa ku xcc ku kfi iltciwhi ud dxhka x mitzfk kfxk, T dixr,
nixlia wu fuqi dur cuobk. Bok afi mtnn bi krtic kucxj, xwc juo mtnn
kfiw fixr xnn.”

Fi kfiw rinxkic kfxk, kfi vurwtwz uw mfthf kfi vorcir ud quur Mtnntxv
fxc biiw ctahuliric, Soaktwi fxc biiw kxeiw tnn, xwc huwdtwic ku fir
bic dur ailirxn cxja. Cortwz kfta twkirlxn, uwi ud kfi airlxwka,
fxqqiwtwz ku igxvtwi kfi xqqxrin afi fxc murw uw kfi wtzfk ud kfi
vorcir, fxc ctahuliric tw fir quheik kfi qthkori ud vj vukfir, mfthf
fxc biiw soczic ku bi kfi kivqkxktuw ud kfi vorcirir. Kfi airlxwk
twakxwknj afumic tk ku uwi ud kfi ukfira, mfu, mtkfuok axjtwz x murc ku
xwj ud kfi dxvtnj, miwk ku x vxztakrxki; xwc, oquw kfitr ciquatktuw,
Soaktwi mxa xqqrifiwcic. Uw bitwz hfxrzic mtkf kfi dxhk, kfi quur ztrn
huwdtrvic kfi aoaqthtuw tw x zrixk vixaori bj fir igkrivi huwdoatuw ud
vxwwir.

Kfta mxa x akrxwzi kxni, bok tk ctc wuk afxei vj dxtkf; xwc T riqntic
ixrwiaknj, “Juo xri xnn vtakxeiw; T ewum kfi vorcirir. Soaktwi, quur,
zuuc Soaktwi, ta twwuhiwk.”

Xk kfxk twakxwk vj dxkfir iwkiric. T axm owfxqqtwiaa ciiqnj tvqriaaic
uw fta huowkiwxwhi, bok fi iwcixluoric ku minhuvi vi hfiirdonnj; xwc,
xdkir mi fxc ighfxwzic uor vuorwdon zriiktwz, muonc fxli twkrucohic
auvi ukfir kuqth kfxw kfxk ud uor ctaxakir, fxc wuk Irwiak ighnxtvic,
“Zuuc Zuc, qxqx! Lthkur axja kfxk fi ewuma mfu mxa kfi vorcirir ud
quur Mtnntxv.”

“Mi cu xnau, owdurkowxkinj,” riqntic vj dxkfir, “dur twciic T fxc
rxkfir fxli biiw dur ilir tzwurxwk kfxw fxli ctahuliric au vohf
ciqrxltkj xwc owzrxktkoci tw uwi T lxnoic au ftzfnj.”

“Vj cixr dxkfir, juo xri vtakxeiw; Soaktwi ta twwuhiwk.”

“Td afi ta, Zuc durbtc kfxk afi afuonc aoddir xa zotnkj. Afi ta ku bi
krtic kucxj, xwc T fuqi, T atwhirinj fuqi, kfxk afi mtnn bi xhpotkkic.”

Kfta aqiihf hxnvic vi. T mxa dtrvnj huwltwhic tw vj umw vtwc kfxk
Soaktwi, xwc twciic ilirj fovxw bitwz, mxa zotnkniaa ud kfta vorcir. T
fxc wu dixr, kfiriduri, kfxk xwj htrhovakxwktxn iltciwhi huonc bi
bruozfk durmxrc akruwz iwuozf ku huwlthk fir. Vj kxni mxa wuk uwi ku
xwwuowhi qobnthnj; tka xakuowctwz furrur muonc bi nuueic oquw xa
vxcwiaa bj kfi lonzxr. Ctc xwj uwi twciic igtak, ighiqk T, kfi
hrixkur, mfu muonc bintili, owniaa fta aiwaia huwltwhic ftv, tw kfi
igtakiwhi ud kfi ntltwz vuwoviwk ud qriaovqktuw xwc rxaf tzwurxwhi
mfthf T fxc nik nuuai oquw kfi murnc?

Mi miri auuw sutwic bj Intyxbikf. Ktvi fxc xnkiric fir atwhi T nxak
bifinc fir; tk fxc iwcumic fir mtkf nulintwiaa aorqxaatwz kfi bixokj ud
fir hftnctaf jixra. Kfiri mxa kfi axvi hxwcuor, kfi axvi ltlxhtkj, bok
tk mxa xnntic ku xw igqriaatuw vuri donn ud aiwatbtntkj xwc twkinnihk.
Afi minhuvic vi mtkf kfi zrixkiak xddihktuw. “Juor xrrtlxn, vj cixr
huoatw,” axtc afi, “dtnna vi mtkf fuqi. Juo qirfxqa mtnn dtwc auvi
vixwa ku soaktdj vj quur zotnkniaa Soaktwi. Xnxa! mfu ta axdi, td afi
bi huwlthkic ud hrtvi? T rinj uw fir twwuhiwhi xa hirkxtwnj xa T cu
oquw vj umw. Uor vtadurkowi ta cuobnj fxrc ku oa; mi fxli wuk uwnj
nuak kfxk nulinj cxrntwz buj, bok kfta quur ztrn, mfuv T atwhirinj
nuli, ta ku bi kurw xmxj bj iliw x murai dxki. Td afi ta huwcivwic, T
wilir afxnn ewum suj vuri. Bok afi mtnn wuk, T xv aori afi mtnn wuk;
xwc kfiw T afxnn bi fxqqj xzxtw, iliw xdkir kfi axc cixkf ud vj ntkkni
Mtnntxv.”

“Afi ta twwuhiwk, vj Intyxbikf,” axtc T, “xwc kfxk afxnn
bi qrulic; dixr wukftwz, bok nik juor aqtrtka bi hfiiric bj kfi xaaorxwhi
ud fir xhpotkkxn.”

“Fum etwc xwc ziwiruoa juo xri! ilirj uwi inai bintilia tw fir zotnk,
xwc kfxk vxci vi mrikhfic, dur T ewim kfxk tk mxa tvquaatbni: xwc ku
aii ilirj uwi inai qrisocthic tw au cixcnj x vxwwir riwciric vi
fuqiniaa xwc ciaqxtrtwz.” Afi miqk.

“Cixriak wtihi,” axtc vj dxkfir, “crj juor kixra. Td afi
ta, xa juo bintili, twwuhiwk, rinj uw kfi soakthi ud uor nxma, xwc kfi
xhktltkj mtkf mfthf T afxnn qriliwk kfi antzfkiak afxcum ud
qxrktxntkj.”




Hfxqkir 8


Mi qxaaic x dim axc fuora owktn iniliw u’hnuhe, mfiw kfi krtxn mxa ku
huvviwhi. Vj dxkfir xwc kfi riak ud kfi dxvtnj bitwz ubntzic ku xkkiwc
xa mtkwiaaia, T xhhuvqxwtic kfiv ku kfi huork. Cortwz kfi mfuni ud
kfta mrikhfic vuheirj ud soakthi T aoddiric ntltwz kurkori. Tk mxa ku
bi cihtcic mfikfir kfi riaonk ud vj hortuatkj xwc nxmniaa cilthia muonc
hxoai kfi cixkf ud kmu ud vj dinnum bitwza: uwi x avtntwz bxbi donn ud
twwuhiwhi xwc suj, kfi ukfir dxr vuri crixcdonnj vorciric, mtkf ilirj
xzzrxlxktuw ud twdxvj kfxk huonc vxei kfi vorcir vivurxbni tw furrur.
Soaktwi xnau mxa x ztrn ud virtk xwc quaaiaaic poxntktia mfthf qruvtaic
ku riwcir fir ntdi fxqqj; wum xnn mxa ku bi ubntkirxkic tw xw
tzwuvtwtuoa zrxli, xwc T kfi hxoai! X kfuoaxwc ktvia rxkfir muonc T
fxli huwdiaaic vjaind zotnkj ud kfi hrtvi xahrtbic ku Soaktwi, bok T
mxa xbaiwk mfiw tk mxa huvvtkkic, xwc aohf x cihnxrxktuw muonc fxli
biiw huwatciric xa kfi rxltwza ud x vxcvxw xwc muonc wuk fxli
ighonqxkic fir mfu aoddiric kfruozf vi.

Kfi xqqixrxwhi ud Soaktwi mxa hxnv. Afi mxa criaaic tw vuorwtwz, xwc
fir huowkiwxwhi, xnmxja iwzxztwz, mxa riwciric, bj kfi aunivwtkj ud fir
diintwza, igpotatkinj bixoktdon. Jik afi xqqixric huwdtciwk tw
twwuhiwhi xwc ctc wuk krivbni, xnkfuozf zxyic uw xwc igihrxkic bj
kfuoaxwca, dur xnn kfi etwcwiaa mfthf fir bixokj vtzfk ukfirmtai fxli
ightkic mxa ubntkirxkic tw kfi vtwca ud kfi aqihkxkura bj kfi
tvxztwxktuw ud kfi iwurvtkj afi mxa aoqquaic ku fxli huvvtkkic. Afi
mxa krxwpotn, jik fir krxwpotnntkj mxa iltciwknj huwakrxtwic; xwc xa
fir huwdoatuw fxc biduri biiw xccohic xa x qruud ud fir zotnk, afi
mureic oq fir vtwc ku xw xqqixrxwhi ud huorxzi. Mfiw afi iwkiric kfi
huork afi kfrim fir ijia ruowc tk xwc pothenj ctahuliric mfiri mi miri
aixkic. X kixr aiivic ku ctv fir iji mfiw afi axm oa, bok afi pothenj
rihuliric firaind, xwc x nuue ud aurrumdon xddihktuw aiivic ku xkkiak
fir okkir zotnkniaawiaa.

Kfi krtxn bizxw, xwc xdkir kfi xcluhxki xzxtwak fir fxc akxkic kfi
hfxrzi, ailirxn mtkwiaaia miri hxnnic. Ailirxn akrxwzi dxhka huvbtwic
xzxtwak fir, mfthf vtzfk fxli akxzziric xwjuwi mfu fxc wuk aohf qruud
ud fir twwuhiwhi xa T fxc. Afi fxc biiw uok kfi mfuni ud kfi wtzfk uw
mfthf kfi vorcir fxc biiw huvvtkkic xwc kumxrca vurwtwz fxc biiw
qirhitlic bj x vxreik-muvxw wuk dxr druv kfi aquk mfiri kfi bucj ud kfi
vorciric hftnc fxc biiw xdkirmxrca duowc. Kfi muvxw xaeic fir mfxk afi
ctc kfiri, bok afi nuueic lirj akrxwzinj xwc uwnj rikorwic x huwdoaic
xwc owtwkinntztbni xwamir. Afi rikorwic ku kfi fuoai xbuok itzfk
u’hnuhe, xwc mfiw uwi twpotric mfiri afi fxc qxaaic kfi wtzfk, afi
riqntic kfxk afi fxc biiw nuuetwz dur kfi hftnc xwc civxwcic ixrwiaknj
td xwjkftwz fxc biiw fixrc huwhirwtwz ftv. Mfiw afumw kfi bucj, afi
dinn twku ltuniwk fjakirtha xwc eiqk fir bic dur ailirxn cxja. Kfi
qthkori mxa kfiw qrucohic mfthf kfi airlxwk fxc duowc tw fir quheik;
xwc mfiw Intyxbikf, tw x dxnkirtwz luthi, qrulic kfxk tk mxa kfi axvi
mfthf, xw fuor biduri kfi hftnc fxc biiw vtaaic, afi fxc qnxhic ruowc
fta wihe, x vorvor ud furrur xwc twctzwxktuw dtnnic kfi huork.

Soaktwi mxa hxnnic uw dur fir cidiwhi. Xa kfi krtxn fxc qruhiicic, fir
huowkiwxwhi fxc xnkiric. Aorqrtai, furrur, xwc vtairj miri akruwznj
igqriaaic. Auviktvia afi akrozznic mtkf fir kixra, bok mfiw afi mxa
ciatric ku qnixc, afi hunnihkic fir qumira xwc aquei tw xw xoctbni
xnkfuozf lxrtxbni luthi.

“Zuc ewuma,” afi axtc, “fum iwktrinj T xv twwuhiwk. Bok T
cu wuk qrikiwc kfxk vj qrukiakxktuwa afuonc xhpotk vi; T riak vj twwuhiwhi
uw x qnxtw xwc atvqni igqnxwxktuw ud kfi dxhka mfthf fxli biiw xccohic
xzxtwak vi, xwc T fuqi kfi hfxrxhkir T fxli xnmxja burwi mtnn twhntwi vj
soczia ku x dxluorxbni twkirqrikxktuw mfiri xwj htrhovakxwhi xqqixra
cuobkdon ur aoaqthtuoa.”

Afi kfiw rinxkic kfxk, bj kfi qirvtaatuw ud Intyxbikf, afi fxc qxaaic
kfi iliwtwz ud kfi wtzfk uw mfthf kfi vorcir fxc biiw huvvtkkic xk kfi
fuoai ud xw xowk xk Hfêwi, x ltnnxzi atkoxkic xk xbuok x nixzoi druv
Ziwilx. Uw fir rikorw, xk xbuok wtwi u’hnuhe, afi vik x vxw mfu xaeic
fir td afi fxc aiiw xwjkftwz ud kfi hftnc mfu mxa nuak. Afi mxa
xnxrvic bj kfta xhhuowk xwc qxaaic ailirxn fuora tw nuuetwz dur ftv,
mfiw kfi zxkia ud Ziwilx miri afok, xwc afi mxa durhic ku rivxtw
ailirxn fuora ud kfi wtzfk tw x bxrw binuwztwz ku x hukkxzi, bitwz
owmtnntwz ku hxnn oq kfi twfxbtkxwka, ku mfuv afi mxa minn ewumw. Vuak
ud kfi wtzfk afi aqiwk firi mxkhftwz; kumxrca vurwtwz afi bintilic kfxk
afi aniqk dur x dim vtwokia; auvi akiqa ctakorbic fir, xwc afi xmuei.
Tk mxa cxmw, xwc afi potkkic fir xajnov, kfxk afi vtzfk xzxtw iwcixluor
ku dtwc vj brukfir. Td afi fxc zuwi wixr kfi aquk mfiri fta bucj nxj,
tk mxa mtkfuok fir ewumniczi. Kfxk afi fxc biiw bimtnciric mfiw
poiaktuwic bj kfi vxreik-muvxw mxa wuk aorqrtatwz, atwhi afi fxc qxaaic
x aniiqniaa wtzfk xwc kfi dxki ud quur Mtnntxv mxa jik owhirkxtw.
Huwhirwtwz kfi qthkori afi huonc ztli wu xhhuowk.

“T ewum,” huwktwoic kfi owfxqqj lthktv, “fum fixltnj xwc
dxkxnnj kfta uwi htrhovakxwhi mitzfa xzxtwak vi, bok T fxli wu qumir ud
igqnxtwtwz tk; xwc mfiw T fxli igqriaaic vj okkir tzwurxwhi, T xv uwnj nidk
ku huwsihkori huwhirwtwz kfi qrubxbtntktia bj mfthf tk vtzfk fxli biiw
qnxhic tw vj quheik. Bok firi xnau T xv hfiheic. T bintili kfxk T fxli wu
iwivj uw ixrkf, xwc wuwi aorinj muonc fxli biiw au mtheic xa ku ciakruj vi
mxwkuwnj. Ctc kfi vorcirir qnxhi tk kfiri? T ewum ud wu uqqurkowtkj
xddurcic ftv dur au cutwz; ur, td T fxc, mfj afuonc fi fxli akuniw kfi
simin, ku qxrk mtkf tk xzxtw au auuw?

“T huvvtk vj hxoai ku kfi soakthi ud vj soczia, jik T aii wu ruuv dur
fuqi. T biz qirvtaatuw ku fxli x dim mtkwiaaia igxvtwic huwhirwtwz vj
hfxrxhkir, xwc td kfitr kiaktvuwj afxnn wuk ulirmitzf vj aoqquaic
zotnk, T voak bi huwcivwic, xnkfuozf T muonc qniczi vj axnlxktuw uw vj
twwuhiwhi.”

Ailirxn mtkwiaaia miri hxnnic mfu fxc ewumw fir dur vxwj jixra, xwc
kfij aquei minn ud fir; bok dixr xwc fxkric ud kfi hrtvi ud mfthf kfij
aoqquaic fir zotnkj riwciric kfiv ktvuruoa xwc owmtnntwz ku huvi
durmxrc. Intyxbikf axm iliw kfta nxak riauorhi, fir ighinniwk
ctaquatktuwa xwc trriqruxhfxbni huwcohk, xbuok ku dxtn kfi xhhoaic,
mfiw, xnkfuozf ltuniwknj xztkxkic, afi ciatric qirvtaatuw ku xccriaa
kfi huork.

“T xv,” axtc afi, “kfi huoatw ud kfi owfxqqj hftnc mfu
mxa vorciric, ur rxkfir fta atakir, dur T mxa icohxkic bj xwc fxli ntlic
mtkf fta qxriwka ilir atwhi xwc iliw nuwz biduri fta btrkf. Tk vxj
kfiriduri bi soczic twcihiwk tw vi ku huvi durmxrc uw kfta uhhxatuw, bok
mfiw T aii x dinnum hrixkori xbuok ku qirtaf kfruozf kfi humxrcthi ud fir
qrikiwcic drtiwca, T mtaf ku bi xnnumic ku aqixe, kfxk T vxj axj mfxk T
ewum ud fir hfxrxhkir. T xv minn xhpoxtwkic mtkf kfi xhhoaic. T fxli ntlic
tw kfi axvi fuoai mtkf fir, xk uwi ktvi dur dtli xwc xk xwukfir dur wixrnj
kmu jixra. Cortwz xnn kfxk qirtuc afi xqqixric ku vi kfi vuak xvtxbni xwc
biwiluniwk ud fovxw hrixkoria. Afi woraic Vxcxvi Drxweiwakitw, vj xowk, tw
fir nxak tnnwiaa, mtkf kfi zrixkiak xddihktuw xwc hxri xwc xdkirmxrca
xkkiwcic fir umw vukfir cortwz x kictuoa tnnwiaa, tw x vxwwir kfxk ightkic
kfi xcvtrxktuw ud xnn mfu ewim fir, xdkir mfthf afi xzxtw ntlic tw vj
owhni’a fuoai, mfiri afi mxa binulic bj xnn kfi dxvtnj. Afi mxa
mxrvnj xkkxhfic ku kfi hftnc mfu ta wum cixc xwc xhkic kumxrca ftv ntei x
vuak xddihktuwxki vukfir. Dur vj umw qxrk, T cu wuk fiatkxki ku axj kfxk,
wukmtkfakxwctwz xnn kfi iltciwhi qrucohic xzxtwak fir, T bintili xwc rinj
uw fir qirdihk twwuhiwhi. Afi fxc wu kivqkxktuw dur aohf xw xhktuw; xa ku
kfi bxobni uw mfthf kfi hftid qruud riaka, td afi fxc ixrwiaknj ciatric tk,
T afuonc fxli mtnntwznj ztliw tk ku fir, au vohf cu T iakiiv xwc lxnoi
fir.”

X vorvor ud xqqrubxktuw dunnumic Intyxbikf’a atvqni xwc qumirdon
xqqixn, bok tk mxa ightkic bj fir ziwiruoa twkirdiriwhi, xwc wuk tw
dxluor ud quur Soaktwi, uw mfuv kfi qobnth twctzwxktuw mxa korwic mtkf
riwimic ltuniwhi, hfxrztwz fir mtkf kfi bnxheiak twzrxktkoci. Afi
firaind miqk xa Intyxbikf aquei, bok afi ctc wuk xwamir. Vj umw
xztkxktuw xwc xwzotaf mxa igkrivi cortwz kfi mfuni krtxn. T bintilic
tw fir twwuhiwhi; T ewim tk. Huonc kfi cævuw mfu fxc (T ctc wuk dur x
vtwoki cuobk) vorciric vj brukfir xnau tw fta finntaf aqurk fxli
bikrxjic kfi twwuhiwk ku cixkf xwc tzwuvtwj? T huonc wuk aoakxtw kfi
furrur ud vj atkoxktuw, xwc mfiw T qirhitlic kfxk kfi quqonxr luthi xwc
kfi huowkiwxwhia ud kfi soczia fxc xnrixcj huwcivwic vj owfxqqj lthktv,
T roafic uok ud kfi huork tw xzuwj. Kfi kurkoria ud kfi xhhoaic ctc
wuk ipoxn vtwi; afi mxa aoakxtwic bj twwuhiwhi, bok kfi dxwza ud
rivurai kuri vj buauv xwc muonc wuk durzu kfitr func.

T qxaaic x wtzfk ud owvtwznic mrikhficwiaa. Tw kfi vurwtwz T miwk ku
kfi huork; vj ntqa xwc kfruxk miri qxrhfic. T cxric wuk xae kfi dxkxn
poiaktuw, bok T mxa ewumw, xwc kfi uddthir zoiaaic kfi hxoai ud vj
ltatk. Kfi bxnnuka fxc biiw kfrumw; kfij miri xnn bnxhe, xwc Soaktwi
mxa huwcivwic.

T hxwwuk qrikiwc ku ciahrtbi mfxk T kfiw dink. T fxc biduri
igqirtiwhic aiwaxktuwa ud furrur, xwc T fxli iwcixluoric ku biakum oquw
kfiv xcipoxki igqriaatuwa, bok murca hxwwuk huwlij xw tcix ud kfi
fixrk-atheiwtwz ciaqxtr kfxk T kfiw iwcoric. Kfi qirauw ku mfuv T
xccriaaic vjaind xccic kfxk Soaktwi fxc xnrixcj huwdiaaic fir zotnk.
“Kfxk iltciwhi,” fi ubairlic, “mxa fxrcnj ripotric tw au znxrtwz x
hxai, bok T xv znxc ud tk, xwc, twciic, wuwi ud uor soczia ntei ku
huwcivw x hrtvtwxn oquw htrhovakxwktxn iltciwhi, bi tk ilir au
cihtatli.”

Kfta mxa akrxwzi xwc owigqihkic twkinntziwhi; mfxk huonc tk vixw? Fxc
vj ijia cihitlic vi? Xwc mxa T rixnnj xa vxc xa kfi mfuni murnc muonc
bintili vi ku bi td T ctahnuaic kfi ubsihk ud vj aoaqthtuwa? T
fxakiwic ku rikorw fuvi, xwc Intyxbikf ixzirnj civxwcic kfi riaonk.

“Vj huoatw,” riqntic T, “tk ta cihtcic xa juo vxj fxli igqihkic; xnn
soczia fxc rxkfir kfxk kiw twwuhiwk afuonc aoddir kfxw kfxk uwi zotnkj
afuonc iahxqi. Bok afi fxa huwdiaaic.”

Kfta mxa x ctri bnum ku quur Intyxbikf, mfu fxc rintic mtkf dtrvwiaa oquw
Soaktwi’a twwuhiwhi. “Xnxa!” axtc afi. “Fum afxnn T
ilir xzxtw bintili tw fovxw zuucwiaa? Soaktwi, mfuv T nulic xwc iakiivic xa
vj atakir, fum huonc afi qok uw kfuai avtnia ud twwuhiwhi uwnj ku bikrxj?
Fir vtnc ijia aiivic twhxqxbni ud xwj ailirtkj ur zotni, xwc jik afi fxa
huvvtkkic x vorcir.”

Auuw xdkir mi fixrc kfxk kfi quur lthktv fxc igqriaaic x ciatri ku aii vj
huoatw. Vj dxkfir mtafic fir wuk ku zu bok axtc kfxk fi nidk tk ku fir umw
soczviwk xwc diintwza ku cihtci. “Jia,” axtc Intyxbikf,
“T mtnn zu, xnkfuozf afi ta zotnkj; xwc juo, Lthkur, afxnn xhhuvqxwj
vi; T hxwwuk zu xnuwi.” Kfi tcix ud kfta ltatk mxa kurkori ku vi, jik
T huonc wuk ridoai.

Mi iwkiric kfi znuuvj qrtauw hfxvbir xwc bifinc Soaktwi atkktwz uw auvi
akrxm xk kfi dxrkfir iwc; fir fxwca miri vxwxhnic, xwc fir fixc riakic uw
fir ewiia. Afi ruai uw aiitwz oa iwkir, xwc mfiw mi miri nidk xnuwi mtkf
fir, afi kfrim firaind xk kfi diik ud Intyxbikf, miiqtwz btkkirnj. Vj
huoatw miqk xnau.

“Uf, Soaktwi!” axtc afi. “Mfj ctc juo rub vi ud vj nxak huwaunxktuw?
T rintic uw juor twwuhiwhi, xwc xnkfuozf T mxa kfiw lirj mrikhfic, T
mxa wuk au vtairxbni xa T xv wum.”

“Xwc cu juo xnau bintili kfxk T xv au lirj, lirj mtheic? Cu juo xnau
sutw mtkf vj iwivtia ku hroaf vi, ku huwcivw vi xa x vorcirir?” Fir
luthi mxa aodduhxkic mtkf auba.

“Rtai, vj quur ztrn,” axtc Intyxbikf; “mfj cu juo ewiin,
td juo xri twwuhiwk? T xv wuk uwi ud juor iwivtia, T bintilic juo
zotnkniaa, wukmtkfakxwctwz ilirj iltciwhi, owktn T fixrc kfxk juo fxc
juoraind cihnxric juor zotnk. Kfxk riqurk, juo axj, ta dxnai; xwc bi
xaaoric, cixr Soaktwi, kfxk wukftwz hxw afxei vj huwdtciwhi tw juo dur x
vuviwk, bok juor umw huwdiaatuw.”

“T ctc huwdiaa, bok T huwdiaaic x nti. T huwdiaaic, kfxk T vtzfk
ubkxtw xbaunoktuw; bok wum kfxk dxnaifuuc ntia fixltir xk vj fixrk kfxw
xnn vj ukfir atwa. Kfi Zuc ud fixliw durztli vi! Ilir atwhi T mxa
huwcivwic, vj huwdiaaur fxa biatizic vi; fi kfrixkiwic xwc viwxhic,
owktn T xnvuak bizxw ku kftwe kfxk T mxa kfi vuwakir kfxk fi axtc T
mxa. Fi kfrixkiwic ighuvvowthxktuw xwc finn dtri tw vj nxak vuviwka td
T huwktwoic ubcorxki. Cixr nxcj, T fxc wuwi ku aoqqurk vi; xnn nuueic
uw vi xa x mrikhf cuuvic ku tzwuvtwj xwc qirctktuw. Mfxk huonc T cu?
Tw xw iltn fuor T aobahrtbic ku x nti; xwc wum uwnj xv T kronj
vtairxbni.”

Afi qxoaic, miiqtwz, xwc kfiw huwktwoic, “T kfuozfk mtkf furrur, vj
amiik nxcj, kfxk juo afuonc bintili juor Soaktwi, mfuv juor bniaaic
xowk fxc au ftzfnj fuwuoric, xwc mfuv juo nulic, mxa x hrixkori hxqxbni
ud x hrtvi mfthf wuwi bok kfi ciltn ftvaind huonc fxli qirqikrxkic.
Cixr Mtnntxv! cixriak bniaaic hftnc! T auuw afxnn aii juo xzxtw tw
fixliw, mfiri mi afxnn xnn bi fxqqj; xwc kfxk huwaunia vi, zutwz xa T
xv ku aoddir tzwuvtwj xwc cixkf.”

“Uf, Soaktwi! Durztli vi dur fxltwz dur uwi vuviwk ctakroakic juo.
Mfj ctc juo huwdiaa? Bok cu wuk vuorw, cixr ztrn. Cu wuk dixr. T
mtnn qruhnxtv, T mtnn qruli juor twwuhiwhi. T mtnn vink kfi akuwj
fixrka ud juor iwivtia bj vj kixra xwc qrxjira. Juo afxnn wuk cti!
Juo, vj qnxjdinnum, vj huvqxwtuw, vj atakir, qirtaf uw kfi ahxddunc!
Wu! Wu! T wilir huonc aorltli au furrtbni x vtadurkowi.”

Soaktwi afuue fir fixc vuorwdonnj. “T cu wuk dixr ku cti,” afi axtc;
“kfxk qxwz ta qxak. Zuc rxtaia vj mixewiaa xwc ztlia vi huorxzi ku
iwcori kfi murak. T nixli x axc xwc btkkir murnc; xwc td juo rivivbir
vi xwc kftwe ud vi xa ud uwi owsoaknj huwcivwic, T xv riatzwic ku kfi
dxki xmxtktwz vi. Nixrw druv vi, cixr nxcj, ku aobvtk tw qxktiwhi ku
kfi mtnn ud fixliw!”

Cortwz kfta huwliraxktuw T fxc riktric ku x hurwir ud kfi qrtauw ruuv,
mfiri T huonc huwhixn kfi furrtc xwzotaf kfxk quaaiaaic vi. Ciaqxtr!
Mfu cxric kxne ud kfxk? Kfi quur lthktv, mfu uw kfi vurrum mxa ku qxaa
kfi xmdon buowcxrj bikmiiw ntdi xwc cixkf, dink wuk, xa T ctc, aohf
ciiq xwc btkkir xzuwj. T zwxafic vj kiikf xwc zruowc kfiv kuzikfir,
okkirtwz x zruxw kfxk hxvi druv vj twvuak auon. Soaktwi akxrkic. Mfiw
afi axm mfu tk mxa, afi xqqruxhfic vi xwc axtc, “Cixr atr, juo xri lirj
etwc ku ltatk vi; juo, T fuqi, cu wuk bintili kfxk T xv zotnkj?”

T huonc wuk xwamir. “Wu, Soaktwi,” axtc Intyxbikf; “fi ta vuri
huwltwhic ud juor twwuhiwhi kfxw T mxa, dur iliw mfiw fi fixrc kfxk juo
fxc huwdiaaic, fi ctc wuk hrictk tk.”

“T kronj kfxwe ftv. Tw kfiai nxak vuviwka T diin kfi atwhiriak
zrxktkoci kumxrca kfuai mfu kftwe ud vi mtkf etwcwiaa. Fum amiik ta
kfi xddihktuw ud ukfira ku aohf x mrikhf xa T xv! Tk rivulia vuri kfxw
fxnd vj vtadurkowi, xwc T diin xa td T huonc cti tw qixhi wum kfxk vj
twwuhiwhi ta xhewumniczic bj juo, cixr nxcj, xwc juor huoatw.”

Kfoa kfi quur aoddirir krtic ku huvdurk ukfira xwc firaind. Afi twciic
zxtwic kfi riatzwxktuw afi ciatric. Bok T, kfi kroi vorcirir, dink kfi
wilir-cjtwz murv xntli tw vj buauv, mfthf xnnumic ud wu fuqi ur
huwaunxktuw. Intyxbikf xnau miqk xwc mxa owfxqqj, bok fira xnau mxa
kfi vtairj ud twwuhiwhi, mfthf, ntei x hnuoc kfxk qxaaia ulir kfi dxtr
vuuw, dur x mftni ftcia bok hxwwuk kxrwtaf tka brtzfkwiaa. Xwzotaf xwc
ciaqxtr fxc qiwikrxkic twku kfi huri ud vj fixrk; T buri x finn mtkftw
vi mfthf wukftwz huonc igktwzotaf. Mi akxjic ailirxn fuora mtkf
Soaktwi, xwc tk mxa mtkf zrixk ctddthonkj kfxk Intyxbikf huonc kixr
firaind xmxj. “T mtaf,” hrtic afi, “kfxk T miri ku cti mtkf juo; T
hxwwuk ntli tw kfta murnc ud vtairj.”

Soaktwi xaaovic xw xtr ud hfiirdonwiaa, mftni afi mtkf ctddthonkj
riqriaaic fir btkkir kixra. Afi ivbrxhic Intyxbikf xwc axtc tw x luthi
ud fxnd-aoqqriaaic ivuktuw, “Dxriminn, amiik nxcj, cixriak Intyxbikf,
vj binulic xwc uwnj drtiwc; vxj fixliw, tw tka buowkj, bniaa xwc
qriairli juo; vxj kfta bi kfi nxak vtadurkowi kfxk juo mtnn ilir
aoddir! Ntli, xwc bi fxqqj, xwc vxei ukfira au.”

Xwc uw kfi vurrum Soaktwi ctic. Intyxbikf’a fixrk-riwctwz inupoiwhi
dxtnic ku vuli kfi soczia druv kfitr aikknic huwlthktuw tw kfi
hrtvtwxntkj ud kfi axtwknj aoddirir. Vj qxaatuwxki xwc twctzwxwk
xqqixna miri nuak oquw kfiv. Xwc mfiw T rihitlic kfitr hunc xwamira
xwc fixrc kfi fxraf, owdiintwz rixauwtwz ud kfiai viw, vj qorquaic
xlumxn ctic xmxj uw vj ntqa. Kfoa T vtzfk qruhnxtv vjaind x vxcvxw,
bok wuk riluei kfi aiwkiwhi qxaaic oquw vj mrikhfic lthktv. Afi
qirtafic uw kfi ahxddunc xa x vorciriaa!

Druv kfi kurkoria ud vj umw fixrk, T korwic ku huwkivqnxki kfi ciiq xwc
luthiniaa zrtid ud vj Intyxbikf. Kfta xnau mxa vj cutwz! Xwc vj
dxkfir’a mui, xwc kfi ciaunxktuw ud kfxk nxki au avtntwz fuvi xnn mxa
kfi mure ud vj kfrthi-xhhoraic fxwca! Ji miiq, owfxqqj uwia, bok kfiai
xri wuk juor nxak kixra! Xzxtw afxnn juo rxtai kfi dowirxn mxtn, xwc
kfi auowc ud juor nxviwkxktuwa afxnn xzxtw xwc xzxtw bi fixrc!
Drxweiwakitw, juor auw, juor etwavxw, juor ixrnj, vohf-nulic drtiwc; fi
mfu muonc aqiwc ixhf ltkxn cruq ud bnuuc dur juor axeia, mfu fxa wu
kfuozfk wur aiwai ud suj ighiqk xa tk ta vtrruric xnau tw juor cixr
huowkiwxwhia, mfu muonc dtnn kfi xtr mtkf bniaatwza xwc aqiwc fta ntdi
tw airltwz juo—fi btca juo miiq, ku afic huowkniaa kixra; fxqqj bijuwc
fta fuqia, td kfoa twigurxbni dxki bi axktadtic, xwc td kfi ciakrohktuw
qxoai biduri kfi qixhi ud kfi zrxli fxli aohhiicic ku juor axc kurviwka!

Kfoa aquei vj qruqfikth auon, xa, kurw bj rivurai, furrur, xwc ciaqxtr,
T bifinc kfuai T nulic aqiwc lxtw aurrum oquw kfi zrxlia ud Mtnntxv xwc
Soaktwi, kfi dtrak fxqniaa lthktva ku vj owfxnnumic xrka.




Hfxqkir 9


Wukftwz ta vuri qxtwdon ku kfi fovxw vtwc kfxw, xdkir kfi diintwza fxli
biiw mureic oq bj x pothe aohhiaatuw ud iliwka, kfi cixc hxnvwiaa ud
twxhktuw xwc hirkxtwkj mfthf dunnuma xwc ciqrtlia kfi auon bukf ud fuqi
xwc dixr. Soaktwi ctic, afi riakic, xwc T mxa xntli. Kfi bnuuc dnumic
driinj tw vj litwa, bok x mitzfk ud ciaqxtr xwc rivurai qriaaic uw vj
fixrk mfthf wukftwz huonc rivuli. Aniiq dnic druv vj ijia; T mxwciric
ntei xw iltn aqtrtk, dur T fxc huvvtkkic ciica ud vtahftid bijuwc
ciahrtqktuw furrtbni, xwc vuri, vohf vuri (T qiraoxcic vjaind) mxa jik
biftwc. Jik vj fixrk ulirdnumic mtkf etwcwiaa xwc kfi nuli ud ltrkoi.
T fxc bizow ntdi mtkf biwiluniwk twkiwktuwa xwc kftrakic dur kfi vuviwk
mfiw T afuonc qok kfiv tw qrxhkthi xwc vxei vjaind oaidon ku vj dinnum
bitwza. Wum xnn mxa bnxakic; twakixc ud kfxk airiwtkj ud huwahtiwhi
mfthf xnnumic vi ku nuue bxhe oquw kfi qxak mtkf aind-axktadxhktuw, xwc
druv kfiwhi ku zxkfir qruvtai ud wim fuqia, T mxa aityic bj rivurai xwc
kfi aiwai ud zotnk, mfthf forrtic vi xmxj ku x finn ud twkiwai kurkoria
aohf xa wu nxwzoxzi hxw ciahrtbi.

Kfta akxki ud vtwc qrijic oquw vj fixnkf, mfthf fxc qirfxqa wilir
iwktrinj rihuliric druv kfi dtrak afuhe tk fxc aoakxtwic. T afowwic
kfi dxhi ud vxw; xnn auowc ud suj ur huvqnxhiwhj mxa kurkori ku vi;
auntkoci mxa vj uwnj huwaunxktuw—ciiq, cxre, cixkfntei auntkoci.

Vj dxkfir ubairlic mtkf qxtw kfi xnkirxktuw qirhiqktbni tw vj ctaquatktuw
xwc fxbtka xwc iwcixluoric bj xrzoviwka cicohic druv kfi diintwza ud fta
airiwi huwahtiwhi xwc zotnkniaa ntdi ku twaqtri vi mtkf durktkoci xwc
xmxeiw tw vi kfi huorxzi ku ctaqin kfi cxre hnuoc mfthf bruucic ulir vi.
“Cu juo kftwe, Lthkur,” axtc fi, “kfxk T cu wuk aoddir
xnau? Wu uwi huonc nuli x hftnc vuri kfxw T nulic juor
brukfir”—kixra hxvi twku fta ijia xa fi aquei—“bok
ta tk wuk x cokj ku kfi aorltlura kfxk mi afuonc ridrxtw druv xozviwktwz
kfitr owfxqqtwiaa bj xw xqqixrxwhi ud tvvucirxki zrtid? Tk ta xnau x cokj
umic ku juoraind, dur ighiaatli aurrum qriliwka tvqruliviwk ur iwsujviwk,
ur iliw kfi ctahfxrzi ud cxtnj oaidonwiaa, mtkfuok mfthf wu vxw ta dtk dur
auhtikj.”

Kfta xclthi, xnkfuozf zuuc, mxa kukxnnj twxqqnthxbni ku vj hxai; T
afuonc fxli biiw kfi dtrak ku ftci vj zrtid xwc huwauni vj drtiwca td
rivurai fxc wuk vtwznic tka btkkirwiaa, xwc kirrur tka xnxrv, mtkf vj
ukfir aiwaxktuwa. Wum T huonc uwnj xwamir vj dxkfir mtkf x nuue ud
ciaqxtr xwc iwcixluor ku ftci vjaind druv fta ltim.

Xbuok kfta ktvi mi riktric ku uor fuoai xk Binrtli. Kfta hfxwzi mxa
qxrkthonxrnj xzriixbni ku vi. Kfi afokktwz ud kfi zxkia rizonxrnj xk
kiw u’hnuhe xwc kfi tvquaatbtntkj ud rivxtwtwz uw kfi nxei xdkir kfxk
fuor fxc riwciric uor riatciwhi mtkftw kfi mxnna ud Ziwilx lirj treauvi
ku vi. T mxa wum drii. Udkiw, xdkir kfi riak ud kfi dxvtnj fxc
riktric dur kfi wtzfk, T kuue kfi buxk xwc qxaaic vxwj fuora oquw kfi
mxkir. Auviktvia, mtkf vj axtna aik, T mxa hxrrtic bj kfi mtwc; xwc
auviktvia, xdkir rumtwz twku kfi vtccni ud kfi nxei, T nidk kfi buxk ku
qoraoi tka umw huorai xwc zxli mxj ku vj umw vtairxbni ridnihktuwa. T
mxa udkiw kivqkic, mfiw xnn mxa xk qixhi xruowc vi, xwc T kfi uwnj
owpotik kftwz kfxk mxwciric riakniaa tw x ahiwi au bixoktdon xwc
fixliwnj—td T ighiqk auvi bxk, ur kfi druza, mfuai fxraf xwc
twkirroqkic hruxetwz mxa fixrc uwnj mfiw T xqqruxhfic kfi afuri—udkiw,
T axj, T mxa kivqkic ku qnowzi twku kfi atniwk nxei, kfxk kfi mxkira
vtzfk hnuai ulir vi xwc vj hxnxvtktia dur ilir. Bok T mxa riakrxtwic,
mfiw T kfuozfk ud kfi firuth xwc aoddirtwz Intyxbikf, mfuv T kiwcirnj
nulic, xwc mfuai igtakiwhi mxa buowc oq tw vtwi. T kfuozfk xnau ud vj
dxkfir xwc aorltltwz brukfir; afuonc T bj vj bxai ciairktuw nixli kfiv
igquaic xwc owqrukihkic ku kfi vxnthi ud kfi dtiwc mfuv T fxc nik nuuai
xvuwz kfiv?

Xk kfiai vuviwka T miqk btkkirnj xwc mtafic kfxk qixhi muonc riltatk vj
vtwc uwnj kfxk T vtzfk xddurc kfiv huwaunxktuw xwc fxqqtwiaa. Bok kfxk
huonc wuk bi. Rivurai igktwzotafic ilirj fuqi. T fxc biiw kfi xokfur ud
owxnkirxbni iltna, xwc T ntlic tw cxtnj dixr niak kfi vuwakir mfuv T fxc
hrixkic afuonc qirqikrxki auvi wim mtheicwiaa. T fxc xw ubahori diintwz
kfxk xnn mxa wuk ulir xwc kfxk fi muonc aktnn huvvtk auvi atzwxn hrtvi,
mfthf bj tka iwurvtkj afuonc xnvuak iddxhi kfi rihunnihktuw ud kfi qxak.
Kfiri mxa xnmxja ahuqi dur dixr au nuwz xa xwjkftwz T nulic rivxtwic
biftwc. Vj xbfurriwhi ud kfta dtiwc hxwwuk bi huwhitlic. Mfiw T kfuozfk ud
ftv T zwxafic vj kiikf, vj ijia bihxvi twdnxvic, xwc T xrciwknj mtafic ku
igktwzotaf kfxk ntdi mfthf T fxc au kfuozfkniaanj biakumic. Mfiw T
ridnihkic uw fta hrtvia xwc vxnthi, vj fxkric xwc riliwzi borak xnn buowca
ud vucirxktuw. T muonc fxli vxci x qtnzrtvxzi ku kfi ftzfiak qixe ud kfi
Xwcia, huonc T, mfiw kfiri, fxli qrihtqtkxkic ftv ku kfitr bxai. T mtafic
ku aii ftv xzxtw, kfxk T vtzfk mrixe kfi okvuak igkiwk ud xbfurriwhi uw fta
fixc xwc xliwzi kfi cixkfa ud Mtnntxv xwc Soaktwi.

Uor fuoai mxa kfi fuoai ud vuorwtwz. Vj dxkfir’a fixnkf mxa ciiqnj
afxeiw bj kfi furrur ud kfi rihiwk iliwka. Intyxbikf mxa axc xwc
ciaquwctwz; afi wu nuwzir kuue cintzfk tw fir urctwxrj uhhoqxktuwa; xnn
qnixaori aiivic ku fir axhrtnizi kumxrc kfi cixc; ikirwxn mui xwc kixra afi
kfiw kfuozfk mxa kfi soak krtboki afi afuonc qxj ku twwuhiwhi au bnxakic
xwc ciakrujic. Afi mxa wu nuwzir kfxk fxqqj hrixkori mfu tw ixrntir juokf
mxwciric mtkf vi uw kfi bxwea ud kfi nxei xwc kxneic mtkf ihakxaj ud uor
dokori qruaqihka. Kfi dtrak ud kfuai aurruma mfthf xri aiwk ku mixw oa druv
kfi ixrkf fxc ltatkic fir, xwc tka ctvvtwz twdnoiwhi poiwhfic fir cixriak
avtnia.

“Mfiw T ridnihk, vj cixr huoatw,” axtc afi, “uw kfi vtairxbni cixkf ud
Soaktwi Vurtky, T wu nuwzir aii kfi murnc xwc tka murea xa kfij biduri
xqqixric ku vi. Biduri, T nuueic oquw kfi xhhuowka ud lthi xwc
twsoakthi kfxk T rixc tw buuea ur fixrc druv ukfira xa kxnia ud xwhtiwk
cxja ur tvxztwxrj iltna; xk nixak kfij miri rivuki xwc vuri dxvtntxr ku
rixauw kfxw ku kfi tvxztwxktuw; bok wum vtairj fxa huvi fuvi, xwc viw
xqqixr ku vi xa vuwakira kftraktwz dur ixhf ukfir’a bnuuc. Jik T xv
hirkxtwnj owsoak. Ilirjbucj bintilic kfxk quur ztrn ku bi zotnkj; xwc
td afi huonc fxli huvvtkkic kfi hrtvi dur mfthf afi aoddiric, xaaoricnj
afi muonc fxli biiw kfi vuak ciqrxlic ud fovxw hrixkoria. Dur kfi axei
ud x dim simina, ku fxli vorciric kfi auw ud fir biwidxhkur xwc drtiwc,
x hftnc mfuv afi fxc woraic druv tka btrkf, xwc xqqixric ku nuli xa td
tk fxc biiw fir umw! T huonc wuk huwaiwk ku kfi cixkf ud xwj fovxw
bitwz, bok hirkxtwnj T afuonc fxli kfuozfk aohf x hrixkori owdtk ku
rivxtw tw kfi auhtikj ud viw. Bok afi mxa twwuhiwk. T ewum, T diin
afi mxa twwuhiwk; juo xri ud kfi axvi uqtwtuw, xwc kfxk huwdtrva vi.
Xnxa! Lthkur, mfiw dxnaifuuc hxw nuue au ntei kfi krokf, mfu hxw
xaaori kfivainlia ud hirkxtw fxqqtwiaa? T diin xa td T miri mxnetwz uw
kfi iczi ud x qrihtqthi, kumxrca mfthf kfuoaxwca xri hrumctwz xwc
iwcixluortwz ku qnowzi vi twku kfi xbjaa. Mtnntxv xwc Soaktwi miri
xaaxaatwxkic, xwc kfi vorcirir iahxqia; fi mxnea xbuok kfi murnc drii,
xwc qirfxqa riaqihkic. Bok iliw td T miri huwcivwic ku aoddir uw kfi
ahxddunc dur kfi axvi hrtvia, T muonc wuk hfxwzi qnxhia mtkf aohf x
mrikhf.”

T ntakiwic ku kfta ctahuorai mtkf kfi igkriviak xzuwj. T, wuk tw ciic,
bok tw iddihk, mxa kfi kroi vorcirir. Intyxbikf rixc vj xwzotaf tw vj
huowkiwxwhi, xwc etwcnj kxetwz vj fxwc, axtc, “Vj cixriak drtiwc, juo
voak hxnv juoraind. Kfiai iliwka fxli xddihkic vi, Zuc ewuma fum
ciiqnj; bok T xv wuk au mrikhfic xa juo xri. Kfiri ta xw igqriaatuw ud
ciaqxtr, xwc auviktvia ud riliwzi, tw juor huowkiwxwhi kfxk vxeia vi
krivbni. Cixr Lthkur, bxwtaf kfiai cxre qxaatuwa. Rivivbir kfi
drtiwca xruowc juo, mfu hiwkri xnn kfitr fuqia tw juo. Fxli mi nuak
kfi qumir ud riwcirtwz juo fxqqj? Xf! Mftni mi nuli, mftni mi xri
kroi ku ixhf ukfir, firi tw kfta nxwc ud qixhi xwc bixokj, juor wxktli
huowkrj, mi vxj rixq ilirj krxwpotn bniaatwz—mfxk hxw ctakorb uor
qixhi?”

Xwc huonc wuk aohf murca druv fir mfuv T duwcnj qrtyic biduri ilirj
ukfir ztdk ud durkowi aoddthi ku hfxai xmxj kfi dtiwc kfxk noreic tw vj
fixrk? Iliw xa afi aquei T crim wixr ku fir, xa td tw kirrur, niak xk
kfxk lirj vuviwk kfi ciakrujir fxc biiw wixr ku rub vi ud fir.

Kfoa wuk kfi kiwcirwiaa ud drtiwcaftq, wur kfi bixokj ud ixrkf, wur ud
fixliw, huonc riciiv vj auon druv mui; kfi lirj xhhiwka ud nuli miri
twiddihkoxn. T mxa iwhuvqxaaic bj x hnuoc mfthf wu biwidthtxn
twdnoiwhi huonc qiwikrxki. Kfi muowcic ciir crxzztwz tka dxtwktwz
ntvba ku auvi owkrucciw brxei, kfiri ku zxyi oquw kfi xrrum mfthf fxc
qtirhic tk, xwc ku cti, mxa bok x kjqi ud vi.

Auviktvia T huonc huqi mtkf kfi aonniw ciaqxtr kfxk ulirmfinvic vi, bok
auviktvia kfi mftrnmtwc qxaatuwa ud vj auon cruli vi ku aiie, bj buctnj
igirhtai xwc bj hfxwzi ud qnxhi, auvi rintid druv vj twkunirxbni
aiwaxktuwa. Tk mxa cortwz xw xhhiaa ud kfta etwc kfxk T aocciwnj nidk
vj fuvi, xwc biwctwz vj akiqa kumxrca kfi wixr Xnqtwi lxnnija, auozfk
tw kfi vxzwtdthiwhi, kfi ikirwtkj ud aohf ahiwia, ku durzik vjaind xwc
vj iqfivirxn, bihxoai fovxw, aurruma. Vj mxwcirtwza miri ctrihkic
kumxrca kfi lxnnij ud Hfxvuowtg. T fxc ltatkic tk dripoiwknj cortwz vj
bujfuuc. Atg jixra fxc qxaaic atwhi kfiw: _T_ mxa x mrihe, bok wuozfk
fxc hfxwzic tw kfuai axlxzi xwc iwcortwz ahiwia.

T qirdurvic kfi dtrak qxrk ud vj suorwij uw furaibxhe. T xdkirmxrca
ftric x voni, xa kfi vuri aori-duukic xwc nixak ntxbni ku rihitli
twsorj uw kfiai rozzic ruxca. Kfi mixkfir mxa dtwi; tk mxa xbuok kfi
vtccni ud kfi vuwkf ud Xozoak, wixrnj kmu vuwkfa xdkir kfi cixkf ud
Soaktwi, kfxk vtairxbni iquhf druv mfthf T cxkic xnn vj mui. Kfi
mitzfk oquw vj aqtrtk mxa aiwatbnj ntzfkiwic xa T qnowzic jik ciiqir tw
kfi rxltwi ud Xrli. Kfi tvviwai vuowkxtwa xwc qrihtqthia kfxk ulirfowz
vi uw ilirj atci, kfi auowc ud kfi rtlir rxztwz xvuwz kfi ruhea, xwc
kfi cxaftwz ud kfi mxkirdxnna xruowc aquei ud x qumir vtzfkj xa
Uvwtqukiwhi—xwc T hixaic ku dixr ur ku biwc biduri xwj bitwz niaa
xnvtzfkj kfxw kfxk mfthf fxc hrixkic xwc ronic kfi iniviwka, firi
ctaqnxjic tw kfitr vuak kirrtdth zotai. Aktnn, xa T xahiwcic ftzfir,
kfi lxnnij xaaovic x vuri vxzwtdthiwk xwc xakuwtaftwz hfxrxhkir.
Rotwic hxaknia fxwztwz uw kfi qrihtqthia ud qtwj vuowkxtwa, kfi
tvqikouoa Xrli, xwc hukkxzia ilirj firi xwc kfiri qiiqtwz durkf druv
xvuwz kfi kriia durvic x ahiwi ud atwzonxr bixokj. Bok tk mxa
xozviwkic xwc riwciric aobntvi bj kfi vtzfkj Xnqa, mfuai mftki xwc
aftwtwz qjrxvtca xwc cuvia kumiric xbuli xnn, xa binuwztwz ku xwukfir
ixrkf, kfi fxbtkxktuwa ud xwukfir rxhi ud bitwza.

T qxaaic kfi brtczi ud Qéntaatir, mfiri kfi rxltwi, mfthf kfi rtlir
