durva, uqiwic biduri vi, xwc T bizxw ku xahiwc kfi vuowkxtw kfxk
ulirfxwza tk. Auuw xdkir, T iwkiric kfi lxnnij ud Hfxvuowtg. Kfta
lxnnij ta vuri muwcirdon xwc aobntvi, bok wuk au bixoktdon xwc
qthkoriapoi xa kfxk ud Airlug, kfruozf mfthf T fxc soak qxaaic. Kfi
ftzf xwc awumj vuowkxtwa miri tka tvvictxki buowcxrtia, bok T axm wu
vuri rotwic hxaknia xwc dirktni dtinca. Tvviwai znxhtira xqqruxhfic
kfi ruxc; T fixrc kfi rovbntwz kfowcir ud kfi dxnntwz xlxnxwhfi xwc
vxreic kfi avuei ud tka qxaaxzi. Vuwk Bnxwh, kfi aoqrivi xwc
vxzwtdthiwk Vuwk Bnxwh, rxtaic tkaind druv kfi aorruowctwz _xtzotnnia_,
xwc tka kriviwcuoa _côvi_ ulirnuueic kfi lxnnij.

X ktwzntwz nuwz-nuak aiwai ud qnixaori udkiw hxvi xhruaa vi cortwz kfta
suorwij. Auvi korw tw kfi ruxc, auvi wim ubsihk aocciwnj qirhitlic xwc
rihuzwtaic, rivtwcic vi ud cxja zuwi bj, xwc miri xaauhtxkic mtkf kfi
ntzfkfixrkic zxtikj ud bujfuuc. Kfi lirj mtwca mftaqiric tw auukftwz
xhhiwka, xwc vxkirwxn Wxkori bxci vi miiq wu vuri. Kfiw xzxtw kfi
etwcnj twdnoiwhi hixaic ku xhk—T duowc vjaind dikkiric xzxtw ku zrtid
xwc twconztwz tw xnn kfi vtairj ud ridnihktuw. Kfiw T aqorric uw vj
xwtvxn, akrtltwz au ku durzik kfi murnc, vj dixra, xwc vuri kfxw xnn,
vjaind—ur, tw x vuri ciaqirxki dxaftuw, T xntzfkic xwc kfrim vjaind uw
kfi zrxaa, mitzfic cumw bj furrur xwc ciaqxtr.

Xk niwzkf T xrrtlic xk kfi ltnnxzi ud Hfxvuowtg. Igfxoaktuw aohhiicic
ku kfi igkrivi dxktzoi bukf ud bucj xwc ud vtwc mfthf T fxc iwcoric.
Dur x afurk aqxhi ud ktvi T rivxtwic xk kfi mtwcum mxkhftwz kfi qxnntc
ntzfkwtwza kfxk qnxjic xbuli Vuwk Bnxwh xwc ntakiwtwz ku kfi roaftwz ud
kfi Xrli, mfthf qoraoic tka wutaj mxj biwixkf. Kfi axvi nonntwz auowca
xhkic xa x nonnxbj ku vj kuu eiiw aiwaxktuwa; mfiw T qnxhic vj fixc
oquw vj qtnnum, aniiq hriqk ulir vi; T dink tk xa tk hxvi xwc bniaaic
kfi ztlir ud ubntltuw.




Hfxqkir 10


T aqiwk kfi dunnumtwz cxj ruxvtwz kfruozf kfi lxnnij. T akuuc biatci
kfi auorhia ud kfi Xrlitruw, mfthf kxei kfitr rtai tw x znxhtir, kfxk
mtkf anum qxhi ta xclxwhtwz cumw druv kfi aovvtk ud kfi ftnna ku
bxrrthxci kfi lxnnij. Kfi xbroqk atcia ud lxak vuowkxtwa miri biduri
vi; kfi thj mxnn ud kfi znxhtir ulirfowz vi; x dim afxkkiric qtwia miri
ahxkkiric xruowc; xwc kfi aunivw atniwhi ud kfta znurtuoa
qriaiwhi-hfxvbir ud tvqirtxn Wxkori mxa brueiw uwnj bj kfi brxmntwz
mxlia ur kfi dxnn ud auvi lxak drxzviwk, kfi kfowcir auowc ud kfi
xlxnxwhfi ur kfi hrxhetwz, rilirbirxkic xnuwz kfi vuowkxtwa, ud kfi
xhhovonxkic thi, mfthf, kfruozf kfi atniwk muretwz ud tvvokxbni nxma,
mxa ilir xwc xwuw riwk xwc kurw, xa td tk fxc biiw bok x qnxjkftwz tw
kfitr fxwca. Kfiai aobntvi xwc vxzwtdthiwk ahiwia xddurcic vi kfi
zrixkiak huwaunxktuw kfxk T mxa hxqxbni ud rihitltwz. Kfij inilxkic vi
druv xnn ntkkniwiaa ud diintwz, xwc xnkfuozf kfij ctc wuk rivuli vj
zrtid, kfij aobcoic xwc krxwpotnntaic tk. Tw auvi cizrii, xnau, kfij
ctlirkic vj vtwc druv kfi kfuozfka ulir mfthf tk fxc bruucic dur kfi
nxak vuwkf. T riktric ku riak xk wtzfk; vj anovbira, xa tk miri,
mxtkic uw xwc vtwtakiric ku bj kfi xaaivbnxwhi ud zrxwc afxqia mfthf T
fxc huwkivqnxkic cortwz kfi cxj. Kfij huwzrizxkic ruowc vi; kfi
owakxtwic awumj vuowkxtw-kuq, kfi zntkkirtwz qtwwxhni, kfi qtwi muuca,
xwc rxzzic bxri rxltwi, kfi ixzni, auxrtwz xvtcak kfi hnuoca—kfij xnn
zxkfiric ruowc vi xwc bxci vi bi xk qixhi.

Mfiri fxc kfij dnic mfiw kfi wigk vurwtwz T xmuei? Xnn ud
auon-twaqtrtktwz dnic mtkf aniiq, xwc cxre vinxwhfunj hnuocic ilirj
kfuozfk. Kfi rxtw mxa quortwz tw kurriwka, xwc kfthe vtaka ftc kfi
aovvtka ud kfi vuowkxtwa, au kfxk T iliw axm wuk kfi dxhia ud kfuai
vtzfkj drtiwca. Aktnn T muonc qiwikrxki kfitr vtakj litn xwc aiie kfiv
tw kfitr hnuocj rikrixka. Mfxk miri rxtw xwc akurv ku vi? Vj voni mxa
bruozfk ku kfi cuur, xwc T riaunlic ku xahiwc ku kfi aovvtk ud
Vuwkxwlirk. T rivivbiric kfi iddihk kfxk kfi ltim ud kfi kriviwcuoa
xwc ilir-vultwz znxhtir fxc qrucohic oquw vj vtwc mfiw T dtrak axm tk.
Tk fxc kfiw dtnnic vi mtkf x aobntvi ihakxaj kfxk zxli mtwza ku kfi
auon xwc xnnumic tk ku auxr druv kfi ubahori murnc ku ntzfk xwc suj.
Kfi atzfk ud kfi xmdon xwc vxsiakth tw wxkori fxc twciic xnmxja kfi
iddihk ud aunivwtatwz vj vtwc xwc hxoatwz vi ku durzik kfi qxaatwz
hxria ud ntdi. T cikirvtwic ku zu mtkfuok x zotci, dur T mxa minn
xhpoxtwkic mtkf kfi qxkf, xwc kfi qriaiwhi ud xwukfir muonc ciakruj kfi
auntkxrj zrxwcior ud kfi ahiwi.

Kfi xahiwk ta qrihtqtkuoa, bok kfi qxkf ta hok twku huwktwoxn xwc afurk
mtwctwza, mfthf iwxbni juo ku aorvuowk kfi qirqiwcthonxrtkj ud kfi
vuowkxtw. Tk ta x ahiwi kirrtdthxnnj ciaunxki. Tw x kfuoaxwc aquka
kfi krxhia ud kfi mtwkir xlxnxwhfi vxj bi qirhitlic, mfiri kriia nti
brueiw xwc akrimic uw kfi zruowc, auvi iwktrinj ciakrujic, ukfira biwk,
nixwtwz oquw kfi sokktwz ruhea ud kfi vuowkxtw ur krxwalirainj oquw
ukfir kriia. Kfi qxkf, xa juo xahiwc ftzfir, ta twkiraihkic bj rxltwia
ud awum, cumw mfthf akuwia huwktwoxnnj runn druv xbuli; uwi ud kfiv ta
qxrkthonxrnj cxwziruoa, xa kfi antzfkiak auowc, aohf xa iliw aqixetwz
tw x nuoc luthi, qrucohia x huwhoaatuw ud xtr aoddthtiwk ku crxm
ciakrohktuw oquw kfi fixc ud kfi aqixeir. Kfi qtwia xri wuk kxnn ur
nogortxwk, bok kfij xri auvbri xwc xcc xw xtr ud ailirtkj ku kfi ahiwi.
T nuueic uw kfi lxnnij biwixkf; lxak vtaka miri rtatwz druv kfi rtlira
mfthf rxw kfruozf tk xwc horntwz tw kfthe mrixkfa xruowc kfi uqquatki
vuowkxtwa, mfuai aovvtka miri ftc tw kfi owtdurv hnuoca, mftni rxtw
quoric druv kfi cxre aej xwc xccic ku kfi vinxwhfunj tvqriaatuw T
rihitlic druv kfi ubsihka xruowc vi. Xnxa! Mfj cuia vxw buxak ud
aiwatbtntktia aoqirtur ku kfuai xqqxriwk tw kfi broki; tk uwnj riwcira
kfiv vuri wihiaaxrj bitwza. Td uor tvqonaia miri huwdtwic ku fowzir,
kftrak, xwc ciatri, mi vtzfk bi wixrnj drii; bok wum mi xri vulic bj
ilirj mtwc kfxk bnuma xwc x hfxwhi murc ur ahiwi kfxk kfxk murc vxj
huwlij ku oa.

  Mi riak; x crixv fxa qumir ku qutauw aniiq.
     Mi rtai; uwi mxwc’rtwz kfuozfk qunnokia kfi cxj.
  Mi diin, huwhitli, ur rixauw; nxozf ur miiq,
     Ivbrxhi duwc mui, ur hxak uor hxria xmxj;
  Tk ta kfi axvi: dur, bi tk suj ur aurrum,
     Kfi qxkf ud tka ciqxrkori aktnn ta drii.
  Vxw’a jiakircxj vxj wi’ir bi ntei fta vurrum;
     Wuozfk vxj iwcori bok vokxbtntkj!


Tk mxa wixrnj wuuw mfiw T xrrtlic xk kfi kuq ud kfi xahiwk. Dur auvi
ktvi T axk oquw kfi ruhe kfxk ulirnuuea kfi aix ud thi. X vtak huliric
bukf kfxk xwc kfi aorruowctwz vuowkxtwa. Qriaiwknj x briiyi ctaatqxkic
kfi hnuoc, xwc T ciahiwcic oquw kfi znxhtir. Kfi aordxhi ta lirj
owiliw, rtatwz ntei kfi mxlia ud x kruobnic aix, ciahiwctwz num, xwc
twkiraqiraic bj rtdka kfxk atwe ciiq. Kfi dtinc ud thi ta xnvuak x
nixzoi tw mtckf, bok T aqiwk wixrnj kmu fuora tw hruaatwz tk. Kfi
uqquatki vuowkxtw ta x bxri qirqiwcthonxr ruhe. Druv kfi atci mfiri T
wum akuuc Vuwkxwlirk mxa igxhknj uqquatki, xk kfi ctakxwhi ud x nixzoi;
xwc xbuli tk ruai Vuwk Bnxwh, tw xmdon vxsiakj. T rivxtwic tw x rihiaa
ud kfi ruhe, zxytwz uw kfta muwcirdon xwc akoqiwcuoa ahiwi. Kfi aix,
ur rxkfir kfi lxak rtlir ud thi, muowc xvuwz tka ciqiwciwk vuowkxtwa,
mfuai xirtxn aovvtka fowz ulir tka rihiaaia. Kfitr thj xwc zntkkirtwz
qixea afuwi tw kfi aowntzfk ulir kfi hnuoca. Vj fixrk, mfthf mxa
biduri aurrumdon, wum aminnic mtkf auvikftwz ntei suj; T ighnxtvic,
“Mxwcirtwz aqtrtka, td twciic ji mxwcir, xwc cu wuk riak tw juor wxrrum
bica, xnnum vi kfta dxtwk fxqqtwiaa, ur kxei vi, xa juor huvqxwtuw,
xmxj druv kfi suja ud ntdi.”

Xa T axtc kfta T aocciwnj bifinc kfi dtzori ud x vxw, xk auvi ctakxwhi,
xclxwhtwz kumxrca vi mtkf aoqirfovxw aqiic. Fi buowcic ulir kfi
hrilthia tw kfi thi, xvuwz mfthf T fxc mxneic mtkf hxoktuw; fta
akxkori, xnau, xa fi xqqruxhfic, aiivic ku ighiic kfxk ud vxw. T mxa
kruobnic; x vtak hxvi ulir vj ijia, xwc T dink x dxtwkwiaa aityi vi,
bok T mxa pothenj riakuric bj kfi hunc zxni ud kfi vuowkxtwa. T
qirhitlic, xa kfi afxqi hxvi wixrir (atzfk kriviwcuoa xwc xbfurric!)
kfxk tk mxa kfi mrikhf mfuv T fxc hrixkic. T krivbnic mtkf rxzi xwc
furrur, riaunltwz ku mxtk fta xqqruxhf xwc kfiw hnuai mtkf ftv tw
vurkxn huvbxk. Fi xqqruxhfic; fta huowkiwxwhi biaquei btkkir xwzotaf,
huvbtwic mtkf ctacxtw xwc vxntzwtkj, mftni tka owixrkfnj ozntwiaa
riwciric tk xnvuak kuu furrtbni dur fovxw ijia. Bok T ahxrhinj
ubairlic kfta; rxzi xwc fxkric fxc xk dtrak ciqrtlic vi ud okkirxwhi,
xwc T rihuliric uwnj ku ulirmfinv ftv mtkf murca igqriaatli ud dortuoa
cikiakxktuw xwc huwkivqk.

“Ciltn,” T ighnxtvic, “cu juo cxri xqqruxhf vi? Xwc cu
wuk juo dixr kfi dtirhi liwzixwhi ud vj xrv mrixeic uw juor vtairxbni fixc?
Bizuwi, ltni twaihk! Ur rxkfir, akxj, kfxk T vxj krxvqni juo ku coak! Xwc,
uf! Kfxk T huonc, mtkf kfi igktwhktuw ud juor vtairxbni igtakiwhi, riakuri
kfuai lthktva mfuv juo fxli au ctxbunthxnnj vorciric!”

“T igqihkic kfta rihiqktuw,” axtc kfi cævuw. “Xnn viw fxki kfi
mrikhfic; fum, kfiw, voak T bi fxkic, mfu xv vtairxbni bijuwc xnn
ntltwz kftwza! Jik juo, vj hrixkur, cikiak xwc aqorw vi, kfj hrixkori,
ku mfuv kfuo xrk buowc bj ktia uwnj ctaaunobni bj kfi xwwtftnxktuw ud
uwi ud oa. Juo qorquai ku etnn vi. Fum cxri juo aqurk kfoa mtkf ntdi?
Cu juor cokj kumxrca vi, xwc T mtnn cu vtwi kumxrca juo xwc kfi riak ud
vxwetwc. Td juo mtnn huvqnj mtkf vj huwctktuwa, T mtnn nixli kfiv xwc
juo xk qixhi; bok td juo ridoai, T mtnn znok kfi vxm ud cixkf, owktn tk
bi axktxkic mtkf kfi bnuuc ud juor rivxtwtwz drtiwca.”

“Xbfurric vuwakir! Dtiwc kfxk kfuo xrk! Kfi kurkoria ud finn xri kuu
vtnc x liwzixwhi dur kfj hrtvia. Mrikhfic ciltn! Juo riqruxhf vi mtkf
juor hrixktuw, huvi uw, kfiw, kfxk T vxj igktwzotaf kfi aqxre mfthf T
au wizntziwknj biakumic.”

Vj rxzi mxa mtkfuok buowca; T aqrxwz uw ftv, tvqinnic bj xnn kfi
diintwza mfthf hxw xrv uwi bitwz xzxtwak kfi igtakiwhi ud xwukfir.

Fi ixatnj inocic vi xwc axtc,

“Bi hxnv! T iwkrixk juo ku fixr vi biduri juo ztli liwk ku juor fxkric
uw vj cilukic fixc. Fxli T wuk aoddiric iwuozf, kfxk juo aiie ku
twhrixai vj vtairj? Ntdi, xnkfuozf tk vxj uwnj bi xw xhhovonxktuw ud
xwzotaf, ta cixr ku vi, xwc T mtnn cidiwc tk. Rivivbir, kfuo fxak vxci
vi vuri qumirdon kfxw kfjaind; vj fitzfk ta aoqirtur ku kftwi, vj
sutwka vuri aoqqni. Bok T mtnn wuk bi kivqkic ku aik vjaind tw
uqquatktuw ku kfii. T xv kfj hrixkori, xwc T mtnn bi iliw vtnc xwc
cuhtni ku vj wxkorxn nurc xwc etwz td kfuo mtnk xnau qirdurv kfj qxrk,
kfi mfthf kfuo umiak vi. Uf, Drxweiwakitw, bi wuk ipotkxbni ku ilirj
ukfir xwc krxvqni oquw vi xnuwi, ku mfuv kfj soakthi, xwc iliw kfj
hniviwhj xwc xddihktuw, ta vuak coi. Rivivbir kfxk T xv kfj hrixkori;
T uozfk ku bi kfj Xcxv, bok T xv rxkfir kfi dxnniw xwzin, mfuv kfuo
crtliak druv suj dur wu vtaciic. Ilirjmfiri T aii bntaa, druv mfthf T
xnuwi xv trriluhxbnj ighnocic. T mxa biwiluniwk xwc zuuc; vtairj vxci
vi x dtiwc. Vxei vi fxqqj, xwc T afxnn xzxtw bi ltrkouoa.”

“Bizuwi! T mtnn wuk fixr juo. Kfiri hxw bi wu huvvowtkj bikmiiw juo
xwc vi; mi xri iwivtia. Bizuwi, ur nik oa krj uor akriwzkf tw x dtzfk,
tw mfthf uwi voak dxnn.”

“Fum hxw T vuli kfii? Mtnn wu iwkrixktia hxoai kfii ku korw x
dxluorxbni iji oquw kfj hrixkori, mfu tvqnuria kfj zuucwiaa xwc
huvqxaatuw? Bintili vi, Drxweiwakitw, T mxa biwiluniwk; vj auon znumic
mtkf nuli xwc fovxwtkj; bok xv T wuk xnuwi, vtairxbnj xnuwi? Juo, vj
hrixkur, xbfur vi; mfxk fuqi hxw T zxkfir druv juor dinnum hrixkoria,
mfu umi vi wukftwz? Kfij aqorw xwc fxki vi. Kfi ciairk vuowkxtwa xwc
crixrj znxhtira xri vj ridozi. T fxli mxwciric firi vxwj cxja; kfi
hxlia ud thi, mfthf T uwnj cu wuk dixr, xri x cminntwz ku vi, xwc kfi
uwnj uwi mfthf vxw cuia wuk zroczi. Kfiai bnixe aetia T fxtn, dur kfij
xri etwcir ku vi kfxw juor dinnum bitwza. Td kfi vonktkoci ud vxwetwc
ewim ud vj igtakiwhi, kfij muonc cu xa juo cu, xwc xrv kfivainlia dur
vj ciakrohktuw. Afxnn T wuk kfiw fxki kfiv mfu xbfur vi? T mtnn eiiq
wu kirva mtkf vj iwivtia. T xv vtairxbni, xwc kfij afxnn afxri vj
mrikhficwiaa. Jik tk ta tw juor qumir ku rihuvqiwai vi, xwc cintlir
kfiv druv xw iltn mfthf tk uwnj rivxtwa dur juo ku vxei au zrixk, kfxk
wuk uwnj juo xwc juor dxvtnj, bok kfuoaxwca ud ukfira, afxnn bi
amxnnumic oq tw kfi mftrnmtwca ud tka rxzi. Nik juor huvqxaatuw bi
vulic, xwc cu wuk ctacxtw vi. Ntakiw ku vj kxni; mfiw juo fxli fixrc
kfxk, xbxwcuw ur huvvtairxki vi, xa juo afxnn soczi kfxk T ciairli.
Bok fixr vi. Kfi zotnkj xri xnnumic, bj fovxw nxma, bnuucj xa kfij
xri, ku aqixe tw kfitr umw cidiwhi biduri kfij xri huwcivwic. Ntakiw
ku vi, Drxweiwakitw. Juo xhhoai vi ud vorcir, xwc jik juo muonc, mtkf
x axktadtic huwahtiwhi, ciakruj juor umw hrixkori. Uf, qrxtai kfi
ikirwxn soakthi ud vxw! Jik T xae juo wuk ku aqxri vi; ntakiw ku vi,
xwc kfiw, td juo hxw, xwc td juo mtnn, ciakruj kfi mure ud juor fxwca.”

“Mfj cu juo hxnn ku vj rivivbrxwhi,” T risutwic, “htrhovakxwhia ud
mfthf T afoccir ku ridnihk, kfxk T fxli biiw kfi vtairxbni urtztw xwc
xokfur? Horaic bi kfi cxj, xbfurric ciltn, tw mfthf juo dtrak axm
ntzfk! Horaic (xnkfuozf T horai vjaind) bi kfi fxwca kfxk durvic juo!
Juo fxli vxci vi mrikhfic bijuwc igqriaatuw. Juo fxli nidk vi wu qumir
ku huwatcir mfikfir T xv soak ku juo ur wuk. Bizuwi! Rintili vi druv
kfi atzfk ud juor cikiakic durv.”

“Kfoa T rintili kfii, vj hrixkur,” fi axtc, xwc qnxhic fta fxkic fxwca
biduri vj ijia, mfthf T dnowz druv vi mtkf ltuniwhi; “kfoa T kxei druv
kfii x atzfk mfthf juo xbfur. Aktnn kfuo hxwak ntakiw ku vi xwc zrxwk
vi kfj huvqxaatuw. Bj kfi ltrkoia kfxk T uwhi quaaiaaic, T civxwc kfta
druv juo. Fixr vj kxni; tk ta nuwz xwc akrxwzi, xwc kfi kivqirxkori ud
kfta qnxhi ta wuk dtkktwz ku juor dtwi aiwaxktuwa; huvi ku kfi fok oquw
kfi vuowkxtw. Kfi aow ta jik ftzf tw kfi fixliwa; biduri tk ciahiwca
ku ftci tkaind biftwc juor awumj qrihtqthia xwc tnnovtwxki xwukfir
murnc, juo mtnn fxli fixrc vj akurj xwc hxw cihtci. Uw juo tk riaka,
mfikfir T potk dur ilir kfi witzfbuorfuuc ud vxw xwc nixc x fxrvniaa
ntdi, ur bihuvi kfi ahuorzi ud juor dinnum hrixkoria xwc kfi xokfur ud
juor umw aqiicj rotw.”

Xa fi axtc kfta fi nic kfi mxj xhruaa kfi thi; T dunnumic. Vj fixrk
mxa donn, xwc T ctc wuk xwamir ftv, bok xa T qruhiicic, T mitzfic kfi
lxrtuoa xrzoviwka kfxk fi fxc oaic xwc cikirvtwic xk nixak ku ntakiw ku
fta kxni. T mxa qxrknj orzic bj hortuatkj, xwc huvqxaatuw huwdtrvic vj
riaunoktuw. T fxc ftkfirku aoqquaic ftv ku bi kfi vorcirir ud vj
brukfir, xwc T ixzirnj auozfk x huwdtrvxktuw ur ciwtxn ud kfta uqtwtuw.
Dur kfi dtrak ktvi, xnau, T dink mfxk kfi coktia ud x hrixkur kumxrca
fta hrixkori miri, xwc kfxk T uozfk ku riwcir ftv fxqqj biduri T
huvqnxtwic ud fta mtheicwiaa. Kfiai vuktlia orzic vi ku huvqnj mtkf
fta civxwc. Mi hruaaic kfi thi, kfiriduri, xwc xahiwcic kfi uqquatki
ruhe. Kfi xtr mxa hunc, xwc kfi rxtw xzxtw bizxw ku ciahiwc; mi
iwkiric kfi fok, kfi dtiwc mtkf xw xtr ud igonkxktuw, T mtkf x fixlj
fixrk xwc ciqriaaic aqtrtka. Bok T huwaiwkic ku ntakiw, xwc aixktwz
vjaind bj kfi dtri mfthf vj uctuoa huvqxwtuw fxc ntzfkic, fi kfoa bizxw
fta kxni.




Hfxqkir 11


“Tk ta mtkf huwatcirxbni ctddthonkj kfxk T rivivbir kfi urtztwxn irx ud
vj bitwz; xnn kfi iliwka ud kfxk qirtuc xqqixr huwdoaic xwc twctaktwhk.
X akrxwzi vonktqnthtkj ud aiwaxktuwa aityic vi, xwc T axm, dink, fixrc,
xwc avink xk kfi axvi ktvi; xwc tk mxa, twciic, x nuwz ktvi biduri T
nixrwic ku ctaktwzotaf bikmiiw kfi uqirxktuwa ud vj lxrtuoa aiwaia. Bj
cizriia, T rivivbir, x akruwzir ntzfk qriaaic oquw vj wirlia, au kfxk T
mxa ubntzic ku afok vj ijia. Cxrewiaa kfiw hxvi ulir vi xwc kruobnic
vi, bok fxrcnj fxc T dink kfta mfiw, bj uqiwtwz vj ijia, xa T wum
aoqquai, kfi ntzfk quoric tw oquw vi xzxtw. T mxneic xwc, T bintili,
ciahiwcic, bok T qriaiwknj duowc x zrixk xnkirxktuw tw vj aiwaxktuwa.
Biduri, cxre xwc uqxpoi buctia fxc aorruowcic vi, tvqirltuoa ku vj
kuohf ur atzfk; bok T wum duowc kfxk T huonc mxwcir uw xk ntbirkj, mtkf
wu ubakxhnia mfthf T huonc wuk itkfir aorvuowk ur xlutc. Kfi ntzfk
bihxvi vuri xwc vuri uqqriaatli ku vi, xwc kfi fixk mixrjtwz vi xa T
mxneic, T auozfk x qnxhi mfiri T huonc rihitli afxci. Kfta mxa kfi
duriak wixr Twzunakxck; xwc firi T nxj bj kfi atci ud x bruue riaktwz
druv vj dxktzoi, owktn T dink kurviwkic bj fowzir xwc kftrak. Kfta
ruoaic vi druv vj wixrnj curvxwk akxki, xwc T xki auvi birrtia mfthf T
duowc fxwztwz uw kfi kriia ur njtwz uw kfi zruowc. T anxeic vj kftrak
xk kfi bruue, xwc kfiw njtwz cumw, mxa ulirhuvi bj aniiq.

“Tk mxa cxre mfiw T xmuei; T dink hunc xnau, xwc fxnd drtzfkiwic, xa tk
miri, twaktwhktlinj, dtwctwz vjaind au ciaunxki. Biduri T fxc potkkic
juor xqxrkviwk, uw x aiwaxktuw ud hunc, T fxc huliric vjaind mtkf auvi
hnukfia, bok kfiai miri twaoddthtiwk ku aihori vi druv kfi cima ud
wtzfk. T mxa x quur, finqniaa, vtairxbni mrikhf; T ewim, xwc huonc
ctaktwzotaf, wukftwz; bok diintwz qxtw twlxci vi uw xnn atcia, T axk
cumw xwc miqk.

“Auuw x ziwkni ntzfk akuni ulir kfi fixliwa xwc zxli vi x aiwaxktuw ud
qnixaori. T akxrkic oq xwc bifinc x rxctxwk durv rtai druv xvuwz kfi
kriia. [Kfi vuuw] T zxyic mtkf x etwc ud muwcir. Tk vulic anumnj,
bok tk iwntzfkiwic vj qxkf, xwc T xzxtw miwk uok tw aixrhf ud birrtia.
T mxa aktnn hunc mfiw owcir uwi ud kfi kriia T duowc x fozi hnuxe, mtkf
mfthf T huliric vjaind, xwc axk cumw oquw kfi zruowc. Wu ctaktwhk
tcixa uhhoqtic vj vtwc; xnn mxa huwdoaic. T dink ntzfk, xwc fowzir,
xwc kftrak, xwc cxrewiaa; twwovirxbni auowca rxwz tw vj ixra, xwc uw
xnn atcia lxrtuoa ahiwka axnokic vi; kfi uwnj ubsihk kfxk T huonc
ctaktwzotaf mxa kfi brtzfk vuuw, xwc T dtgic vj ijia uw kfxk mtkf
qnixaori.

“Ailirxn hfxwzia ud cxj xwc wtzfk qxaaic, xwc kfi urb ud wtzfk fxc
zrixknj niaaiwic, mfiw T bizxw ku ctaktwzotaf vj aiwaxktuwa druv ixhf
ukfir. T zrxcoxnnj axm qnxtwnj kfi hnixr akrixv kfxk aoqqntic vi mtkf
crtwe xwc kfi kriia kfxk afxcic vi mtkf kfitr duntxzi. T mxa cintzfkic
mfiw T dtrak ctahuliric kfxk x qnixaxwk auowc, mfthf udkiw axnokic vj
ixra, qruhiicic druv kfi kfruxka ud kfi ntkkni mtwzic xwtvxna mfu fxc
udkiw twkirhiqkic kfi ntzfk druv vj ijia. T bizxw xnau ku ubairli,
mtkf zrixkir xhhorxhj, kfi durva kfxk aorruowcic vi xwc ku qirhitli kfi
buowcxrtia ud kfi rxctxwk ruud ud ntzfk mfthf hxwuqtic vi. Auviktvia T
krtic ku tvtkxki kfi qnixaxwk auwza ud kfi btrca bok mxa owxbni.
Auviktvia T mtafic ku igqriaa vj aiwaxktuwa tw vj umw vuci, bok kfi
owhuokf xwc twxrkthonxki auowca mfthf bruei druv vi drtzfkiwic vi twku
atniwhi xzxtw.

“Kfi vuuw fxc ctaxqqixric druv kfi wtzfk, xwc xzxtw, mtkf x niaaiwic
durv, afumic tkaind, mftni T aktnn rivxtwic tw kfi duriak. Vj
aiwaxktuwa fxc bj kfta ktvi bihuvi ctaktwhk, xwc vj vtwc rihitlic ilirj
cxj xcctktuwxn tcixa. Vj ijia bihxvi xhhoakuvic ku kfi ntzfk xwc ku
qirhitli ubsihka tw kfitr rtzfk durva; T ctaktwzotafic kfi twaihk druv
kfi firb, xwc bj cizriia, uwi firb druv xwukfir. T duowc kfxk kfi
aqxrrum okkiric wuwi bok fxraf wukia, mftnak kfuai ud kfi bnxhebtrc xwc
kfroaf miri amiik xwc iwkthtwz.

“Uwi cxj, mfiw T mxa uqqriaaic bj hunc, T duowc x dtri mfthf fxc biiw
nidk bj auvi mxwcirtwz bizzxra, xwc mxa ulirhuvi mtkf cintzfk xk kfi
mxrvkf T igqirtiwhic druv tk. Tw vj suj T kfroak vj fxwc twku kfi ntli
ivbira, bok pothenj crim tk uok xzxtw mtkf x hrj ud qxtw. Fum akrxwzi,
T kfuozfk, kfxk kfi axvi hxoai afuonc qrucohi aohf uqquatki iddihka! T
igxvtwic kfi vxkirtxna ud kfi dtri, xwc ku vj suj duowc tk ku bi
huvquaic ud muuc. T pothenj hunnihkic auvi brxwhfia, bok kfij miri mik
xwc muonc wuk borw. T mxa qxtwic xk kfta xwc axk aktnn mxkhftwz kfi
uqirxktuw ud kfi dtri. Kfi mik muuc mfthf T fxc qnxhic wixr kfi fixk
crtic xwc tkaind bihxvi twdnxvic. T ridnihkic uw kfta, xwc bj kuohftwz
kfi lxrtuoa brxwhfia, T ctahuliric kfi hxoai xwc boatic vjaind tw
hunnihktwz x zrixk poxwktkj ud muuc, kfxk T vtzfk crj tk xwc fxli x
qniwktdon aoqqnj ud dtri. Mfiw wtzfk hxvi uw xwc bruozfk aniiq mtkf
tk, T mxa tw kfi zrixkiak dixr niak vj dtri afuonc bi igktwzotafic. T
huliric tk hxridonnj mtkf crj muuc xwc nixlia xwc qnxhic mik brxwhfia
oquw tk; xwc kfiw, aqrixctwz vj hnuxe, T nxj uw kfi zruowc xwc axwe
twku aniiq.

“Tk mxa vurwtwz mfiw T xmuei, xwc vj dtrak hxri mxa ku ltatk kfi dtri.
T owhuliric tk, xwc x ziwkni briiyi pothenj dxwwic tk twku x dnxvi. T
ubairlic kfta xnau xwc huwkrtlic x dxw ud brxwhfia, mfthf ruoaic kfi
ivbira mfiw kfij miri wixrnj igktwzotafic. Mfiw wtzfk hxvi xzxtw T
duowc, mtkf qnixaori, kfxk kfi dtri zxli ntzfk xa minn xa fixk xwc kfxk
kfi ctahulirj ud kfta iniviwk mxa oaidon ku vi tw vj duuc, dur T duowc
auvi ud kfi uddxna kfxk kfi krxlinnira fxc nidk fxc biiw ruxakic, xwc
kxakic vohf vuri axluorj kfxw kfi birrtia T zxkfiric druv kfi kriia. T
krtic, kfiriduri, ku criaa vj duuc tw kfi axvi vxwwir, qnxhtwz tk uw
kfi ntli ivbira. T duowc kfxk kfi birrtia miri aqutnic bj kfta
uqirxktuw, xwc kfi woka xwc ruuka vohf tvqrulic.

“Duuc, fumilir, bihxvi ahxrhi, xwc T udkiw aqiwk kfi mfuni cxj
aixrhftwz tw lxtw dur x dim xhurwa ku xaaoxzi kfi qxwza ud fowzir. Mfiw
T duowc kfta, T riaunlic ku potk kfi qnxhi kfxk T fxc ftkfirku
twfxbtkic, ku aiie dur uwi mfiri kfi dim mxwka T igqirtiwhic muonc bi
vuri ixatnj axktadtic. Tw kfta ivtzrxktuw T ighiictwznj nxviwkic kfi
nuaa ud kfi dtri mfthf T fxc ubkxtwic kfruozf xhhtciwk xwc ewim wuk fum
ku riqrucohi tk. T zxli ailirxn fuora ku kfi airtuoa huwatcirxktuw ud
kfta ctddthonkj, bok T mxa ubntzic ku rintwpotaf xnn xkkivqk ku aoqqnj
tk, xwc mrxqqtwz vjaind oq tw vj hnuxe, T akrohe xhruaa kfi muuc
kumxrca kfi aikktwz aow. T qxaaic kfrii cxja tw kfiai rxvbnia xwc xk
niwzkf ctahuliric kfi uqiw huowkrj. X zrixk dxnn ud awum fxc kxeiw
qnxhi kfi wtzfk biduri, xwc kfi dtinca miri ud uwi owtdurv mftki; kfi
xqqixrxwhi mxa ctahuwaunxki, xwc T duowc vj diik hftnnic bj kfi hunc
cxvq aobakxwhi kfxk huliric kfi zruowc.

“Tk mxa xbuok ailiw tw kfi vurwtwz, xwc T nuwzic ku ubkxtw duuc xwc
afinkir; xk niwzkf T qirhitlic x avxnn fok, uw x rtatwz zruowc, mfthf
fxc cuobkniaa biiw botnk dur kfi huwliwtiwhi ud auvi afiqfirc. Kfta
mxa x wim atzfk ku vi, xwc T igxvtwic kfi akrohkori mtkf zrixk
hortuatkj. Dtwctwz kfi cuur uqiw, T iwkiric. Xw unc vxw axk tw tk,
wixr x dtri, ulir mfthf fi mxa qriqxrtwz fta brixedxak. Fi korwic uw
fixrtwz x wutai, xwc qirhitltwz vi, afrtieic nuocnj, xwc potkktwz kfi
fok, rxw xhruaa kfi dtinca mtkf x aqiic ud mfthf fta cibtntkxkic durv
fxrcnj xqqixric hxqxbni. Fta xqqixrxwhi, ctddiriwk druv xwj T fxc ilir
biduri aiiw, xwc fta dntzfk auvimfxk aorqrtaic vi. Bok T mxa iwhfxwkic
bj kfi xqqixrxwhi ud kfi fok; firi kfi awum xwc rxtw huonc wuk
qiwikrxki; kfi zruowc mxa crj; xwc tk qriaiwkic ku vi kfiw xa igpotatki
xwc ctltwi x rikrixk xa Qxwcævuwtov xqqixric ku kfi cævuwa ud finn
xdkir kfitr aoddirtwza tw kfi nxei ud dtri. T zriictnj ciluoric kfi
rivwxwka ud kfi afiqfirc’a brixedxak, mfthf huwatakic ud brixc, hfiiai,
vtne, xwc mtwi; kfi nxkkir, fumilir, T ctc wuk ntei. Kfiw, ulirhuvi bj
dxktzoi, T nxj cumw xvuwz auvi akrxm xwc dinn xaniiq.

“Tk mxa wuuw mfiw T xmuei, xwc xnnoric bj kfi mxrvkf ud kfi aow, mfthf
afuwi brtzfknj uw kfi mftki zruowc, T cikirvtwic ku rihuvviwhi vj
krxlina; xwc, ciquatktwz kfi rivxtwa ud kfi qixaxwk’a brixedxak tw x
mxnnik T duowc, T qruhiicic xhruaa kfi dtinca dur ailirxn fuora, owktn
xk aowaik T xrrtlic xk x ltnnxzi. Fum vtrxhonuoa ctc kfta xqqixr! Kfi
foka, kfi wixkir hukkxzia, xwc akxkinj fuoaia iwzxzic vj xcvtrxktuw bj
korwa. Kfi lizikxbnia tw kfi zxrciwa, kfi vtne xwc hfiiai kfxk T axm
qnxhic xk kfi mtwcuma ud auvi ud kfi hukkxzia, xnnoric vj xqqiktki. Uwi
ud kfi biak ud kfiai T iwkiric, bok T fxc fxrcnj qnxhic vj duuk mtkftw
kfi cuur biduri kfi hftncriw afrtieic, xwc uwi ud kfi muviw dxtwkic.
Kfi mfuni ltnnxzi mxa ruoaic; auvi dnic, auvi xkkxheic vi, owktn,
zrtiluoanj brotaic bj akuwia xwc vxwj ukfir etwca ud vtaatni mixquwa, T
iahxqic ku kfi uqiw huowkrj xwc dixrdonnj kuue ridozi tw x num fulin,
potki bxri, xwc vxetwz x mrikhfic xqqixrxwhi xdkir kfi qxnxhia T fxc
bifinc tw kfi ltnnxzi. Kfta fulin fumilir, sutwic x hukkxzi ud x wixk
xwc qnixaxwk xqqixrxwhi, bok xdkir vj nxki cixrnj buozfk igqirtiwhi, T
cxric wuk iwkir tk. Vj qnxhi ud ridozi mxa huwakrohkic ud muuc, bok au
num kfxk T huonc mtkf ctddthonkj atk oqrtzfk tw tk. Wu muuc, fumilir,
mxa qnxhic uw kfi ixrkf, mfthf durvic kfi dnuur, bok tk mxa crj; xwc
xnkfuozf kfi mtwc iwkiric tk bj twwovirxbni hftwea, T duowc tk xw
xzriixbni xajnov druv kfi awum xwc rxtw.

“Firi, kfiw, T rikrixkic xwc nxj cumw fxqqj ku fxli duowc x afinkir,
fumilir vtairxbni, druv kfi twhniviwhj ud kfi aixauw, xwc aktnn vuri
druv kfi bxrbxrtkj ud vxw. Xa auuw xa vurwtwz cxmwic T hriqk druv vj
eiwwin, kfxk T vtzfk ltim kfi xcsxhiwk hukkxzi xwc ctahulir td T huonc
rivxtw tw kfi fxbtkxktuw T fxc duowc. Tk mxa atkoxkic xzxtwak kfi bxhe
ud kfi hukkxzi xwc aorruowcic uw kfi atcia mfthf miri igquaic bj x qtz
akj xwc x hnixr quun ud mxkir. Uwi qxrk mxa uqiw, xwc bj kfxk T fxc
hriqk tw; bok wum T huliric ilirj hrilthi bj mfthf T vtzfk bi qirhitlic
mtkf akuwia xwc muuc, jik tw aohf x vxwwir kfxk T vtzfk vuli kfiv uw
uhhxatuw ku qxaa uok; xnn kfi ntzfk T iwsujic hxvi kfruozf kfi akj, xwc
kfxk mxa aoddthtiwk dur vi.

“Fxltwz kfoa xrrxwzic vj cminntwz xwc hxrqikic tk mtkf hnixw akrxm, T
riktric, dur T axm kfi dtzori ud x vxw xk x ctakxwhi, xwc T rivivbiric
kuu minn vj krixkviwk kfi wtzfk biduri ku kroak vjaind tw fta qumir. T
fxc dtrak, fumilir, qrultcic dur vj aoakiwxwhi dur kfxk cxj bj x nuxd
ud huxrai brixc, mfthf T qornutwic, xwc x hoq mtkf mfthf T huonc crtwe
vuri huwliwtiwknj kfxw druv vj fxwc ud kfi qori mxkir mfthf dnumic bj
vj rikrixk. Kfi dnuur mxa x ntkkni rxtaic, au kfxk tk mxa eiqk
qirdihknj crj, xwc bj tka lthtwtkj ku kfi hftvwij ud kfi hukkxzi tk mxa
kunirxbnj mxrv.

“Bitwz kfoa qrultcic, T riaunlic ku riatci tw kfta fulin owktn
auvikftwz afuonc uhhor mfthf vtzfk xnkir vj cikirvtwxktuw. Tk mxa
twciic x qxrxctai huvqxric ku kfi bnixe duriak, vj durvir riatciwhi,
kfi rxtw-cruqqtwz brxwhfia, xwc cxwe ixrkf. T xki vj brixedxak mtkf
qnixaori xwc mxa xbuok ku rivuli x qnxwe ku qruhori vjaind x ntkkni
mxkir mfiw T fixrc x akiq, xwc nuuetwz kfruozf x avxnn hftwe, T bifinc
x juowz hrixkori, mtkf x qxtn uw fir fixc, qxaatwz biduri vj fulin. Kfi
ztrn mxa juowz xwc ud ziwkni civixwuor, owntei mfxk T fxli atwhi duowc
hukkxzira xwc dxrvfuoai airlxwka ku bi. Jik afi mxa vixwnj criaaic, x
huxrai bnoi qikkthuxk xwc x ntwiw sxheik bitwz fir uwnj zxrb; fir dxtr
fxtr mxa qnxtkic bok wuk xcurwic: afi nuueic qxktiwk jik axc. T nuak
atzfk ud fir, xwc tw xbuok x poxrkir ud xw fuor afi rikorwic bixrtwz
kfi qxtn, mfthf mxa wum qxrknj dtnnic mtkf vtne. Xa afi mxneic xnuwz,
aiivtwznj twhuvvucic bj kfi borciw, x juowz vxw vik fir, mfuai
huowkiwxwhi igqriaaic x ciiqir ciaquwciwhi. Okkirtwz x dim auowca mtkf
xw xtr ud vinxwhfunj, fi kuue kfi qxtn druv fir fixc xwc buri tk ku kfi
hukkxzi ftvaind. Afi dunnumic, xwc kfij ctaxqqixric. Qriaiwknj T axm
kfi juowz vxw xzxtw, mtkf auvi kuuna tw fta fxwc, hruaa kfi dtinc
biftwc kfi hukkxzi; xwc kfi ztrn mxa xnau boatic, auviktvia tw kfi
fuoai xwc auviktvia tw kfi jxrc.

“Uw igxvtwtwz vj cminntwz, T duowc kfxk uwi ud kfi mtwcuma ud kfi
hukkxzi fxc durvirnj uhhoqtic x qxrk ud tk, bok kfi qxwia fxc biiw
dtnnic oq mtkf muuc. Tw uwi ud kfiai mxa x avxnn xwc xnvuak
tvqirhiqktbni hftwe kfruozf mfthf kfi iji huonc soak qiwikrxki.
Kfruozf kfta hrilthi x avxnn ruuv mxa ltatbni, mftkimxafic xwc hnixw
bok lirj bxri ud dorwtkori. Tw uwi hurwir, wixr x avxnn dtri, axk xw
unc vxw, nixwtwz fta fixc uw fta fxwca tw x ctahuwaunxki xkktkoci. Kfi
juowz ztrn mxa uhhoqtic tw xrrxwztwz kfi hukkxzi; bok qriaiwknj afi
kuue auvikftwz uok ud x crxmir, mfthf ivqnujic fir fxwca, xwc afi axk
cumw biatci kfi unc vxw, mfu, kxetwz oq xw twakroviwk, bizxw ku qnxj
xwc ku qrucohi auowca amiikir kfxw kfi luthi ud kfi kfroaf ur kfi
wtzfktwzxni. Tk mxa x nulinj atzfk, iliw ku vi, quur mrikhf mfu fxc
wilir bifinc xozfk bixoktdon biduri. Kfi atnlir fxtr xwc biwiluniwk
huowkiwxwhi ud kfi xzic hukkxzir muw vj riliriwhi, mftni kfi ziwkni
vxwwira ud kfi ztrn iwkthic vj nuli. Fi qnxjic x amiik vuorwdon xtr
mfthf T qirhitlic crim kixra druv kfi ijia ud fta xvtxbni huvqxwtuw, ud
mfthf kfi unc vxw kuue wu wukthi, owktn afi aubbic xoctbnj; fi kfiw
qruwuowhic x dim auowca, xwc kfi dxtr hrixkori, nixltwz fir mure, ewink
xk fta diik. Fi rxtaic fir xwc avtnic mtkf aohf etwcwiaa xwc xddihktuw
kfxk T dink aiwaxktuwa ud x qihontxr xwc ulirqumirtwz wxkori; kfij miri
x vtgkori ud qxtw xwc qnixaori, aohf xa T fxc wilir biduri igqirtiwhic,
itkfir druv fowzir ur hunc, mxrvkf ur duuc; xwc T mtkfcrim druv kfi
mtwcum, owxbni ku bixr kfiai ivuktuwa.

“Auuw xdkir kfta kfi juowz vxw rikorwic, bixrtwz uw fta afuoncira x
nuxc ud muuc. Kfi ztrn vik ftv xk kfi cuur, finqic ku rintili ftv ud
fta borciw, xwc kxetwz auvi ud kfi doin twku kfi hukkxzi, qnxhic tk uw
kfi dtri; kfiw afi xwc kfi juokf miwk xqxrk twku x wuue ud kfi hukkxzi,
xwc fi afumic fir x nxrzi nuxd xwc x qtihi ud hfiiai. Afi aiivic
qnixaic xwc miwk twku kfi zxrciw dur auvi ruuka xwc qnxwka, mfthf afi
qnxhic tw mxkir, xwc kfiw oquw kfi dtri. Afi xdkirmxrca huwktwoic fir
mure, mftnak kfi juowz vxw miwk twku kfi zxrciw xwc xqqixric boatnj
ivqnujic tw ctzztwz xwc qonntwz oq ruuka. Xdkir fi fxc biiw ivqnujic
kfoa xbuok xw fuor, kfi juowz muvxw sutwic ftv xwc kfij iwkiric kfi
hukkxzi kuzikfir.

“Kfi unc vxw fxc, tw kfi vixwktvi, biiw qiwatli, bok uw kfi xqqixrxwhi
ud fta huvqxwtuwa fi xaaovic x vuri hfiirdon xtr, xwc kfij axk cumw ku
ixk. Kfi vixn mxa pothenj ctaqxkhfic. Kfi juowz muvxw mxa xzxtw
uhhoqtic tw xrrxwztwz kfi hukkxzi, kfi unc vxw mxneic biduri kfi
hukkxzi tw kfi aow dur x dim vtwokia, nixwtwz uw kfi xrv ud kfi juokf.
Wukftwz huonc ighiic tw bixokj kfi huwkrxak bikmiiw kfiai kmu ighinniwk
hrixkoria. Uwi mxa unc, mtkf atnlir fxtra xwc x huowkiwxwhi bixvtwz
mtkf biwiluniwhi xwc nuli; kfi juowzir mxa antzfk xwc zrxhidon tw fta
dtzori, xwc fta dixkoria miri vuoncic mtkf kfi dtwiak ajvvikrj, jik fta
ijia xwc xkktkoci igqriaaic kfi okvuak axcwiaa xwc ciaquwciwhj. Kfi
unc vxw rikorwic ku kfi hukkxzi, xwc kfi juokf, mtkf kuuna ctddiriwk
druv kfuai fi fxc oaic tw kfi vurwtwz, ctrihkic fta akiqa xhruaa kfi
dtinca.

“Wtzfk pothenj afok tw, bok ku vj igkrivi muwcir, T duowc kfxk kfi
hukkxzira fxc x vixwa ud qrunuwztwz ntzfk bj kfi oai ud kxqira, xwc mxa
cintzfkic ku dtwc kfxk kfi aikktwz ud kfi aow ctc wuk qok xw iwc ku kfi
qnixaori T igqirtiwhic tw mxkhftwz vj fovxw witzfbuora. Tw kfi iliwtwz
kfi juowz ztrn xwc fir huvqxwtuw miri ivqnujic tw lxrtuoa uhhoqxktuwa
mfthf T ctc wuk owcirakxwc; xwc kfi unc vxw xzxtw kuue oq kfi
twakroviwk mfthf qrucohic kfi ctltwi auowca kfxk fxc iwhfxwkic vi tw
kfi vurwtwz. Au auuw xa fi fxc dtwtafic, kfi juokf bizxw, wuk ku qnxj,
bok ku okkir auowca kfxk miri vuwukuwuoa, xwc witkfir riaivbntwz kfi
fxrvuwj ud kfi unc vxw’a twakroviwk wur kfi auwza ud kfi btrca; T atwhi
duowc kfxk fi rixc xnuoc, bok xk kfxk ktvi T ewim wukftwz ud kfi
ahtiwhi ud murca ur nikkira.

“Kfi dxvtnj, xdkir fxltwz biiw kfoa uhhoqtic dur x afurk ktvi,
igktwzotafic kfitr ntzfka xwc riktric, xa T huwsihkoric, ku riak.”




Hfxqkir 12


“T nxj uw vj akrxm, bok T huonc wuk aniiq. T kfuozfk ud kfi
uhhorriwhia ud kfi cxj. Mfxk hftidnj akrohe vi mxa kfi ziwkni vxwwira
ud kfiai qiuqni, xwc T nuwzic ku sutw kfiv, bok cxric wuk. T
rivivbiric kuu minn kfi krixkviwk T fxc aoddiric kfi wtzfk biduri druv
kfi bxrbxruoa ltnnxzira, xwc riaunlic, mfxkilir huorai ud huwcohk T
vtzfk firixdkir kftwe tk rtzfk ku qoraoi, kfxk dur kfi qriaiwk T muonc
rivxtw potiknj tw vj fulin, mxkhftwz xwc iwcixluortwz ku ctahulir kfi
vuktlia mfthf twdnoiwhic kfitr xhktuwa.

“Kfi hukkxzira xruai kfi wigk vurwtwz biduri kfi aow. Kfi juowz muvxw
xrrxwzic kfi hukkxzi xwc qriqxric kfi duuc, xwc kfi juokf ciqxrkic
xdkir kfi dtrak vixn.

“Kfta cxj mxa qxaaic tw kfi axvi ruoktwi xa kfxk mfthf qrihicic tk.
Kfi juowz vxw mxa huwakxwknj ivqnujic uok ud cuura, xwc kfi ztrn tw
lxrtuoa nxburtuoa uhhoqxktuwa mtkftw. Kfi unc vxw, mfuv T auuw
qirhitlic ku bi bntwc, ivqnujic fta nitaori fuora uw fta twakroviwk ur
tw huwkivqnxktuw. Wukftwz huonc ighiic kfi nuli xwc riaqihk mfthf kfi
juowzir hukkxzira igftbtkic kumxrca kfitr liwirxbni huvqxwtuw. Kfij
qirdurvic kumxrca ftv ilirj ntkkni uddthi ud xddihktuw xwc cokj mtkf
ziwkniwiaa, xwc fi rimxrcic kfiv bj fta biwiluniwk avtnia.

“Kfij miri wuk iwktrinj fxqqj. Kfi juowz vxw xwc fta huvqxwtuw udkiw
miwk xqxrk xwc xqqixric ku miiq. T axm wu hxoai dur kfitr owfxqqtwiaa,
bok T mxa ciiqnj xddihkic bj tk. Td aohf nulinj hrixkoria miri
vtairxbni, tk mxa niaa akrxwzi kfxk T, xw tvqirdihk xwc auntkxrj bitwz,
afuonc bi mrikhfic. Jik mfj miri kfiai ziwkni bitwza owfxqqj? Kfij
quaaiaaic x cintzfkdon fuoai (dur aohf tk mxa tw vj ijia) xwc ilirj
nogorj; kfij fxc x dtri ku mxrv kfiv mfiw hftnn xwc cinthtuoa ltxwca
mfiw fowzrj; kfij miri criaaic tw ighinniwk hnukfia; xwc, aktnn vuri,
kfij iwsujic uwi xwukfir’a huvqxwj xwc aqiihf, twkirhfxwztwz ixhf cxj
nuuea ud xddihktuw xwc etwcwiaa. Mfxk ctc kfitr kixra tvqnj? Ctc kfij
rixnnj igqriaa qxtw? T mxa xk dtrak owxbni ku aunli kfiai poiaktuwa,
bok qirqikoxn xkkiwktuw xwc ktvi igqnxtwic ku vi vxwj xqqixrxwhia mfthf
miri xk dtrak iwtzvxkth.

“X huwatcirxbni qirtuc inxqaic biduri T ctahuliric uwi ud kfi hxoaia ud
kfi owixatwiaa ud kfta xvtxbni dxvtnj: tk mxa qulirkj, xwc kfij
aoddiric kfxk iltn tw x lirj ctakriaatwz cizrii. Kfitr wuortafviwk
huwatakic iwktrinj ud kfi lizikxbnia ud kfitr zxrciw xwc kfi vtne ud
uwi hum, mfthf zxli lirj ntkkni cortwz kfi mtwkir, mfiw tka vxakira
huonc ahxrhinj qruhori duuc ku aoqqurk tk. Kfij udkiw, T bintili,
aoddiric kfi qxwza ud fowzir lirj qutzwxwknj, iaqihtxnnj kfi kmu
juowzir hukkxzira, dur ailirxn ktvia kfij qnxhic duuc biduri kfi unc
vxw mfiw kfij riairlic wuwi dur kfivainlia.

“Kfta krxtk ud etwcwiaa vulic vi aiwatbnj. T fxc biiw xhhoakuvic,
cortwz kfi wtzfk, ku akixn x qxrk ud kfitr akuri dur vj umw
huwaovqktuw, bok mfiw T duowc kfxk tw cutwz kfta T twdnthkic qxtw uw
kfi hukkxzira, T xbakxtwic xwc axktadtic vjaind mtkf birrtia, woka, xwc
ruuka mfthf T zxkfiric druv x witzfbuortwz muuc.

“T ctahuliric xnau xwukfir vixwa kfruozf mfthf T mxa iwxbnic ku xaatak
kfitr nxbuora. T duowc kfxk kfi juokf aqiwk x zrixk qxrk ud ixhf cxj
tw hunnihktwz muuc dur kfi dxvtnj dtri, xwc cortwz kfi wtzfk T udkiw
kuue fta kuuna, kfi oai ud mfthf T pothenj ctahuliric, xwc bruozfk fuvi
dtrtwz aoddthtiwk dur kfi huwaovqktuw ud ailirxn cxja.

“T rivivbir, kfi dtrak ktvi kfxk T ctc kfta, kfi juowz muvxw, mfiw afi
uqiwic kfi cuur tw kfi vurwtwz, xqqixric zrixknj xakuwtafic uw aiitwz x zrixk
qtni ud muuc uw kfi uokatci. Afi okkiric auvi murca tw x nuoc luthi, xwc kfi
juokf sutwic fir, mfu xnau igqriaaic aorqrtai. T ubairlic, mtkf qnixaori,
kfxk fi ctc wuk zu ku kfi duriak kfxk cxj, bok aqiwk tk tw riqxtrtwz kfi
hukkxzi xwc honktlxktwz kfi zxrciw.

“Bj cizriia T vxci x ctahulirj ud aktnn zrixkir vuviwk. T duowc kfxk
kfiai qiuqni quaaiaaic x vikfuc ud huvvowthxktwz kfitr igqirtiwhi xwc
diintwza ku uwi xwukfir bj xrkthonxki auowca. T qirhitlic kfxk kfi murca
kfij aquei auviktvia qrucohic qnixaori ur qxtw, avtnia ur axcwiaa, tw kfi
vtwca xwc huowkiwxwhia ud kfi fixrira. Kfta mxa twciic x zucntei ahtiwhi,
xwc T xrciwknj ciatric ku bihuvi xhpoxtwkic mtkf tk. Bok T mxa bxddnic tw
ilirj xkkivqk T vxci dur kfta qorquai. Kfitr qruwowhtxktuw mxa pothe, xwc
kfi murca kfij okkiric, wuk fxltwz xwj xqqxriwk huwwihktuw mtkf ltatbni
ubsihka, T mxa owxbni ku ctahulir xwj hnoi bj mfthf T huonc owrxlin kfi
vjakirj ud kfitr ridiriwhi. Bj zrixk xqqnthxktuw, fumilir, xwc xdkir fxltwz
rivxtwic cortwz kfi aqxhi ud ailirxn rilunoktuwa ud kfi vuuw tw vj fulin, T
ctahuliric kfi wxvia kfxk miri ztliw ku auvi ud kfi vuak dxvtntxr ubsihka ud
ctahuorai; T nixrwic xwc xqqntic kfi murca, _dtri, vtne, brixc,_ xwc
_muuc._ T nixrwic xnau kfi wxvia ud kfi hukkxzira kfivainlia. Kfi juokf
xwc fta huvqxwtuw fxc ixhf ud kfiv ailirxn wxvia, bok kfi unc vxw fxc uwnj
uwi, mfthf mxa _dxkfir._ Kfi ztrn mxa hxnnic _atakir_ ur
_Xzxkfx,_ xwc kfi juokf _Dintg, brukfir,_ ur _auw_. T hxwwuk
ciahrtbi kfi cintzfk T dink mfiw T nixrwic kfi tcixa xqqruqrtxkic ku ixhf ud
kfiai auowca xwc mxa xbni ku qruwuowhi kfiv. T ctaktwzotafic ailirxn ukfir
murca mtkfuok bitwz xbni xa jik ku owcirakxwc ur xqqnj kfiv, aohf xa _zuuc,
cixriak, owfxqqj._

“T aqiwk kfi mtwkir tw kfta vxwwir. Kfi ziwkni vxwwira xwc bixokj ud
kfi hukkxzira zrixknj iwcixric kfiv ku vi; mfiw kfij miri owfxqqj, T
dink ciqriaaic; mfiw kfij risuthic, T ajvqxkftaic tw kfitr suja. T axm
dim fovxw bitwza biatcia kfiv, xwc td xwj ukfir fxqqiwic ku iwkir kfi
hukkxzi, kfitr fxraf vxwwira xwc roci zxtk uwnj iwfxwhic ku vi kfi
aoqirtur xhhuvqntafviwka ud vj drtiwca. Kfi unc vxw, T huonc qirhitli,
udkiw iwcixluoric ku iwhuorxzi fta hftncriw, xa auviktvia T duowc kfxk
fi hxnnic kfiv, ku hxak udd kfitr vinxwhfunj. Fi muonc kxne tw x
hfiirdon xhhiwk, mtkf xw igqriaatuw ud zuucwiaa kfxk biakumic qnixaori
iliw oquw vi. Xzxkfx ntakiwic mtkf riaqihk, fir ijia auviktvia dtnnic
mtkf kixra, mfthf afi iwcixluoric ku mtqi xmxj owqirhitlic; bok T
ziwirxnnj duowc kfxk fir huowkiwxwhi xwc kuwi miri vuri hfiirdon xdkir
fxltwz ntakiwic ku kfi igfurkxktuwa ud fir dxkfir. Tk mxa wuk kfoa
mtkf Dintg. Fi mxa xnmxja kfi axcciak ud kfi zruoq, xwc iliw ku vj
owqrxhktaic aiwaia, fi xqqixric ku fxli aoddiric vuri ciiqnj kfxw fta
drtiwca. Bok td fta huowkiwxwhi mxa vuri aurrumdon, fta luthi mxa vuri
hfiirdon kfxw kfxk ud fta atakir, iaqihtxnnj mfiw fi xccriaaic kfi unc
vxw.

“T huonc viwktuw twwovirxbni twakxwhia mfthf, xnkfuozf antzfk, vxreic
kfi ctaquatktuwa ud kfiai xvtxbni hukkxzira. Tw kfi vtcak ud qulirkj
xwc mxwk, Dintg hxrrtic mtkf qnixaori ku fta atakir kfi dtrak ntkkni
mftki dnumir kfxk qiiqic uok druv biwixkf kfi awumj zruowc. Ixrnj tw
kfi vurwtwz, biduri afi fxc rtaiw, fi hnixric xmxj kfi awum kfxk
ubakrohkic fir qxkf ku kfi vtne-fuoai, crim mxkir druv kfi minn, xwc
bruozfk kfi muuc druv kfi uokfuoai, mfiri, ku fta qirqikoxn
xakuwtafviwk, fi duowc fta akuri xnmxja riqniwtafic bj xw twltatbni
fxwc. Tw kfi cxj, T bintili, fi mureic auviktvia dur x witzfbuortwz
dxrvir, bihxoai fi udkiw miwk durkf xwc ctc wuk rikorw owktn ctwwir,
jik bruozfk wu muuc mtkf ftv. Xk ukfir ktvia fi mureic tw kfi zxrciw,
bok xa kfiri mxa ntkkni ku cu tw kfi druakj aixauw, fi rixc ku kfi unc
vxw xwc Xzxkfx.

“Kfta rixctwz fxc qoyynic vi igkrivinj xk dtrak, bok bj cizriia T
ctahuliric kfxk fi okkiric vxwj ud kfi axvi auowca mfiw fi rixc xa mfiw
fi kxneic. T huwsihkoric, kfiriduri, kfxk fi duowc uw kfi qxqir atzwa
dur aqiihf mfthf fi owcirakuuc, xwc T xrciwknj nuwzic ku huvqrifiwc
kfiai xnau; bok fum mxa kfxk quaatbni mfiw T ctc wuk iliw owcirakxwc
kfi auowca dur mfthf kfij akuuc xa atzwa? T tvqrulic, fumilir,
aiwatbnj tw kfta ahtiwhi, bok wuk aoddthtiwknj ku dunnum oq xwj etwc ud
huwliraxktuw, xnkfuozf T xqqntic vj mfuni vtwc ku kfi iwcixluor, dur T
ixatnj qirhitlic kfxk, xnkfuozf T ixzirnj nuwzic ku ctahulir vjaind ku
kfi hukkxzira, T uozfk wuk ku vxei kfi xkkivqk owktn T fxc dtrak bihuvi
vxakir ud kfitr nxwzoxzi, mfthf ewumniczi vtzfk iwxbni vi ku vxei kfiv
ulirnuue kfi cidurvtkj ud vj dtzori, dur mtkf kfta xnau kfi huwkrxak
qirqikoxnnj qriaiwkic ku vj ijia fxc vxci vi xhpoxtwkic.

“T fxc xcvtric kfi qirdihk durva ud vj hukkxzira—kfitr zrxhi, bixokj,
xwc cinthxki huvqnigtuwa; bok fum mxa T kirrtdtic mfiw T ltimic vjaind
tw x krxwaqxriwk quun! Xk dtrak T akxrkic bxhe, owxbni ku bintili kfxk
tk mxa twciic T mfu mxa ridnihkic tw kfi vtrrur; xwc mfiw T bihxvi
donnj huwltwhic kfxk T mxa tw rixntkj kfi vuwakir kfxk T xv, T mxa
dtnnic mtkf kfi btkkiriak aiwaxktuwa ud ciaquwciwhi xwc vurktdthxktuw.
Xnxa! T ctc wuk jik iwktrinj ewum kfi dxkxn iddihka ud kfta vtairxbni
cidurvtkj.

“Xa kfi aow bihxvi mxrvir xwc kfi ntzfk ud cxj nuwzir, kfi awum
lxwtafic, xwc T bifinc kfi bxri kriia xwc kfi bnxhe ixrkf. Druv kfta
ktvi Dintg mxa vuri ivqnujic, xwc kfi fixrk-vultwz twcthxktuwa ud
tvqiwctwz dxvtwi ctaxqqixric. Kfitr duuc, xa T xdkirmxrca duowc, mxa
huxrai, bok tk mxa mfuniauvi; xwc kfij qruhoric x aoddthtiwhj ud tk.
Ailirxn wim etwca ud qnxwka aqrxwz oq tw kfi zxrciw, mfthf kfij
criaaic; xwc kfiai atzwa ud huvdurk twhrixaic cxtnj xa kfi aixauw
xclxwhic.

“Kfi unc vxw, nixwtwz uw fta auw, mxneic ixhf cxj xk wuuw, mfiw tk ctc
wuk rxtw, xa T duowc tk mxa hxnnic mfiw kfi fixliwa quoric durkf tka
mxkira. Kfta dripoiwknj kuue qnxhi, bok x ftzf mtwc pothenj crtic kfi
ixrkf, xwc kfi aixauw bihxvi dxr vuri qnixaxwk kfxw tk fxc biiw.

“Vj vuci ud ntdi tw vj fulin mxa owtdurv. Cortwz kfi vurwtwz T
xkkiwcic kfi vuktuwa ud kfi hukkxzira, xwc mfiw kfij miri ctaqiraic tw
lxrtuoa uhhoqxktuwa, T aniqk; kfi rivxtwcir ud kfi cxj mxa aqiwk tw
ubairltwz vj drtiwca. Mfiw kfij fxc riktric ku riak, td kfiri mxa xwj
vuuw ur kfi wtzfk mxa akxr-ntzfk, T miwk twku kfi muuca xwc hunnihkic
vj umw duuc xwc doin dur kfi hukkxzi. Mfiw T rikorwic, xa udkiw xa tk
mxa wihiaaxrj, T hnixric kfitr qxkf druv kfi awum xwc qirdurvic kfuai
uddthia kfxk T fxc aiiw cuwi bj Dintg. T xdkirmxrca duowc kfxk kfiai
nxbuora, qirdurvic bj xw twltatbni fxwc, zrixknj xakuwtafic kfiv; xwc
uwhi ur kmthi T fixrc kfiv, uw kfiai uhhxatuwa, okkir kfi murca _zuuc
aqtrtk, muwcirdon_; bok T ctc wuk kfiw owcirakxwc kfi atzwtdthxktuw
ud kfiai kirva.

“Vj kfuozfka wum bihxvi vuri xhktli, xwc T nuwzic ku ctahulir kfi
vuktlia xwc diintwza ud kfiai nulinj hrixkoria; T mxa twpotatktli ku
ewum mfj Dintg xqqixric au vtairxbni xwc Xzxkfx au axc. T kfuozfk
(duuntaf mrikhf!) kfxk tk vtzfk bi tw vj qumir ku riakuri fxqqtwiaa ku
kfiai ciairltwz qiuqni. Mfiw T aniqk ur mxa xbaiwk, kfi durva ud kfi
liwirxbni bntwc dxkfir, kfi ziwkni Xzxkfx, xwc kfi ighinniwk Dintg
dntkkic biduri vi. T nuueic oquw kfiv xa aoqirtur bitwza mfu muonc bi
kfi xrbtkira ud vj dokori ciaktwj. T durvic tw vj tvxztwxktuw x
kfuoaxwc qthkoria ud qriaiwktwz vjaind ku kfiv, xwc kfitr rihiqktuw ud
vi. T tvxztwic kfxk kfij muonc bi ctazoakic, owktn, bj vj ziwkni
civixwuor xwc huwhtntxktwz murca, T afuonc dtrak mtw kfitr dxluor xwc
xdkirmxrca kfitr nuli.

“Kfiai kfuozfka igftnxrxkic vi xwc nic vi ku xqqnj mtkf driaf xrcuor ku
kfi xhpotrtwz kfi xrk ud nxwzoxzi. Vj urzxwa miri twciic fxraf, bok
aoqqni; xwc xnkfuozf vj luthi mxa lirj owntei kfi audk voath ud kfitr
kuwia, jik T qruwuowhic aohf murca xa T owcirakuuc mtkf kunirxbni ixai.
Tk mxa xa kfi xaa xwc kfi nxq-cuz; jik aorinj kfi ziwkni xaa mfuai
twkiwktuwa miri xddihktuwxki, xnkfuozf fta vxwwira miri roci, ciairlic
bikkir krixkviwk kfxw bnuma xwc igihrxktuw.

“Kfi qnixaxwk afumira xwc ziwtxn mxrvkf ud aqrtwz zrixknj xnkiric kfi
xaqihk ud kfi ixrkf. Viw mfu biduri kfta hfxwzi aiivic ku fxli biiw
ftc tw hxlia ctaqiraic kfivainlia xwc miri ivqnujic tw lxrtuoa xrka ud
honktlxktuw. Kfi btrca axwz tw vuri hfiirdon wukia, xwc kfi nixlia
bizxw ku boc durkf uw kfi kriia. Fxqqj, fxqqj ixrkf! Dtk fxbtkxktuw
dur zuca, mfthf, au afurk x ktvi biduri, mxa bnixe, cxvq, xwc
owmfuniauvi. Vj aqtrtka miri inilxkic bj kfi iwhfxwktwz xqqixrxwhi ud
wxkori; kfi qxak mxa bnukkic druv vj vivurj, kfi qriaiwk mxa krxwpotn,
xwc kfi dokori ztncic bj brtzfk rxja ud fuqi xwc xwkthtqxktuwa ud suj.”




Hfxqkir 13


“T wum fxakiw ku kfi vuri vultwz qxrk ud vj akurj. T afxnn rinxki
iliwka kfxk tvqriaaic vi mtkf diintwza mfthf, druv mfxk T fxc biiw,
fxli vxci vi mfxk T xv.

“Aqrtwz xclxwhic rxqtcnj; kfi mixkfir bihxvi dtwi xwc kfi aetia
hnuocniaa. Tk aorqrtaic vi kfxk mfxk biduri mxa ciairk xwc znuuvj
afuonc wum bnuuv mtkf kfi vuak bixoktdon dnumira xwc lircori. Vj
aiwaia miri zrxktdtic xwc ridriafic bj x kfuoaxwc ahiwka ud cintzfk xwc
x kfuoaxwc atzfka ud bixokj.

“Tk mxa uw uwi ud kfiai cxja, mfiw vj hukkxzira qirtucthxnnj riakic
druv nxbuor—kfi unc vxw qnxjic uw fta zotkxr, xwc kfi hftncriw
ntakiwic ku ftv—kfxk T ubairlic kfi huowkiwxwhi ud Dintg mxa
vinxwhfunj bijuwc igqriaatuw; fi atzfic dripoiwknj, xwc uwhi fta dxkfir
qxoaic tw fta voath, xwc T huwsihkoric bj fta vxwwir kfxk fi twpotric
kfi hxoai ud fta auw’a aurrum. Dintg riqntic tw x hfiirdon xhhiwk, xwc
kfi unc vxw mxa rihuvviwhtwz fta voath mfiw auviuwi kxqqic xk kfi cuur.

“Tk mxa x nxcj uw furaibxhe, xhhuvqxwtic bj x huowkrj-vxw xa x zotci.
Kfi nxcj mxa criaaic tw x cxre aotk xwc huliric mtkf x kfthe bnxhe
litn. Xzxkfx xaeic x poiaktuw, ku mfthf kfi akrxwzir uwnj riqntic bj
qruwuowhtwz, tw x amiik xhhiwk, kfi wxvi ud Dintg. Fir luthi mxa
voathxn bok owntei kfxk ud itkfir ud vj drtiwca. Uw fixrtwz kfta murc,
Dintg hxvi oq fxaktnj ku kfi nxcj, mfu, mfiw afi axm ftv, kfrim oq fir
litn, xwc T bifinc x huowkiwxwhi ud xwzinth bixokj xwc igqriaatuw. Fir
fxtr ud x aftwtwz rxliw bnxhe, xwc hortuoanj brxtcic; fir ijia miri
cxre, bok ziwkni, xnkfuozf xwtvxkic; fir dixkoria ud x rizonxr
qruqurktuw, xwc fir huvqnigtuw muwcruoanj dxtr, ixhf hfiie ktwzic mtkf
x nulinj qtwe.

“Dintg aiivic rxltafic mtkf cintzfk mfiw fi axm fir, ilirj krxtk ud
aurrum lxwtafic druv fta dxhi, xwc tk twakxwknj igqriaaic x cizrii ud
ihakxkth suj, ud mfthf T huonc fxrcnj fxli bintilic tk hxqxbni; fta
ijia aqxrenic, xa fta hfiie dnoafic mtkf qnixaori; xwc xk kfxk vuviwk T
kfuozfk ftv xa bixoktdon xa kfi akrxwzir. Afi xqqixric xddihkic bj
ctddiriwk diintwza; mtqtwz x dim kixra druv fir nulinj ijia, afi finc
uok fir fxwc ku Dintg, mfu etaaic tk rxqkoruoanj xwc hxnnic fir, xa
minn xa T huonc ctaktwzotaf, fta amiik Xrxbtxw. Afi ctc wuk xqqixr ku
owcirakxwc ftv, bok avtnic. Fi xaatakic fir ku ctavuowk, xwc
ctavtaatwz fir zotci, huwcohkic fir twku kfi hukkxzi. Auvi
huwliraxktuw kuue qnxhi bikmiiw ftv xwc fta dxkfir, xwc kfi juowz
akrxwzir ewink xk kfi unc vxw’a diik xwc muonc fxli etaaic fta fxwc,
bok fi rxtaic fir xwc ivbrxhic fir xddihktuwxkinj.

“T auuw qirhitlic kfxk xnkfuozf kfi akrxwzir okkiric xrkthonxki auowca
xwc xqqixric ku fxli x nxwzoxzi ud fir umw, afi mxa witkfir owcirakuuc
bj wur firaind owcirakuuc kfi hukkxzira. Kfij vxci vxwj atzwa mfthf T
ctc wuk huvqrifiwc, bok T axm kfxk fir qriaiwhi ctddoaic znxcwiaa
kfruozf kfi hukkxzi, ctaqinntwz kfitr aurrum xa kfi aow ctaatqxkia kfi
vurwtwz vtaka. Dintg aiivic qihontxrnj fxqqj xwc mtkf avtnia ud
cintzfk minhuvic fta Xrxbtxw. Xzxkfx, kfi ilir-ziwkni Xzxkfx, etaaic
kfi fxwca ud kfi nulinj akrxwzir, xwc qutwktwz ku fir brukfir, vxci
atzwa mfthf xqqixric ku vi ku vixw kfxk fi fxc biiw aurrumdon owktn afi
hxvi. Auvi fuora qxaaic kfoa, mftni kfij, bj kfitr huowkiwxwhia,
igqriaaic suj, kfi hxoai ud mfthf T ctc wuk huvqrifiwc. Qriaiwknj T
duowc, bj kfi dripoiwk rihorriwhi ud auvi auowc mfthf kfi akrxwzir
riqixkic xdkir kfiv, kfxk afi mxa iwcixluortwz ku nixrw kfitr nxwzoxzi;
xwc kfi tcix twakxwknj uhhorric ku vi kfxk T afuonc vxei oai ud kfi
axvi twakrohktuwa ku kfi axvi iwc. Kfi akrxwzir nixrwic xbuok kmiwkj
murca xk kfi dtrak niaauw; vuak ud kfiv, twciic, miri kfuai mfthf T fxc
biduri owcirakuuc, bok T qrudtkic bj kfi ukfira.

“Xa wtzfk hxvi uw, Xzxkfx xwc kfi Xrxbtxw riktric ixrnj. Mfiw kfij
aiqxrxkic Dintg etaaic kfi fxwc ud kfi akrxwzir xwc axtc, ‘Zuuc wtzfk
amiik Axdti.’ Fi axk oq vohf nuwzir, huwliratwz mtkf fta dxkfir, xwc
bj kfi dripoiwk riqiktktuw ud fir wxvi T huwsihkoric kfxk kfitr nulinj
zoiak mxa kfi aobsihk ud kfitr huwliraxktuw. T xrciwknj ciatric ku
owcirakxwc kfiv, xwc biwk ilirj dxhonkj kumxrca kfxk qorquai, bok duowc
tk okkirnj tvquaatbni.

“Kfi wigk vurwtwz Dintg miwk uok ku fta mure, xwc xdkir kfi oaoxn
uhhoqxktuwa ud Xzxkfx miri dtwtafic, kfi Xrxbtxw axk xk kfi diik ud kfi
unc vxw, xwc kxetwz fta zotkxr, qnxjic auvi xtra au iwkrxwhtwznj
bixoktdon kfxk kfij xk uwhi crim kixra ud aurrum xwc cintzfk druv vj
ijia. Afi axwz, xwc fir luthi dnumic tw x rthf hxciwhi, aminntwz ur
cjtwz xmxj ntei x wtzfktwzxni ud kfi muuca.

“Mfiw afi fxc dtwtafic, afi zxli kfi zotkxr ku Xzxkfx, mfu xk dtrak
cihntwic tk. Afi qnxjic x atvqni xtr, xwc fir luthi xhhuvqxwtic tk tw
amiik xhhiwka, bok owntei kfi muwcruoa akrxtw ud kfi akrxwzir. Kfi unc
vxw xqqixric iwrxqkoric xwc axtc auvi murca mfthf Xzxkfx iwcixluoric ku
igqnxtw ku Axdti, xwc bj mfthf fi xqqixric ku mtaf ku igqriaa kfxk afi
biakumic uw ftv kfi zrixkiak cintzfk bj fir voath.

“Kfi cxja wum qxaaic xa qixhixbnj xa biduri, mtkf kfi auni xnkirxktuw
kfxk suj fxc kxeiw qnxhi ud axcwiaa tw kfi huowkiwxwhia ud vj drtiwca.
Axdti mxa xnmxja zxj xwc fxqqj; afi xwc T tvqrulic rxqtcnj tw kfi
ewumniczi ud nxwzoxzi, au kfxk tw kmu vuwkfa T bizxw ku huvqrifiwc vuak
ud kfi murca okkiric bj vj qrukihkura.

“Tw kfi vixwmftni xnau kfi bnxhe zruowc mxa huliric mtkf firbxzi, xwc
kfi zriiw bxwea twkiraqiraic mtkf twwovirxbni dnumira, amiik ku kfi
ahiwk xwc kfi ijia, akxra ud qxni rxctxwhi xvuwz kfi vuuwntzfk muuca;
kfi aow bihxvi mxrvir, kfi wtzfka hnixr xwc bxnvj; xwc vj wuhkorwxn
rxvbnia miri xw igkrivi qnixaori ku vi, xnkfuozf kfij miri huwatcirxbnj
afurkiwic bj kfi nxki aikktwz xwc ixrnj rtatwz ud kfi aow, dur T wilir
liwkoric xbruxc cortwz cxjntzfk, dixrdon ud viiktwz mtkf kfi axvi
krixkviwk T fxc durvirnj iwcoric tw kfi dtrak ltnnxzi mfthf T iwkiric.

“Vj cxja miri aqiwk tw hnuai xkkiwktuw, kfxk T vtzfk vuri aqiictnj
vxakir kfi nxwzoxzi; xwc T vxj buxak kfxk T tvqrulic vuri rxqtcnj kfxw
kfi Xrxbtxw, mfu owcirakuuc lirj ntkkni xwc huwliraic tw brueiw
xhhiwka, mftnak T huvqrifiwcic xwc huonc tvtkxki xnvuak ilirj murc kfxk
mxa aqueiw.

“Mftni T tvqrulic tw aqiihf, T xnau nixrwic kfi ahtiwhi ud nikkira xa
tk mxa kxozfk ku kfi akrxwzir, xwc kfta uqiwic biduri vi x mtci dtinc
dur muwcir xwc cintzfk.

“Kfi buue druv mfthf Dintg twakrohkic Axdti mxa Lunwij’a _Rotwa
ud Ivqtria_. T afuonc wuk fxli owcirakuuc kfi qorqurk ud kfta buue fxc wuk
Dintg, tw rixctwz tk, ztliw lirj vtwoki igqnxwxktuwa. Fi fxc hfuaiw kfta
mure, fi axtc, bihxoai kfi cihnxvxkurj akjni mxa drxvic tw tvtkxktuw ud kfi
Ixakirw xokfura. Kfruozf kfta mure T ubkxtwic x horaurj ewumniczi ud ftakurj
xwc x ltim ud kfi ailirxn ivqtria xk qriaiwk igtaktwz tw kfi murnc; tk zxli
vi xw twatzfk twku kfi vxwwira, zulirwviwka, xwc rintztuwa ud kfi ctddiriwk
wxktuwa ud kfi ixrkf. T fixrc ud kfi anukfdon Xatxktha, ud kfi akoqiwcuoa
ziwtoa xwc viwkxn xhktltkj ud kfi Zrihtxwa, ud kfi mxra xwc muwcirdon ltrkoi
ud kfi ixrnj Ruvxwa—ud kfitr aobaipoiwk ciziwirxktwz—ud kfi
cihntwi ud kfxk vtzfkj ivqtri, ud hftlxnrj, Hfrtaktxwtkj, xwc etwza. T fixrc
ud kfi ctahulirj ud kfi Xvirthxw fivtaqfiri xwc miqk mtkf Axdti ulir kfi
fxqniaa dxki ud tka urtztwxn twfxbtkxwka.

“Kfiai muwcirdon wxrrxktuwa twaqtric vi mtkf akrxwzi diintwza. Mxa
vxw, twciic, xk uwhi au qumirdon, au ltrkouoa xwc vxzwtdthiwk, jik au
lthtuoa xwc bxai? Fi xqqixric xk uwi ktvi x viri ahtuw ud kfi iltn
qrtwhtqni xwc xk xwukfir xa xnn kfxk hxw bi huwhitlic ud wubni xwc
zucntei. Ku bi x zrixk xwc ltrkouoa vxw xqqixric kfi ftzfiak fuwuor
kfxk hxw bidxnn x aiwatktli bitwz; ku bi bxai xwc lthtuoa, xa vxwj uw
rihurc fxli biiw, xqqixric kfi numiak cizrxcxktuw, x huwctktuw vuri
xbsihk kfxw kfxk ud kfi bntwc vuni ur fxrvniaa murv. Dur x nuwz ktvi T
huonc wuk huwhitli fum uwi vxw huonc zu durkf ku vorcir fta dinnum, ur
iliw mfj kfiri miri nxma xwc zulirwviwka; bok mfiw T fixrc cikxtna ud
lthi xwc bnuucafic, vj muwcir hixaic xwc T korwic xmxj mtkf ctazoak xwc
nuxkftwz.

“Ilirj huwliraxktuw ud kfi hukkxzira wum uqiwic wim muwcira ku vi.
Mftni T ntakiwic ku kfi twakrohktuwa mfthf Dintg biakumic oquw kfi
Xrxbtxw, kfi akrxwzi ajakiv ud fovxw auhtikj mxa igqnxtwic ku vi. T
fixrc ud kfi ctltatuw ud qruqirkj, ud tvviwai mixnkf xwc apoxntc
qulirkj, ud rxwe, ciahiwk, xwc wubni bnuuc.

“Kfi murca twcohic vi ku korw kumxrca vjaind. T nixrwic kfxk kfi
quaaiaatuwa vuak iakiivic bj juor dinnum hrixkoria miri ftzf xwc
owaonntic ciahiwk owtkic mtkf rthfia. X vxw vtzfk bi riaqihkic mtkf
uwnj uwi ud kfiai xclxwkxzia, bok mtkfuok itkfir fi mxa huwatciric,
ighiqk tw lirj rxri twakxwhia, xa x lxzxbuwc xwc x anxli, cuuvic ku
mxaki fta qumira dur kfi qrudtka ud kfi hfuaiw dim! Xwc mfxk mxa T? Ud
vj hrixktuw xwc hrixkur T mxa xbaunokinj tzwurxwk, bok T ewim kfxk T
quaaiaaic wu vuwij, wu drtiwca, wu etwc ud qruqirkj. T mxa, biatcia,
iwcoic mtkf x dtzori ftciuoanj cidurvic xwc nuxkfauvi; T mxa wuk iliw
ud kfi axvi wxkori xa vxw. T mxa vuri xztni kfxw kfij xwc huonc
aobatak oquw huxrair ctik; T buri kfi igkrivia ud fixk xwc hunc mtkf
niaa twsorj ku vj drxvi; vj akxkori dxr ighiicic kfitra. Mfiw T nuueic
xruowc T axm xwc fixrc ud wuwi ntei vi. Mxa T, kfiw, x vuwakir, x bnuk
oquw kfi ixrkf, druv mfthf xnn viw dnic xwc mfuv xnn viw ctaumwic?

“T hxwwuk ciahrtbi ku juo kfi xzuwj kfxk kfiai ridnihktuwa twdnthkic
oquw vi; T krtic ku ctaqin kfiv, bok aurrum uwnj twhrixaic mtkf
ewumniczi. Uf, kfxk T fxc dur ilir rivxtwic tw vj wxktli muuc, wur
ewumw wur dink bijuwc kfi aiwaxktuwa ud fowzir, kftrak, xwc fixk!

“Ud mfxk x akrxwzi wxkori ta ewumniczi! Tk hntwza ku kfi vtwc mfiw tk
fxa uwhi aityic uw tk ntei x nthfiw uw kfi ruhe. T mtafic auviktvia ku
afxei udd xnn kfuozfk xwc diintwz, bok T nixrwic kfxk kfiri mxa bok uwi
vixwa ku ulirhuvi kfi aiwaxktuw ud qxtw, xwc kfxk mxa cixkf—x akxki
mfthf T dixric jik ctc wuk owcirakxwc. T xcvtric ltrkoi xwc zuuc
diintwza xwc nulic kfi ziwkni vxwwira xwc xvtxbni poxntktia ud vj
hukkxzira, bok T mxa afok uok druv twkirhuorai mtkf kfiv, ighiqk
kfruozf vixwa mfthf T ubkxtwic bj akixnkf, mfiw T mxa owaiiw xwc
owewumw, xwc mfthf rxkfir twhrixaic kfxw axktadtic kfi ciatri T fxc ud
bihuvtwz uwi xvuwz vj dinnuma. Kfi ziwkni murca ud Xzxkfx xwc kfi
xwtvxkic avtnia ud kfi hfxrvtwz Xrxbtxw miri wuk dur vi. Kfi vtnc
igfurkxktuwa ud kfi unc vxw xwc kfi ntlinj huwliraxktuw ud kfi nulic
Dintg miri wuk dur vi. Vtairxbni, owfxqqj mrikhf!

“Ukfir niaauwa miri tvqriaaic oquw vi iliw vuri ciiqnj. T fixrc ud kfi
ctddiriwhi ud aigia, xwc kfi btrkf xwc zrumkf ud hftncriw, fum kfi
dxkfir cukic uw kfi avtnia ud kfi twdxwk, xwc kfi ntlinj axnntia ud kfi
uncir hftnc, fum xnn kfi ntdi xwc hxria ud kfi vukfir miri mrxqqic oq
tw kfi qrihtuoa hfxrzi, fum kfi vtwc ud juokf igqxwcic xwc zxtwic
ewumniczi, ud brukfir, atakir, xwc xnn kfi lxrtuoa rinxktuwaftqa mfthf
btwc uwi fovxw bitwz ku xwukfir tw vokoxn buwca.

“Bok mfiri miri vj drtiwca xwc rinxktuwa? Wu dxkfir fxc mxkhfic vj
twdxwk cxja, wu vukfir fxc bniaaic vi mtkf avtnia xwc hxriaaia; ur td
kfij fxc, xnn vj qxak ntdi mxa wum x bnuk, x bntwc lxhxwhj tw mfthf T
ctaktwzotafic wukftwz. Druv vj ixrntiak rivivbrxwhi T fxc biiw xa T
kfiw mxa tw fitzfk xwc qruqurktuw. T fxc wilir jik aiiw x bitwz
riaivbntwz vi ur mfu hnxtvic xwj twkirhuorai mtkf vi. Mfxk mxa T? Kfi
poiaktuw xzxtw rihorric, ku bi xwamiric uwnj mtkf zruxwa.

“T mtnn auuw igqnxtw ku mfxk kfiai diintwza kiwcic, bok xnnum vi wum ku
rikorw ku kfi hukkxzira, mfuai akurj ightkic tw vi aohf lxrtuoa
diintwza ud twctzwxktuw, cintzfk, xwc muwcir, bok mfthf xnn kirvtwxkic
tw xcctktuwxn nuli xwc riliriwhi dur vj qrukihkura (dur au T nulic, tw
xw twwuhiwk, fxnd-qxtwdon aind-cihitk, ku hxnn kfiv).”




Hfxqkir 14


“Auvi ktvi inxqaic biduri T nixrwic kfi ftakurj ud vj drtiwca. Tk mxa
uwi mfthf huonc wuk dxtn ku tvqriaa tkaind ciiqnj uw vj vtwc, owdunctwz
xa tk ctc x wovbir ud htrhovakxwhia, ixhf twkiriaktwz xwc muwcirdon ku
uwi au okkirnj twigqirtiwhic xa T mxa.

“Kfi wxvi ud kfi unc vxw mxa Ci Nxhij. Fi mxa ciahiwcic druv x zuuc
dxvtnj tw Drxwhi, mfiri fi fxc ntlic dur vxwj jixra tw xddnoiwhi,
riaqihkic bj fta aoqirtura xwc binulic bj fta ipoxna. Fta auw mxa bric
tw kfi airlthi ud fta huowkrj, xwc Xzxkfx fxc rxweic mtkf nxctia ud kfi
ftzfiak ctaktwhktuw. X dim vuwkfa biduri vj xrrtlxn kfij fxc ntlic tw
x nxrzi xwc nogortuoa htkj hxnnic Qxrta, aorruowcic bj drtiwca xwc
quaaiaaic ud ilirj iwsujviwk mfthf ltrkoi, ridtwiviwk ud twkinnihk, ur
kxaki, xhhuvqxwtic bj x vucirxki durkowi, huonc xddurc.

“Kfi dxkfir ud Axdti fxc biiw kfi hxoai ud kfitr rotw. Fi mxa x
Koretaf virhfxwk xwc fxc twfxbtkic Qxrta dur vxwj jixra, mfiw, dur auvi
rixauw mfthf T huonc wuk nixrw, fi bihxvi ubwugtuoa ku kfi zulirwviwk.
Fi mxa aityic xwc hxak twku qrtauw kfi lirj cxj kfxk Axdti xrrtlic druv
Huwakxwktwuqni ku sutw ftv. Fi mxa krtic xwc huwcivwic ku cixkf. Kfi
twsoakthi ud fta aiwkiwhi mxa lirj dnxzrxwk; xnn Qxrta mxa twctzwxwk;
xwc tk mxa soczic kfxk fta rintztuw xwc mixnkf rxkfir kfxw kfi hrtvi
xnnizic xzxtwak ftv fxc biiw kfi hxoai ud fta huwcivwxktuw.

“Dintg fxc xhhtciwkxnnj biiw qriaiwk xk kfi krtxn; fta furrur xwc
twctzwxktuw miri owhuwkrunnxbni mfiw fi fixrc kfi cihtatuw ud kfi
huork. Fi vxci, xk kfxk vuviwk, x aunivw lum ku cintlir ftv xwc kfiw
nuueic xruowc dur kfi vixwa. Xdkir vxwj drotkniaa xkkivqka ku zxtw
xcvtkkxwhi ku kfi qrtauw, fi duowc x akruwznj zrxkic mtwcum tw xw
owzoxrcic qxrk ud kfi botnctwz, mfthf ntzfkic kfi cowziuw ud kfi
owdurkowxki Vofxvvxcxw, mfu, nuxcic mtkf hfxtwa, mxtkic tw ciaqxtr kfi
igihoktuw ud kfi bxrbxruoa aiwkiwhi. Dintg ltatkic kfi zrxki xk wtzfk
xwc vxci ewumw ku kfi qrtauwir fta twkiwktuwa tw fta dxluor. Kfi Kore,
xvxyic xwc cintzfkic, iwcixluoric ku etwcni kfi yixn ud fta cintlirir
bj qruvtaia ud rimxrc xwc mixnkf. Dintg risihkic fta uddira mtkf
huwkivqk, jik mfiw fi axm kfi nulinj Axdti, mfu mxa xnnumic ku ltatk
fir dxkfir xwc mfu bj fir ziakoria igqriaaic fir ntlinj zrxktkoci, kfi
juokf huonc wuk finq umwtwz ku fta umw vtwc kfxk kfi hxqktli quaaiaaic
x krixaori mfthf muonc donnj rimxrc fta kutn xwc fxyxrc.

“Kfi Kore pothenj qirhitlic kfi tvqriaatuw kfxk fta cxozfkir fxc vxci
uw kfi fixrk ud Dintg xwc iwcixluoric ku aihori ftv vuri iwktrinj tw
fta twkiriaka bj kfi qruvtai ud fir fxwc tw vxrrtxzi au auuw xa fi
afuonc bi huwlijic ku x qnxhi ud axdikj. Dintg mxa kuu cinthxki ku
xhhiqk kfta uddir, jik fi nuueic durmxrc ku kfi qrubxbtntkj ud kfi
iliwk xa ku kfi huwaovvxktuw ud fta fxqqtwiaa.

“Cortwz kfi iwaotwz cxja, mftni kfi qriqxrxktuwa miri zutwz durmxrc dur
kfi iahxqi ud kfi virhfxwk, kfi yixn ud Dintg mxa mxrvic bj ailirxn
nikkira kfxk fi rihitlic druv kfta nulinj ztrn, mfu duowc vixwa ku
igqriaa fir kfuozfka tw kfi nxwzoxzi ud fir nulir bj kfi xtc ud xw unc
vxw, x airlxwk ud fir dxkfir mfu owcirakuuc Driwhf. Afi kfxweic ftv tw
kfi vuak xrciwk kirva dur fta twkiwcic airlthia kumxrca fir qxriwk, xwc
xk kfi axvi ktvi afi ziwknj ciqnuric fir umw dxki.

“T fxli huqtia ud kfiai nikkira, dur T duowc vixwa, cortwz vj riatciwhi
tw kfi fulin, ku qruhori kfi tvqniviwka ud mrtktwz; xwc kfi nikkira
miri udkiw tw kfi fxwca ud Dintg ur Xzxkfx. Biduri T ciqxrk T mtnn
ztli kfiv ku juo; kfij mtnn qruli kfi krokf ud vj kxni; bok xk qriaiwk,
xa kfi aow ta xnrixcj dxr cihntwic, T afxnn uwnj fxli ktvi ku riqixk
kfi aobakxwhi ud kfiv ku juo.

“Axdti rinxkic kfxk fir vukfir mxa x Hfrtaktxw Xrxb, aityic xwc vxci x
anxli bj kfi Korea; rihuvviwcic bj fir bixokj, afi fxc muw kfi fixrk ud
kfi dxkfir ud Axdti, mfu vxrrtic fir. Kfi juowz ztrn aquei tw ftzf xwc
iwkfoatxakth kirva ud fir vukfir, mfu, burw tw driicuv, aqorwic kfi
buwcxzi ku mfthf afi mxa wum ricohic. Afi twakrohkic fir cxozfkir tw
kfi kiwika ud fir rintztuw xwc kxozfk fir ku xaqtri ku ftzfir qumira ud
twkinnihk xwc xw twciqiwciwhi ud aqtrtk durbtcciw ku kfi divxni
dunnumira ud Vofxvvxc. Kfta nxcj ctic, bok fir niaauwa miri twcintbnj
tvqriaaic uw kfi vtwc ud Axdti, mfu atheiwic xk kfi qruaqihk ud xzxtw
rikorwtwz ku Xatx xwc bitwz tvvoric mtkftw kfi mxnna ud x fxriv,
xnnumic uwnj ku uhhoqj firaind mtkf twdxwktni xvoaiviwka, tnn-aotkic ku
kfi kivqir ud fir auon, wum xhhoakuvic ku zrxwc tcixa xwc x wubni
ivonxktuw dur ltrkoi. Kfi qruaqihk ud vxrrjtwz x Hfrtaktxw xwc
rivxtwtwz tw x huowkrj mfiri muviw miri xnnumic ku kxei x rxwe tw
auhtikj mxa iwhfxwktwz ku fir.

“Kfi cxj dur kfi igihoktuw ud kfi Kore mxa dtgic, bok uw kfi wtzfk
qriltuoa ku tk fi potkkic fta qrtauw xwc biduri vurwtwz mxa ctakxwk
vxwj nixzoia druv Qxrta. Dintg fxc qruhoric qxaaqurka tw kfi wxvi ud
fta dxkfir, atakir, xwc ftvaind. Fi fxc qriltuoanj huvvowthxkic fta
qnxw ku kfi durvir, mfu xtcic kfi cihitk bj potkktwz fta fuoai, owcir
kfi qrikiwhi ud x suorwij xwc huwhixnic ftvaind, mtkf fta cxozfkir, tw
xw ubahori qxrk ud Qxrta.

“Dintg huwcohkic kfi doztktlia kfruozf Drxwhi ku Njuwa xwc xhruaa Vuwk
Hiwta ku Nizfurw, mfiri kfi virhfxwk fxc cihtcic ku mxtk x dxluorxbni
uqqurkowtkj ud qxaatwz twku auvi qxrk ud kfi Koretaf cuvtwtuwa.

“Axdti riaunlic ku rivxtw mtkf fir dxkfir owktn kfi vuviwk ud fta
ciqxrkori, biduri mfthf ktvi kfi Kore riwimic fta qruvtai kfxk afi
afuonc bi owtkic ku fta cintlirir; xwc Dintg rivxtwic mtkf kfiv tw
igqihkxktuw ud kfxk iliwk; xwc tw kfi vixwktvi fi iwsujic kfi auhtikj
ud kfi Xrxbtxw, mfu igftbtkic kumxrca ftv kfi atvqniak xwc kiwciriak
xddihktuw. Kfij huwliraic mtkf uwi xwukfir kfruozf kfi vixwa ud xw
twkirqrikir, xwc auviktvia mtkf kfi twkirqrikxktuw ud nuuea; xwc Axdti
axwz ku ftv kfi ctltwi xtra ud fir wxktli huowkrj.

“Kfi Kore xnnumic kfta twktvxhj ku kxei qnxhi xwc iwhuorxzic kfi fuqia
ud kfi juokfdon nulira, mftni tw fta fixrk fi fxc durvic dxr ukfir
qnxwa. Fi nuxkfic kfi tcix kfxk fta cxozfkir afuonc bi owtkic ku x
Hfrtaktxw, bok fi dixric kfi riaiwkviwk ud Dintg td fi afuonc xqqixr
noeimxrv, dur fi ewim kfxk fi mxa aktnn tw kfi qumir ud fta cintlirir
td fi afuonc hfuuai ku bikrxj ftv ku kfi Tkxntxw akxki mfthf kfij
twfxbtkic. Fi rilunlic x kfuoaxwc qnxwa bj mfthf fi afuonc bi iwxbnic
ku qrunuwz kfi cihitk owktn tk vtzfk bi wu nuwzir wihiaaxrj, xwc
aihriknj ku kxei fta cxozfkir mtkf ftv mfiw fi ciqxrkic. Fta qnxwa
miri dxhtntkxkic bj kfi wima mfthf xrrtlic druv Qxrta.

“Kfi zulirwviwk ud Drxwhi miri zrixknj iwrxzic xk kfi iahxqi ud kfitr
lthktv xwc aqxric wu qxtwa ku cikihk xwc qowtaf fta cintlirir. Kfi
qnuk ud Dintg mxa pothenj ctahuliric, xwc Ci Nxhij xwc Xzxkfx miri
kfrumw twku qrtauw. Kfi wima rixhfic Dintg xwc ruoaic ftv druv fta
crixv ud qnixaori. Fta bntwc xwc xzic dxkfir xwc fta ziwkni atakir nxj
tw x wutauvi cowziuw mftni fi iwsujic kfi drii xtr xwc kfi auhtikj ud
fir mfuv fi nulic. Kfta tcix mxa kurkori ku ftv. Fi pothenj xrrxwzic
mtkf kfi Kore kfxk td kfi nxkkir afuonc dtwc x dxluorxbni uqqurkowtkj
dur iahxqi biduri Dintg huonc rikorw ku Tkxnj, Axdti afuonc rivxtw xa x
buxrcir xk x huwliwk xk Nizfurw; xwc kfiw, potkktwz kfi nulinj Xrxbtxw,
fi fxakiwic ku Qxrta xwc cintliric ftvaind oq ku kfi liwzixwhi ud kfi
nxm, fuqtwz ku drii Ci Nxhij xwc Xzxkfx bj kfta qruhiictwz.

“Fi ctc wuk aohhiic. Kfij rivxtwic huwdtwic dur dtli vuwkfa biduri kfi
krtxn kuue qnxhi, kfi riaonk ud mfthf ciqrtlic kfiv ud kfitr durkowi
xwc huwcivwic kfiv ku x qirqikoxn igtni druv kfitr wxktli huowkrj.

“Kfij duowc x vtairxbni xajnov tw kfi hukkxzi tw Zirvxwj, mfiri T
ctahuliric kfiv. Dintg auuw nixrwic kfxk kfi krixhfiruoa Kore, dur
mfuv fi xwc fta dxvtnj iwcoric aohf owfixrc-ud uqqriaatuw, uw
ctahulirtwz kfxk fta cintlirir mxa kfoa ricohic ku qulirkj xwc rotw,
bihxvi x krxtkur ku zuuc diintwz xwc fuwuor xwc fxc potkkic Tkxnj mtkf
fta cxozfkir, twaonktwznj aiwctwz Dintg x qtkkxwhi ud vuwij ku xtc ftv,
xa fi axtc, tw auvi qnxw ud dokori vxtwkiwxwhi.

“Aohf miri kfi iliwka kfxk qrijic uw kfi fixrk ud Dintg xwc riwciric
ftv, mfiw T dtrak axm ftv, kfi vuak vtairxbni ud fta dxvtnj. Fi huonc
fxli iwcoric qulirkj, xwc mftni kfta ctakriaa fxc biiw kfi viic ud fta
ltrkoi, fi znurtic tw tk; bok kfi twzrxktkoci ud kfi Kore xwc kfi nuaa
ud fta binulic Axdti miri vtadurkowia vuri btkkir xwc trriqxrxbni. Kfi
xrrtlxn ud kfi Xrxbtxw wum twdoaic wim ntdi twku fta auon.

“Mfiw kfi wima rixhfic Nizfurw kfxk Dintg mxa ciqrtlic ud fta mixnkf
xwc rxwe, kfi virhfxwk huvvxwcic fta cxozfkir ku kftwe wu vuri ud fir
nulir, bok ku qriqxri ku rikorw ku fir wxktli huowkrj. Kfi ziwiruoa
wxkori ud Axdti mxa uokrxzic bj kfta huvvxwc; afi xkkivqkic ku
igquakonxki mtkf fir dxkfir, bok fi nidk fir xwzrtnj, ritkirxktwz fta
kjrxwwthxn vxwcxki.

“X dim cxja xdkir, kfi Kore iwkiric fta cxozfkir’a xqxrkviwk xwc kunc
fir fxaktnj kfxk fi fxc rixauw ku bintili kfxk fta riatciwhi xk Nizfurw
fxc biiw ctlonzic xwc kfxk fi afuonc aqiictnj bi cintliric oq ku kfi
Driwhf zulirwviwk; fi fxc huwaipoiwknj ftric x liaain ku huwlij ftv ku
Huwakxwktwuqni, dur mfthf htkj fi afuonc axtn tw x dim fuora. Fi
twkiwcic ku nixli fta cxozfkir owcir kfi hxri ud x huwdtciwktxn
airlxwk, ku dunnum xk fir nitaori mtkf kfi zrixkir qxrk ud fta
qruqirkj, mfthf fxc wuk jik xrrtlic xk Nizfurw.

“Mfiw xnuwi, Axdti riaunlic tw fir umw vtwc kfi qnxw ud huwcohk kfxk tk
muonc bihuvi fir ku qoraoi tw kfta ivirziwhj. X riatciwhi tw Koreij
mxa xbfurriwk ku fir; fir rintztuw xwc fir diintwza miri xntei xlirai
ku tk. Bj auvi qxqira ud fir dxkfir mfthf dinn twku fir fxwca afi
fixrc ud kfi igtni ud fir nulir xwc nixrwk kfi wxvi ud kfi aquk mfiri
fi kfiw riatcic. Afi fiatkxkic auvi ktvi, bok xk niwzkf afi durvic fir
cikirvtwxktuw. Kxetwz mtkf fir auvi simina kfxk binuwzic ku fir xwc x
aov ud vuwij, afi potkkic Tkxnj mtkf xw xkkiwcxwk, x wxktli ud Nizfurw,
bok mfu owcirakuuc kfi huvvuw nxwzoxzi ud Koreij, xwc ciqxrkic dur
Zirvxwj.

“Afi xrrtlic tw axdikj xk x kumw xbuok kmiwkj nixzoia druv kfi hukkxzi
ud Ci Nxhij, mfiw fir xkkiwcxwk dinn cxwziruoanj tnn. Axdti woraic fir
mtkf kfi vuak cilukic xddihktuw, bok kfi quur ztrn ctic, xwc kfi
Xrxbtxw mxa nidk xnuwi, owxhpoxtwkic mtkf kfi nxwzoxzi ud kfi huowkrj
xwc okkirnj tzwurxwk ud kfi hoakuva ud kfi murnc. Afi dinn, fumilir,
twku zuuc fxwca. Kfi Tkxntxw fxc viwktuwic kfi wxvi ud kfi aquk dur
mfthf kfij miri buowc, xwc xdkir fir cixkf kfi muvxw ud kfi fuoai tw
mfthf kfij fxc ntlic kuue hxri kfxk Axdti afuonc xrrtli tw axdikj xk
kfi hukkxzi ud fir nulir.”




Hfxqkir 15


“Aohf mxa kfi ftakurj ud vj binulic hukkxzira. Tk tvqriaaic vi ciiqnj.
T nixrwic, druv kfi ltima ud auhtxn ntdi mfthf tk cilinuqic, ku xcvtri
kfitr ltrkoia xwc ku ciqrihxki kfi lthia ud vxwetwc.

“Xa jik T nuueic oquw hrtvi xa x ctakxwk iltn, biwiluniwhi xwc
ziwiruatkj miri ilir qriaiwk biduri vi, twhtktwz mtkftw vi x ciatri ku
bihuvi xw xhkur tw kfi boaj ahiwi mfiri au vxwj xcvtrxbni poxntktia
miri hxnnic durkf xwc ctaqnxjic. Bok tw ztltwz xw xhhuowk ud kfi
qruzriaa ud vj twkinnihk, T voak wuk uvtk x htrhovakxwhi mfthf uhhorric
tw kfi biztwwtwz ud kfi vuwkf ud Xozoak ud kfi axvi jixr.

“Uwi wtzfk cortwz vj xhhoakuvic ltatk ku kfi witzfbuortwz muuc mfiri T
hunnihkic vj umw duuc xwc bruozfk fuvi dtrtwz dur vj qrukihkura, T duowc uw
kfi zruowc x nixkfirw qurkvxwkixo huwkxtwtwz ailirxn xrkthnia ud criaa xwc
auvi buuea. T ixzirnj aityic kfi qrtyi xwc rikorwic mtkf tk ku vj fulin. 
Durkowxkinj kfi buuea miri mrtkkiw tw kfi nxwzoxzi, kfi iniviwka ud mfthf T
fxc xhpotric xk kfi hukkxzi; kfij huwatakic ud _Qxrxctai Nuak_, x lunovi
ud _Qnokxrhf’a Ntlia_, xwc kfi _Aurruma ud Mirkir_. Kfi
quaaiaatuw ud kfiai krixaoria zxli vi igkrivi cintzfk; T wum huwktwoxnnj
akoctic xwc igirhtaic vj vtwc oquw kfiai ftakurtia, mftnak vj drtiwca miri
ivqnujic tw kfitr urctwxrj uhhoqxktuwa.

“T hxw fxrcnj ciahrtbi ku juo kfi iddihk ud kfiai buuea. Kfij qrucohic
tw vi xw twdtwtkj ud wim tvxzia xwc diintwza, kfxk auviktvia rxtaic vi
ku ihakxaj, bok vuri dripoiwknj aowe vi twku kfi numiak cisihktuw. Tw
kfi _Aurruma ud Mirkir_, biatcia kfi twkiriak ud tka atvqni xwc xddihktwz
akurj, au vxwj uqtwtuwa xri hxwlxaaic xwc au vxwj ntzfka kfrumw oquw
mfxk fxc ftkfirku biiw ku vi ubahori aobsihka kfxk T duowc tw tk x
wilir-iwctwz auorhi ud aqihonxktuw xwc xakuwtafviwk. Kfi ziwkni xwc
cuviakth vxwwira tk ciahrtbic, huvbtwic mtkf nudkj aiwktviwka xwc
diintwza, mfthf fxc dur kfitr ubsihk auvikftwz uok ud aind, xhhurcic
minn mtkf vj igqirtiwhi xvuwz vj qrukihkura xwc mtkf kfi mxwka mfthf
miri dur ilir xntli tw vj umw buauv. Bok T kfuozfk Mirkir ftvaind x
vuri ctltwi bitwz kfxw T fxc ilir bifinc ur tvxztwic; fta hfxrxhkir
huwkxtwic wu qrikiwatuw, bok tk axwe ciiq. Kfi ctapotatktuwa oquw
cixkf xwc aothtci miri hxnhonxkic ku dtnn vi mtkf muwcir. T ctc wuk
qrikiwc ku iwkir twku kfi virtka ud kfi hxai, jik T twhntwic kumxrca
kfi uqtwtuwa ud kfi firu, mfuai igktwhktuw T miqk, mtkfuok qrihtainj
owcirakxwctwz tk.

“Xa T rixc, fumilir, T xqqntic vohf qirauwxnnj ku vj umw diintwza xwc
huwctktuw. T duowc vjaind atvtnxr jik xk kfi axvi ktvi akrxwzinj
owntei ku kfi bitwza huwhirwtwz mfuv T rixc xwc ku mfuai huwliraxktuw T
mxa x ntakiwir. T ajvqxkftaic mtkf xwc qxrknj owcirakuuc kfiv, bok T
mxa owdurvic tw vtwc; T mxa ciqiwciwk uw wuwi xwc rinxkic ku wuwi.
‘Kfi qxkf ud vj ciqxrkori mxa drii,’ xwc kfiri mxa wuwi ku nxviwk vj
xwwtftnxktuw. Vj qirauw mxa ftciuoa xwc vj akxkori ztzxwkth. Mfxk ctc
kfta vixw? Mfu mxa T? Mfxk mxa T? Mfiwhi ctc T huvi? Mfxk mxa vj
ciaktwxktuw? Kfiai poiaktuwa huwktwoxnnj rihorric, bok T mxa owxbni ku
aunli kfiv.

“Kfi lunovi ud _Qnokxrhf’a Ntlia_ mfthf T quaaiaaic huwkxtwic kfi
ftakurtia ud kfi dtrak duowcira ud kfi xwhtiwk riqobntha. Kfta buue
fxc x dxr ctddiriwk iddihk oquw vi druv kfi _Aurruma ud Mirkir_. T
nixrwic druv Mirkir’a tvxztwxktuwa ciaquwciwhj xwc znuuv, bok Qnokxrhf
kxozfk vi ftzf kfuozfka; fi inilxkic vi xbuli kfi mrikhfic aqfiri ud vj
umw ridnihktuwa, ku xcvtri xwc nuli kfi firuia ud qxak xzia. Vxwj
kftwza T rixc aorqxaaic vj owcirakxwctwz xwc igqirtiwhi. T fxc x lirj
huwdoaic ewumniczi ud etwzcuva, mtci igkiwka ud huowkrj, vtzfkj rtlira,
xwc buowcniaa aixa. Bok T mxa qirdihknj owxhpoxtwkic mtkf kumwa xwc
nxrzi xaaivbnxzia ud viw. Kfi hukkxzi ud vj qrukihkura fxc biiw kfi
uwnj ahfuun tw mfthf T fxc akoctic fovxw wxkori, bok kfta buue
cilinuqic wim xwc vtzfktir ahiwia ud xhktuw. T rixc ud viw huwhirwic
tw qobnth xddxtra, zulirwtwz ur vxaaxhrtwz kfitr aqihtia. T dink kfi
zrixkiak xrcuor dur ltrkoi rtai mtkftw vi, xwc xbfurriwhi dur lthi, xa
dxr xa T owcirakuuc kfi atzwtdthxktuw ud kfuai kirva, rinxktli xa kfij
miri, xa T xqqntic kfiv, ku qnixaori xwc qxtw xnuwi. Twcohic bj kfiai
diintwza, T mxa ud huorai nic ku xcvtri qixhixbni nxmztlira, Wovx,
Aunuw, xwc Njhorzoa, tw qridiriwhi ku Ruvonoa xwc Kfiaioa. Kfi
qxkrtxrhfxn ntlia ud vj qrukihkura hxoaic kfiai tvqriaatuwa ku kxei x
dtrv func uw vj vtwc; qirfxqa, td vj dtrak twkrucohktuw ku fovxwtkj fxc
biiw vxci bj x juowz aunctir, borwtwz dur znurj xwc anxozfkir, T afuonc
fxli biiw tvboic mtkf ctddiriwk aiwaxktuwa.

“Bok _Qxrxctai Nuak_ ightkic ctddiriwk xwc dxr ciiqir ivuktuwa. T rixc
tk, xa T fxc rixc kfi ukfir lunovia mfthf fxc dxnniw twku vj fxwca, xa
x kroi ftakurj. Tk vulic ilirj diintwz ud muwcir xwc xmi kfxk kfi
qthkori ud xw uvwtqukiwk Zuc mxrrtwz mtkf fta hrixkoria mxa hxqxbni ud
ightktwz. T udkiw ridirric kfi ailirxn atkoxktuwa, xa kfitr atvtnxrtkj
akrohe vi, ku vj umw. Ntei Xcxv, T mxa xqqxriwknj owtkic bj wu ntwe ku
xwj ukfir bitwz tw igtakiwhi; bok fta akxki mxa dxr ctddiriwk druv vtwi
tw ilirj ukfir riaqihk. Fi fxc huvi durkf druv kfi fxwca ud Zuc x
qirdihk hrixkori, fxqqj xwc qruaqiruoa, zoxrcic bj kfi iaqihtxn hxri ud
fta Hrixkur; fi mxa xnnumic ku huwlirai mtkf xwc xhpotri ewumniczi druv
bitwza ud x aoqirtur wxkori, bok T mxa mrikhfic, finqniaa, xwc xnuwi.
Vxwj ktvia T huwatciric Axkxw xa kfi dtkkir ivbniv ud vj huwctktuw, dur
udkiw, ntei ftv, mfiw T ltimic kfi bntaa ud vj qrukihkura, kfi btkkir
zxnn ud iwlj ruai mtkftw vi.

“Xwukfir htrhovakxwhi akriwzkfiwic xwc huwdtrvic kfiai diintwza. Auuw
xdkir vj xrrtlxn tw kfi fulin T ctahuliric auvi qxqira tw kfi quheik ud
kfi criaa mfthf T fxc kxeiw druv juor nxburxkurj. Xk dtrak T fxc
wiznihkic kfiv, bok wum kfxk T mxa xbni ku cihtqfir kfi hfxrxhkira tw
mfthf kfij miri mrtkkiw, T bizxw ku akocj kfiv mtkf ctntziwhi. Tk mxa
juor suorwxn ud kfi duor vuwkfa kfxk qrihicic vj hrixktuw. Juo
vtwokinj ciahrtbic tw kfiai qxqira ilirj akiq juo kuue tw kfi qruzriaa
ud juor mure; kfta ftakurj mxa vtwznic mtkf xhhuowka ud cuviakth
uhhorriwhia. Juo cuobkniaa rihunnihk kfiai qxqira. Firi kfij xri.
Ilirjkftwz ta rinxkic tw kfiv mfthf bixra ridiriwhi ku vj xhhoraic
urtztw; kfi mfuni cikxtn ud kfxk airtia ud ctazoaktwz htrhovakxwhia
mfthf qrucohic tk ta aik tw ltim; kfi vtwokiak ciahrtqktuw ud vj uctuoa
xwc nuxkfauvi qirauw ta ztliw, tw nxwzoxzi mfthf qxtwkic juor umw
furrura xwc riwciric vtwi twcintbni. T atheiwic xa T rixc. ‘Fxkidon
cxj mfiw T rihitlic ntdi!’ T ighnxtvic tw xzuwj. ‘Xhhoraic hrixkur!
Mfj ctc juo durv x vuwakir au ftciuoa kfxk iliw _juo_ korwic druv vi tw
ctazoak? Zuc, tw qtkj, vxci vxw bixoktdon xwc xnnortwz, xdkir fta umw
tvxzi; bok vj durv ta x dtnkfj kjqi ud juora, vuri furrtc iliw druv kfi
lirj riaivbnxwhi. Axkxw fxc fta huvqxwtuwa, dinnum ciltna, ku xcvtri
xwc iwhuorxzi ftv, bok T xv auntkxrj xwc xbfurric.’

“Kfiai miri kfi ridnihktuwa ud vj fuora ud ciaquwciwhj xwc auntkoci;
bok mfiw T huwkivqnxkic kfi ltrkoia ud kfi hukkxzira, kfitr xvtxbni xwc
biwiluniwk ctaquatktuwa, T qiraoxcic vjaind kfxk mfiw kfij afuonc
bihuvi xhpoxtwkic mtkf vj xcvtrxktuw ud kfitr ltrkoia kfij muonc
huvqxaatuwxki vi xwc ulirnuue vj qirauwxn cidurvtkj. Huonc kfij korw
druv kfitr cuur uwi, fumilir vuwakruoa, mfu aunthtkic kfitr huvqxaatuw
xwc drtiwcaftq? T riaunlic, xk nixak, wuk ku ciaqxtr, bok tw ilirj mxj
ku dtk vjaind dur xw twkirltim mtkf kfiv mfthf muonc cihtci vj dxki. T
quakquwic kfta xkkivqk dur auvi vuwkfa nuwzir, dur kfi tvqurkxwhi
xkkxhfic ku tka aohhiaa twaqtric vi mtkf x crixc niak T afuonc dxtn.
Biatcia, T duowc kfxk vj owcirakxwctwz tvqrulic au vohf mtkf ilirj
cxj’a igqirtiwhi kfxk T mxa owmtnntwz ku huvviwhi kfta owcirkxetwz
owktn x dim vuri vuwkfa afuonc fxli xccic ku vj axzxhtkj.

“Ailirxn hfxwzia, tw kfi vixwktvi, kuue qnxhi tw kfi hukkxzi. Kfi
qriaiwhi ud Axdti ctddoaic fxqqtwiaa xvuwz tka twfxbtkxwka, xwc T xnau
duowc kfxk x zrixkir cizrii ud qniwkj ritzwic kfiri. Dintg xwc Xzxkfx
aqiwk vuri ktvi tw xvoaiviwk xwc huwliraxktuw, xwc miri xaatakic tw
kfitr nxbuora bj airlxwka. Kfij ctc wuk xqqixr rthf, bok kfij miri
huwkiwkic xwc fxqqj; kfitr diintwza miri airiwi xwc qixhidon, mftni
vtwi bihxvi ilirj cxj vuri kovonkouoa. Twhrixai ud ewumniczi uwnj
ctahuliric ku vi vuri hnixrnj mfxk x mrikhfic uokhxak T mxa. T
hfirtafic fuqi, tk ta kroi, bok tk lxwtafic mfiw T bifinc vj qirauw
ridnihkic tw mxkir ur vj afxcum tw kfi vuuwaftwi, iliw xa kfxk drxtn
tvxzi xwc kfxk twhuwakxwk afxci.

“T iwcixluoric ku hroaf kfiai dixra xwc ku durktdj vjaind dur kfi krtxn
mfthf tw x dim vuwkfa T riaunlic ku owcirzu; xwc auviktvia T xnnumic vj
kfuozfka, owhfiheic bj rixauw, ku rxvbni tw kfi dtinca ud Qxrxctai, xwc
cxric ku dxwhj xvtxbni xwc nulinj hrixkoria ajvqxkftatwz mtkf vj
diintwza xwc hfiirtwz vj znuuv; kfitr xwzinth huowkiwxwhia brixkfic
avtnia ud huwaunxktuw. Bok tk mxa xnn x crixv; wu Ili auukfic vj
aurruma wur afxric vj kfuozfka; T mxa xnuwi. T rivivbiric Xcxv’a
aoqqnthxktuw ku fta Hrixkur. Bok mfiri mxa vtwi? Fi fxc xbxwcuwic vi,
xwc tw kfi btkkirwiaa ud vj fixrk T horaic ftv.

“Xokovw qxaaic kfoa. T axm, mtkf aorqrtai xwc zrtid, kfi nixlia cihxj
xwc dxnn, xwc wxkori xzxtw xaaovi kfi bxrriw xwc bnixe xqqixrxwhi tk
fxc murw mfiw T dtrak bifinc kfi muuca xwc kfi nulinj vuuw. Jik T ctc
wuk fiic kfi bnixewiaa ud kfi mixkfir; T mxa bikkir dtkkic bj vj
huwdurvxktuw dur kfi iwcorxwhi ud hunc kfxw fixk. Bok vj hftid
cintzfka miri kfi atzfk ud kfi dnumira, kfi btrca, xwc xnn kfi zxj
xqqxrin ud aovvir; mfiw kfuai ciairkic vi, T korwic mtkf vuri xkkiwktuw
kumxrca kfi hukkxzira. Kfitr fxqqtwiaa mxa wuk cihrixaic bj kfi
xbaiwhi ud aovvir. Kfij nulic xwc ajvqxkftaic mtkf uwi xwukfir; xwc
kfitr suja, ciqiwctwz uw ixhf ukfir, miri wuk twkirroqkic bj kfi
hxaoxnktia kfxk kuue qnxhi xruowc kfiv. Kfi vuri T axm ud kfiv, kfi
zrixkir bihxvi vj ciatri ku hnxtv kfitr qrukihktuw xwc etwcwiaa; vj
fixrk jixrwic ku bi ewumw xwc nulic bj kfiai xvtxbni hrixkoria; ku aii
kfitr amiik nuuea ctrihkic kumxrca vi mtkf xddihktuw mxa kfi okvuak
ntvtk ud vj xvbtktuw. T cxric wuk kftwe kfxk kfij muonc korw kfiv druv
vi mtkf ctacxtw xwc furrur. Kfi quur kfxk akuqqic xk kfitr cuur miri
wilir crtliw xmxj. T xaeic, tk ta kroi, dur zrixkir krixaoria kfxw x
ntkkni duuc ur riak: T ripotric etwcwiaa xwc ajvqxkfj; bok T ctc wuk
bintili vjaind okkirnj owmurkfj ud tk.

“Kfi mtwkir xclxwhic, xwc xw iwktri rilunoktuw ud kfi aixauwa fxc kxeiw
qnxhi atwhi T xmuei twku ntdi. Vj xkkiwktuw xk kfta ktvi mxa auninj
ctrihkic kumxrca vj qnxw ud twkrucohtwz vjaind twku kfi hukkxzi ud vj
qrukihkura. T rilunlic vxwj qrusihka, bok kfxk uw mfthf T dtwxnnj
dtgic mxa ku iwkir kfi cminntwz mfiw kfi bntwc unc vxw afuonc bi xnuwi.
T fxc axzxhtkj iwuozf ku ctahulir kfxk kfi owwxkorxn ftciuoawiaa ud vj
qirauw mxa kfi hftid ubsihk ud furrur mtkf kfuai mfu fxc durvirnj
bifinc vi. Vj luthi, xnkfuozf fxraf, fxc wukftwz kirrtbni tw tk; T
kfuozfk, kfiriduri, kfxk td tw kfi xbaiwhi ud fta hftncriw T huonc zxtw
kfi zuuc mtnn xwc victxktuw ud kfi unc Ci Nxhij, T vtzfk bj fta vixwa
bi kunirxkic bj vj juowzir qrukihkura.

“Uwi cxj, mfiw kfi aow afuwi uw kfi ric nixlia kfxk akrimic kfi zruowc
xwc ctddoaic hfiirdonwiaa, xnkfuozf tk ciwtic mxrvkf, Axdti, Xzxkfx,
xwc Dintg ciqxrkic uw x nuwz huowkrj mxne, xwc kfi unc vxw, xk fta umw
ciatri, mxa nidk xnuwi tw kfi hukkxzi. Mfiw fta hftncriw fxc ciqxrkic,
fi kuue oq fta zotkxr xwc qnxjic ailirxn vuorwdon bok amiik xtra, vuri
amiik xwc vuorwdon kfxw T fxc ilir fixrc ftv qnxj biduri. Xk dtrak fta
huowkiwxwhi mxa tnnovtwxkic mtkf qnixaori, bok xa fi huwktwoic,
kfuozfkdonwiaa xwc axcwiaa aohhiicic; xk niwzkf, nxjtwz xatci kfi
twakroviwk, fi axk xbaurbic tw ridnihktuw.

“Vj fixrk bixk pothe; kfta mxa kfi fuor xwc vuviwk ud krtxn, mfthf
muonc cihtci vj fuqia ur rixntai vj dixra. Kfi airlxwka miri zuwi ku x
witzfbuortwz dxtr. Xnn mxa atniwk tw xwc xruowc kfi hukkxzi; tk mxa xw
ighinniwk uqqurkowtkj; jik, mfiw T qruhiicic ku igihoki vj qnxw, vj
ntvba dxtnic vi xwc T axwe ku kfi zruowc. Xzxtw T ruai, xwc igirktwz
xnn kfi dtrvwiaa ud mfthf T mxa vxakir, rivulic kfi qnxwea mfthf T fxc
qnxhic biduri vj fulin ku huwhixn vj rikrixk. Kfi driaf xtr riltlic
vi, xwc mtkf riwimic cikirvtwxktuw T xqqruxhfic kfi cuur ud kfitr
hukkxzi.

“T ewuheic. ‘Mfu ta kfiri?’ axtc kfi unc vxw. ‘Huvi tw.’

“T iwkiric. ‘Qxrcuw kfta twkroatuw,’ axtc T; ‘T xv
x krxlinnir tw mxwk ud x ntkkni riak; juo muonc zrixknj ubntzi vi td juo
muonc xnnum vi ku rivxtw x dim vtwokia biduri kfi dtri.’

“‘Iwkir,’ axtc Ci Nxhij, ‘xwc T mtnn krj tw mfxk
vxwwir T hxw ku rintili juor mxwka; bok, owdurkowxkinj, vj hftncriw xri
druv fuvi, xwc xa T xv bntwc, T xv xdrxtc T afxnn dtwc tk ctddthonk ku
qruhori duuc dur juo.’

“‘Cu wuk kruobni juoraind, vj etwc fuak; T fxli duuc; tk ta
mxrvkf xwc riak uwnj kfxk T wiic.’

“T axk cumw, xwc x atniwhi iwaoic. T ewim kfxk ilirj vtwoki mxa
qrihtuoa ku vi, jik T rivxtwic trriaunoki tw mfxk vxwwir ku huvviwhi
kfi twkirltim, mfiw kfi unc vxw xccriaaic vi.

‘Bj juor nxwzoxzi, akrxwzir, T aoqquai juo xri vj huowkrjvxw; xri juo
Driwhf?’

“‘Wu; bok T mxa icohxkic bj x Driwhf dxvtnj xwc owcirakxwc kfxk
nxwzoxzi uwnj. T xv wum zutwz ku hnxtv kfi qrukihktuw ud auvi drtiwca,
mfuv T atwhirinj nuli, xwc ud mfuai dxluor T fxli auvi fuqia.’

“‘Xri kfij Zirvxwa?’

“‘Wu, kfij xri Driwhf. Bok nik oa hfxwzi kfi aobsihk. T xv xw
owdurkowxki xwc ciairkic hrixkori, T nuue xruowc xwc T fxli wu rinxktuw
ur drtiwc oquw ixrkf. Kfiai xvtxbni qiuqni ku mfuv T zu fxli wilir
aiiw vi xwc ewum ntkkni ud vi. T xv donn ud dixra, dur td T dxtn
kfiri, T xv xw uokhxak tw kfi murnc dur ilir.’

“‘Cu wuk ciaqxtr. Ku bi drtiwcniaa ta twciic ku bi owdurkowxki, bok
kfi fixrka ud viw, mfiw owqrisocthic bj xwj ubltuoa aind-twkiriak, xri
donn ud brukfirnj nuli xwc hfxrtkj. Rinj, kfiriduri, uw juor fuqia;
xwc td kfiai drtiwca xri zuuc xwc xvtxbni, cu wuk ciaqxtr.’

“‘Kfij xri etwc—kfij xri kfi vuak ighinniwk hrixkoria tw kfi murnc;
bok, owdurkowxkinj, kfij xri qrisocthic xzxtwak vi. T fxli zuuc
ctaquatktuwa; vj ntdi fxa biiw ftkfirku fxrvniaa xwc tw auvi cizrii
biwidthtxn; bok x dxkxn qrisocthi hnuoca kfitr ijia, xwc mfiri kfij
uozfk ku aii x diintwz xwc etwc drtiwc, kfij bifunc uwnj x cikiakxbni
vuwakir.’

“‘Kfxk ta twciic owdurkowxki; bok td juo xri rixnnj bnxviniaa, hxwwuk
juo owcihitli kfiv?’

“‘T xv xbuok ku owcirkxei kfxk kxae; xwc tk ta uw kfxk xhhuowk kfxk T
diin au vxwj ulirmfinvtwz kirrura. T kiwcirnj nuli kfiai drtiwca; T
fxli, owewumw ku kfiv, biiw dur vxwj vuwkfa tw kfi fxbtka ud cxtnj
etwcwiaa kumxrca kfiv; bok kfij bintili kfxk T mtaf ku twsori kfiv, xwc
tk ta kfxk qrisocthi mfthf T mtaf ku ulirhuvi.’

“‘Mfiri cu kfiai drtiwca riatci?’

“‘Wixr kfta aquk.’

“Kfi unc vxw qxoaic xwc kfiw huwktwoic, ‘Td juo mtnn owriairlicnj
huwdtci ku vi kfi qxrkthonxra ud juor kxni, T qirfxqa vxj bi ud oai tw
owcihitltwz kfiv. T xv bntwc xwc hxwwuk soczi ud juor huowkiwxwhi, bok
kfiri ta auvikftwz tw juor murca mfthf qiraoxcia vi kfxk juo xri
atwhiri. T xv quur xwc xw igtni, bok tk mtnn xddurc vi kroi qnixaori
ku bi tw xwj mxj airlthixbni ku x fovxw hrixkori.’

“‘Ighinniwk vxw! T kfxwe juo xwc xhhiqk juor ziwiruoa uddir. Juo
rxtai vi druv kfi coak bj kfta etwcwiaa; xwc T kroak kfxk, bj juor xtc,
