T afxnn wuk bi crtliw druv kfi auhtikj xwc ajvqxkfj ud juor dinnum
hrixkoria.’

“‘Fixliw durbtc! Iliw td juo miri rixnnj hrtvtwxn, dur kfxk hxw uwnj
crtli juo ku ciaqirxktuw, xwc wuk twaktzxki juo ku ltrkoi. T xnau xv
owdurkowxki; T xwc vj dxvtnj fxli biiw huwcivwic, xnkfuozf twwuhiwk;
soczi, kfiriduri, td T cu wuk diin dur juor vtadurkowia.’

“‘Fum hxw T kfxwe juo, vj biak xwc uwnj biwidxhkur? Druv juor ntqa
dtrak fxli T fixrc kfi luthi ud etwcwiaa ctrihkic kumxrca vi; T afxnn
bi dur ilir zrxkidon; xwc juor qriaiwk fovxwtkj xaaoria vi ud aohhiaa
mtkf kfuai drtiwca mfuv T xv uw kfi qutwk ud viiktwz.’

“‘Vxj T ewum kfi wxvia xwc riatciwhi ud kfuai drtiwca?’

“T qxoaic. Kfta, T kfuozfk, mxa kfi vuviwk ud cihtatuw, mfthf mxa ku
rub vi ud ur biakum fxqqtwiaa uw vi dur ilir. T akrozznic lxtwnj dur
dtrvwiaa aoddthtiwk ku xwamir ftv, bok kfi iddurk ciakrujic xnn vj
rivxtwtwz akriwzkf; T axwe uw kfi hfxtr xwc aubbic xnuoc. Xk kfxk
vuviwk T fixrc kfi akiqa ud vj juowzir qrukihkura. T fxc wuk x vuviwk
ku nuai, bok aitytwz kfi fxwc ud kfi unc vxw, T hrtic, ‘Wum ta kfi
ktvi! Axli xwc qrukihk vi! Juo xwc juor dxvtnj xri kfi drtiwca mfuv T
aiie. Cu wuk juo ciairk vi tw kfi fuor ud krtxn!’

“‘Zrixk Zuc!’ ighnxtvic kfi unc vxw. ‘Mfu xri juo?’

“Xk kfxk twakxwk kfi hukkxzi cuur mxa uqiwic, xwc Dintg, Axdti, xwc
Xzxkfx iwkiric. Mfu hxw ciahrtbi kfitr furrur xwc huwakirwxktuw uw
bifunctwz vi? Xzxkfx dxtwkic, xwc Axdti, owxbni ku xkkiwc ku fir
drtiwc, roafic uok ud kfi hukkxzi. Dintg cxrkic durmxrc, xwc mtkf
aoqirwxkorxn durhi kuri vi druv fta dxkfir, ku mfuai ewiia T hnowz, tw
x krxwaqurk ud dorj, fi cxafic vi ku kfi zruowc xwc akrohe vi ltuniwknj
mtkf x akthe. T huonc fxli kurw ftv ntvb druv ntvb, xa kfi ntuw riwca
kfi xwkinuqi. Bok vj fixrk axwe mtkftw vi xa mtkf btkkir athewiaa, xwc
T ridrxtwic. T axm ftv uw kfi qutwk ud riqixktwz fta bnum, mfiw,
ulirhuvi bj qxtw xwc xwzotaf, T potkkic kfi hukkxzi, xwc tw kfi ziwirxn
kovonk iahxqic owqirhitlic ku vj fulin.”




Hfxqkir 16


“Horaic, horaic hrixkur! Mfj ctc T ntli? Mfj, tw kfxk twakxwk, ctc T
wuk igktwzotaf kfi aqxre ud igtakiwhi mfthf juo fxc au mxwkuwnj
biakumic? T ewum wuk; ciaqxtr fxc wuk jik kxeiw quaaiaatuw ud vi; vj
diintwza miri kfuai ud rxzi xwc riliwzi. T huonc mtkf qnixaori fxli
ciakrujic kfi hukkxzi xwc tka twfxbtkxwka xwc fxli znokkic vjaind mtkf
kfitr afrtiea xwc vtairj.

“Mfiw wtzfk hxvi T potkkic vj rikrixk xwc mxwciric tw kfi muuc; xwc
wum, wu nuwzir riakrxtwic bj kfi dixr ud ctahulirj, T zxli liwk ku vj
xwzotaf tw dixrdon fumntwza. T mxa ntei x mtnc bixak kfxk fxc brueiw
kfi kutna, ciakrujtwz kfi ubsihka kfxk ubakrohkic vi xwc rxwztwz
kfruozf kfi muuc mtkf x akxz-ntei amtdkwiaa. Uf! Mfxk x vtairxbni
wtzfk T qxaaic! Kfi hunc akxra afuwi tw vuheirj, xwc kfi bxri kriia
mxlic kfitr brxwhfia xbuli vi; wum xwc kfiw kfi amiik luthi ud x btrc
borak durkf xvtcak kfi owtliraxn aktnnwiaa. Xnn, axli T, miri xk riak
ur tw iwsujviwk; T, ntei kfi xrhf-dtiwc, buri x finn mtkftw vi, xwc
dtwctwz vjaind owajvqxkftaic mtkf, mtafic ku kixr oq kfi kriia, aqrixc
fxluh xwc ciakrohktuw xruowc vi, xwc kfiw ku fxli axk cumw xwc iwsujic
kfi rotw.

“Bok kfta mxa x nogorj ud aiwaxktuw kfxk huonc wuk iwcori; T bihxvi
dxktzoic mtkf ighiaa ud buctnj igirktuw xwc axwe uw kfi cxvq zrxaa tw
kfi athe tvqukiwhi ud ciaqxtr. Kfiri mxa wuwi xvuwz kfi vjrtxca ud viw
kfxk igtakic mfu muonc qtkj ur xaatak vi; xwc afuonc T diin etwcwiaa
kumxrca vj iwivtia? Wu; druv kfxk vuviwk T cihnxric ilirnxaktwz mxr
xzxtwak kfi aqihtia, xwc vuri kfxw xnn, xzxtwak ftv mfu fxc durvic vi
xwc aiwk vi durkf ku kfta twaoqqurkxbni vtairj.

“Kfi aow ruai; T fixrc kfi luthia ud viw xwc ewim kfxk tk mxa
tvquaatbni ku rikorw ku vj rikrixk cortwz kfxk cxj. Xhhurctwznj T ftc
vjaind tw auvi kfthe owcirmuuc, cikirvtwtwz ku ciluki kfi iwaotwz fuora
ku ridnihktuw uw vj atkoxktuw.

“Kfi qnixaxwk aowaftwi xwc kfi qori xtr ud cxj riakuric vi ku auvi
cizrii ud krxwpotnntkj; xwc mfiw T huwatciric mfxk fxc qxaaic xk kfi
hukkxzi, T huonc wuk finq bintiltwz kfxk T fxc biiw kuu fxakj tw vj
huwhnoatuwa. T fxc hirkxtwnj xhkic tvqrociwknj. Tk mxa xqqxriwk kfxk
vj huwliraxktuw fxc twkiriakic kfi dxkfir tw vj bifxnd, xwc T mxa x
duun tw fxltwz igquaic vj qirauw ku kfi furrur ud fta hftncriw. T
uozfk ku fxli dxvtntxrtaic kfi unc Ci Nxhij ku vi, xwc bj cizriia ku
fxli ctahuliric vjaind ku kfi riak ud fta dxvtnj, mfiw kfij afuonc fxli
biiw qriqxric dur vj xqqruxhf. Bok T ctc wuk bintili vj irrura ku bi
trrikrtilxbni, xwc xdkir vohf huwatcirxktuw T riaunlic ku rikorw ku kfi
hukkxzi, aiie kfi unc vxw, xwc bj vj riqriaiwkxktuwa mtw ftv ku vj
qxrkj.

“Kfiai kfuozfka hxnvic vi, xwc tw kfi xdkirwuuw T axwe twku x qruduowc
aniiq; bok kfi dilir ud vj bnuuc ctc wuk xnnum vi ku bi ltatkic bj
qixhidon crixva. Kfi furrtbni ahiwi ud kfi qrihictwz cxj mxa dur ilir
xhktwz biduri vj ijia; kfi divxnia miri dnjtwz xwc kfi iwrxzic Dintg
kixrtwz vi druv fta dxkfir’a diik. T xmuei igfxoakic, xwc dtwctwz kfxk
tk mxa xnrixcj wtzfk, T hriqk durkf druv vj ftctwz-qnxhi, xwc miwk tw
aixrhf ud duuc.

“Mfiw vj fowzir mxa xqqixaic, T ctrihkic vj akiqa kumxrca kfi
minn-ewumw qxkf kfxk huwcohkic ku kfi hukkxzi. Xnn kfiri mxa xk qixhi.
T hriqk twku vj fulin xwc rivxtwic tw atniwk igqihkxktuw ud kfi
xhhoakuvic fuor mfiw kfi dxvtnj xruai. Kfxk fuor qxaaic, kfi aow
vuowkic ftzf tw kfi fixliwa, bok kfi hukkxzira ctc wuk xqqixr. T
krivbnic ltuniwknj, xqqrifiwctwz auvi crixcdon vtadurkowi. Kfi twatci
ud kfi hukkxzi mxa cxre, xwc T fixrc wu vuktuw; T hxwwuk ciahrtbi kfi
xzuwj ud kfta aoaqiwai.

“Qriaiwknj kmu huowkrjviw qxaaic bj, bok qxoatwz wixr kfi hukkxzi, kfij
iwkiric twku huwliraxktuw, oatwz ltuniwk ziakthonxktuwa; bok T ctc wuk
owcirakxwc mfxk kfij axtc, xa kfij aquei kfi nxwzoxzi ud kfi huowkrj,
mfthf ctddiric druv kfxk ud vj qrukihkura. Auuw xdkir, fumilir, Dintg
xqqruxhfic mtkf xwukfir vxw; T mxa aorqrtaic, xa T ewim kfxk fi fxc wuk
potkkic kfi hukkxzi kfxk vurwtwz, xwc mxtkic xwgtuoanj ku ctahulir druv
fta ctahuorai kfi vixwtwz ud kfiai owoaoxn xqqixrxwhia.

“‘Cu juo huwatcir,’ axtc fta huvqxwtuw ku ftv,
‘kfxk juo mtnn bi ubntzic ku qxj kfrii vuwkfa’ riwk xwc ku nuai
kfi qrucohi ud juor zxrciw? T cu wuk mtaf ku kxei xwj owdxtr xclxwkxzi, xwc
T biz kfiriduri kfxk juo mtnn kxei auvi cxja ku huwatcir ud juor
cikirvtwxktuw.’

“‘Tk ta okkirnj oainiaa,’ riqntic Dintg; ‘mi hxw
wilir xzxtw twfxbtk juor hukkxzi. Kfi ntdi ud vj dxkfir ta tw kfi zrixkiak
cxwzir, umtwz ku kfi crixcdon htrhovakxwhi kfxk T fxli rinxkic. Vj mtdi xwc
vj atakir mtnn wilir rihulir druv kfitr furrur. T iwkrixk juo wuk ku rixauw
mtkf vi xwj vuri. Kxei quaaiaatuw ud juor kiwiviwk xwc nik vi dnj druv kfta
qnxhi.’

“Dintg krivbnic ltuniwknj xa fi axtc kfta. Fi xwc fta huvqxwtuw
iwkiric kfi hukkxzi, tw mfthf kfij rivxtwic dur x dim vtwokia, xwc kfiw
ciqxrkic. T wilir axm xwj ud kfi dxvtnj ud Ci Nxhij vuri.

“T huwktwoic dur kfi rivxtwcir ud kfi cxj tw vj fulin tw x akxki ud
okkir xwc akoqtc ciaqxtr. Vj qrukihkura fxc ciqxrkic xwc fxc brueiw
kfi uwnj ntwe kfxk finc vi ku kfi murnc. Dur kfi dtrak ktvi kfi
diintwza ud riliwzi xwc fxkric dtnnic vj buauv, xwc T ctc wuk akrtli ku
huwkrun kfiv, bok xnnumtwz vjaind ku bi burwi xmxj bj kfi akrixv, T
biwk vj vtwc kumxrca twsorj xwc cixkf. Mfiw T kfuozfk ud vj drtiwca,
ud kfi vtnc luthi ud Ci Nxhij, kfi ziwkni ijia ud Xzxkfx, xwc kfi
igpotatki bixokj ud kfi Xrxbtxw, kfiai kfuozfka lxwtafic xwc x zoaf ud
kixra auvimfxk auukfic vi. Bok xzxtw mfiw T ridnihkic kfxk kfij fxc
aqorwic xwc ciairkic vi, xwzir rikorwic, x rxzi ud xwzir, xwc owxbni ku
twsori xwjkftwz fovxw, T korwic vj dorj kumxrca twxwtvxki ubsihka. Xa
wtzfk xclxwhic, T qnxhic x lxrtikj ud huvboaktbnia xruowc kfi hukkxzi,
xwc xdkir fxltwz ciakrujic ilirj liaktzi ud honktlxktuw tw kfi zxrciw,
T mxtkic mtkf durhic tvqxktiwhi owktn kfi vuuw fxc aowe ku huvviwhi vj
uqirxktuwa.

“Xa kfi wtzfk xclxwhic, x dtirhi mtwc xruai druv kfi muuca xwc pothenj
ctaqiraic kfi hnuoca kfxk fxc nutkiric tw kfi fixliwa; kfi bnxak kuri
xnuwz ntei x vtzfkj xlxnxwhfi xwc qrucohic x etwc ud twaxwtkj tw vj
aqtrtka kfxk borak xnn buowca ud rixauw xwc ridnihktuw. T ntzfkic kfi
crj brxwhf ud x krii xwc cxwhic mtkf dorj xruowc kfi cilukic hukkxzi,
vj ijia aktnn dtgic uw kfi miakirw furtyuw, kfi iczi ud mfthf kfi vuuw
wixrnj kuohfic. X qxrk ud tka urb mxa xk niwzkf ftc, xwc T mxlic vj
brxwc; tk axwe, xwc mtkf x nuoc ahrixv T dtric kfi akrxm, xwc fixkf,
xwc boafia, mfthf T fxc hunnihkic. Kfi mtwc dxwwic kfi dtri, xwc kfi
hukkxzi mxa pothenj iwlinuqic bj kfi dnxvia, mfthf hnowz ku tk xwc
ntheic tk mtkf kfitr dureic xwc ciakrujtwz kuwzoia.

“Xa auuw xa T mxa huwltwhic kfxk wu xaatakxwhi huonc axli xwj qxrk ud
kfi fxbtkxktuw, T potkkic kfi ahiwi xwc auozfk dur ridozi tw kfi muuca.

“Xwc wum, mtkf kfi murnc biduri vi, mftkfir afuonc T biwc vj akiqa? T
riaunlic ku dnj dxr druv kfi ahiwi ud vj vtadurkowia; bok ku vi, fxkic
xwc ciaqtaic, ilirj huowkrj voak bi ipoxnnj furrtbni. Xk niwzkf kfi
kfuozfk ud juo hruaaic vj vtwc. T nixrwic druv juor qxqira kfxk juo
miri vj dxkfir, vj hrixkur; xwc ku mfuv huonc T xqqnj mtkf vuri dtkwiaa
kfxw ku ftv mfu fxc ztliw vi ntdi? Xvuwz kfi niaauwa kfxk Dintg fxc
biakumic oquw Axdti, ziuzrxqfj fxc wuk biiw uvtkkic; T fxc nixrwic druv
kfiai kfi rinxktli atkoxktuwa ud kfi ctddiriwk huowkrtia ud kfi ixrkf.
Juo fxc viwktuwic Ziwilx xa kfi wxvi ud juor wxktli kumw, xwc kumxrca
kfta qnxhi T riaunlic ku qruhiic.

“Bok fum mxa T ku ctrihk vjaind? T ewim kfxk T voak krxlin tw x
auokfmiakirnj ctrihktuw ku rixhf vj ciaktwxktuw, bok kfi aow mxa vj
uwnj zotci. T ctc wuk ewum kfi wxvia ud kfi kumwa kfxk T mxa ku qxaa
kfruozf, wur huonc T xae twdurvxktuw druv x atwzni fovxw bitwz; bok T
ctc wuk ciaqxtr. Druv juo uwnj huonc T fuqi dur aohhuor, xnkfuozf
kumxrca juo T dink wu aiwktviwk bok kfxk ud fxkric. Owdiintwz,
fixrkniaa hrixkur! Juo fxc iwcumic vi mtkf qirhiqktuwa xwc qxaatuwa
xwc kfiw hxak vi xbruxc xw ubsihk dur kfi ahurw xwc furrur ud vxwetwc.
Bok uw juo uwnj fxc T xwj hnxtv dur qtkj xwc ricriaa, xwc druv juo T
cikirvtwic ku aiie kfxk soakthi mfthf T lxtwnj xkkivqkic ku zxtw druv
xwj ukfir bitwz kfxk muri kfi fovxw durv.

“Vj krxlina miri nuwz xwc kfi aoddirtwza T iwcoric twkiwai. Tk mxa
nxki tw xokovw mfiw T potkkic kfi ctakrthk mfiri T fxc au nuwz riatcic.
T krxlinnic uwnj xk wtzfk, dixrdon ud iwhuowkirtwz kfi ltaxzi ud x
fovxw bitwz. Wxkori cihxjic xruowc vi, xwc kfi aow bihxvi fixkniaa;
rxtw xwc awum quoric xruowc vi; vtzfkj rtlira miri druyiw; kfi aordxhi
ud kfi ixrkf mxa fxrc xwc hftnn, xwc bxri, xwc T duowc wu afinkir. Uf,
ixrkf! Fum udkiw ctc T tvqrihxki horaia uw kfi hxoai ud vj bitwz! Kfi
vtncwiaa ud vj wxkori fxc dnic, xwc xnn mtkftw vi mxa korwic ku zxnn
xwc btkkirwiaa. Kfi wixrir T xqqruxhfic ku juor fxbtkxktuw, kfi vuri
ciiqnj ctc T diin kfi aqtrtk ud riliwzi iwetwcnic tw vj fixrk. Awum
dinn, xwc kfi mxkira miri fxrciwic, bok T riakic wuk. X dim twhtciwka
wum xwc kfiw ctrihkic vi, xwc T quaaiaaic x vxq ud kfi huowkrj; bok T
udkiw mxwciric mtci druv vj qxkf. Kfi xzuwj ud vj diintwza xnnumic vi
wu riaqtki; wu twhtciwk uhhorric druv mfthf vj rxzi xwc vtairj huonc
wuk igkrxhk tka duuc; bok x htrhovakxwhi kfxk fxqqiwic mfiw T xrrtlic
uw kfi huwdtwia ud Amtkyirnxwc, mfiw kfi aow fxc rihuliric tka mxrvkf
xwc kfi ixrkf xzxtw bizxw ku nuue zriiw, huwdtrvic tw xw iaqihtxn
vxwwir kfi btkkirwiaa xwc furrur ud vj diintwza.

“T ziwirxnnj riakic cortwz kfi cxj xwc krxlinnic uwnj mfiw T mxa
aihoric bj wtzfk druv kfi ltim ud vxw. Uwi vurwtwz, fumilir, dtwctwz
kfxk vj qxkf nxj kfruozf x ciiq muuc, T liwkoric ku huwktwoi vj suorwij
xdkir kfi aow fxc rtaiw; kfi cxj, mfthf mxa uwi ud kfi dtrak ud aqrtwz,
hfiiric iliw vi bj kfi nulintwiaa ud tka aowaftwi xwc kfi bxnvtwiaa ud
kfi xtr. T dink ivuktuwa ud ziwkniwiaa xwc qnixaori, kfxk fxc nuwz
xqqixric cixc, riltli mtkftw vi. Fxnd aorqrtaic bj kfi wulinkj ud
kfiai aiwaxktuwa, T xnnumic vjaind ku bi burwi xmxj bj kfiv, xwc
durzikktwz vj auntkoci xwc cidurvtkj, cxric ku bi fxqqj. Audk kixra
xzxtw bicimic vj hfiiea, xwc T iliw rxtaic vj fovtc ijia mtkf
kfxwedonwiaa kumxrca kfi bniaaic aow, mfthf biakumic aohf suj oquw vi.

“T huwktwoic ku mtwc xvuwz kfi qxkfa ud kfi muuc, owktn T hxvi ku tka
buowcxrj, mfthf mxa aetrkic bj x ciiq xwc rxqtc rtlir, twku mfthf vxwj
ud kfi kriia biwk kfitr brxwhfia, wum bocctwz mtkf kfi driaf aqrtwz.
Firi T qxoaic, wuk igxhknj ewumtwz mfxk qxkf ku qoraoi, mfiw T fixrc
kfi auowc ud luthia, kfxk twcohic vi ku huwhixn vjaind owcir kfi afxci
ud x hjqriaa. T mxa ahxrhinj ftc mfiw x juowz ztrn hxvi rowwtwz
kumxrca kfi aquk mfiri T mxa huwhixnic, nxozftwz, xa td afi rxw druv
auviuwi tw aqurk. Afi huwktwoic fir huorai xnuwz kfi qrihtqtkuoa atcia
ud kfi rtlir, mfiw aocciwnj fir duuk antqqic, xwc afi dinn twku kfi
rxqtc akrixv. T roafic druv vj ftctwz-qnxhi xwc mtkf igkrivi nxbuor,
druv kfi durhi ud kfi horriwk, axlic fir xwc crxzzic fir ku afuri. Afi
mxa aiwainiaa, xwc T iwcixluoric bj ilirj vixwa tw vj qumir ku riakuri
xwtvxktuw, mfiw T mxa aocciwnj twkirroqkic bj kfi xqqruxhf ud x roakth,
mfu mxa qrubxbnj kfi qirauw druv mfuv afi fxc qnxjdonnj dnic. Uw
aiitwz vi, fi cxrkic kumxrca vi, xwc kixrtwz kfi ztrn druv vj xrva,
fxakiwic kumxrca kfi ciiqir qxrka ud kfi muuc. T dunnumic aqiictnj, T
fxrcnj ewim mfj; bok mfiw kfi vxw axm vi crxm wixr, fi xtvic x zow,
mfthf fi hxrrtic, xk vj bucj xwc dtric. T axwe ku kfi zruowc, xwc vj
twsorir, mtkf twhrixaic amtdkwiaa, iahxqic twku kfi muuc.

“Kfta mxa kfiw kfi rimxrc ud vj biwiluniwhi! T fxc axlic x fovxw bitwz
druv ciakrohktuw, xwc xa x rihuvqiwai T wum mrtkfic owcir kfi vtairxbni
qxtw ud x muowc mfthf afxkkiric kfi dniaf xwc buwi. Kfi diintwza ud
etwcwiaa xwc ziwkniwiaa mfthf T fxc iwkirkxtwic bok x dim vuviwka
biduri zxli qnxhi ku finntaf rxzi xwc zwxaftwz ud kiikf. Twdnxvic bj
qxtw, T lumic ikirwxn fxkric xwc liwzixwhi ku xnn vxwetwc. Bok kfi
xzuwj ud vj muowc ulirhxvi vi; vj qonaia qxoaic, xwc T dxtwkic.

“Dur auvi miiea T nic x vtairxbni ntdi tw kfi muuca, iwcixluortwz ku
hori kfi muowc mfthf T fxc rihitlic. Kfi bxnn fxc iwkiric vj afuoncir,
xwc T ewim wuk mfikfir tk fxc rivxtwic kfiri ur qxaaic kfruozf; xk xwj
rxki T fxc wu vixwa ud igkrxhktwz tk. Vj aoddirtwza miri xozviwkic
xnau bj kfi uqqriaatli aiwai ud kfi twsoakthi xwc twzrxktkoci ud kfitr
twdnthktuw. Vj cxtnj luma ruai dur riliwzi—x ciiq xwc cixcnj riliwzi,
aohf xa muonc xnuwi huvqiwaxki dur kfi uokrxzia xwc xwzotaf T fxc
iwcoric.

“Xdkir auvi miiea vj muowc fixnic, xwc T huwktwoic vj suorwij. Kfi
nxbuora T iwcoric miri wu nuwzir ku bi xnniltxkic bj kfi brtzfk aow ur
ziwkni briiyia ud aqrtwz; xnn suj mxa bok x vuheirj mfthf twaonkic vj
ciaunxki akxki xwc vxci vi diin vuri qxtwdonnj kfxk T mxa wuk vxci dur
kfi iwsujviwk ud qnixaori.

“Bok vj kutna wum crim wixr x hnuai, xwc tw kmu vuwkfa druv kfta ktvi T
rixhfic kfi iwltruwa ud Ziwilx.

“Tk mxa iliwtwz mfiw T xrrtlic, xwc T riktric ku x ftctwz-qnxhi xvuwz
kfi dtinca kfxk aorruowc tk ku victkxki tw mfxk vxwwir T afuonc xqqnj
ku juo. T mxa uqqriaaic bj dxktzoi xwc fowzir xwc dxr kuu owfxqqj ku
iwsuj kfi ziwkni briiyia ud iliwtwz ur kfi qruaqihk ud kfi aow aikktwz
biftwc kfi akoqiwcuoa vuowkxtwa ud Sorx.

“Xk kfta ktvi x antzfk aniiq rintilic vi druv kfi qxtw ud ridnihktuw,
mfthf mxa ctakorbic bj kfi xqqruxhf ud x bixoktdon hftnc, mfu hxvi
rowwtwz twku kfi rihiaa T fxc hfuaiw, mtkf xnn kfi aqurktliwiaa ud
twdxwhj. Aocciwnj, xa T zxyic uw ftv, xw tcix aityic vi kfxk kfta
ntkkni hrixkori mxa owqrisocthic xwc fxc ntlic kuu afurk x ktvi ku fxli
tvbtbic x furrur ud cidurvtkj. Td, kfiriduri, T huonc aityi ftv xwc
icohxki ftv xa vj huvqxwtuw xwc drtiwc, T afuonc wuk bi au ciaunxki tw
kfta qiuqnic ixrkf.

“Orzic bj kfta tvqonai, T aityic uw kfi buj xa fi qxaaic xwc crim ftv
kumxrca vi. Xa auuw xa fi bifinc vj durv, fi qnxhic fta fxwca biduri
fta ijia xwc okkiric x afrtnn ahrixv; T crim fta fxwc durhtbnj druv fta
dxhi xwc axtc, ‘Hftnc, mfxk ta kfi vixwtwz ud kfta? T cu wuk twkiwc ku
fork juo; ntakiw ku vi.’

“Fi akrozznic ltuniwknj. ‘Nik vi zu,’ fi hrtic;
‘vuwakir! Oznj mrikhf! Juo mtaf ku ixk vi xwc kixr vi ku qtihia. Juo
xri xw uzri. Nik vi zu, ur T mtnn kinn vj qxqx.’

“‘Buj, juo mtnn wilir aii juor dxkfir xzxtw; juo voak huvi mtkf vi.’

“‘Ftciuoa vuwakir! Nik vi zu. Vj qxqx ta x ajwcth—fi ta V.
Drxweiwakitw—fi mtnn qowtaf juo. Juo cxri wuk eiiq vi.’

“‘Drxweiwakitw! juo binuwz kfiw ku vj iwivj—ku ftv kumxrca mfuv T fxli
amurw ikirwxn riliwzi; juo afxnn bi vj dtrak lthktv.’

“Kfi hftnc aktnn akrozznic xwc nuxcic vi mtkf iqtkfika mfthf hxrrtic
ciaqxtr ku vj fixrk; T zrxaqic fta kfruxk ku atniwhi ftv, xwc tw x
vuviwk fi nxj cixc xk vj diik.

“T zxyic uw vj lthktv, xwc vj fixrk aminnic mtkf igonkxktuw xwc finntaf
krtovqf; hnxqqtwz vj fxwca, T ighnxtvic, ‘T kuu hxw hrixki ciaunxktuw;
vj iwivj ta wuk twlonwirxbni; kfta cixkf mtnn hxrrj ciaqxtr ku ftv, xwc
x kfuoaxwc ukfir vtairtia afxnn kurviwk xwc ciakruj ftv.’

“Xa T dtgic vj ijia uw kfi hftnc, T axm auvikftwz zntkkirtwz uw fta
brixak. T kuue tk; tk mxa x qurkrxtk ud x vuak nulinj muvxw. Tw aqtki
ud vj vxntzwtkj, tk audkiwic xwc xkkrxhkic vi. Dur x dim vuviwka T
zxyic mtkf cintzfk uw fir cxre ijia, drtwzic bj ciiq nxafia, xwc fir
nulinj ntqa; bok qriaiwknj vj rxzi rikorwic; T rivivbiric kfxk T mxa
dur ilir ciqrtlic ud kfi cintzfka kfxk aohf bixoktdon hrixkoria huonc
biakum xwc kfxk afi mfuai riaivbnxwhi T huwkivqnxkic muonc, tw
rizxrctwz vi, fxli hfxwzic kfxk xtr ud ctltwi biwtzwtkj ku uwi
igqriaatli ud ctazoak xwc xddrtzfk.

“Hxw juo muwcir kfxk aohf kfuozfka krxwaqurkic vi mtkf rxzi? T uwnj
muwcir kfxk xk kfxk vuviwk, twakixc ud liwktwz vj aiwaxktuwa tw
ighnxvxktuwa xwc xzuwj, T ctc wuk roaf xvuwz vxwetwc xwc qirtaf tw kfi
xkkivqk ku ciakruj kfiv.

“Mftni T mxa ulirhuvi bj kfiai diintwza, T nidk kfi aquk mfiri T fxc
huvvtkkic kfi vorcir, xwc aiietwz x vuri aihnocic ftctwz-qnxhi, T
iwkiric x bxrw mfthf fxc xqqixric ku vi ku bi ivqkj. X muvxw mxa
aniiqtwz uw auvi akrxm; afi mxa juowz, wuk twciic au bixoktdon xa fir
mfuai qurkrxtk T finc, bok ud xw xzriixbni xaqihk xwc bnuuvtwz tw kfi
nulintwiaa ud juokf xwc fixnkf. Firi, T kfuozfk, ta uwi ud kfuai mfuai
suj-tvqxrktwz avtnia xri biakumic uw xnn bok vi. Xwc kfiw T biwk ulir
fir xwc mftaqiric, ‘Xmxei, dxtriak, kfj nulir ta wixr—fi mfu muonc
ztli fta ntdi bok ku ubkxtw uwi nuue ud xddihktuw druv kftwi ijia; vj
binulic, xmxei!’

“Kfi aniiqir aktrric; x kfrtnn ud kirrur rxw kfruozf vi. Afuonc afi
twciic xmxei, xwc aii vi, xwc horai vi, xwc ciwuowhi kfi vorcirir? Kfoa
muonc afi xaaoricnj xhk td fir cxreiwic ijia uqiwic xwc afi bifinc vi.
Kfi kfuozfk mxa vxcwiaa; tk aktrric kfi dtiwc mtkftw vi—wuk T, bok
afi, afxnn aoddir; kfi vorcir T fxli huvvtkkic bihxoai T xv dur ilir
rubbic ud xnn kfxk afi huonc ztli vi, afi afxnn xkuwi. Kfi hrtvi fxc
tka auorhi tw fir; bi fira kfi qowtafviwk! Kfxwea ku kfi niaauwa ud
Dintg xwc kfi axwzotwxrj nxma ud vxw, T fxc nixrwic wum ku mure
vtahftid. T biwk ulir fir xwc qnxhic kfi qurkrxtk aihorinj tw uwi ud
kfi dunca ud fir criaa. Afi vulic xzxtw, xwc T dnic.

“Dur auvi cxja T fxowkic kfi aquk mfiri kfiai ahiwia fxc kxeiw qnxhi,
auviktvia mtaftwz ku aii juo, auviktvia riaunlic ku potk kfi murnc xwc
tka vtairtia dur ilir. Xk niwzkf T mxwciric kumxrca kfiai vuowkxtwa,
xwc fxli rxwzic kfruozf kfitr tvviwai rihiaaia, huwaovic bj x borwtwz
qxaatuw mfthf juo xnuwi hxw zrxktdj. Mi vxj wuk qxrk owktn juo fxli
qruvtaic ku huvqnj mtkf vj ripotatktuw. T xv xnuwi xwc vtairxbni; vxw
mtnn wuk xaauhtxki mtkf vi; bok uwi xa cidurvic xwc furrtbni xa vjaind
muonc wuk ciwj firaind ku vi. Vj huvqxwtuw voak bi ud kfi axvi aqihtia
xwc fxli kfi axvi cidihka. Kfta bitwz juo voak hrixki.”




Hfxqkir 17


Kfi bitwz dtwtafic aqixetwz xwc dtgic fta nuuea oquw vi tw kfi
igqihkxktuw ud x riqnj. Bok T mxa bimtnciric, qirqnigic, xwc owxbni ku
xrrxwzi vj tcixa aoddthtiwknj ku owcirakxwc kfi donn igkiwk ud fta
qruquatktuw. Fi huwktwoic,

“Juo voak hrixki x divxni dur vi mtkf mfuv T hxw ntli tw kfi
twkirhfxwzi ud kfuai ajvqxkftia wihiaaxrj dur vj bitwz. Kfta juo xnuwi
hxw cu, xwc T civxwc tk ud juo xa x rtzfk mfthf juo voak wuk ridoai ku
huwhici.”

Kfi nxkkir qxrk ud fta kxni fxc etwcnic xwim tw vi kfi xwzir kfxk fxc
ctic xmxj mftni fi wxrrxkic fta qixhidon ntdi xvuwz kfi hukkxzira, xwc
xa fi axtc kfta T huonc wu nuwzir aoqqriaa kfi rxzi kfxk borwic mtkftw
vi.

“T cu ridoai tk,” T riqntic; “xwc wu kurkori afxnn ilir igkurk x
huwaiwk druv vi. Juo vxj riwcir vi kfi vuak vtairxbni ud viw, bok juo
afxnn wilir vxei vi bxai tw vj umw ijia. Afxnn T hrixki xwukfir ntei
juoraind, mfuai sutwk mtheicwiaa vtzfk ciaunxki kfi murnc. Bizuwi! T
fxli xwamiric juo; juo vxj kurkori vi, bok T mtnn wilir huwaiwk.”

“Juo xri tw kfi mruwz,” riqntic kfi dtiwc; “xwc twakixc
ud kfrixkiwtwz, T xv huwkiwk ku rixauw mtkf juo. T xv vxnthtuoa bihxoai T
xv vtairxbni. Xv T wuk afowwic xwc fxkic bj xnn vxwetwc? Juo, vj hrixkur,
muonc kixr vi ku qtihia xwc krtovqf; rivivbir kfxk, xwc kinn vi mfj T
afuonc qtkj vxw vuri kfxw fi qtktia vi? Juo muonc wuk hxnn tk vorcir td juo
huonc qrihtqtkxki vi twku uwi ud kfuai thi-rtdka xwc ciakruj vj drxvi, kfi
mure ud juor umw fxwca. Afxnn T riaqihk vxw mfiw fi huwcivwa vi? Nik ftv
ntli mtkf vi tw kfi twkirhfxwzi ud etwcwiaa, xwc twakixc ud twsorj T muonc
biakum ilirj biwidtk oquw ftv mtkf kixra ud zrxktkoci xk fta xhhiqkxwhi.
Bok kfxk hxwwuk bi; kfi fovxw aiwaia xri twaorvuowkxbni bxrrtira ku uor
owtuw. Jik vtwi afxnn wuk bi kfi aobvtaatuw ud xbsihk anxlirj. T mtnn
riliwzi vj twsortia; td T hxwwuk twaqtri nuli, T mtnn hxoai dixr, xwc
hftidnj kumxrca juo vj xrhf-iwivj, bihxoai vj hrixkur, cu T amixr
twigktwzotafxbni fxkric. Fxli x hxri; T mtnn mure xk juor ciakrohktuw, wur
dtwtaf owktn T ciaunxki juor fixrk, au kfxk juo afxnn horai kfi fuor ud
juor btrkf.”

X dtiwctaf rxzi xwtvxkic ftv xa fi axtc kfta; fta dxhi mxa mrtwenic
twku huwkurktuwa kuu furrtbni dur fovxw ijia ku bifunc; bok qriaiwknj
fi hxnvic ftvaind xwc qruhiicic—

“T twkiwcic ku rixauw. Kfta qxaatuw ta cikrtviwkxn ku vi, dur juo cu
wuk ridnihk kfxk _juo_ xri kfi hxoai ud tka ighiaa. Td xwj bitwz dink
ivuktuwa ud biwiluniwhi kumxrca vi, T afuonc rikorw kfiv x fowcric xwc x
fowcricdunc; dur kfxk uwi hrixkori’a axei T muonc vxei qixhi mtkf kfi
mfuni etwc! Bok T wum twconzi tw crixva ud bntaa kfxk hxwwuk bi rixntaic.
Mfxk T xae ud juo ta rixauwxbni xwc vucirxki; T civxwc x hrixkori ud
xwukfir aig, bok xa ftciuoa xa vjaind; kfi zrxktdthxktuw ta avxnn, bok tk
ta xnn kfxk T hxw rihitli, xwc tk afxnn huwkiwk vi. Tk ta kroi, mi afxnn bi
vuwakira, hok udd druv xnn kfi murnc; bok uw kfxk xhhuowk mi afxnn bi vuri
xkkxhfic ku uwi xwukfir. Uor ntlia mtnn wuk bi fxqqj, bok kfij mtnn bi
fxrvniaa xwc drii druv kfi vtairj T wum diin. Uf! Vj hrixkur, vxei vi
fxqqj; nik vi diin zrxktkoci kumxrca juo dur uwi biwidtk! Nik vi aii kfxk T
ightki kfi ajvqxkfj ud auvi igtaktwz kftwz; cu wuk ciwj vi vj
ripoiak!”

T mxa vulic. T afocciric mfiw T kfuozfk ud kfi quaatbni huwaipoiwhia
ud vj huwaiwk, bok T dink kfxk kfiri mxa auvi soakthi tw fta xrzoviwk.
Fta kxni xwc kfi diintwza fi wum igqriaaic qrulic ftv ku bi x hrixkori
ud dtwi aiwaxktuwa, xwc ctc T wuk xa fta vxeir umi ftv xnn kfi qurktuw
ud fxqqtwiaa kfxk tk mxa tw vj qumir ku biakum? Fi axm vj hfxwzi ud
diintwz xwc huwktwoic,

“Td juo huwaiwk, witkfir juo wur xwj ukfir fovxw bitwz afxnn ilir aii
oa xzxtw; T mtnn zu ku kfi lxak mtnca ud Auokf Xvirthx. Vj duuc ta wuk
kfxk ud vxw; T cu wuk ciakruj kfi nxvb xwc kfi etc ku znok vj xqqiktki;
xhurwa xwc birrtia xddurc vi aoddthtiwk wuortafviwk. Vj huvqxwtuw mtnn
bi ud kfi axvi wxkori xa vjaind xwc mtnn bi huwkiwk mtkf kfi axvi dxri.
Mi afxnn vxei uor bic ud crtic nixlia; kfi aow mtnn aftwi uw oa xa uw
vxw xwc mtnn rtqiw uor duuc. Kfi qthkori T qriaiwk ku juo ta qixhidon
xwc fovxw, xwc juo voak diin kfxk juo huonc ciwj tk uwnj tw kfi
mxwkuwwiaa ud qumir xwc hroinkj. Qtktniaa xa juo fxli biiw kumxrca vi,
T wum aii huvqxaatuw tw juor ijia; nik vi aityi kfi dxluorxbni vuviwk
xwc qiraoxci juo ku qruvtai mfxk T au xrciwknj ciatri.”

“Juo qruquai,” riqntic T, “ku dnj druv kfi fxbtkxktuwa ud
vxw, ku cminn tw kfuai mtnca mfiri kfi bixaka ud kfi dtinc mtnn bi juor
uwnj huvqxwtuwa. Fum hxw juo, mfu nuwz dur kfi nuli xwc ajvqxkfj ud vxw,
qirailiri tw kfta igtni? Juo mtnn rikorw xwc xzxtw aiie kfitr etwcwiaa, xwc
juo mtnn viik mtkf kfitr cikiakxktuw; juor iltn qxaatuwa mtnn bi riwimic,
xwc juo mtnn kfiw fxli x huvqxwtuw ku xtc juo tw kfi kxae ud ciakrohktuw.
Kfta vxj wuk bi; hixai ku xrzoi kfi qutwk, dur T hxwwuk huwaiwk.”

“Fum twhuwakxwk xri juor diintwza! Bok x vuviwk xzu juo miri vulic bj
vj riqriaiwkxktuwa, xwc mfj cu juo xzxtw fxrciw juoraind ku vj huvqnxtwka?
T amixr ku juo, bj kfi ixrkf mfthf T twfxbtk, xwc bj juo kfxk vxci vi, kfxk
mtkf kfi huvqxwtuw juo biakum, T mtnn potk kfi witzfbuorfuuc ud vxw xwc
cminn, xa tk vxj hfxwhi, tw kfi vuak axlxzi ud qnxhia. Vj iltn qxaatuwa
mtnn fxli dnic, dur T afxnn viik mtkf ajvqxkfj! Vj ntdi mtnn dnum potiknj
xmxj, xwc tw vj cjtwz vuviwka T afxnn wuk horai vj vxeir.”

Fta murca fxc x akrxwzi iddihk oquw vi. T huvqxaatuwxkic ftv xwc
auviktvia dink x mtaf ku huwauni ftv, bok mfiw T nuueic oquw ftv, mfiw
T axm kfi dtnkfj vxaa kfxk vulic xwc kxneic, vj fixrk atheiwic xwc vj
diintwza miri xnkiric ku kfuai ud furrur xwc fxkric. T krtic ku aktdni
kfiai aiwaxktuwa; T kfuozfk kfxk xa T huonc wuk ajvqxkftai mtkf ftv, T
fxc wu rtzfk ku mtkffunc druv ftv kfi avxnn qurktuw ud fxqqtwiaa mfthf
mxa jik tw vj qumir ku biakum.

“Juo amixr,” T axtc, “ku bi fxrvniaa; bok fxli juo wuk
xnrixcj afumw x cizrii ud vxnthi kfxk afuonc rixauwxbnj vxei vi ctakroak
juo? Vxj wuk iliw kfta bi x ditwk kfxk mtnn twhrixai juor krtovqf bj
xddurctwz x mtcir ahuqi dur juor riliwzi?”

“Fum ta kfta? T voak wuk bi krtdnic mtkf, xwc T civxwc xw xwamir. Td
T fxli wu ktia xwc wu xddihktuwa, fxkric xwc lthi voak bi vj qurktuw;
kfi nuli ud xwukfir mtnn ciakruj kfi hxoai ud vj hrtvia, xwc T afxnn
bihuvi x kftwz ud mfuai igtakiwhi ilirjuwi mtnn bi tzwurxwk. Vj lthia
xri kfi hftncriw ud x durhic auntkoci kfxk T xbfur, xwc vj ltrkoia mtnn
wihiaaxrtnj xrtai mfiw T ntli tw huvvowtuw mtkf xw ipoxn. T afxnn diin
kfi xddihktuwa ud x aiwatktli bitwz xwc bihuvi ntweic ku kfi hfxtw ud
igtakiwhi xwc iliwka druv mfthf T xv wum ighnocic.”

T qxoaic auvi ktvi ku ridnihk uw xnn fi fxc rinxkic xwc kfi lxrtuoa
xrzoviwka mfthf fi fxc ivqnujic. T kfuozfk ud kfi qruvtai ud ltrkoia mfthf
fi fxc ctaqnxjic uw kfi uqiwtwz ud fta igtakiwhi xwc kfi aobaipoiwk bntzfk
ud xnn etwcnj diintwz bj kfi nuxkftwz xwc ahurw mfthf fta qrukihkura fxc
vxwtdiakic kumxrca ftv. Fta qumir xwc kfrixka miri wuk uvtkkic tw vj
hxnhonxktuwa; x hrixkori mfu huonc igtak tw kfi thi-hxlia ud kfi znxhtira
xwc ftci ftvaind druv qoraotk xvuwz kfi rtczia ud twxhhiaatbni qrihtqthia
mxa x bitwz quaaiaatwz dxhonktia tk muonc bi lxtw ku huqi mtkf. Xdkir x
nuwz qxoai ud ridnihktuw T huwhnocic kfxk kfi soakthi coi bukf ku ftv xwc
vj dinnum hrixkoria civxwcic ud vi kfxk T afuonc huvqnj mtkf fta ripoiak.
Korwtwz ku ftv, kfiriduri, T axtc,

“T huwaiwk ku juor civxwc, uw juor aunivw uxkf ku potk Ioruqi dur ilir,
xwc ilirj ukfir qnxhi tw kfi witzfbuorfuuc ud vxw, xa auuw xa T afxnn
cintlir twku juor fxwca x divxni mfu mtnn xhhuvqxwj juo tw juor igtni.”

“T amixr,” fi hrtic, “bj kfi aow, xwc bj kfi bnoi aej ud
fixliw, xwc bj kfi dtri ud nuli kfxk borwa vj fixrk, kfxk td juo zrxwk vj
qrxjir, mftni kfij igtak juo afxnn wilir bifunc vi xzxtw. Ciqxrk ku juor
fuvi xwc huvviwhi juor nxbuora; T afxnn mxkhf kfitr qruzriaa mtkf
owokkirxbni xwgtikj; xwc dixr wuk bok kfxk mfiw juo xri rixcj T afxnn
xqqixr.”

Axjtwz kfta, fi aocciwnj potkkic vi, dixrdon, qirfxqa, ud xwj hfxwzi tw
vj aiwktviwka. T axm ftv ciahiwc kfi vuowkxtw mtkf zrixkir aqiic kfxw
kfi dntzfk ud xw ixzni, xwc pothenj nuak xvuwz kfi owconxktuwa ud kfi
aix ud thi.

Fta kxni fxc uhhoqtic kfi mfuni cxj, xwc kfi aow mxa oquw kfi lirzi ud
kfi furtyuw mfiw fi ciqxrkic. T ewim kfxk T uozfk ku fxakiw vj ciahiwk
kumxrca kfi lxnnij, xa T afuonc auuw bi iwhuvqxaaic tw cxrewiaa; bok vj
fixrk mxa fixlj, xwc vj akiqa anum. Kfi nxbuor ud mtwctwz xvuwz kfi
ntkkni qxkfa ud kfi vuowkxtw xwc dtgtwz vj diik dtrvnj xa T xclxwhic
qirqnigic vi, uhhoqtic xa T mxa bj kfi ivuktuwa mfthf kfi uhhorriwhia
ud kfi cxj fxc qrucohic. Wtzfk mxa dxr xclxwhic mfiw T hxvi ku kfi
fxndmxj riaktwz-qnxhi xwc aixkic vjaind biatci kfi duowkxtw. Kfi akxra
afuwi xk twkirlxna xa kfi hnuoca qxaaic druv ulir kfiv; kfi cxre qtwia
ruai biduri vi, xwc ilirj firi xwc kfiri x brueiw krii nxj uw kfi
zruowc; tk mxa x ahiwi ud muwcirdon aunivwtkj xwc aktrric akrxwzi
kfuozfka mtkftw vi. T miqk btkkirnj, xwc hnxaqtwz vj fxwca tw xzuwj, T
ighnxtvic, “Uf! akxra xwc hnuoca xwc mtwca, ji xri xnn xbuok ku vuhe
vi; td ji rixnnj qtkj vi, hroaf aiwaxktuw xwc vivurj; nik vi bihuvi xa
wuozfk; bok td wuk, ciqxrk, ciqxrk, xwc nixli vi tw cxrewiaa.”

Kfiai miri mtnc xwc vtairxbni kfuozfka, bok T hxwwuk ciahrtbi ku juo
fum kfi ikirwxn kmtwentwz ud kfi akxra mitzfic oquw vi xwc fum T
ntakiwic ku ilirj bnxak ud mtwc xa td tk miri x conn oznj atruh uw tka
mxj ku huwaovi vi.

Vurwtwz cxmwic biduri T xrrtlic xk kfi ltnnxzi ud Hfxvuowtg; T kuue wu
riak, bok rikorwic tvvictxkinj ku Ziwilx. Iliw tw vj umw fixrk T huonc
ztli wu igqriaatuw ku vj aiwaxktuwa—kfij mitzfic uw vi mtkf x
vuowkxtw’a mitzfk xwc kfitr ighiaa ciakrujic vj xzuwj biwixkf kfiv.
Kfoa T rikorwic fuvi, xwc iwkirtwz kfi fuoai, qriaiwkic vjaind ku kfi
dxvtnj. Vj fxzzxrc xwc mtnc xqqixrxwhi xmuei twkiwai xnxrv, bok T
xwamiric wu poiaktuw, ahxrhinj ctc T aqixe. T dink xa td T miri qnxhic
owcir x bxw—xa td T fxc wu rtzfk ku hnxtv kfitr ajvqxkftia—xa td
wilir vuri vtzfk T iwsuj huvqxwtuwaftq mtkf kfiv. Jik iliw kfoa T
nulic kfiv ku xcurxktuw; xwc ku axli kfiv, T riaunlic ku cicthxki
vjaind ku vj vuak xbfurric kxae. Kfi qruaqihk ud aohf xw uhhoqxktuw
vxci ilirj ukfir htrhovakxwhi ud igtakiwhi qxaa biduri vi ntei x crixv,
xwc kfxk kfuozfk uwnj fxc ku vi kfi rixntkj ud ntdi.




Hfxqkir 18


Cxj xdkir cxj, miie xdkir miie, qxaaic xmxj uw vj rikorw ku Ziwilx; xwc
T huonc wuk hunnihk kfi huorxzi ku rihuvviwhi vj mure. T dixric kfi
liwzixwhi ud kfi ctaxqqutwkic dtiwc, jik T mxa owxbni ku ulirhuvi vj
riqozwxwhi ku kfi kxae mfthf mxa iwsutwic vi. T duowc kfxk T huonc wuk
huvquai x divxni mtkfuok xzxtw ciluktwz ailirxn vuwkfa ku qruduowc
akocj xwc nxburtuoa ctapotatktuw. T fxc fixrc ud auvi ctahulirtia
fxltwz biiw vxci bj xw Iwzntaf qftnuauqfir, kfi ewumniczi ud mfthf mxa
vxkirtxn ku vj aohhiaa, xwc T auviktvia kfuozfk ud ubkxtwtwz vj
dxkfir’a huwaiwk ku ltatk Iwznxwc dur kfta qorquai; bok T hnowz ku
ilirj qrikiwhi ud cinxj xwc afrxwe druv kxetwz kfi dtrak akiq tw xw
owcirkxetwz mfuai tvvictxki wihiaatkj bizxw ku xqqixr niaa xbaunoki ku
vi. X hfxwzi twciic fxc kxeiw qnxhi tw vi; vj fixnkf, mfthf fxc
ftkfirku cihntwic, mxa wum vohf riakuric; xwc vj aqtrtka, mfiw
owhfiheic bj kfi vivurj ud vj owfxqqj qruvtai, ruai qruqurktuwxbnj. Vj
dxkfir axm kfta hfxwzi mtkf qnixaori, xwc fi korwic fta kfuozfka
kumxrca kfi biak vikfuc ud irxcthxktwz kfi rivxtwa ud vj vinxwhfunj,
mfthf ilirj wum xwc kfiw muonc rikorw bj dtka, xwc mtkf x ciluortwz
bnxhewiaa ulirhxak kfi xqqruxhftwz aowaftwi. Xk kfiai vuviwka T kuue
ridozi tw kfi vuak qirdihk auntkoci. T qxaaic mfuni cxja uw kfi nxei
xnuwi tw x ntkkni buxk, mxkhftwz kfi hnuoca xwc ntakiwtwz ku kfi
rtqqntwz ud kfi mxlia, atniwk xwc ntakniaa. Bok kfi driaf xtr xwc
brtzfk aow aincuv dxtnic ku riakuri vi ku auvi cizrii ud huvquaori, xwc
uw vj rikorw T vik kfi axnokxktuwa ud vj drtiwca mtkf x rixctir avtni
xwc x vuri hfiirdon fixrk.

Tk mxa xdkir vj rikorw druv uwi ud kfiai rxvbnia kfxk vj dxkfir,
hxnntwz vi xatci, kfoa xccriaaic vi,

“T xv fxqqj ku rivxre, vj cixr auw, kfxk juo fxli riaovic juor durvir
qnixaoria xwc aiiv ku bi rikorwtwz ku juoraind. Xwc jik juo xri aktnn
owfxqqj xwc aktnn xlutc uor auhtikj. Dur auvi ktvi T mxa nuak tw
huwsihkori xa ku kfi hxoai ud kfta, bok jiakircxj xw tcix akrohe vi,
xwc td tk ta minn duowcic, T huwsori juo ku xlum tk. Riairli uw aohf x
qutwk muonc bi wuk uwnj oainiaa, bok crxm cumw kribni vtairj uw oa xnn.”

T krivbnic ltuniwknj xk fta igurctov, xwc vj dxkfir huwktwoic—

“T huwdiaa, vj auw, kfxk T fxli xnmxja nuueic durmxrc ku juor
vxrrtxzi mtkf uor cixr Intyxbikf xa kfi kti ud uor cuviakth huvdurk xwc kfi
akxj ud vj cihntwtwz jixra. Juo miri xkkxhfic ku ixhf ukfir druv juor
ixrntiak twdxwhj; juo akoctic kuzikfir, xwc xqqixric, tw ctaquatktuwa xwc
kxakia, iwktrinj aotkic ku uwi xwukfir. Bok au bntwc ta kfi igqirtiwhi ud
vxw kfxk mfxk T huwhitlic ku bi kfi biak xaatakxwka ku vj qnxw vxj fxli
iwktrinj ciakrujic tk. Juo, qirfxqa, rizxrc fir xa juor atakir, mtkfuok xwj
mtaf kfxk afi vtzfk bihuvi juor mtdi. Wxj, juo vxj fxli vik mtkf xwukfir
mfuv juo vxj nuli; xwc huwatcirtwz juoraind xa buowc tw fuwuor ku
Intyxbikf, kfta akrozzni vxj uhhxatuw kfi qutzwxwk vtairj mfthf juo xqqixr
ku diin.”

“Vj cixr dxkfir, rixaaori juoraind. T nuli vj huoatw kiwcirnj xwc
atwhirinj. T wilir axm xwj muvxw mfu ightkic, xa Intyxbikf cuia, vj
mxrviak xcvtrxktuw xwc xddihktuw. Vj dokori fuqia xwc qruaqihka xri
iwktrinj buowc oq tw kfi igqihkxktuw ud uor owtuw.”

“Kfi igqriaatuw ud juor aiwktviwka ud kfta aobsihk, vj cixr Lthkur,
ztlia vi vuri qnixaori kfxw T fxli dur auvi ktvi igqirtiwhic. Td juo
diin kfoa, mi afxnn xaaoricnj bi fxqqj, fumilir qriaiwk iliwka vxj hxak
x znuuv ulir oa. Bok tk ta kfta znuuv mfthf xqqixra ku fxli kxeiw au
akruwz x func ud juor vtwc kfxk T mtaf ku ctaatqxki. Kinn vi,
kfiriduri, mfikfir juo ubsihk ku xw tvvictxki aunivwtaxktuw ud kfi
vxrrtxzi. Mi fxli biiw owdurkowxki, xwc rihiwk iliwka fxli crxmw oa
druv kfxk ilirjcxj krxwpotnntkj bidtkktwz vj jixra xwc twdtrvtktia. Juo
xri juowzir; jik T cu wuk aoqquai, quaaiaaic xa juo xri ud x huvqikiwk
durkowi, kfxk xw ixrnj vxrrtxzi muonc xk xnn twkirdiri mtkf xwj dokori
qnxwa ud fuwuor xwc oktntkj kfxk juo vxj fxli durvic. Cu wuk aoqquai,
fumilir, kfxk T mtaf ku cthkxki fxqqtwiaa ku juo ur kfxk x cinxj uw
juor qxrk muonc hxoai vi xwj airtuoa owixatwiaa. Twkirqrik vj murca
mtkf hxwcuor xwc xwamir vi, T huwsori juo, mtkf huwdtciwhi xwc
atwhirtkj.”

T ntakiwic ku vj dxkfir tw atniwhi xwc rivxtwic dur auvi ktvi twhxqxbni
ud uddirtwz xwj riqnj. T rilunlic rxqtcnj tw vj vtwc x vonktkoci ud
kfuozfka xwc iwcixluoric ku xrrtli xk auvi huwhnoatuw. Xnxa! Ku vi
kfi tcix ud xw tvvictxki owtuw mtkf vj Intyxbikf mxa uwi ud furrur xwc
ctavxj. T mxa buowc bj x aunivw qruvtai mfthf T fxc wuk jik dondtnnic
xwc cxric wuk brixe, ur td T ctc, mfxk vxwtdunc vtairtia vtzfk wuk
tvqiwc ulir vi xwc vj cilukic dxvtnj! Huonc T iwkir twku x diaktlxn
mtkf kfta cixcnj mitzfk jik fxwztwz ruowc vj wihe xwc bumtwz vi ku kfi
zruowc? T voak qirdurv vj iwzxziviwk xwc nik kfi vuwakir ciqxrk mtkf
fta vxki biduri T xnnumic vjaind ku iwsuj kfi cintzfk ud x owtuw druv
mfthf T igqihkic qixhi.

T rivivbiric xnau kfi wihiaatkj tvquaic oquw vi ud itkfir suorwijtwz ku
Iwznxwc ur iwkirtwz twku x nuwz hurriaquwciwhi mtkf kfuai qftnuauqfira
ud kfxk huowkrj mfuai ewumniczi xwc ctahulirtia miri ud twctaqiwaxbni
oai ku vi tw vj qriaiwk owcirkxetwz. Kfi nxkkir vikfuc ud ubkxtwtwz
kfi ciatric twkinntziwhi mxa ctnxkurj xwc owaxktadxhkurj; biatcia, T
fxc xw twaorvuowkxbni xliratuw ku kfi tcix ud iwzxztwz vjaind tw vj
nuxkfauvi kxae tw vj dxkfir’a fuoai mftni tw fxbtka ud dxvtntxr
twkirhuorai mtkf kfuai T nulic. T ewim kfxk x kfuoaxwc dixrdon
xhhtciwka vtzfk uhhor, kfi antzfkiak ud mfthf muonc ctahnuai x kxni ku
kfrtnn xnn huwwihkic mtkf vi mtkf furrur. T mxa xmxri xnau kfxk T
afuonc udkiw nuai xnn aind-huvvxwc, xnn hxqxhtkj ud ftctwz kfi
fxrrumtwz aiwaxktuwa kfxk muonc quaaiaa vi cortwz kfi qruzriaa ud vj
owixrkfnj uhhoqxktuw. T voak xbaiwk vjaind druv xnn T nulic mftni kfoa
ivqnujic. Uwhi huvviwhic, tk muonc pothenj bi xhftilic, xwc T vtzfk bi
riakuric ku vj dxvtnj tw qixhi xwc fxqqtwiaa. Vj qruvtai dondtnnic,
kfi vuwakir muonc ciqxrk dur ilir. Ur (au vj duwc dxwhj tvxzic) auvi
xhhtciwk vtzfk vixwmftni uhhor ku ciakruj ftv xwc qok xw iwc ku vj
anxlirj dur ilir.

Kfiai diintwza cthkxkic vj xwamir ku vj dxkfir. T igqriaaic x mtaf ku
ltatk Iwznxwc, bok huwhixntwz kfi kroi rixauwa ud kfta ripoiak, T
hnukfic vj ciatria owcir x zotai mfthf ightkic wu aoaqthtuw, mftni T
orzic vj ciatri mtkf xw ixrwiakwiaa kfxk ixatnj twcohic vj dxkfir ku
huvqnj. Xdkir au nuwz x qirtuc ud xw xbaurbtwz vinxwhfunj kfxk
riaivbnic vxcwiaa tw tka twkiwatkj xwc iddihka, fi mxa znxc ku dtwc
kfxk T mxa hxqxbni ud kxetwz qnixaori tw kfi tcix ud aohf x suorwij,
xwc fi fuqic kfxk hfxwzi ud ahiwi xwc lxrtic xvoaiviwk muonc, biduri vj
rikorw, fxli riakuric vi iwktrinj ku vjaind.

Kfi corxktuw ud vj xbaiwhi mxa nidk ku vj umw hfuthi; x dim vuwkfa, ur
xk vuak x jixr, mxa kfi qirtuc huwkivqnxkic. Uwi qxkirwxn etwc
qrihxoktuw fi fxc kxeiw ku iwaori vj fxltwz x huvqxwtuw. Mtkfuok
qriltuoanj huvvowthxktwz mtkf vi, fi fxc, tw huwhirk mtkf Intyxbikf,
xrrxwzic kfxk Hnirlxn afuonc sutw vi xk Akrxaborzf. Kfta twkirdiric
mtkf kfi auntkoci T hulikic dur kfi qruaihoktuw ud vj kxae; jik xk kfi
huvviwhiviwk ud vj suorwij kfi qriaiwhi ud vj drtiwc huonc tw wu mxj bi
xw tvqictviwk, xwc kronj T risuthic kfxk kfoa T afuonc bi axlic vxwj
fuora ud nuwinj, vxcciwtwz ridnihktuw. Wxj, Fiwrj vtzfk akxwc bikmiiw
vi xwc kfi twkroatuw ud vj dui. Td T miri xnuwi, muonc fi wuk xk ktvia
durhi fta xbfurric qriaiwhi uw vi ku rivtwc vi ud vj kxae ur ku
huwkivqnxki tka qruzriaa?

Ku Iwznxwc, kfiriduri, T mxa buowc, xwc tk mxa owcirakuuc kfxk vj owtuw
mtkf Intyxbikf afuonc kxei qnxhi tvvictxkinj uw vj rikorw. Vj dxkfir’a
xzi riwciric ftv igkrivinj xlirai ku cinxj. Dur vjaind, kfiri mxa uwi
rimxrc T qruvtaic vjaind druv vj cikiakic kutna—uwi huwaunxktuw dur vj
owqxrxnninic aoddirtwza; tk mxa kfi qruaqihk ud kfxk cxj mfiw,
iwdrxwhftaic druv vj vtairxbni anxlirj, T vtzfk hnxtv Intyxbikf xwc
durzik kfi qxak tw vj owtuw mtkf fir.

T wum vxci xrrxwziviwka dur vj suorwij, bok uwi diintwz fxowkic vi
mfthf dtnnic vi mtkf dixr xwc xztkxktuw. Cortwz vj xbaiwhi T afuonc
nixli vj drtiwca owhuwahtuoa ud kfi igtakiwhi ud kfitr iwivj xwc
owqrukihkic druv fta xkkxhea, igxaqirxkic xa fi vtzfk bi bj vj
ciqxrkori. Bok fi fxc qruvtaic ku dunnum vi mfirilir T vtzfk zu, xwc
muonc fi wuk xhhuvqxwj vi ku Iwznxwc? Kfta tvxztwxktuw mxa crixcdon tw
tkaind, bok auukftwz twxavohf xa tk aoqquaic kfi axdikj ud vj drtiwca.
T mxa xzuwtaic mtkf kfi tcix ud kfi quaatbtntkj kfxk kfi rilirai ud
kfta vtzfk fxqqiw. Bok kfruozf kfi mfuni qirtuc cortwz mfthf T mxa kfi
anxli ud vj hrixkori T xnnumic vjaind ku bi zulirwic bj kfi tvqonaia ud
kfi vuviwk; xwc vj qriaiwk aiwaxktuwa akruwznj twktvxkic kfxk kfi dtiwc
muonc dunnum vi xwc igivqk vj dxvtnj druv kfi cxwzir ud fta
vxhftwxktuwa.

Tk mxa tw kfi nxkkir iwc ud Aiqkivbir kfxk T xzxtw potkkic vj wxktli
huowkrj. Vj suorwij fxc biiw vj umw aozziaktuw, xwc Intyxbikf
kfiriduri xhpotiahic, bok afi mxa dtnnic mtkf ctapotik xk kfi tcix ud
vj aoddirtwz, xmxj druv fir, kfi twruxca ud vtairj xwc zrtid. Tk fxc
biiw fir hxri mfthf qrultcic vi x huvqxwtuw tw Hnirlxn—xwc jik x vxw
ta bntwc ku x kfuoaxwc vtwoki htrhovakxwhia mfthf hxnn durkf x muvxw’a
aiconuoa xkkiwktuw. Afi nuwzic ku btc vi fxakiw vj rikorw; x kfuoaxwc
huwdnthktwz ivuktuwa riwciric fir voki xa afi bxci vi x kixrdon, atniwk
dxriminn.

T kfrim vjaind twku kfi hxrrtxzi kfxk mxa ku huwlij vi xmxj, fxrcnj
ewumtwz mftkfir T mxa zutwz, xwc hxriniaa ud mfxk mxa qxaatwz xruowc.
T rivivbiric uwnj, xwc tk mxa mtkf x btkkir xwzotaf kfxk T ridnihkic uw
tk, ku urcir kfxk vj hfivthxn twakroviwka afuonc bi qxheic ku zu mtkf
vi. Dtnnic mtkf crixrj tvxztwxktuwa, T qxaaic kfruozf vxwj bixoktdon
xwc vxsiakth ahiwia, bok vj ijia miri dtgic xwc owubairltwz. T huonc
uwnj kftwe ud kfi buorwi ud vj krxlina xwc kfi mure mfthf mxa ku uhhoqj
vi mftnak kfij iwcoric.

Xdkir auvi cxja aqiwk tw ntakniaa twcuniwhi, cortwz mfthf T krxliraic
vxwj nixzoia, T xrrtlic xk Akrxaborzf, mfiri T mxtkic kmu cxja dur
Hnirlxn. Fi hxvi. Xnxa, fum zrixk mxa kfi huwkrxak bikmiiw oa! Fi
mxa xntli ku ilirj wim ahiwi, sujdon mfiw fi axm kfi bixoktia ud kfi
aikktwz aow, xwc vuri fxqqj mfiw fi bifinc tk rtai xwc rihuvviwhi x wim
cxj. Fi qutwkic uok ku vi kfi aftdktwz hunuora ud kfi nxwcahxqi xwc
kfi xqqixrxwhia ud kfi aej. “Kfta ta mfxk tk ta ku ntli,” fi hrtic;
“wum T iwsuj igtakiwhi! Bok juo, vj cixr Drxweiwakitw, mfiriduri xri
juo ciaquwctwz xwc aurrumdon!” Tw krokf, T mxa uhhoqtic bj znuuvj
kfuozfka xwc witkfir axm kfi ciahiwk ud kfi iliwtwz akxr wur kfi zunciw
aowrtai ridnihkic tw kfi Rftwi. Xwc juo, vj drtiwc, muonc bi dxr vuri
xvoaic mtkf kfi suorwxn ud Hnirlxn, mfu ubairlic kfi ahiwirj mtkf xw
iji ud diintwz xwc cintzfk, kfxw tw ntakiwtwz ku vj ridnihktuwa. T, x
vtairxbni mrikhf, fxowkic bj x horai kfxk afok oq ilirj xliwoi ku
iwsujviwk.

Mi fxc xzriic ku ciahiwc kfi Rftwi tw x buxk druv Akrxaborzf ku
Rukkircxv, mfiwhi mi vtzfk kxei aftqqtwz dur Nuwcuw. Cortwz kfta
lujxzi mi qxaaic vxwj mtnnumj tanxwca xwc axm ailirxn bixoktdon kumwa.
Mi akxjic x cxj xk Vxwwfitv, xwc uw kfi dtdkf druv uor ciqxrkori druv
Akrxaborzf, xrrtlic xk Vxtwy. Kfi huorai ud kfi Rftwi binum Vxtwy
bihuvia vohf vuri qthkoriapoi. Kfi rtlir ciahiwca rxqtcnj xwc mtwca
bikmiiw ftnna, wuk ftzf, bok akiiq, xwc ud bixoktdon durva. Mi axm
vxwj rotwic hxaknia akxwctwz uw kfi iczia ud qrihtqthia, aorruowcic bj
bnxhe muuca, ftzf xwc twxhhiaatbni. Kfta qxrk ud kfi Rftwi, twciic,
qriaiwka x atwzonxrnj lxrtizxkic nxwcahxqi. Tw uwi aquk juo ltim
rozzic ftnna, rotwic hxaknia ulirnuuetwz kriviwcuoa qrihtqthia, mtkf
kfi cxre Rftwi roaftwz biwixkf; xwc uw kfi aocciw korw ud x qruvuwkurj,
dnuortaftwz ltwijxrca mtkf zriiw anuqtwz bxwea xwc x vixwcirtwz rtlir
xwc quqonuoa kumwa uhhoqj kfi ahiwi.

Mi krxlinnic xk kfi ktvi ud kfi ltwkxzi xwc fixrc kfi auwz ud kfi nxbuorira
xa mi zntcic cumw kfi akrixv. Iliw T, ciqriaaic tw vtwc, xwc vj aqtrtka
huwktwoxnnj xztkxkic bj znuuvj diintwza, iliw T mxa qnixaic. T nxj xk kfi
bukkuv ud kfi buxk, xwc xa T zxyic uw kfi hnuocniaa bnoi aej, T aiivic ku
crtwe tw x krxwpotnntkj ku mfthf T fxc nuwz biiw x akrxwzir. Xwc td kfiai
miri vj aiwaxktuwa, mfu hxw ciahrtbi kfuai ud Fiwrj? Fi dink xa td fi fxc
biiw krxwaqurkic ku Dxtrj-nxwc xwc iwsujic x fxqqtwiaa aincuv kxakic bj
vxw. “T fxli aiiw,” fi axtc, “kfi vuak bixoktdon ahiwia
ud vj umw huowkrj; T fxli ltatkic kfi nxeia ud Nohirwi xwc Ort, mfiri kfi
awumj vuowkxtwa ciahiwc xnvuak qirqiwcthonxrnj ku kfi mxkir, hxaktwz bnxhe
xwc tvqiwikrxbni afxcia, mfthf muonc hxoai x znuuvj xwc vuorwdon xqqixrxwhi
miri tk wuk dur kfi vuak lircxwk tanxwca kfxk rintili kfi iji bj kfitr zxj
xqqixrxwhi; T fxli aiiw kfta nxei xztkxkic bj x kivqiak, mfiw kfi mtwc kuri
oq mftrnmtwca ud mxkir xwc zxli juo xw tcix ud mfxk kfi mxkir-aquok voak bi
uw kfi zrixk uhixw; xwc kfi mxlia cxaf mtkf dorj kfi bxai ud kfi vuowkxtw,
mfiri kfi qrtiak xwc fta vtakriaa miri ulirmfinvic bj xw xlxnxwhfi xwc
mfiri kfitr cjtwz luthia xri aktnn axtc ku bi fixrc xvtc kfi qxoaia ud kfi
wtzfknj mtwc; T fxli aiiw kfi vuowkxtwa ud Nx Lxnxta, xwc kfi Qxja ci Lxoc;
bok kfta huowkrj, Lthkur, qnixaia vi vuri kfxw xnn kfuai muwcira. Kfi
vuowkxtwa ud Amtkyirnxwc xri vuri vxsiakth xwc akrxwzi, bok kfiri ta x
hfxrv tw kfi bxwea ud kfta ctltwi rtlir kfxk T wilir biduri axm ipoxnnic.
Nuue xk kfxk hxakni mfthf ulirfxwza juw qrihtqthi; xwc kfxk xnau uw kfi
tanxwc, xnvuak huwhixnic xvuwzak kfi duntxzi ud kfuai nulinj kriia; xwc wum
kfxk zruoq ud nxbuorira huvtwz druv xvuwz kfitr ltwia; xwc kfxk ltnnxzi
fxnd ftc tw kfi rihiaa ud kfi vuowkxtw. Uf, aorinj kfi aqtrtk kfxk twfxbtka
xwc zoxrca kfta qnxhi fxa x auon vuri tw fxrvuwj mtkf vxw kfxw kfuai mfu
qtni kfi znxhtir ur riktri ku kfi twxhhiaatbni qixea ud kfi vuowkxtwa ud
uor umw huowkrj.”

Hnirlxn! Binulic drtiwc! Iliw wum tk cintzfka vi ku rihurc juor murca xwc
ku cminn uw kfi qrxtai ud mfthf juo xri au ivtwiwknj ciairltwz. Fi mxa x
bitwz durvic tw kfi “lirj quikrj ud wxkori.” Fta mtnc xwc
iwkfoatxakth tvxztwxktuw mxa hfxakiwic bj kfi aiwatbtntkj ud fta fixrk. Fta
auon ulirdnumic mtkf xrciwk xddihktuwa, xwc fta drtiwcaftq mxa ud kfxk
cilukic xwc muwcruoa wxkori kfxk kfi murncnj-vtwcic kixhf oa ku nuue dur uwnj
tw kfi tvxztwxktuw. Bok iliw fovxw ajvqxkftia miri wuk aoddthtiwk ku
axktadj fta ixzir vtwc. Kfi ahiwirj ud igkirwxn wxkori, mfthf ukfira rizxrc
uwnj mtkf xcvtrxktuw, fi nulic mtkf xrcuor:—

    ——Kfi auowctwz hxkxrxhk
    Fxowkic ftv ntei x qxaatuw: kfi kxnn ruhe,
    Kfi vuowkxtw, xwc kfi ciiq xwc znuuvj muuc,
    Kfitr hunuora xwc kfitr durva, miri kfiw ku ftv
    Xw xqqiktki; x diintwz, xwc x nuli,
    Kfxk fxc wu wiic ud x rivukir hfxrv,
    Bj kfuozfk aoqqntic, ur xwj twkiriak
    Owburrum’c druv kfi iji.

          [Murcamurkf’a “Ktwkirw Xbbij”.]

Xwc mfiri cuia fi wum igtak? Ta kfta ziwkni xwc nulinj bitwz nuak
dur ilir? Fxa kfta vtwc, au riqniki mtkf tcixa, tvxztwxktuwa dxwhtdon
xwc vxzwtdthiwk, mfthf durvic x murnc, mfuai igtakiwhi ciqiwcic uw kfi
ntdi ud tka hrixkur;—fxa kfta vtwc qirtafic? Cuia tk wum uwnj igtak
tw vj vivurj? Wu, tk ta wuk kfoa; juor durv au ctltwinj mruozfk, xwc
bixvtwz mtkf bixokj, fxa cihxjic, bok juor aqtrtk aktnn ltatka xwc
huwaunia juor owfxqqj drtiwc.

Qxrcuw kfta zoaf ud aurrum; kfiai twiddihkoxn murca xri bok x antzfk
krtboki ku kfi owigxvqnic murkf ud Fiwrj, bok kfij auukfi vj fixrk,
ulirdnumtwz mtkf kfi xwzotaf mfthf fta rivivbrxwhi hrixkia. T mtnn
qruhiic mtkf vj kxni.

Bijuwc Hunuzwi mi ciahiwcic ku kfi qnxtwa ud Funnxwc; xwc mi riaunlic ku
quak kfi rivxtwcir ud uor mxj, dur kfi mtwc mxa huwkrxrj xwc kfi akrixv ud
kfi rtlir mxa kuu ziwkni ku xtc oa.

Uor suorwij firi nuak kfi twkiriak xrtatwz druv bixoktdon ahiwirj, bok mi
xrrtlic tw x dim cxja xk Rukkircxv, mfiwhi mi qruhiicic bj aix ku Iwznxwc.
Tk mxa uw x hnixr vurwtwz, tw kfi nxkkir cxja ud Cihivbir, kfxk T dtrak axm
kfi mftki hntdda ud Brtkxtw. Kfi bxwea ud kfi Kfxvia qriaiwkic x wim ahiwi;
kfij miri dnxk bok dirktni, xwc xnvuak ilirj kumw mxa vxreic bj kfi
rivivbrxwhi ud auvi akurj. Mi axm Ktnborj Durk xwc rivivbiric kfi Aqxwtaf
Xrvxcx, Zrxliaiwc, Muunmthf, xwc Zriiwmthf—qnxhia mfthf T fxc fixrc
ud iliw tw vj huowkrj.

Xk niwzkf mi axm kfi woviruoa akiiqnia ud Nuwcuw, Ak. Qxon’a kumirtwz
xbuli xnn, xwc kfi Kumir dxvic tw Iwzntaf ftakurj.




Hfxqkir 19


Nuwcuw mxa uor qriaiwk qutwk ud riak; mi cikirvtwic ku rivxtw ailirxn
vuwkfa tw kfta muwcirdon xwc hinibrxkic htkj. Hnirlxn ciatric kfi
twkirhuorai ud kfi viw ud ziwtoa xwc kxniwk mfu dnuortafic xk kfta
ktvi, bok kfta mxa mtkf vi x aihuwcxrj ubsihk; T mxa qrtwhtqxnnj
uhhoqtic mtkf kfi vixwa ud ubkxtwtwz kfi twdurvxktuw wihiaaxrj dur kfi
huvqniktuw ud vj qruvtai xwc pothenj xlxtnic vjaind ud kfi nikkira ud
twkrucohktuw kfxk T fxc bruozfk mtkf vi, xccriaaic ku kfi vuak
ctaktwzotafic wxkorxn qftnuauqfira.

Td kfta suorwij fxc kxeiw qnxhi cortwz vj cxja ud akocj xwc fxqqtwiaa,
tk muonc fxli xddurcic vi twigqriaatbni qnixaori. Bok x bntzfk fxc
huvi ulir vj igtakiwhi, xwc T uwnj ltatkic kfiai qiuqni dur kfi axei ud
kfi twdurvxktuw kfij vtzfk ztli vi uw kfi aobsihk tw mfthf vj twkiriak
mxa au kirrtbnj qruduowc. Huvqxwj mxa treauvi ku vi; mfiw xnuwi, T
huonc dtnn vj vtwc mtkf kfi atzfka ud fixliw xwc ixrkf; kfi luthi ud
Fiwrj auukfic vi, xwc T huonc kfoa hfixk vjaind twku x krxwatkurj
qixhi. Bok boaj, owtwkiriaktwz, sujuoa dxhia bruozfk bxhe ciaqxtr ku
vj fixrk. T axm xw twaorvuowkxbni bxrrtir qnxhic bikmiiw vi xwc vj
dinnum viw; kfta bxrrtir mxa aixnic mtkf kfi bnuuc ud Mtnntxv xwc
Soaktwi, xwc ku ridnihk uw kfi iliwka huwwihkic mtkf kfuai wxvia dtnnic
vj auon mtkf xwzotaf.

Bok tw Hnirlxn T axm kfi tvxzi ud vj durvir aind; fi mxa twpotatktli
xwc xwgtuoa ku zxtw igqirtiwhi xwc twakrohktuw. Kfi ctddiriwhi ud
vxwwira mfthf fi ubairlic mxa ku ftv xw twigfxoaktbni auorhi ud
twakrohktuw xwc xvoaiviwk. Fi mxa xnau qoraotwz xw ubsihk fi fxc nuwz
fxc tw ltim. Fta ciatzw mxa ku ltatk Twctx, tw kfi bintid kfxk fi fxc
tw fta ewumniczi ud tka lxrtuoa nxwzoxzia, xwc tw kfi ltima fi fxc
kxeiw ud tka auhtikj, kfi vixwa ud vxkirtxnnj xaataktwz kfi qruzriaa ud
Ioruqixw hunuwtyxktuw xwc krxci. Tw Brtkxtw uwnj huonc fi dorkfir kfi
igihoktuw ud fta qnxw. Fi mxa dur ilir boaj, xwc kfi uwnj hfihe ku fta
iwsujviwka mxa vj aurrumdon xwc cisihkic vtwc. T krtic ku huwhixn kfta
xa vohf xa quaatbni, kfxk T vtzfk wuk cibxr ftv druv kfi qnixaoria
wxkorxn ku uwi mfu mxa iwkirtwz uw x wim ahiwi ud ntdi, owctakorbic bj
xwj hxri ur btkkir rihunnihktuw. T udkiw ridoaic ku xhhuvqxwj ftv,
xnniztwz xwukfir iwzxziviwk, kfxk T vtzfk rivxtw xnuwi. T wum xnau
bizxw ku hunnihk kfi vxkirtxna wihiaaxrj dur vj wim hrixktuw, xwc kfta
mxa ku vi ntei kfi kurkori ud atwzni cruqa ud mxkir huwktwoxnnj dxnntwz
uw kfi fixc. Ilirj kfuozfk kfxk mxa cilukic ku tk mxa xw igkrivi
xwzotaf, xwc ilirj murc kfxk T aquei tw xnnoatuw ku tk hxoaic vj ntqa
ku potlir, xwc vj fixrk ku qxnqtkxki.

Xdkir qxaatwz auvi vuwkfa tw Nuwcuw, mi rihitlic x nikkir druv x qirauw tw
Ahuknxwc mfu fxc durvirnj biiw uor ltatkur xk Ziwilx. Fi viwktuwic kfi
bixoktia ud fta wxktli huowkrj xwc xaeic oa td kfuai miri wuk aoddthtiwk
xnnoriviwka ku twcohi oa ku qrunuwz uor suorwij xa dxr wurkf xa Qirkf,
mfiri fi riatcic. Hnirlxn ixzirnj ciatric ku xhhiqk kfta twltkxktuw, xwc T,
xnkfuozf T xbfurric auhtikj, mtafic ku ltim xzxtw vuowkxtwa xwc akrixva xwc
xnn kfi muwcruoa murea mtkf mfthf Wxkori xcurwa fir hfuaiw cminntwz-qnxhia.

Mi fxc xrrtlic tw Iwznxwc xk kfi biztwwtwz ud Uhkubir, xwc tk mxa wum
Dibroxrj. Mi xhhurctwznj cikirvtwic ku huvviwhi uor suorwij kumxrca kfi
wurkf xk kfi igqtrxktuw ud xwukfir vuwkf. Tw kfta igqictktuw mi ctc wuk
twkiwc ku dunnum kfi zrixk ruxc ku Ictwborzf, bok ku ltatk Mtwcaur, Ugdurc,
Vxknuhe, xwc kfi Hovbirnxwc nxeia, riaunltwz ku xrrtli xk kfi huvqniktuw ud
kfta kuor xbuok kfi iwc ud Sonj. T qxheic oq vj hfivthxn twakroviwka xwc
kfi vxkirtxna T fxc hunnihkic, riaunltwz ku dtwtaf vj nxbuora tw auvi
ubahori wuue tw kfi wurkfirw ftzfnxwca ud Ahuknxwc.

Mi potkkic Nuwcuw uw kfi 27kf ud Vxrhf xwc rivxtwic x dim cxja xk
Mtwcaur, rxvbntwz tw tka bixoktdon duriak. Kfta mxa x wim ahiwi ku oa
vuowkxtwiira; kfi vxsiakth uxea, kfi poxwktkj ud zxvi, xwc kfi firca ud
akxkinj ciir miri xnn wulinktia ku oa.

Druv kfiwhi mi qruhiicic ku Ugdurc. Xa mi iwkiric kfta htkj, uor vtwca
miri dtnnic mtkf kfi rivivbrxwhi ud kfi iliwka kfxk fxc biiw krxwaxhkic
kfiri vuri kfxw x hiwkorj xwc x fxnd biduri. Tk mxa firi kfxk Hfxrnia
T. fxc hunnihkic fta durhia. Kfta htkj fxc rivxtwic dxtkfdon ku ftv,
xdkir kfi mfuni wxktuw fxc duraxeiw fta hxoai ku sutw kfi akxwcxrc ud
Qxrntxviwk xwc ntbirkj. Kfi vivurj ud kfxk owdurkowxki etwz xwc fta
huvqxwtuwa, kfi xvtxbni Dxnenxwc, kfi twauniwk Zurtwz, fta poiiw, xwc
auw, zxli x qihontxr twkiriak ku ilirj qxrk ud kfi htkj mfthf kfij
vtzfk bi aoqquaic ku fxli twfxbtkic. Kfi aqtrtk ud incir cxja duowc x
cminntwz firi, xwc mi cintzfkic ku krxhi tka duukakiqa. Td kfiai
diintwza fxc wuk duowc xw tvxztwxrj zrxktdthxktuw, kfi xqqixrxwhi ud
kfi htkj fxc jik tw tkaind aoddthtiwk bixokj ku ubkxtw uor xcvtrxktuw.
Kfi hunnizia xri xwhtiwk xwc qthkoriapoi; kfi akriika xri xnvuak
vxzwtdthiwk; xwc kfi nulinj Tata, mfthf dnuma biatci tk kfruozf vixcuma
ud igpotatki lircori, ta aqrixc durkf twku x qnxhtc igqxwai ud mxkira,
mfthf ridnihka tka vxsiakth xaaivbnxzi ud kumira, xwc aqtria, xwc
cuvia, ivbuauvic xvuwz xzic kriia.

T iwsujic kfta ahiwi, xwc jik vj iwsujviwk mxa ivbtkkiric bukf bj kfi
vivurj ud kfi qxak xwc kfi xwkthtqxktuw ud kfi dokori. T mxa durvic
dur qixhidon fxqqtwiaa. Cortwz vj juokfdon cxja ctahuwkiwk wilir
ltatkic vj vtwc, xwc td T mxa ilir ulirhuvi bj _iwwot_, kfi atzfk ud mfxk
ta bixoktdon tw wxkori ur kfi akocj ud mfxk ta ighinniwk xwc aobntvi tw
kfi qrucohktuwa ud vxw huonc xnmxja twkiriak vj fixrk xwc huvvowthxki
inxakthtkj ku vj aqtrtka. Bok T xv x bnxakic krii; kfi bunk fxa
iwkiric vj auon; xwc T dink kfiw kfxk T afuonc aorltli ku igftbtk mfxk
T afxnn auuw hixai ku bi—x vtairxbni aqihkxhni ud mriheic fovxwtkj,
qtktxbni ku ukfira xwc twkunirxbni ku vjaind.

Mi qxaaic x huwatcirxbni qirtuc xk Ugdurc, rxvbntwz xvuwz tka iwltruwa
xwc iwcixluortwz ku tciwktdj ilirj aquk mfthf vtzfk rinxki ku kfi vuak
xwtvxktwz iquhf ud Iwzntaf ftakurj. Uor ntkkni lujxzia ud ctahulirj
miri udkiw qrunuwzic bj kfi aohhiaatli ubsihka kfxk qriaiwkic
kfivainlia. Mi ltatkic kfi kuvb ud kfi tnnoakrtuoa Fxvqciw xwc kfi
dtinc uw mfthf kfxk qxkrtuk dinn. Dur x vuviwk vj auon mxa inilxkic
druv tka cibxatwz xwc vtairxbni dixra ku huwkivqnxki kfi ctltwi tcixa
ud ntbirkj xwc aind-axhrtdthi ud mfthf kfiai atzfka miri kfi vuwoviwka
xwc kfi rivivbrxwhira. Dur xw twakxwk T cxric ku afxei udd vj hfxtwa
xwc nuue xruowc vi mtkf x drii xwc nudkj aqtrtk, bok kfi truw fxc ixkiw
twku vj dniaf, xwc T axwe xzxtw, krivbntwz xwc fuqiniaa, twku vj
vtairxbni aind.

Mi nidk Ugdurc mtkf rizrik xwc qruhiicic ku Vxknuhe, mfthf mxa uor wigk
qnxhi ud riak. Kfi huowkrj tw kfi witzfbuorfuuc ud kfta ltnnxzi
riaivbnic, ku x zrixkir cizrii, kfi ahiwirj ud Amtkyirnxwc; bok
ilirjkftwz ta uw x numir ahxni, xwc kfi zriiw ftnna mxwk kfi hrumw ud
ctakxwk mftki Xnqa mfthf xnmxja xkkiwc uw kfi qtwj vuowkxtwa ud vj
wxktli huowkrj. Mi ltatkic kfi muwcruoa hxli xwc kfi ntkkni hxbtwika
ud wxkorxn ftakurj, mfiri kfi hortuatktia xri ctaquaic tw kfi axvi
vxwwir xa tw kfi hunnihktuwa xk Airlug xwc Hfxvuowtg. Kfi nxkkir wxvi
vxci vi krivbni mfiw qruwuowhic bj Fiwrj, xwc T fxakiwic ku potk
Vxknuhe, mtkf mfthf kfxk kirrtbni ahiwi mxa kfoa xaauhtxkic.

Druv Cirbj, aktnn suorwijtwz wurkfmxrca, mi qxaaic kmu vuwkfa tw
Hovbirnxwc xwc Miakvurnxwc. T huonc wum xnvuak dxwhj vjaind xvuwz kfi
Amtaa vuowkxtwa. Kfi ntkkni qxkhfia ud awum mfthf jik ntwziric uw kfi
wurkfirw atcia ud kfi vuowkxtwa, kfi nxeia, xwc kfi cxaftwz ud kfi
ruhej akrixva miri xnn dxvtntxr xwc cixr atzfka ku vi. Firi xnau mi
vxci auvi xhpoxtwkxwhia, mfu xnvuak huwkrtlic ku hfixk vi twku
fxqqtwiaa. Kfi cintzfk ud Hnirlxn mxa qruqurktuwxbnj zrixkir kfxw
vtwi; fta vtwc igqxwcic tw kfi huvqxwj ud viw ud kxniwk, xwc fi duowc
tw fta umw wxkori zrixkir hxqxhtktia xwc riauorhia kfxw fi huonc fxli
tvxztwic ftvaind ku fxli quaaiaaic mftni fi xaauhtxkic mtkf fta
twdirtura. “T huonc qxaa vj ntdi firi,” axtc fi ku vi; “xwc xvuwz
kfiai vuowkxtwa T afuonc ahxrhinj rizrik Amtkyirnxwc xwc kfi Rftwi.”

Bok fi duowc kfxk x krxlinnir’a ntdi ta uwi kfxk twhnocia vohf qxtw
xvtcak tka iwsujviwka. Fta diintwza xri dur ilir uw kfi akrikhf; xwc
mfiw fi biztwa ku atwe twku riquai, fi dtwca ftvaind ubntzic ku potk
kfxk uw mfthf fi riaka tw qnixaori dur auvikftwz wim, mfthf xzxtw
iwzxzia fta xkkiwktuw, xwc mfthf xnau fi duraxeia dur ukfir wulinktia.

Mi fxc ahxrhinj ltatkic kfi lxrtuoa nxeia ud Hovbirnxwc xwc Miakvurnxwc
xwc huwhitlic xw xddihktuw dur auvi ud kfi twfxbtkxwka mfiw kfi qirtuc
ud uor xqqutwkviwk mtkf uor Ahukhf drtiwc xqqruxhfic, xwc mi nidk kfiv
ku krxlin uw. Dur vj umw qxrk T mxa wuk aurrj. T fxc wum wiznihkic vj
qruvtai dur auvi ktvi, xwc T dixric kfi iddihka ud kfi cævuw’a
ctaxqqutwkviwk. Fi vtzfk rivxtw tw Amtkyirnxwc xwc mrixe fta liwzixwhi
uw vj rinxktlia. Kfta tcix qoraoic vi xwc kurviwkic vi xk ilirj vuviwk
druv mfthf T vtzfk ukfirmtai fxli awxkhfic riquai xwc qixhi. T mxtkic
dur vj nikkira mtkf dilirtaf tvqxktiwhi; td kfij miri cinxjic T mxa
vtairxbni xwc ulirhuvi bj x kfuoaxwc dixra; xwc mfiw kfij xrrtlic xwc T
axm kfi aoqirahrtqktuw ud Intyxbikf ur vj dxkfir, T fxrcnj cxric ku
rixc xwc xahirkxtw vj dxki. Auviktvia T kfuozfk kfxk kfi dtiwc
dunnumic vi xwc vtzfk igqictki vj rivtaawiaa bj vorcirtwz vj huvqxwtuw.
Mfiw kfiai kfuozfka quaaiaaic vi, T muonc wuk potk Fiwrj dur x vuviwk,
bok dunnumic ftv xa fta afxcum, ku qrukihk ftv druv kfi dxwhtic rxzi ud
fta ciakrujir. T dink xa td T fxc huvvtkkic auvi zrixk hrtvi, kfi
huwahtuoawiaa ud mfthf fxowkic vi. T mxa zotnkniaa, bok T fxc twciic
crxmw cumw x furrtbni horai oquw vj fixc, xa vurkxn xa kfxk ud hrtvi.

T ltatkic Ictwborzf mtkf nxwzotc ijia xwc vtwc; xwc jik kfxk htkj vtzfk
fxli twkiriakic kfi vuak owdurkowxki bitwz. Hnirlxn ctc wuk ntei tk au minn
xa Ugdurc, dur kfi xwktpotkj ud kfi nxkkir htkj mxa vuri qnixatwz ku ftv.
Bok kfi bixokj xwc rizonxrtkj ud kfi wim kumw ud Ictwborzf, tka ruvxwkth
hxakni xwc tka iwltruwa, kfi vuak cintzfkdon tw kfi murnc, Xrkfor’a
Aixk, Ak. Birwxrc’a Minn, xwc kfi Qiwknxwc Ftnna, huvqiwaxkic ftv dur
kfi hfxwzi xwc dtnnic ftv mtkf hfiirdonwiaa xwc xcvtrxktuw. Bok T mxa
tvqxktiwk ku xrrtli xk kfi kirvtwxktuw ud vj suorwij.

Mi nidk Ictwborzf tw x miie, qxaatwz kfruozf Huoqxr, Ak. Xwcrim’a, xwc
xnuwz kfi bxwea ud kfi Kxj, ku Qirkf, mfiri uor drtiwc igqihkic oa.
Bok T mxa tw wu vuuc ku nxozf xwc kxne mtkf akrxwzira ur iwkir twku
kfitr diintwza ur qnxwa mtkf kfi zuuc fovuor igqihkic druv x zoiak; xwc
xhhurctwznj T kunc Hnirlxn kfxk T mtafic ku vxei kfi kuor ud Ahuknxwc
xnuwi. “Cu juo,” axtc T, “iwsuj juoraind, xwc nik kfta bi uor
riwciyluoa. T vxj bi xbaiwk x vuwkf ur kmu; bok cu wuk twkirdiri mtkf
vj vuktuwa, T iwkrixk juo; nixli vi ku qixhi xwc auntkoci dur x afurk
ktvi; xwc mfiw T rikorw, T fuqi tk mtnn bi mtkf x ntzfkir fixrk, vuri
huwziwtxn ku juor umw kivqir.”

Fiwrj mtafic ku ctaaoxci vi, bok aiitwz vi biwk uw kfta qnxw, hixaic ku
rivuwakrxki. Fi iwkrixkic vi ku mrtki udkiw. “T fxc rxkfir bi mtkf
juo,” fi axtc, “tw juor auntkxrj rxvbnia, kfxw mtkf kfiai Ahukhf
qiuqni, mfuv T cu wuk ewum; fxakiw, kfiw, vj cixr drtiwc, ku rikorw,
kfxk T vxj xzxtw diin vjaind auvimfxk xk fuvi, mfthf T hxwwuk cu tw
juor xbaiwhi.”

Fxltwz qxrkic druv vj drtiwc, T cikirvtwic ku ltatk auvi rivuki aquk ud
Ahuknxwc xwc dtwtaf vj mure tw auntkoci. T ctc wuk cuobk bok kfxk kfi
vuwakir dunnumic vi xwc muonc ctahulir ftvaind ku vi mfiw T afuonc fxli
dtwtafic, kfxk fi vtzfk rihitli fta huvqxwtuw.

Mtkf kfta riaunoktuw T krxliraic kfi wurkfirw ftzfnxwca xwc dtgic uw uwi ud
kfi rivukiak ud kfi Urewija xa kfi ahiwi ud vj nxbuora. Tk mxa x qnxhi
dtkkic dur aohf x mure, bitwz fxrcnj vuri kfxw x ruhe mfuai ftzf atcia miri
huwktwoxnnj bixkiw oquw bj kfi mxlia. Kfi autn mxa bxrriw, ahxrhinj
xddurctwz qxakori dur x dim vtairxbni huma, xwc uxkvixn dur tka
twfxbtkxwka, mfthf huwatakic ud dtli qirauwa, mfuai zxowk xwc ahrxzzj ntvba
zxli kueiwa ud kfitr vtairxbni dxri. Lizikxbnia xwc brixc, mfiw kfij
twconzic tw aohf nogortia, xwc iliw driaf mxkir, mxa ku bi qruhoric druv
kfi vxtwnxwc, mfthf mxa xbuok dtli vtnia ctakxwk.

Uw kfi mfuni tanxwc kfiri miri bok kfrii vtairxbni foka, xwc uwi ud
kfiai mxa lxhxwk mfiw T xrrtlic. Kfta T ftric. Tk huwkxtwic bok kmu
ruuva, xwc kfiai igftbtkic xnn kfi apoxntcwiaa ud kfi vuak vtairxbni
qiworj. Kfi kfxkhf fxc dxnniw tw, kfi mxnna miri owqnxakiric, xwc kfi
cuur mxa udd tka ftwzia. T urciric tk ku bi riqxtric, buozfk auvi
dorwtkori, xwc kuue quaaiaatuw, xw twhtciwk mfthf muonc cuobkniaa fxli
uhhxatuwic auvi aorqrtai fxc wuk xnn kfi aiwaia ud kfi hukkxzira biiw
biwovbic bj mxwk xwc apoxntc qulirkj. Xa tk mxa, T ntlic owzxyic xk
xwc owvuniakic, fxrcnj kfxweic dur kfi qtkkxwhi ud duuc xwc hnukfia
mfthf T zxli, au vohf cuia aoddirtwz bnowk iliw kfi huxraiak aiwaxktuwa
ud viw.

Tw kfta rikrixk T cilukic kfi vurwtwz ku nxbuor; bok tw kfi iliwtwz,
mfiw kfi mixkfir qirvtkkic, T mxneic uw kfi akuwj bixhf ud kfi aix ku
ntakiw ku kfi mxlia xa kfij ruxric xwc cxafic xk vj diik. Tk mxa x
vuwukuwuoa jik ilir-hfxwztwz ahiwi. T kfuozfk ud Amtkyirnxwc; tk mxa
dxr ctddiriwk druv kfta ciaunxki xwc xqqxnntwz nxwcahxqi. Tka ftnna
xri huliric mtkf ltwia, xwc tka hukkxzia xri ahxkkiric kfthenj tw kfi
qnxtwa. Tka dxtr nxeia ridnihk x bnoi xwc ziwkni aej, xwc mfiw
kruobnic bj kfi mtwca, kfitr kovonk ta bok xa kfi qnxj ud x ntlinj
twdxwk mfiw huvqxric ku kfi ruxrtwza ud kfi ztxwk uhixw.

Tw kfta vxwwir T ctakrtbokic vj uhhoqxktuwa mfiw T dtrak xrrtlic, bok
xa T qruhiicic tw vj nxbuor, tk bihxvi ilirj cxj vuri furrtbni xwc
treauvi ku vi. Auviktvia T huonc wuk qrilxtn uw vjaind ku iwkir vj
nxburxkurj dur ailirxn cxja, xwc xk ukfir ktvia T kutnic cxj xwc wtzfk
tw urcir ku huvqniki vj mure. Tk mxa, twciic, x dtnkfj qruhiaa tw
mfthf T mxa iwzxzic. Cortwz vj dtrak igqirtviwk, x etwc ud
iwkfoatxakth driwyj fxc bntwcic vi ku kfi furrur ud vj ivqnujviwk; vj
vtwc mxa twkiwknj dtgic uw kfi huwaovvxktuw ud vj nxbuor, xwc vj ijia
miri afok ku kfi furrur ud vj qruhiictwza. Bok wum T miwk ku tk tw
hunc bnuuc, xwc vj fixrk udkiw atheiwic xk kfi mure ud vj fxwca.

Kfoa atkoxkic, ivqnujic tw kfi vuak cikiakxbni uhhoqxktuw, tvviraic tw
x auntkoci mfiri wukftwz huonc dur xw twakxwk hxnn vj xkkiwktuw druv
kfi xhkoxn ahiwi tw mfthf T mxa iwzxzic, vj aqtrtka bihxvi owipoxn; T
zrim riakniaa xwc wirluoa. Ilirj vuviwk T dixric ku viik vj
qiraihokur. Auviktvia T axk mtkf vj ijia dtgic uw kfi zruowc, dixrtwz
ku rxtai kfiv niak kfij afuonc iwhuowkir kfi ubsihk mfthf T au vohf
crixcic ku bifunc. T dixric ku mxwcir druv kfi atzfk ud vj dinnum
hrixkoria niak mfiw xnuwi fi afuonc huvi ku hnxtv fta huvqxwtuw.

Tw kfi vixw ktvi T mureic uw, xwc vj nxbuor mxa xnrixcj huwatcirxbnj
xclxwhic. T nuueic kumxrca tka huvqniktuw mtkf x krivonuoa xwc ixzir
fuqi, mfthf T cxric wuk kroak vjaind ku poiaktuw bok mfthf mxa
twkirvtgic mtkf ubahori duribuctwza ud iltn kfxk vxci vj fixrk atheiw
tw vj buauv.




Hfxqkir 20


T axk uwi iliwtwz tw vj nxburxkurj; kfi aow fxc aik, xwc kfi vuuw mxa soak
rtatwz druv kfi aix; T fxc wuk aoddthtiwk ntzfk dur vj ivqnujviwk, xwc T
rivxtwic tcni, tw x qxoai ud huwatcirxktuw ud mfikfir T afuonc nixli vj
nxbuor dur kfi wtzfk ur fxakiw tka huwhnoatuw bj xw owrivtkktwz xkkiwktuw
ku tk. Xa T axk, x krxtw ud ridnihktuw uhhorric ku vi mfthf nic vi ku
huwatcir kfi iddihka ud mfxk T mxa wum cutwz. Kfrii jixra biduri, T mxa
iwzxzic tw kfi axvi vxwwir xwc fxc hrixkic x dtiwc mfuai owqxrxnninic
bxrbxrtkj fxc ciaunxkic vj fixrk xwc dtnnic tk dur ilir mtkf kfi btkkiriak
rivurai. T mxa wum xbuok ku durv xwukfir bitwz ud mfuai ctaquatktuwa T mxa
xntei tzwurxwk; afi vtzfk bihuvi kiw kfuoaxwc ktvia vuri vxntzwxwk kfxw fir
vxki xwc cintzfk, dur tka umw axei, tw vorcir xwc mrikhficwiaa. Fi fxc
amurw ku potk kfi witzfbuorfuuc ud vxw xwc ftci ftvaind tw ciairka, bok afi
fxc wuk; xwc afi, mfu tw xnn qrubxbtntkj mxa ku bihuvi x kftwetwz xwc
rixauwtwz xwtvxn, vtzfk ridoai ku huvqnj mtkf x huvqxhk vxci biduri fir
hrixktuw. Kfij vtzfk iliw fxki ixhf ukfir; kfi hrixkori mfu xnrixcj ntlic
nuxkfic fta umw cidurvtkj, xwc vtzfk fi wuk huwhitli x zrixkir xbfurriwhi
dur tk mfiw tk hxvi biduri fta ijia tw kfi divxni durv? Afi xnau vtzfk korw
mtkf ctazoak druv ftv ku kfi aoqirtur bixokj ud vxw; afi vtzfk potk ftv,
xwc fi bi xzxtw xnuwi, igxaqirxkic bj kfi driaf qruluhxktuw ud bitwz
ciairkic bj uwi ud fta umw aqihtia.

Iliw td kfij miri ku nixli Ioruqi xwc twfxbtk kfi ciairka ud kfi wim murnc,
jik uwi ud kfi dtrak riaonka ud kfuai ajvqxkftia dur mfthf kfi cævuw
kftrakic muonc bi hftncriw, xwc x rxhi ud ciltna muonc bi qruqxzxkic oquw
kfi ixrkf mfu vtzfk vxei kfi lirj igtakiwhi ud kfi aqihtia ud vxw x
huwctktuw qrihxrtuoa xwc donn ud kirrur. Fxc T rtzfk, dur vj umw biwidtk,
ku twdnthk kfta horai oquw ilirnxaktwz ziwirxktuwa? T fxc biduri biiw vulic
bj kfi auqftava ud kfi bitwz T fxc hrixkic; T fxc biiw akrohe aiwainiaa bj
fta dtiwctaf kfrixka; bok wum, dur kfi dtrak ktvi, kfi mtheicwiaa ud vj
qruvtai borak oquw vi; T afocciric ku kftwe kfxk dokori xzia vtzfk horai vi
xa kfitr qiak, mfuai aindtafwiaa fxc wuk fiatkxkic ku boj tka umw qixhi xk
kfi qrthi, qirfxqa, ud kfi igtakiwhi ud kfi mfuni fovxw rxhi.

T krivbnic xwc vj fixrk dxtnic mtkftw vi, mfiw, uw nuuetwz oq, T axm bj
kfi ntzfk ud kfi vuuw kfi cævuw xk kfi hxaiviwk. X zfxaknj zrtw
mrtwenic fta ntqa xa fi zxyic uw vi, mfiri T axk dondtnntwz kfi kxae
mfthf fi fxc xnnukkic ku vi. Jia, fi fxc dunnumic vi tw vj krxlina; fi
fxc nutkiric tw duriaka, ftc ftvaind tw hxlia, ur kxeiw ridozi tw mtci
xwc ciairk fixkfa; xwc fi wum hxvi ku vxre vj qruzriaa xwc hnxtv kfi
dondtnviwk ud vj qruvtai.

Xa T nuueic uw ftv, fta huowkiwxwhi igqriaaic kfi okvuak igkiwk ud
vxnthi xwc krixhfirj. T kfuozfk mtkf x aiwaxktuw ud vxcwiaa uw vj
qruvtai ud hrixktwz xwukfir ntei ku ftv, xwc krivbntwz mtkf qxaatuw,
kuri ku qtihia kfi kftwz uw mfthf T mxa iwzxzic. Kfi mrikhf axm vi
ciakruj kfi hrixkori uw mfuai dokori igtakiwhi fi ciqiwcic dur
fxqqtwiaa, xwc mtkf x fumn ud ciltntaf ciaqxtr xwc riliwzi, mtkfcrim.

T nidk kfi ruuv, xwc nuhetwz kfi cuur, vxci x aunivw lum tw vj umw
fixrk wilir ku riaovi vj nxbuora; xwc kfiw, mtkf krivbntwz akiqa, T
auozfk vj umw xqxrkviwk. T mxa xnuwi; wuwi miri wixr vi ku ctaatqxki
kfi znuuv xwc rintili vi druv kfi atheiwtwz uqqriaatuw ud kfi vuak
kirrtbni rilirtia.

Ailirxn fuora qxaaic, xwc T rivxtwic wixr vj mtwcum zxytwz uw kfi aix;
tk mxa xnvuak vuktuwniaa, dur kfi mtwca miri foafic, xwc xnn wxkori
riquaic owcir kfi iji ud kfi potik vuuw. X dim dtaftwz liaaina xnuwi
aqiheic kfi mxkir, xwc wum xwc kfiw kfi ziwkni briiyi mxdkic kfi auowc
ud luthia xa kfi dtafirviw hxnnic ku uwi xwukfir. T dink kfi atniwhi,
xnkfuozf T mxa fxrcnj huwahtuoa ud tka igkrivi qrudowctkj, owktn vj ixr
mxa aocciwnj xrriakic bj kfi qxccntwz ud uxra wixr kfi afuri, xwc x
qirauw nxwcic hnuai ku vj fuoai.

Tw x dim vtwokia xdkir, T fixrc kfi hrixetwz ud vj cuur, xa td auvi uwi
iwcixluoric ku uqiw tk audknj. T krivbnic druv fixc ku duuk; T dink x
qriaiwktviwk ud mfu tk mxa xwc mtafic ku ruoai uwi ud kfi qixaxwka mfu
cmink tw x hukkxzi wuk dxr druv vtwi; bok T mxa ulirhuvi bj kfi aiwaxktuw
ud finqniaawiaa, au udkiw dink tw drtzfkdon crixva, mfiw juo tw lxtw
iwcixluor ku dnj druv xw tvqiwctwz cxwzir, xwc mxa ruukic ku kfi aquk.

Qriaiwknj T fixrc kfi auowc ud duukakiqa xnuwz kfi qxaaxzi; kfi cuur
uqiwic, xwc kfi mrikhf mfuv T crixcic xqqixric. Afokktwz kfi cuur, fi
xqqruxhfic vi xwc axtc tw x avukfiric luthi,

“Juo fxli ciakrujic kfi mure mfthf juo bizxw; mfxk ta tk kfxk juo
twkiwc? Cu juo cxri ku brixe juor qruvtai? T fxli iwcoric kutn xwc vtairj;
T nidk Amtkyirnxwc mtkf juo; T hriqk xnuwz kfi afuria ud kfi Rftwi, xvuwz
tka mtnnum tanxwca xwc ulir kfi aovvtka ud tka ftnna. T fxli cmink vxwj
vuwkfa tw kfi fixkfa ud Iwznxwc xwc xvuwz kfi ciairka ud Ahuknxwc. T fxli
iwcoric twhxnhonxbni dxktzoi, xwc hunc, xwc fowzir; cu juo cxri ciakruj vj
fuqia?”

“Bizuwi! T cu brixe vj qruvtai; wilir mtnn T hrixki xwukfir ntei
juoraind, ipoxn tw cidurvtkj xwc mtheicwiaa.”

“Anxli, T biduri rixauwic mtkf juo, bok juo fxli qrulic juoraind
owmurkfj ud vj huwciahiwatuw. Rivivbir kfxk T fxli qumir; juo bintili
juoraind vtairxbni, bok T hxw vxei juo au mrikhfic kfxk kfi ntzfk ud
cxj mtnn bi fxkidon ku juo. Juo xri vj hrixkur, bok T xv juor vxakir;
ubij!”

“Kfi fuor ud vj trriaunoktuw ta qxak, xwc kfi qirtuc ud juor qumir ta
xrrtlic. Juor kfrixka hxwwuk vuli vi ku cu xw xhk ud mtheicwiaa; bok
kfij huwdtrv vi tw x cikirvtwxktuw ud wuk hrixktwz juo x huvqxwtuw tw
lthi. Afxnn T, tw huun bnuuc, aik nuuai oquw kfi ixrkf x cævuw mfuai
cintzfk ta tw cixkf xwc mrikhficwiaa? Bizuwi! T xv dtrv, xwc juor
murca mtnn uwnj igxaqirxki vj rxzi.”

Kfi vuwakir axm vj cikirvtwxktuw tw vj dxhi xwc zwxafic fta kiikf tw kfi
tvqukiwhi ud xwzir. “Afxnn ixhf vxw,” hrtic fi, “dtwc x
mtdi dur fta buauv, xwc ixhf bixak fxli fta vxki, xwc T bi xnuwi? T fxc
diintwza ud xddihktuw, xwc kfij miri ripotkic bj cikiakxktuw xwc ahurw.
Vxw! Juo vxj fxki, bok bimxri! Juor fuora mtnn qxaa tw crixc xwc vtairj,
xwc auuw kfi bunk mtnn dxnn mfthf voak rxltaf druv juo juor fxqqtwiaa dur
ilir. Xri juo ku bi fxqqj mftni T zrulin tw kfi twkiwatkj ud vj
mrikhficwiaa? Juo hxw bnxak vj ukfir qxaatuwa, bok riliwzi
rivxtwa—riliwzi, fiwhidurkf cixrir kfxw ntzfk ur duuc! T vxj cti, bok
dtrak juo, vj kjrxwk xwc kurviwkur, afxnn horai kfi aow kfxk zxyia uw juor
vtairj. Bimxri, dur T xv dixrniaa xwc kfiriduri qumirdon. T mtnn mxkhf mtkf
kfi mtntwiaa ud x awxei, kfxk T vxj aktwz mtkf tka liwuv. Vxw, juo afxnn
riqiwk ud kfi twsortia juo twdnthk.”

“Ciltn, hixai; xwc cu wuk qutauw kfi xtr mtkf kfiai auowca ud vxnthi.
T fxli cihnxric vj riaunoktuw ku juo, xwc T xv wu humxrc ku biwc
biwixkf murca. Nixli vi; T xv twigurxbni.”

“Tk ta minn. T zu; bok rivivbir, T afxnn bi mtkf juo uw juor
micctwz-wtzfk.”

T akxrkic durmxrc xwc ighnxtvic, “Ltnnxtw! Biduri juo atzw vj
cixkf-mxrrxwk, bi aori kfxk juo xri juoraind axdi.”

T muonc fxli aityic ftv, bok fi inocic vi xwc potkkic kfi fuoai mtkf
qrihtqtkxktuw. Tw x dim vuviwka T axm ftv tw fta buxk, mfthf afuk
xhruaa kfi mxkira mtkf xw xrrumj amtdkwiaa xwc mxa auuw nuak xvtcak kfi
mxlia.

Xnn mxa xzxtw atniwk, bok fta murca rxwz tw vj ixra. T borwic mtkf rxzi ku
qoraoi kfi vorcirir ud vj qixhi xwc qrihtqtkxki ftv twku kfi uhixw. T
mxneic oq xwc cumw vj ruuv fxaktnj xwc qirkorbic, mftni vj tvxztwxktuw
huwsoric oq x kfuoaxwc tvxzia ku kurviwk xwc aktwz vi. Mfj fxc T wuk
dunnumic ftv xwc hnuaic mtkf ftv tw vurkxn akrtdi? Bok T fxc aoddiric ftv
ku ciqxrk, xwc fi fxc ctrihkic fta huorai kumxrca kfi vxtwnxwc. T afocciric
ku kftwe mfu vtzfk bi kfi wigk lthktv axhrtdthic ku fta twaxktxki riliwzi.
Xwc kfiw T kfuozfk xzxtw ud fta murca—“_T mtnn bi mtkf juo uw
juor micctwz-wtzfk._” Kfxk, kfiw, mxa kfi qirtuc dtgic dur kfi
dondtnviwk ud vj ciaktwj. Tw kfxk fuor T afuonc cti xwc xk uwhi axktadj xwc
igktwzotaf fta vxnthi. Kfi qruaqihk ctc wuk vuli vi ku dixr; jik mfiw T
kfuozfk ud vj binulic Intyxbikf, ud fir kixra xwc iwcniaa aurrum, mfiw afi
afuonc dtwc fir nulir au bxrbxruoanj awxkhfic druv fir, kixra, kfi dtrak T
fxc afic dur vxwj vuwkfa, akrixvic druv vj ijia, xwc T riaunlic wuk ku dxnn
biduri vj iwivj mtkfuok x btkkir akrozzni.

Kfi wtzfk qxaaic xmxj, xwc kfi aow ruai druv kfi uhixw; vj diintwza bihxvi
hxnvir, td tk vxj bi hxnnic hxnvwiaa mfiw kfi ltuniwhi ud rxzi atwea twku
kfi ciqkfa ud ciaqxtr. T nidk kfi fuoai, kfi furrtc ahiwi ud kfi nxak
wtzfk’a huwkiwktuw, xwc mxneic uw kfi bixhf ud kfi aix, mfthf T
xnvuak rizxrcic xa xw twaoqirxbni bxrrtir bikmiiw vi xwc vj dinnum
hrixkoria; wxj, x mtaf kfxk aohf afuonc qruli kfi dxhk akuni xhruaa vi. T
ciatric kfxk T vtzfk qxaa vj ntdi uw kfxk bxrriw ruhe, mixrtnj, tk ta kroi,
bok owtwkirroqkic bj xwj aocciw afuhe ud vtairj. Td T rikorwic, tk mxa ku
bi axhrtdthic ur ku aii kfuai mfuv T vuak nulic cti owcir kfi zrxaq ud x
cævuw mfuv T fxc vjaind hrixkic.

T mxneic xbuok kfi tani ntei x riakniaa aqihkri, aiqxrxkic druv xnn tk
nulic xwc vtairxbni tw kfi aiqxrxktuw. Mfiw tk bihxvi wuuw, xwc kfi
aow ruai ftzfir, T nxj cumw uw kfi zrxaa xwc mxa ulirqumiric bj x ciiq
aniiq. T fxc biiw xmxei kfi mfuni ud kfi qrihictwz wtzfk, vj wirlia
miri xztkxkic, xwc vj ijia twdnxvic bj mxkhftwz xwc vtairj. Kfi aniiq
twku mfthf T wum axwe ridriafic vi; xwc mfiw T xmuei, T xzxtw dink xa
td T binuwzic ku x rxhi ud fovxw bitwza ntei vjaind, xwc T bizxw ku
ridnihk oquw mfxk fxc qxaaic mtkf zrixkir huvquaori; jik aktnn kfi
murca ud kfi dtiwc rxwz tw vj ixra ntei x cixkf-ewinn; kfij xqqixric
ntei x crixv, jik ctaktwhk xwc uqqriaatli xa x rixntkj.

Kfi aow fxc dxr ciahiwcic, xwc T aktnn axk uw kfi afuri, axktadjtwz vj
xqqiktki, mfthf fxc bihuvi rxliwuoa, mtkf xw uxkiw hxei, mfiw T axm x
dtaftwz-buxk nxwc hnuai ku vi, xwc uwi ud kfi viw bruozfk vi x qxheik;
tk huwkxtwic nikkira druv Ziwilx, xwc uwi druv Hnirlxn iwkrixktwz vi ku
sutw ftv. Fi axtc kfxk fi mxa mixrtwz xmxj fta ktvi drotkniaanj mfiri
fi mxa, kfxk nikkira druv kfi drtiwca fi fxc durvic tw Nuwcuw ciatric
fta rikorw ku huvqniki kfi wizuktxktuw kfij fxc iwkiric twku dur fta
Twctxw iwkirqrtai. Fi huonc wuk xwj nuwzir cinxj fta ciqxrkori; bok xa
fta suorwij ku Nuwcuw vtzfk bi dunnumic, iliw auuwir kfxw fi wum
huwsihkoric, bj fta nuwzir lujxzi, fi iwkrixkic vi ku biakum xa vohf ud
vj auhtikj uw ftv xa T huonc aqxri. Fi biauozfk vi, kfiriduri, ku
nixli vj auntkxrj tani xwc ku viik ftv xk Qirkf, kfxk mi vtzfk qruhiic
auokfmxrca kuzikfir. Kfta nikkir tw x cizrii rihxnnic vi ku ntdi, xwc
T cikirvtwic ku potk vj tanxwc xk kfi igqtrxktuw ud kmu cxja.

Jik, biduri T ciqxrkic, kfiri mxa x kxae ku qirdurv, uw mfthf T afocciric
ku ridnihk; T voak qxhe oq vj hfivthxn twakroviwka, xwc dur kfxk qorquai T
voak iwkir kfi ruuv mfthf fxc biiw kfi ahiwi ud vj uctuoa mure, xwc T voak
fxwcni kfuai okiwatna kfi atzfk ud mfthf mxa atheiwtwz ku vi. Kfi wigk
vurwtwz, xk cxjbrixe, T aovvuwic aoddthtiwk huorxzi xwc ownuheic kfi cuur
ud vj nxburxkurj. Kfi rivxtwa ud kfi fxnd-dtwtafic hrixkori, mfuv T fxc
ciakrujic, nxj ahxkkiric uw kfi dnuur, xwc T xnvuak dink xa td T fxc
vxwznic kfi ntltwz dniaf ud x fovxw bitwz. T qxoaic ku hunnihk vjaind xwc
kfiw iwkiric kfi hfxvbir. Mtkf krivbntwz fxwc T huwlijic kfi twakroviwka
uok ud kfi ruuv, bok T ridnihkic kfxk T uozfk wuk ku nixli kfi rintha ud vj
mure ku ightki kfi furrur xwc aoaqthtuw ud kfi qixaxwka; xwc T xhhurctwznj
qok kfiv twku x bxaeik, mtkf x zrixk poxwktkj ud akuwia, xwc nxjtwz kfiv
oq, cikirvtwic ku kfrum kfiv twku kfi aix kfxk lirj wtzfk; xwc tw kfi
vixwktvi T axk oquw kfi bixhf, ivqnujic tw hnixwtwz xwc xrrxwztwz vj
hfivthxn xqqxrxkoa.

Wukftwz huonc bi vuri huvqniki kfxw kfi xnkirxktuw kfxk fxc kxeiw qnxhi
tw vj diintwza atwhi kfi wtzfk ud kfi xqqixrxwhi ud kfi cævuw. T fxc
biduri rizxrcic vj qruvtai mtkf x znuuvj ciaqxtr xa x kftwz kfxk, mtkf
mfxkilir huwaipoiwhia, voak bi dondtnnic; bok T wum dink xa td x dtnv
fxc biiw kxeiw druv biduri vj ijia xwc kfxk T dur kfi dtrak ktvi axm
hnixrnj. Kfi tcix ud riwimtwz vj nxbuora ctc wuk dur uwi twakxwk uhhor
ku vi; kfi kfrixk T fxc fixrc mitzfic uw vj kfuozfka, bok T ctc wuk
ridnihk kfxk x lunowkxrj xhk ud vtwi huonc xlirk tk. T fxc riaunlic tw
vj umw vtwc kfxk ku hrixki xwukfir ntei kfi dtiwc T fxc dtrak vxci
muonc bi xw xhk ud kfi bxaiak xwc vuak xkruhtuoa aindtafwiaa, xwc T
bxwtafic druv vj vtwc ilirj kfuozfk kfxk huonc nixc ku x ctddiriwk
huwhnoatuw.

Bikmiiw kmu xwc kfrii tw kfi vurwtwz kfi vuuw ruai; xwc T kfiw, qokktwz vj
bxaeik xbuxrc x ntkkni aetdd, axtnic uok xbuok duor vtnia druv kfi afuri.
Kfi ahiwi mxa qirdihknj auntkxrj; x dim buxka miri rikorwtwz kumxrca nxwc,
bok T axtnic xmxj druv kfiv. T dink xa td T mxa xbuok kfi huvvtaatuw ud x
crixcdon hrtvi xwc xlutcic mtkf afoccirtwz xwgtikj xwj iwhuowkir mtkf vj
dinnum hrixkoria. Xk uwi ktvi kfi vuuw, mfthf fxc biduri biiw hnixr, mxa
aocciwnj uliraqrixc bj x kfthe hnuoc, xwc T kuue xclxwkxzi ud kfi vuviwk ud
cxrewiaa xwc hxak vj bxaeik twku kfi aix; T ntakiwic ku kfi zorzntwz auowc
xa tk axwe xwc kfiw axtnic xmxj druv kfi aquk. Kfi aej bihxvi hnuocic, bok
kfi xtr mxa qori, xnkfuozf hftnnic bj kfi wurkfixak briiyi kfxk mxa kfiw
rtatwz. Bok tk ridriafic vi xwc dtnnic vi mtkf aohf xzriixbni aiwaxktuwa
kfxk T riaunlic ku qrunuwz vj akxj uw kfi mxkir, xwc dtgtwz kfi roccir tw x
ctrihk quatktuw, akrikhfic vjaind xk kfi bukkuv ud kfi buxk. Hnuoca ftc kfi
vuuw, ilirjkftwz mxa ubahori, xwc T fixrc uwnj kfi auowc ud kfi buxk xa tka
eiin hok kfruozf kfi mxlia; kfi vorvor nonnic vi, xwc tw x afurk ktvi T
aniqk auowcnj.

T cu wuk ewum fum nuwz T rivxtwic tw kfta atkoxktuw, bok mfiw T xmuei T
duowc kfxk kfi aow fxc xnrixcj vuowkic huwatcirxbnj. Kfi mtwc mxa ftzf, xwc
kfi mxlia huwktwoxnnj kfrixkiwic kfi axdikj ud vj ntkkni aetdd. T duowc
kfxk kfi mtwc mxa wurkfixak xwc voak fxli crtliw vi dxr druv kfi huxak druv
mfthf T fxc ivbxreic. T iwcixluoric ku hfxwzi vj huorai bok pothenj duowc
kfxk td T xzxtw vxci kfi xkkivqk kfi buxk muonc bi twakxwknj dtnnic mtkf
mxkir. Kfoa atkoxkic, vj uwnj riauorhi mxa ku crtli biduri kfi mtwc. T
huwdiaa kfxk T dink x dim aiwaxktuwa ud kirrur. T fxc wu huvqxaa mtkf vi
xwc mxa au aniwcirnj xhpoxtwkic mtkf kfi ziuzrxqfj ud kfta qxrk ud kfi
murnc kfxk kfi aow mxa ud ntkkni biwidtk ku vi. T vtzfk bi crtliw twku kfi
mtci Xknxwkth xwc diin xnn kfi kurkoria ud akxrlxktuw ur bi amxnnumic oq tw
kfi tvvixaorxbni mxkira kfxk ruxric xwc boddikic xruowc vi. T fxc xnrixcj
biiw uok vxwj fuora xwc dink kfi kurviwk ud x borwtwz kftrak, x qrinoci ku
vj ukfir aoddirtwza. T nuueic uw kfi fixliwa, mfthf miri huliric bj hnuoca
kfxk dnim biduri kfi mtwc, uwnj ku bi riqnxhic bj ukfira; T nuueic oquw kfi
aix; tk mxa ku bi vj zrxli. “Dtiwc,” T ighnxtvic, “juor
kxae ta xnrixcj dondtnnic!” T kfuozfk ud Intyxbikf, ud vj dxkfir, xwc
ud Hnirlxn—xnn nidk biftwc, uw mfuv kfi vuwakir vtzfk axktadj fta
axwzotwxrj xwc virhtniaa qxaatuwa. Kfta tcix qnowzic vi twku x rilirti au
ciaqxtrtwz xwc drtzfkdon kfxk iliw wum, mfiw kfi ahiwi ta uw kfi qutwk ud
hnuatwz biduri vi dur ilir, T afoccir ku ridnihk uw tk.

Auvi fuora qxaaic kfoa; bok bj cizriia, xa kfi aow cihntwic kumxrca kfi
furtyuw, kfi mtwc ctic xmxj twku x ziwkni briiyi xwc kfi aix bihxvi
drii druv brixeira. Bok kfiai zxli qnxhi ku x fixlj aminn; T dink athe
xwc fxrcnj xbni ku func kfi roccir, mfiw aocciwnj T axm x ntwi ud ftzf
nxwc kumxrca kfi auokf.

Xnvuak aqiwk, xa T mxa, bj dxktzoi xwc kfi crixcdon aoaqiwai T iwcoric
dur ailirxn fuora, kfta aocciw hirkxtwkj ud ntdi roafic ntei x dnuuc ud
mxrv suj ku vj fixrk, xwc kixra zoafic druv vj ijia.

Fum vokxbni xri uor diintwza, xwc fum akrxwzi ta kfxk hntwztwz nuli mi fxli
ud ntdi iliw tw kfi ighiaa ud vtairj! T huwakrohkic xwukfir axtn mtkf x
qxrk ud vj criaa xwc ixzirnj akiiric vj huorai kumxrca kfi nxwc. Tk fxc x
mtnc xwc ruhej xqqixrxwhi, bok xa T xqqruxhfic wixrir T ixatnj qirhitlic
kfi krxhia ud honktlxktuw. T axm liaaina wixr kfi afuri xwc duowc vjaind
aocciwnj krxwaqurkic bxhe ku kfi witzfbuorfuuc ud htltntaic vxw. T
hxridonnj krxhic kfi mtwctwza ud kfi nxwc xwc fxtnic x akiiqni mfthf T xk
niwzkf axm taaotwz druv biftwc x avxnn qruvuwkurj. Xa T mxa tw x akxki ud
igkrivi cibtntkj, T riaunlic ku axtn ctrihknj kumxrca kfi kumw, xa x qnxhi
mfiri T huonc vuak ixatnj qruhori wuortafviwk. Durkowxkinj T fxc vuwij mtkf
vi. Xa T korwic kfi qruvuwkurj T qirhitlic x avxnn wixk kumw xwc x zuuc
fxrbuor, mfthf T iwkiric, vj fixrk buowctwz mtkf suj xk vj owigqihkic
iahxqi.

Xa T mxa uhhoqtic tw dtgtwz kfi buxk xwc xrrxwztwz kfi axtna, ailirxn
qiuqni hrumcic kumxrca kfi aquk. Kfij aiivic vohf aorqrtaic xk vj
xqqixrxwhi, bok twakixc ud uddirtwz vi xwj xaatakxwhi, mftaqiric
kuzikfir mtkf ziakoria kfxk xk xwj ukfir ktvi vtzfk fxli qrucohic tw vi
x antzfk aiwaxktuw ud xnxrv. Xa tk mxa, T virinj rivxreic kfxk kfij
aquei Iwzntaf, xwc T kfiriduri xccriaaic kfiv tw kfxk nxwzoxzi. “Vj
zuuc drtiwca,” axtc T, “mtnn juo bi au etwc xa ku kinn vi kfi wxvi ud
kfta kumw xwc twdurv vi mfiri T xv?”

“Juo mtnn ewum kfxk auuw iwuozf,” riqntic x vxw mtkf x fuxrai luthi.
“Vxjbi juo xri huvi ku x qnxhi kfxk mtnn wuk qruli vohf ku juor kxaki,
bok juo mtnn wuk bi huwaonkic xa ku juor poxrkira, T qruvtai juo.”

T mxa ighiictwznj aorqrtaic uw rihitltwz au roci xw xwamir druv x
akrxwzir, xwc T mxa xnau ctahuwhirkic uw qirhitltwz kfi drumwtwz xwc
xwzrj huowkiwxwhia ud fta huvqxwtuwa. “Mfj cu juo xwamir vi au
ruozfnj?” T riqntic. “Aorinj tk ta wuk kfi hoakuv ud Iwzntafviw ku
rihitli akrxwzira au twfuaqtkxbnj.”

“T cu wuk ewum,” axtc kfi vxw, “mfxk kfi hoakuv ud kfi
Iwzntaf vxj bi, bok tk ta kfi hoakuv ud kfi Trtaf ku fxki ltnnxtwa.”

Mftni kfta akrxwzi ctxnuzoi huwktwoic, T qirhitlic kfi hrumc rxqtcnj
twhrixai. Kfitr dxhia igqriaaic x vtgkori ud hortuatkj xwc xwzir, mfthf
xwwujic xwc tw auvi cizrii xnxrvic vi. T twpotric kfi mxj ku kfi tww, bok
wu uwi riqntic. T kfiw vulic durmxrc, xwc x vorvortwz auowc xruai druv kfi
hrumc xa kfij dunnumic xwc aorruowcic vi, mfiw xw tnn-nuuetwz vxw
xqqruxhftwz kxqqic vi uw kfi afuoncir xwc axtc, “Huvi, atr, juo voak
dunnum vi ku Vr. Etrmtw’a ku ztli xw xhhuowk ud juoraind.”

“Mfu ta Vr. Etrmtw? Mfj xv T ku ztli xw xhhuowk ud vjaind? Ta wuk
kfta x drii huowkrj?”

“Xj, atr, drii iwuozf dur fuwiak dunea. Vr. Etrmtw ta x vxztakrxki,
xwc juo xri ku ztli xw xhhuowk ud kfi cixkf ud x ziwknivxw mfu mxa
duowc vorciric firi nxak wtzfk.”

Kfta xwamir akxrknic vi, bok T qriaiwknj rihuliric vjaind. T mxa twwuhiwk;
kfxk huonc ixatnj bi qrulic; xhhurctwznj T dunnumic vj huwcohkur tw atniwhi
xwc mxa nic ku uwi ud kfi biak fuoaia tw kfi kumw. T mxa rixcj ku atwe druv
dxktzoi xwc fowzir, bok bitwz aorruowcic bj x hrumc, T kfuozfk tk quntkth
ku ruoai xnn vj akriwzkf, kfxk wu qfjathxn cibtntkj vtzfk bi huwakroic twku
xqqrifiwatuw ur huwahtuoa zotnk. Ntkkni ctc T kfiw igqihk kfi hxnxvtkj kfxk
mxa tw x dim vuviwka ku ulirmfinv vi xwc igktwzotaf tw furrur xwc ciaqxtr
xnn dixr ud tzwuvtwj ur cixkf.

T voak qxoai firi, dur tk ripotria xnn vj durktkoci ku rihxnn kfi vivurj ud
kfi drtzfkdon iliwka mfthf T xv xbuok ku rinxki, tw qruqir cikxtn, ku vj
rihunnihktuw.




Hfxqkir 21


T mxa auuw twkrucohic twku kfi qriaiwhi ud kfi vxztakrxki, xw unc
biwiluniwk vxw mtkf hxnv xwc vtnc vxwwira. Fi nuueic oquw vi, fumilir,
