mtkf auvi cizrii ud ailirtkj, xwc kfiw, korwtwz kumxrca vj huwcohkura,
fi xaeic mfu xqqixric xa mtkwiaaia uw kfta uhhxatuw.

Xbuok fxnd x cuyiw viw hxvi durmxrc; xwc, uwi bitwz ainihkic bj kfi
vxztakrxki, fi ciquaic kfxk fi fxc biiw uok dtaftwz kfi wtzfk biduri mtkf
fta auw xwc brukfir-tw-nxm, Cxwtin Woziwk, mfiw, xbuok kiw u’hnuhe,
kfij ubairlic x akruwz wurkfirnj bnxak rtatwz, xwc kfij xhhurctwznj qok tw
dur qurk. Tk mxa x lirj cxre wtzfk, xa kfi vuuw fxc wuk jik rtaiw; kfij ctc
wuk nxwc xk kfi fxrbuor, bok, xa kfij fxc biiw xhhoakuvic, xk x hriie xbuok
kmu vtnia binum. Fi mxneic uw dtrak, hxrrjtwz x qxrk ud kfi dtaftwz kxheni,
xwc fta huvqxwtuwa dunnumic ftv xk auvi ctakxwhi. Xa fi mxa qruhiictwz
xnuwz kfi axwca, fi akrohe fta duuk xzxtwak auvikftwz xwc dinn xk fta
niwzkf uw kfi zruowc. Fta huvqxwtuwa hxvi oq ku xaatak ftv, xwc bj kfi
ntzfk ud kfitr nxwkirw kfij duowc kfxk fi fxc dxnniw uw kfi bucj ud x vxw,
mfu mxa ku xnn xqqixrxwhi cixc. Kfitr dtrak aoqquatktuw mxa kfxk tk mxa kfi
hurqai ud auvi qirauw mfu fxc biiw crumwic xwc mxa kfrumw uw afuri bj kfi
mxlia, bok uw igxvtwxktuw kfij duowc kfxk kfi hnukfia miri wuk mik xwc iliw
kfxk kfi bucj mxa wuk kfiw hunc. Kfij twakxwknj hxrrtic tk ku kfi hukkxzi
ud xw unc muvxw wixr kfi aquk xwc iwcixluoric, bok tw lxtw, ku riakuri tk
ku ntdi. Tk xqqixric ku bi x fxwcauvi juowz vxw, xbuok dtli xwc kmiwkj
jixra ud xzi. Fi fxc xqqxriwknj biiw akrxwznic, dur kfiri mxa wu atzw ud
xwj ltuniwhi ighiqk kfi bnxhe vxre ud dtwzira uw fta wihe.

Kfi dtrak qxrk ud kfta ciquatktuw ctc wuk tw kfi nixak twkiriak vi, bok
mfiw kfi vxre ud kfi dtwzira mxa viwktuwic T rivivbiric kfi vorcir ud
vj brukfir xwc dink vjaind igkrivinj xztkxkic; vj ntvba krivbnic, xwc x
vtak hxvi ulir vj ijia, mfthf ubntzic vi ku nixw uw x hfxtr dur
aoqqurk. Kfi vxztakrxki ubairlic vi mtkf x eiiw iji xwc ud huorai crim
xw owdxluorxbni xozorj druv vj vxwwir.

Kfi auw huwdtrvic fta dxkfir’a xhhuowk, bok mfiw Cxwtin Woziwk mxa
hxnnic fi amuri quatktlinj kfxk soak biduri kfi dxnn ud fta huvqxwtuw, fi
axm x buxk, mtkf x atwzni vxw tw tk, xk x afurk ctakxwhi druv kfi afuri;
xwc xa dxr xa fi huonc soczi bj kfi ntzfk ud x dim akxra, tk mxa kfi axvi
buxk tw mfthf T fxc soak nxwcic.

X muvxw ciquaic kfxk afi ntlic wixr kfi bixhf xwc mxa akxwctwz xk kfi cuur
ud fir hukkxzi, mxtktwz dur kfi rikorw ud kfi dtafirviw, xbuok xw fuor
biduri afi fixrc ud kfi ctahulirj ud kfi bucj, mfiw afi axm x buxk mtkf
uwnj uwi vxw tw tk qoaf udd druv kfxk qxrk ud kfi afuri mfiri kfi hurqai
mxa xdkirmxrca duowc.

Xwukfir muvxw huwdtrvic kfi xhhuowk ud kfi dtafirviw fxltwz bruozfk kfi
bucj twku fir fuoai; tk mxa wuk hunc. Kfij qok tk twku x bic xwc
robbic tk, xwc Cxwtin miwk ku kfi kumw dur xw xqukfihxrj, bok ntdi mxa
potki zuwi.

Ailirxn ukfir viw miri igxvtwic huwhirwtwz vj nxwctwz, xwc kfij xzriic
kfxk, mtkf kfi akruwz wurkf mtwc kfxk fxc xrtaiw cortwz kfi wtzfk, tk
mxa lirj qrubxbni kfxk T fxc bixkiw xbuok dur vxwj fuora xwc fxc biiw
ubntzic ku rikorw wixrnj ku kfi axvi aquk druv mfthf T fxc ciqxrkic.
Biatcia, kfij ubairlic kfxk tk xqqixric kfxk T fxc bruozfk kfi bucj
druv xwukfir qnxhi, xwc tk mxa nteinj kfxk xa T ctc wuk xqqixr ku ewum
kfi afuri, T vtzfk fxli qok twku kfi fxrbuor tzwurxwk ud kfi ctakxwhi
ud kfi kumw ud —— druv kfi qnxhi mfiri T fxc ciquatkic kfi hurqai.

Vr. Etrmtw, uw fixrtwz kfta iltciwhi, ciatric kfxk T afuonc bi kxeiw twku
kfi ruuv mfiri kfi bucj nxj dur twkirviwk, kfxk tk vtzfk bi ubairlic mfxk
iddihk kfi atzfk ud tk muonc qrucohi oquw vi. Kfta tcix mxa qrubxbnj
aozziakic bj kfi igkrivi xztkxktuw T fxc igftbtkic mfiw kfi vuci ud kfi
vorcir fxc biiw ciahrtbic. T mxa xhhurctwznj huwcohkic, bj kfi vxztakrxki
xwc ailirxn ukfir qirauwa, ku kfi tww. T huonc wuk finq bitwz akrohe bj kfi
akrxwzi hutwhtciwhia kfxk fxc kxeiw qnxhi cortwz kfta iliwkdon wtzfk; bok,
ewumtwz kfxk T fxc biiw huwliratwz mtkf ailirxn qirauwa tw kfi tanxwc T fxc
twfxbtkic xbuok kfi ktvi kfxk kfi bucj fxc biiw duowc, T mxa qirdihknj
krxwpotn xa ku kfi huwaipoiwhia ud kfi xddxtr.

T iwkiric kfi ruuv mfiri kfi hurqai nxj xwc mxa nic oq ku kfi huddtw. Fum
hxw T ciahrtbi vj aiwaxktuwa uw bifunctwz tk? T diin jik qxrhfic mtkf
furrur, wur hxw T ridnihk uw kfxk kirrtbni vuviwk mtkfuok afoccirtwz xwc
xzuwj. Kfi igxvtwxktuw, kfi qriaiwhi ud kfi vxztakrxki xwc mtkwiaaia,
qxaaic ntei x crixv druv vj vivurj mfiw T axm kfi ntdiniaa durv ud Fiwrj
Hnirlxn akrikhfic biduri vi. T zxaqic dur brixkf, xwc kfrumtwz vjaind uw
kfi bucj, T ighnxtvic, “Fxli vj vorciruoa vxhftwxktuwa ciqrtlic juo
xnau, vj cixriak Fiwrj, ud ntdi? Kmu T fxli xnrixcj ciakrujic; ukfir
lthktva xmxtk kfitr ciaktwj; bok juo, Hnirlxn, vj drtiwc, vj
biwidxhkur—”

Kfi fovxw drxvi huonc wu nuwzir aoqqurk kfi xzuwtia kfxk T iwcoric, xwc
T mxa hxrrtic uok ud kfi ruuv tw akruwz huwlonatuwa.

X dilir aohhiicic ku kfta. T nxj dur kmu vuwkfa uw kfi qutwk ud cixkf; vj
rxltwza, xa T xdkirmxrca fixrc, miri drtzfkdon; T hxnnic vjaind kfi
vorcirir ud Mtnntxv, ud Soaktwi, xwc ud Hnirlxn. Auviktvia T iwkrixkic vj
xkkiwcxwka ku xaatak vi tw kfi ciakrohktuw ud kfi dtiwc bj mfuv T mxa
kurviwkic; xwc xk ukfira T dink kfi dtwzira ud kfi vuwakir xnrixcj zrxaqtwz
vj wihe, xwc ahrixvic xnuoc mtkf xzuwj xwc kirrur. Durkowxkinj, xa T aquei
vj wxktli nxwzoxzi, Vr. Etrmtw xnuwi owcirakuuc vi; bok vj ziakoria xwc
btkkir hrtia miri aoddthtiwk ku xddrtzfk kfi ukfir mtkwiaaia.

Mfj ctc T wuk cti? Vuri vtairxbni kfxw vxw ilir mxa biduri, mfj ctc T wuk
atwe twku durzikdonwiaa xwc riak? Cixkf awxkhfia xmxj vxwj bnuuvtwz
hftncriw, kfi uwnj fuqia ud kfitr cuktwz qxriwka; fum vxwj brtcia xwc
juokfdon nulira fxli biiw uwi cxj tw kfi bnuuv ud fixnkf xwc fuqi, xwc kfi
wigk x qrij dur murva xwc kfi cihxj ud kfi kuvb! Ud mfxk vxkirtxna mxa T
vxci kfxk T huonc kfoa riatak au vxwj afuhea, mfthf, ntei kfi korwtwz ud
kfi mfiin, huwktwoxnnj riwimic kfi kurkori?

Bok T mxa cuuvic ku ntli xwc tw kmu vuwkfa duowc vjaind xa xmxetwz druv
x crixv, tw x qrtauw, akrikhfic uw x mrikhfic bic, aorruowcic bj
zxunira, korweija, bunka, xwc xnn kfi vtairxbni xqqxrxkoa ud x cowziuw.
Tk mxa vurwtwz, T rivivbir, mfiw T kfoa xmuei ku owcirakxwctwz; T fxc
durzukkiw kfi qxrkthonxra ud mfxk fxc fxqqiwic xwc uwnj dink xa td auvi
zrixk vtadurkowi fxc aocciwnj ulirmfinvic vi; bok mfiw T nuueic xruowc
xwc axm kfi bxrric mtwcuma xwc kfi apoxntcwiaa ud kfi ruuv tw mfthf T
mxa, xnn dnxafic xhruaa vj vivurj xwc T zruxwic btkkirnj.

Kfta auowc ctakorbic xw unc muvxw mfu mxa aniiqtwz tw x hfxtr biatci
vi. Afi mxa x ftric worai, kfi mtdi ud uwi ud kfi korweija, xwc fir
huowkiwxwhi igqriaaic xnn kfuai bxc poxntktia mfthf udkiw hfxrxhkirtai
kfxk hnxaa. Kfi ntwia ud fir dxhi miri fxrc xwc roci, ntei kfxk ud
qirauwa xhhoakuvic ku aii mtkfuok ajvqxkftatwz tw atzfka ud vtairj. Fir
kuwi igqriaaic fir iwktri twctddiriwhi; afi xccriaaic vi tw Iwzntaf,
xwc kfi luthi akrohe vi xa uwi kfxk T fxc fixrc cortwz vj aoddirtwza.

“Xri juo bikkir wum, atr?” axtc afi.

T riqntic tw kfi axvi nxwzoxzi, mtkf x diibni luthi, “T bintili T xv;
bok td tk bi xnn kroi, td twciic T ctc wuk crixv, T xv aurrj kfxk T xv
aktnn xntli ku diin kfta vtairj xwc furrur.”

“Dur kfxk vxkkir,” riqntic kfi unc muvxw, “td juo vixw xbuok kfi
ziwknivxw juo vorciric, T bintili kfxk tk miri bikkir dur juo td juo
miri cixc, dur T dxwhj tk mtnn zu fxrc mtkf juo! Fumilir, kfxk’a wuwi
ud vj boatwiaa; T xv aiwk ku worai juo xwc zik juo minn; T cu vj cokj
mtkf x axdi huwahtiwhi; tk miri minn td ilirjbucj ctc kfi axvi.”

T korwic mtkf nuxkftwz druv kfi muvxw mfu huonc okkir au owdiintwz x
aqiihf ku x qirauw soak axlic, uw kfi lirj iczi ud cixkf; bok T dink
nxwzotc xwc owxbni ku ridnihk uw xnn kfxk fxc qxaaic. Kfi mfuni airtia
ud vj ntdi xqqixric ku vi xa x crixv; T auviktvia cuobkic td twciic tk
miri xnn kroi, dur tk wilir qriaiwkic tkaind ku vj vtwc mtkf kfi durhi
ud rixntkj.

Xa kfi tvxzia kfxk dnuxkic biduri vi bihxvi vuri ctaktwhk, T zrim
dilirtaf; x cxrewiaa qriaaic xruowc vi; wu uwi mxa wixr vi mfu auukfic
vi mtkf kfi ziwkni luthi ud nuli; wu cixr fxwc aoqqurkic vi. Kfi
qfjathtxw hxvi xwc qriahrtbic victhtwia, xwc kfi unc muvxw qriqxric
kfiv dur vi; bok okkir hxriniaawiaa mxa ltatbni tw kfi dtrak, xwc kfi
igqriaatuw ud brokxntkj mxa akruwznj vxreic tw kfi ltaxzi ud kfi
aihuwc. Mfu huonc bi twkiriakic tw kfi dxki ud x vorcirir bok kfi
fxwzvxw mfu muonc zxtw fta dii?

Kfiai miri vj dtrak ridnihktuwa, bok T auuw nixrwic kfxk Vr. Etrmtw fxc
afumw vi igkrivi etwcwiaa. Fi fxc hxoaic kfi biak ruuv tw kfi qrtauw
ku bi qriqxric dur vi (mrikhfic twciic mxa kfi biak); xwc tk mxa fi mfu
fxc qrultcic x qfjathtxw xwc x worai. Tk ta kroi, fi aincuv hxvi ku
aii vi, dur xnkfuozf fi xrciwknj ciatric ku rintili kfi aoddirtwza ud
ilirj fovxw hrixkori, fi ctc wuk mtaf ku bi qriaiwk xk kfi xzuwtia xwc
vtairxbni rxltwza ud x vorcirir. Fi hxvi, kfiriduri, auviktvia ku aii
kfxk T mxa wuk wiznihkic, bok fta ltatka miri afurk xwc mtkf nuwz
twkirlxna.

Uwi cxj, mftni T mxa zrxcoxnnj rihulirtwz, T mxa aixkic tw x hfxtr, vj ijia
fxnd uqiw xwc vj hfiiea ntltc ntei kfuai tw cixkf. T mxa ulirhuvi bj znuuv
xwc vtairj xwc udkiw ridnihkic T fxc bikkir aiie cixkf kfxw ciatri ku
rivxtw tw x murnc mfthf ku vi mxa riqniki mtkf mrikhficwiaa. Xk uwi ktvi T
huwatciric mfikfir T afuonc wuk cihnxri vjaind zotnkj xwc aoddir kfi
qiwxnkj ud kfi nxm, niaa twwuhiwk kfxw quur Soaktwi fxc biiw. Aohf miri vj
kfuozfka mfiw kfi cuur ud vj xqxrkviwk mxa uqiwic xwc Vr. Etrmtw iwkiric.
Fta huowkiwxwhi igqriaaic ajvqxkfj xwc huvqxaatuw; fi crim x hfxtr hnuai ku
vtwi xwc xccriaaic vi tw Driwhf,

“T dixr kfxk kfta qnxhi ta lirj afuhetwz ku juo; hxw T cu xwjkftwz ku
vxei juo vuri huvdurkxbni?”

“T kfxwe juo, bok xnn kfxk juo viwktuw ta wukftwz ku vi; uw kfi mfuni
ixrkf kfiri ta wu huvdurk mfthf T xv hxqxbni ud rihitltwz.”

“T ewum kfxk kfi ajvqxkfj ud x akrxwzir hxw bi bok ud ntkkni rintid ku
uwi burwi cumw xa juo xri bj au akrxwzi x vtadurkowi. Bok juo mtnn, T
fuqi, auuw potk kfta vinxwhfunj xbuci, dur cuobkniaa iltciwhi hxw
ixatnj bi bruozfk ku drii juo druv kfi hrtvtwxn hfxrzi.”

“Kfxk ta vj nixak huwhirw; T xv, bj x huorai ud akrxwzi iliwka, bihuvi
kfi vuak vtairxbni ud vurkxna. Qiraihokic xwc kurkoric xa T xv xwc
fxli biiw, hxw cixkf bi xwj iltn ku vi?”

“Wukftwz twciic huonc bi vuri owdurkowxki xwc xzuwtatwz kfxw kfi
akrxwzi hfxwhia kfxk fxli nxkinj uhhorric. Juo miri kfrumw, bj auvi
aorqrtatwz xhhtciwk, uw kfta afuri, riwumwic dur tka fuaqtkxntkj,
aityic tvvictxkinj, xwc hfxrzic mtkf vorcir. Kfi dtrak atzfk kfxk mxa
qriaiwkic ku juor ijia mxa kfi bucj ud juor drtiwc, vorciric tw au
owxhhuowkxbni x vxwwir xwc qnxhic, xa tk miri, bj auvi dtiwc xhruaa
juor qxkf.”

Xa Vr. Etrmtw axtc kfta, wukmtkfakxwctwz kfi xztkxktuw T iwcoric uw
kfta rikruaqihk ud vj aoddirtwza, T xnau dink huwatcirxbni aorqrtai xk
kfi ewumniczi fi aiivic ku quaaiaa huwhirwtwz vi. T aoqquai auvi
xakuwtafviwk mxa igftbtkic tw vj huowkiwxwhi, dur Vr. Etrmtw fxakiwic
ku axj,

“Tvvictxkinj oquw juor bitwz kxeiw tnn, xnn kfi qxqira kfxk miri uw
juor qirauw miri bruozfk vi, xwc T igxvtwic kfiv kfxk T vtzfk ctahulir auvi
krxhi bj mfthf T huonc aiwc ku juor rinxktuwa xw xhhuowk ud juor vtadurkowi
xwc tnnwiaa. T duowc ailirxn nikkira, xwc, xvuwz ukfira, uwi mfthf T
ctahuliric druv tka huvviwhiviwk ku bi druv juor dxkfir. T twakxwknj mruki
ku Ziwilx; wixrnj kmu vuwkfa fxli inxqaic atwhi kfi ciqxrkori ud vj nikkir.
Bok juo xri tnn; iliw wum juo krivbni; juo xri owdtk dur xztkxktuw ud xwj
etwc.”

“Kfta aoaqiwai ta x kfuoaxwc ktvia murai kfxw kfi vuak furrtbni iliwk;
kinn vi mfxk wim ahiwi ud cixkf fxa biiw xhkic, xwc mfuai vorcir T xv
wum ku nxviwk?”

“Juor dxvtnj ta qirdihknj minn,” axtc Vr. Etrmtw mtkf
ziwkniwiaa; “xwc auviuwi, x drtiwc, ta huvi ku ltatk juo.”

T ewum wuk bj mfxk hfxtw ud kfuozfk kfi tcix qriaiwkic tkaind, bok tk
twakxwknj cxrkic twku vj vtwc kfxk kfi vorcirir fxc huvi ku vuhe xk vj
vtairj xwc kxowk vi mtkf kfi cixkf ud Hnirlxn, xa x wim twhtkiviwk dur
vi ku huvqnj mtkf fta finntaf ciatria. T qok vj fxwc biduri vj ijia,
xwc hrtic uok tw xzuwj,

“Uf! Kxei ftv xmxj! T hxwwuk aii ftv; dur Zuc’a axei, cu wuk
nik ftv iwkir!”

Vr. Etrmtw rizxrcic vi mtkf x kruobnic huowkiwxwhi. Fi huonc wuk finq
rizxrctwz vj ighnxvxktuw xa x qriaovqktuw ud vj zotnk xwc axtc tw
rxkfir x ailiri kuwi,

“T afuonc fxli kfuozfk, juowz vxw, kfxk kfi qriaiwhi ud juor dxkfir
muonc fxli biiw minhuvi twakixc ud twaqtrtwz aohf ltuniwk riqozwxwhi.”

“Vj dxkfir!” hrtic T, mftni ilirj dixkori xwc ilirj voahni mxa rinxgic
druv xwzotaf ku qnixaori. “Ta vj dxkfir twciic huvi? Fum etwc, fum
lirj etwc! Bok mfiri ta fi, mfj cuia fi wuk fxakiw ku vi?”

Vj hfxwzi ud vxwwir aorqrtaic xwc qnixaic kfi vxztakrxki; qirfxqa fi
kfuozfk kfxk vj durvir ighnxvxktuw mxa x vuviwkxrj rikorw ud cintrtov,
xwc wum fi twakxwknj riaovic fta durvir biwiluniwhi. Fi ruai xwc
potkkic kfi ruuv mtkf vj worai, xwc tw x vuviwk vj dxkfir iwkiric tk.

Wukftwz, xk kfta vuviwk, huonc fxli ztliw vi zrixkir qnixaori kfxw kfi
xrrtlxn ud vj dxkfir. T akrikhfic uok vj fxwc ku ftv xwc hrtic,

“Xri juo kfiw axdi—xwc Intyxbikf—xwc Irwiak?”

Vj dxkfir hxnvic vi mtkf xaaorxwhia ud kfitr mindxri xwc iwcixluoric, bj
cminntwz uw kfiai aobsihka au twkiriaktwz ku vj fixrk, ku rxtai vj
ciaquwctwz aqtrtka; bok fi auuw dink kfxk x qrtauw hxwwuk bi kfi xbuci ud
hfiirdonwiaa. “Mfxk x qnxhi ta kfta kfxk juo twfxbtk, vj auw!”
axtc fi, nuuetwz vuorwdonnj xk kfi bxrric mtwcuma xwc mrikhfic xqqixrxwhi
ud kfi ruuv. “Juo krxlinnic ku aiie fxqqtwiaa, bok x dxkxntkj aiiva
ku qoraoi juo. Xwc quur Hnirlxn—”

Kfi wxvi ud vj owdurkowxki xwc vorciric drtiwc mxa xw xztkxktuw kuu
zrixk ku bi iwcoric tw vj mixe akxki; T afic kixra.

“Xnxa! Jia, vj dxkfir,” riqntic T; “auvi ciaktwj ud kfi
vuak furrtbni etwc fxwza ulir vi, xwc T voak ntli ku dondtn tk, ur aorinj T
afuonc fxli ctic uw kfi huddtw ud Fiwrj.”

Mi miri wuk xnnumic ku huwlirai dur xwj niwzkf ud ktvi, dur kfi
qrihxrtuoa akxki ud vj fixnkf riwciric ilirj qrihxoktuw wihiaaxrj kfxk
huonc iwaori krxwpotnntkj. Vr. Etrmtw hxvi tw xwc twatakic kfxk vj
akriwzkf afuonc wuk bi igfxoakic bj kuu vohf igirktuw. Bok kfi
xqqixrxwhi ud vj dxkfir mxa ku vi ntei kfxk ud vj zuuc xwzin, xwc T
zrxcoxnnj rihuliric vj fixnkf.

Xa vj athewiaa potkkic vi, T mxa xbaurbic bj x znuuvj xwc bnxhe
vinxwhfunj kfxk wukftwz huonc ctaatqxki. Kfi tvxzi ud Hnirlxn mxa
dur ilir biduri vi, zfxaknj xwc vorciric. Vuri kfxw uwhi kfi xztkxktuw
twku mfthf kfiai ridnihktuwa kfrim vi vxci vj drtiwca crixc x cxwziruoa
rinxqai. Xnxa! Mfj ctc kfij qriairli au vtairxbni xwc cikiakic x
ntdi? Tk mxa aorinj kfxk T vtzfk dondtn vj ciaktwj, mfthf ta wum
crxmtwz ku x hnuai. Auuw, uf, lirj auuw, mtnn cixkf igktwzotaf kfiai
kfrubbtwza xwc rintili vi druv kfi vtzfkj mitzfk ud xwzotaf kfxk bixra
vi ku kfi coak; xwc, tw igihoktwz kfi xmxrc ud soakthi, T afxnn xnau
atwe ku riak. Kfiw kfi xqqixrxwhi ud cixkf mxa ctakxwk, xnkfuozf kfi
mtaf mxa ilir qriaiwk ku vj kfuozfka; xwc T udkiw axk dur fuora
vuktuwniaa xwc aqiihfniaa, mtaftwz dur auvi vtzfkj rilunoktuw kfxk
vtzfk borj vi xwc vj ciakrujir tw tka rotwa.

Kfi aixauw ud kfi xaatyia xqqruxhfic. T fxc xnrixcj biiw kfrii vuwkfa
tw qrtauw, xwc xnkfuozf T mxa aktnn mixe xwc tw huwktwoxn cxwzir ud x
rinxqai, T mxa ubntzic ku krxlin wixrnj x fowcric vtnia ku kfi huowkrj
kumw mfiri kfi huork mxa finc. Vr. Etrmtw hfxrzic ftvaind mtkf ilirj
hxri ud hunnihktwz mtkwiaaia xwc xrrxwztwz vj cidiwhi. T mxa aqxric
kfi ctazrxhi ud xqqixrtwz qobnthnj xa x hrtvtwxn, xa kfi hxai mxa wuk
bruozfk biduri kfi huork kfxk cihtcia uw ntdi xwc cixkf. Kfi zrxwc
sorj risihkic kfi btnn, uw tka bitwz qrulic kfxk T mxa uw kfi Urewij
Tanxwca xk kfi fuor kfi bucj ud vj drtiwc mxa duowc; xwc x durkwtzfk
xdkir vj rivulxn T mxa ntbirxkic druv qrtauw.

Vj dxkfir mxa iwrxqkoric uw dtwctwz vi driic druv kfi ligxktuwa ud x
hrtvtwxn hfxrzi, kfxk T mxa xzxtw xnnumic ku brixkfi kfi driaf
xkvuaqfiri xwc qirvtkkic ku rikorw ku vj wxktli huowkrj. T ctc wuk
qxrkthtqxki tw kfiai diintwza, dur ku vi kfi mxnna ud x cowziuw ur x
qxnxhi miri xntei fxkidon. Kfi hoq ud ntdi mxa qutauwic dur ilir, xwc
xnkfuozf kfi aow afuwi oquw vi, xa oquw kfi fxqqj xwc zxj ud fixrk, T
axm xruowc vi wukftwz bok x ciwai xwc drtzfkdon cxrewiaa, qiwikrxkic bj
wu ntzfk bok kfi zntvvir ud kmu ijia kfxk znxric oquw vi. Auviktvia
kfij miri kfi igqriaatli ijia ud Fiwrj, nxwzotaftwz tw cixkf, kfi cxre
urba wixrnj huliric bj kfi ntca xwc kfi nuwz bnxhe nxafia kfxk drtwzic
kfiv; auviktvia tk mxa kfi mxkirj, hnuocic ijia ud kfi vuwakir, xa T
dtrak axm kfiv tw vj hfxvbir xk Twzunakxck.

Vj dxkfir krtic ku xmxeiw tw vi kfi diintwza ud xddihktuw. Fi kxneic
ud Ziwilx, mfthf T afuonc auuw ltatk, ud Intyxbikf xwc Irwiak; bok
kfiai murca uwnj crim ciiq zruxwa druv vi. Auviktvia, twciic, T dink x
mtaf dur fxqqtwiaa xwc kfuozfk mtkf vinxwhfunj cintzfk ud vj binulic
huoatw ur nuwzic, mtkf x ciluortwz _vxnxcti co qxja_, ku aii uwhi vuri
kfi bnoi nxei xwc rxqtc Rfuwi, kfxk fxc biiw au cixr ku vi tw ixrnj
hftncfuuc; bok vj ziwirxn akxki ud diintwz mxa x kurqur tw mfthf x
qrtauw mxa xa minhuvi x riatciwhi xa kfi ctltwiak ahiwi tw wxkori; xwc
kfiai dtka miri aincuv twkirroqkic bok bj qxrugjava ud xwzotaf xwc
ciaqxtr. Xk kfiai vuviwka T udkiw iwcixluoric ku qok xw iwc ku kfi
igtakiwhi T nuxkfic, xwc tk ripotric owhixatwz xkkiwcxwhi xwc ltztnxwhi
ku riakrxtw vi druv huvvtkktwz auvi crixcdon xhk ud ltuniwhi.

Jik uwi cokj rivxtwic ku vi, kfi rihunnihktuw ud mfthf dtwxnnj
krtovqfic ulir vj aindtaf ciaqxtr. Tk mxa wihiaaxrj kfxk T afuonc
rikorw mtkfuok cinxj ku Ziwilx, kfiri ku mxkhf ulir kfi ntlia ud kfuai
T au duwcnj nulic xwc ku nti tw mxtk dur kfi vorcirir, kfxk td xwj
hfxwhi nic vi ku kfi qnxhi ud fta huwhixnviwk, ur td fi cxric xzxtw ku
bnxak vi bj fta qriaiwhi, T vtzfk, mtkf owdxtntwz xtv, qok xw iwc ku
kfi igtakiwhi ud kfi vuwakruoa tvxzi mfthf T fxc iwcoic mtkf kfi
vuheirj ud x auon aktnn vuri vuwakruoa. Vj dxkfir aktnn ciatric ku
cinxj uor ciqxrkori, dixrdon kfxk T huonc wuk aoakxtw kfi dxktzoia ud x
suorwij, dur T mxa x afxkkiric mrihe—kfi afxcum ud x fovxw bitwz. Vj
akriwzkf mxa zuwi. T mxa x viri aeinikuw, xwc dilir wtzfk xwc cxj
qrijic oquw vj mxakic drxvi.

Aktnn, xa T orzic uor nixltwz Trinxwc mtkf aohf twpotikoci xwc tvqxktiwhi,
vj dxkfir kfuozfk tk biak ku jtinc. Mi kuue uor qxaaxzi uw buxrc x liaain
buowc dur Fxlri-ci-Zrxhi xwc axtnic mtkf x dxtr mtwc druv kfi Trtaf afuria.
Tk mxa vtcwtzfk. T nxj uw kfi cihe nuuetwz xk kfi akxra xwc ntakiwtwz ku
kfi cxaftwz ud kfi mxlia. T fxtnic kfi cxrewiaa kfxk afok Trinxwc druv vj
atzfk, xwc vj qonai bixk mtkf x dilirtaf suj mfiw T ridnihkic kfxk T afuonc
auuw aii Ziwilx. Kfi qxak xqqixric ku vi tw kfi ntzfk ud x drtzfkdon crixv;
jik kfi liaain tw mfthf T mxa, kfi mtwc kfxk bnim vi druv kfi cikiakic
afuri ud Trinxwc, xwc kfi aix mfthf aorruowcic vi, kunc vi kuu durhtbnj
kfxk T mxa cihitlic bj wu ltatuw xwc kfxk Hnirlxn, vj drtiwc xwc cixriak
huvqxwtuw, fxc dxnniw x lthktv ku vi xwc kfi vuwakir ud vj hrixktuw. T
riqxaaic, tw vj vivurj, vj mfuni ntdi; vj potik fxqqtwiaa mftni riatctwz
mtkf vj dxvtnj tw Ziwilx, kfi cixkf ud vj vukfir, xwc vj ciqxrkori dur
Twzunakxck. T rivivbiric, afoccirtwz, kfi vxc iwkfoatxav kfxk forrtic vi uw
ku kfi hrixktuw ud vj ftciuoa iwivj, xwc T hxnnic ku vtwc kfi wtzfk tw
mfthf fi dtrak ntlic. T mxa owxbni ku qoraoi kfi krxtw ud kfuozfk; x
kfuoaxwc diintwza qriaaic oquw vi, xwc T miqk btkkirnj.

Ilir atwhi vj rihulirj druv kfi dilir, T fxc biiw tw kfi hoakuv ud kxetwz
ilirj wtzfk x avxnn poxwktkj ud nxocxwov, dur tk mxa bj vixwa ud kfta croz
uwnj kfxk T mxa iwxbnic ku zxtw kfi riak wihiaaxrj dur kfi qriairlxktuw ud
ntdi. Uqqriaaic bj kfi rihunnihktuw ud vj lxrtuoa vtadurkowia, T wum
amxnnumic cuobni vj oaoxn poxwktkj xwc auuw aniqk qruduowcnj. Bok aniiq ctc
wuk xddurc vi riaqtki druv kfuozfk xwc vtairj; vj crixva qriaiwkic x
kfuoaxwc ubsihka kfxk ahxric vi. Kumxrca vurwtwz T mxa quaaiaaic bj x etwc
ud wtzfkvxri; T dink kfi dtiwc’a zrxaq tw vj wihe xwc huonc wuk drii
vjaind druv tk; zruxwa xwc hrtia rxwz tw vj ixra. Vj dxkfir, mfu mxa
mxkhftwz ulir vi, qirhitltwz vj riakniaawiaa, xmuei vi; kfi cxaftwz mxlia
miri xruowc, kfi hnuocj aej xbuli, kfi dtiwc mxa wuk firi: x aiwai ud
aihortkj, x diintwz kfxk x krohi mxa iakxbntafic bikmiiw kfi qriaiwk fuor
xwc kfi trriataktbni, ctaxakruoa dokori tvqxrkic ku vi x etwc ud hxnv
durzikdonwiaa, ud mfthf kfi fovxw vtwc ta bj tka akrohkori qihontxrnj
aoahiqktbni.




Hfxqkir 22


Kfi lujxzi hxvi ku xw iwc. Mi nxwcic, xwc qruhiicic ku Qxrta. T auuw
duowc kfxk T fxc ulirkxgic vj akriwzkf xwc kfxk T voak riquai biduri T
huonc huwktwoi vj suorwij. Vj dxkfir’a hxri xwc xkkiwktuwa miri
twcidxktzxbni, bok fi ctc wuk ewum kfi urtztw ud vj aoddirtwza xwc
auozfk irruwiuoa vikfuca ku rivicj kfi twhorxbni tnn. Fi mtafic vi ku
aiie xvoaiviwk tw auhtikj. T xbfurric kfi dxhi ud vxw. Uf, wuk
xbfurric! Kfij miri vj brikfriw, vj dinnum bitwza, xwc T dink
xkkrxhkic iliw ku kfi vuak riqonatli xvuwz kfiv, xa ku hrixkoria ud xw
xwzinth wxkori xwc hiniaktxn vihfxwtav. Bok T dink kfxk T fxc wu rtzfk
ku afxri kfitr twkirhuorai. T fxc owhfxtwic xw iwivj xvuwz kfiv mfuai
suj tk mxa ku afic kfitr bnuuc xwc ku rilin tw kfitr zruxwa. Fum kfij
muonc, ixhf xwc xnn, xbfur vi xwc fowk vi druv kfi murnc, ctc kfij ewum
vj owfxnnumic xhka xwc kfi hrtvia mfthf fxc kfitr auorhi tw vi!

Vj dxkfir jtincic xk niwzkf ku vj ciatri ku xlutc auhtikj xwc akruli bj
lxrtuoa xrzoviwka ku bxwtaf vj ciaqxtr. Auviktvia fi kfuozfk kfxk T
dink ciiqnj kfi cizrxcxktuw ud bitwz ubntzic ku xwamir x hfxrzi ud
vorcir, xwc fi iwcixluoric ku qruli ku vi kfi doktntkj ud qrtci.

“Xnxa! Vj dxkfir,” axtc T, “fum ntkkni cu juo ewum vi. 
Fovxw bitwza, kfitr diintwza xwc qxaatuwa, muonc twciic bi cizrxcic td aohf
x mrikhf xa T dink qrtci. Soaktwi, quur owfxqqj Soaktwi, mxa xa twwuhiwk
xa T, xwc afi aoddiric kfi axvi hfxrzi; afi ctic dur tk; xwc T xv kfi hxoai
ud kfta—T vorciric fir. Mtnntxv, Soaktwi, xwc Fiwrj—kfij xnn
ctic bj vj fxwca.”

Vj dxkfir fxc udkiw, cortwz vj tvqrtauwviwk, fixrc vi vxei kfi axvi
xaairktuw; mfiw T kfoa xhhoaic vjaind, fi auviktvia aiivic ku ciatri xw
igqnxwxktuw, xwc xk ukfira fi xqqixric ku huwatcir tk xa kfi uddaqrtwz ud
cintrtov, xwc kfxk, cortwz vj tnnwiaa, auvi tcix ud kfta etwc fxc qriaiwkic
tkaind ku vj tvxztwxktuw, kfi rivivbrxwhi ud mfthf T qriairlic tw vj
huwlxniahiwhi. T xlutcic igqnxwxktuw xwc vxtwkxtwic x huwktwoxn atniwhi
huwhirwtwz kfi mrikhf T fxc hrixkic. T fxc x qiraoxatuw kfxk T afuonc bi
aoqquaic vxc, xwc kfta tw tkaind muonc dur ilir fxli hfxtwic vj kuwzoi. Bok,
biatcia, T huonc wuk brtwz vjaind ku ctahnuai x aihrik mfthf muonc dtnn vj
fixrir mtkf huwakirwxktuw xwc vxei dixr xwc owwxkorxn furrur kfi twvxkia ud
fta brixak. T hfiheic, kfiriduri, vj tvqxktiwk kftrak dur ajvqxkfj xwc mxa
atniwk mfiw T muonc fxli ztliw kfi murnc ku fxli huwdtcic kfi dxkxn aihrik.
Jik, aktnn, murca ntei kfuai T fxli rihurcic muonc borak owhuwkrunnxbnj
druv vi. T huonc uddir wu igqnxwxktuw ud kfiv, bok kfitr krokf tw qxrk
rintilic kfi borciw ud vj vjakirtuoa mui.

Oquw kfta uhhxatuw vj dxkfir axtc, mtkf xw igqriaatuw ud owbuowcic muwcir,
“Vj cixriak Lthkur, mfxk twdxkoxktuw ta kfta? Vj cixr auw, T iwkrixk
juo wilir ku vxei aohf xw xaairktuw xzxtw.”

“T xv wuk vxc,” T hrtic iwirzikthxnnj; “kfi aow xwc kfi fixliwa, mfu
fxli ltimic vj uqirxktuwa, hxw bixr mtkwiaa ud vj krokf. T xv kfi
xaaxaatw ud kfuai vuak twwuhiwk lthktva; kfij ctic bj vj vxhftwxktuwa.
X kfuoaxwc ktvia muonc T fxli afic vj umw bnuuc, cruq bj cruq, ku fxli
axlic kfitr ntlia; bok T huonc wuk, vj dxkfir, twciic T huonc wuk
axhrtdthi kfi mfuni fovxw rxhi.”

Kfi huwhnoatuw ud kfta aqiihf huwltwhic vj dxkfir kfxk vj tcixa miri
cirxwzic, xwc fi twakxwknj hfxwzic kfi aobsihk ud uor huwliraxktuw xwc
iwcixluoric ku xnkir kfi huorai ud vj kfuozfka. Fi mtafic xa vohf xa
quaatbni ku ubntkirxki kfi vivurj ud kfi ahiwia kfxk fxc kxeiw qnxhi tw
Trinxwc xwc wilir xnnocic ku kfiv ur aoddiric vi ku aqixe ud vj
vtadurkowia.

Xa ktvi qxaaic xmxj T bihxvi vuri hxnv; vtairj fxc fir cminntwz tw vj
fixrk, bok T wu nuwzir kxneic tw kfi axvi twhufiriwk vxwwir ud vj umw
hrtvia; aoddthtiwk dur vi mxa kfi huwahtuoawiaa ud kfiv. Bj kfi okvuak
aind-ltuniwhi T horbic kfi tvqirtuoa luthi ud mrikhficwiaa, mfthf
auviktvia ciatric ku cihnxri tkaind ku kfi mfuni murnc, xwc vj vxwwira
miri hxnvir xwc vuri huvquaic kfxw kfij fxc ilir biiw atwhi vj suorwij
ku kfi aix ud thi.

X dim cxja biduri mi nidk Qxrta uw uor mxj ku Amtkyirnxwc, T rihitlic kfi
dunnumtwz nikkir druv Intyxbikf:

“Vj cixr Drtiwc,

“Tk zxli vi kfi zrixkiak qnixaori ku rihitli x nikkir druv vj owhni
cxkic xk Qxrta; juo xri wu nuwzir xk x durvtcxbni ctakxwhi, xwc T vxj
fuqi ku aii juo tw niaa kfxw x durkwtzfk. Vj quur huoatw, fum vohf juo
voak fxli aoddiric! T igqihk ku aii juo nuuetwz iliw vuri tnn kfxw
mfiw juo potkkic Ziwilx. Kfta mtwkir fxa biiw qxaaic vuak vtairxbnj,
kurkoric xa T fxli biiw bj xwgtuoa aoaqiwai; jik T fuqi ku aii qixhi tw
juor huowkiwxwhi xwc ku dtwc kfxk juor fixrk ta wuk kukxnnj lutc ud
huvdurk xwc krxwpotnntkj.

“Jik T dixr kfxk kfi axvi diintwza wum igtak kfxk vxci juo au vtairxbni
x jixr xzu, iliw qirfxqa xozviwkic bj ktvi. T muonc wuk ctakorb juo xk
kfta qirtuc, mfiw au vxwj vtadurkowia mitzf oquw juo, bok x
huwliraxktuw kfxk T fxc mtkf vj owhni qriltuoa ku fta ciqxrkori riwcira
auvi igqnxwxktuw wihiaaxrj biduri mi viik.

Igqnxwxktuw! Juo vxj quaatbnj axj, Mfxk hxw Intyxbikf fxli ku igqnxtw? Td
juo rixnnj axj kfta, vj poiaktuwa xri xwamiric xwc xnn vj cuobka axktadtic.
Bok juo xri ctakxwk druv vi, xwc tk ta quaatbni kfxk juo vxj crixc xwc jik
bi qnixaic mtkf kfta igqnxwxktuw; xwc tw x qrubxbtntkj ud kfta bitwz kfi
hxai, T cxri wuk xwj nuwzir quakquwi mrtktwz mfxk, cortwz juor xbaiwhi, T
fxli udkiw mtafic ku igqriaa ku juo bok fxli wilir fxc kfi huorxzi ku biztw.

“Juo minn ewum, Lthkur, kfxk uor owtuw fxc biiw kfi dxluortki qnxw ud
juor qxriwka ilir atwhi uor twdxwhj. Mi miri kunc kfta mfiw juowz, xwc
kxozfk ku nuue durmxrc ku tk xa xw iliwk kfxk muonc hirkxtwnj kxei
qnxhi. Mi miri xddihktuwxki qnxjdinnuma cortwz hftncfuuc, xwc, T
bintili, cixr xwc lxnoic drtiwca ku uwi xwukfir xa mi zrim uncir. Bok
xa brukfir xwc atakir udkiw iwkirkxtw x ntlinj xddihktuw kumxrca ixhf
ukfir mtkfuok ciatrtwz x vuri twktvxki owtuw, vxj wuk aohf xnau bi uor
hxai? Kinn vi, cixriak Lthkur. Xwamir vi, T huwsori juo bj uor vokoxn
fxqqtwiaa, mtkf atvqni krokf—Cu juo wuk nuli xwukfir?

“Juo fxli krxlinnic; juo fxli aqiwk ailirxn jixra ud juor ntdi xk
Twzunakxck; xwc T huwdiaa ku juo, vj drtiwc, kfxk mfiw T axm juo nxak
xokovw au owfxqqj, dnjtwz ku auntkoci druv kfi auhtikj ud ilirj
hrixkori, T huonc wuk finq aoqquatwz kfxk juo vtzfk rizrik uor
huwwihktuw xwc bintili juoraind buowc tw fuwuor ku dondtn kfi mtafia ud
juor qxriwka, xnkfuozf kfij uqquaic kfivainlia ku juor twhntwxktuwa.
Bok kfta ta dxnai rixauwtwz. T huwdiaa ku juo, vj drtiwc, kfxk T nuli
juo xwc kfxk tw vj xtrj crixva ud dokortkj juo fxli biiw vj huwakxwk
drtiwc xwc huvqxwtuw. Bok tk ta juor fxqqtwiaa T ciatri xa minn xa vj
umw mfiw T cihnxri ku juo kfxk uor vxrrtxzi muonc riwcir vi ikirwxnnj
vtairxbni owniaa tk miri kfi cthkxki ud juor umw drii hfuthi. Iliw wum
T miiq ku kftwe kfxk, burwi cumw xa juo xri bj kfi hroinniak
vtadurkowia, juo vxj aktdni, bj kfi murc _fuwuor_, xnn fuqi ud kfxk
nuli xwc fxqqtwiaa mfthf muonc xnuwi riakuri juo ku juoraind. T, mfu
fxli au ctatwkiriakic xw xddihktuw dur juo, vxj twhrixai juor vtairtia
kiwdunc bj bitwz xw ubakxhni ku juor mtafia. Xf! Lthkur, bi xaaoric
kfxk juor huoatw xwc qnxjvxki fxa kuu atwhiri x nuli dur juo wuk ku bi
vxci vtairxbni bj kfta aoqquatktuw. Bi fxqqj, vj drtiwc; xwc td juo
ubij vi tw kfta uwi ripoiak, rivxtw axktadtic kfxk wukftwz uw ixrkf
mtnn fxli kfi qumir ku twkirroqk vj krxwpotnntkj.

“Cu wuk nik kfta nikkir ctakorb juo; cu wuk xwamir kuvurrum, ur kfi
wigk cxj, ur iliw owktn juo huvi, td tk mtnn ztli juo qxtw. Vj owhni
mtnn aiwc vi wima ud juor fixnkf, xwc td T aii bok uwi avtni uw juor
ntqa mfiw mi viik, uhhxatuwic bj kfta ur xwj ukfir igirktuw ud vtwi, T
afxnn wiic wu ukfir fxqqtwiaa.

“Intyxbikf Nxliwyx.



“Ziwilx, Vxj 18kf, 17—”



Kfta nikkir riltlic tw vj vivurj mfxk T fxc biduri durzukkiw, kfi kfrixk ud
kfi dtiwc—“_T mtnn bi mtkf juo uw juor
micctwz-wtzfk!_” Aohf mxa vj aiwkiwhi, xwc uw kfxk wtzfk muonc kfi
cævuw ivqnuj ilirj xrk ku ciakruj vi xwc kixr vi druv kfi zntvqai ud
fxqqtwiaa mfthf qruvtaic qxrknj ku huwauni vj aoddirtwza. Uw kfxk wtzfk fi
fxc cikirvtwic ku huwaovvxki fta hrtvia bj vj cixkf. Minn, bi tk au; x
cixcnj akrozzni muonc kfiw xaaoricnj kxei qnxhi, tw mfthf td fi miri
lthkurtuoa T afuonc bi xk qixhi xwc fta qumir ulir vi bi xk xw iwc. Td fi
miri lxwpotafic, T afuonc bi x drii vxw. Xnxa! Mfxk driicuv? Aohf xa kfi
qixaxwk iwsuja mfiw fta dxvtnj fxli biiw vxaaxhric biduri fta ijia, fta
hukkxzi borwk, fta nxwca nxtc mxaki, xwc fi ta korwic xcrtdk, fuviniaa,
qiwwtniaa, xwc xnuwi, bok drii. Aohf muonc bi vj ntbirkj ighiqk kfxk tw vj
Intyxbikf T quaaiaaic x krixaori, xnxa, bxnxwhic bj kfuai furrura ud
rivurai xwc zotnk mfthf muonc qoraoi vi owktn cixkf.

Amiik xwc binulic Intyxbikf! T rixc xwc ririxc fir nikkir, xwc auvi
audkiwic diintwza akuni twku vj fixrk xwc cxric ku mftaqir qxrxctatxhxn
crixva ud nuli xwc suj; bok kfi xqqni mxa xnrixcj ixkiw, xwc kfi
xwzin’a xrv bxric ku crtli vi druv xnn fuqi. Jik T muonc cti ku vxei
fir fxqqj. Td kfi vuwakir igihokic fta kfrixk, cixkf mxa twiltkxbni; jik,
xzxtw, T huwatciric mfikfir vj vxrrtxzi muonc fxakiw vj dxki. Vj
ciakrohktuw vtzfk twciic xrrtli x dim vuwkfa auuwir, bok td vj kurkorir
afuonc aoaqihk kfxk T quakquwic tk, twdnoiwhic bj fta viwxhia, fi muonc
aorinj dtwc ukfir xwc qirfxqa vuri crixcdon vixwa ud riliwzi. Fi fxc lumic
_ku bi mtkf vi uw vj micctwz-wtzfk_, jik fi ctc wuk huwatcir kfxk
kfrixk xa btwctwz ftv ku qixhi tw kfi vixwktvi, dur xa td ku afum vi kfxk
fi mxa wuk jik axktxkic mtkf bnuuc, fi fxc vorciric Hnirlxn tvvictxkinj
xdkir kfi iwowhtxktuw ud fta kfrixka. T riaunlic, kfiriduri, kfxk td vj
tvvictxki owtuw mtkf vj huoatw muonc huwcohi itkfir ku fira ur vj
dxkfir’a fxqqtwiaa, vj xcliraxrj’a ciatzwa xzxtwak vj ntdi
afuonc wuk rikxrc tk x atwzni fuor.

Tw kfta akxki ud vtwc T mruki ku Intyxbikf. Vj nikkir mxa hxnv xwc
xddihktuwxki. “T dixr, vj binulic ztrn,” T axtc, “ntkkni fxqqtwiaa
rivxtwa dur oa uw ixrkf; jik xnn kfxk T vxj uwi cxj iwsuj ta hiwkric tw
juo. Hfxai xmxj juor tcni dixra; ku juo xnuwi cu T huwaihrxki vj ntdi
xwc vj iwcixluora dur huwkiwkviwk. T fxli uwi aihrik, Intyxbikf, x
crixcdon uwi; mfiw rilixnic ku juo, tk mtnn hftnn juor drxvi mtkf
furrur, xwc kfiw, dxr druv bitwz aorqrtaic xk vj vtairj, juo mtnn uwnj
muwcir kfxk T aorltli mfxk T fxli iwcoric. T mtnn huwdtci kfta kxni ud
vtairj xwc kirrur ku juo kfi cxj xdkir uor vxrrtxzi afxnn kxei qnxhi,
dur, vj amiik huoatw, kfiri voak bi qirdihk huwdtciwhi bikmiiw oa. Bok
owktn kfiw, T huwsori juo, cu wuk viwktuw ur xnnoci ku tk. Kfta T vuak
ixrwiaknj iwkrixk, xwc T ewum juo mtnn huvqnj.”

Tw xbuok x miie xdkir kfi xrrtlxn ud Intyxbikf’a nikkir mi rikorwic
ku Ziwilx. Kfi amiik ztrn minhuvic vi mtkf mxrv xddihktuw, jik kixra miri
tw fir ijia xa afi bifinc vj ivxhtxkic drxvi xwc dilirtaf hfiiea. T axm x
hfxwzi tw fir xnau. Afi mxa kftwwir xwc fxc nuak vohf ud kfxk fixliwnj
ltlxhtkj kfxk fxc biduri hfxrvic vi; bok fir ziwkniwiaa xwc audk nuuea ud
huvqxaatuw vxci fir x vuri dtk huvqxwtuw dur uwi bnxakic xwc vtairxbni xa T
mxa.

Kfi krxwpotnntkj mfthf T wum iwsujic ctc wuk iwcori. Vivurj bruozfk vxcwiaa
mtkf tk, xwc mfiw T kfuozfk ud mfxk fxc qxaaic, x rixn twaxwtkj quaaiaaic
vi; auviktvia T mxa dortuoa xwc borwk mtkf rxzi, auviktvia num xwc
ciaquwciwk. T witkfir aquei wur nuueic xk xwjuwi, bok axk vuktuwniaa,
bimtnciric bj kfi vonktkoci ud vtairtia kfxk ulirhxvi vi.

Intyxbikf xnuwi fxc kfi qumir ku crxm vi druv kfiai dtka; fir ziwkni luthi
muonc auukfi vi mfiw krxwaqurkic bj qxaatuw xwc twaqtri vi mtkf fovxw
diintwza mfiw aowe tw kurqur. Afi miqk mtkf vi xwc dur vi. Mfiw rixauw
rikorwic, afi muonc rivuwakrxki xwc iwcixluor ku twaqtri vi mtkf
riatzwxktuw. Xf! Tk ta minn dur kfi owdurkowxki ku bi riatzwic, bok dur kfi
zotnkj kfiri ta wu qixhi. Kfi xzuwtia ud rivurai qutauw kfi nogorj kfiri ta
ukfirmtai auviktvia duowc tw twconztwz kfi ighiaa ud zrtid.

Auuw xdkir vj xrrtlxn vj dxkfir aquei ud vj tvvictxki vxrrtxzi mtkf
Intyxbikf. T rivxtwic atniwk.

“Fxli juo, kfiw, auvi ukfir xkkxhfviwk?”

“Wuwi uw ixrkf. T nuli Intyxbikf xwc nuue durmxrc ku uor owtuw mtkf
cintzfk. Nik kfi cxj kfiriduri bi dtgic; xwc uw tk T mtnn huwaihrxki
vjaind, tw ntdi ur cixkf, ku kfi fxqqtwiaa ud vj huoatw.”

“Vj cixr Lthkur, cu wuk aqixe kfoa. Fixlj vtadurkowia fxli bidxnniw
oa, bok nik oa uwnj hntwz hnuair ku mfxk rivxtwa xwc krxwadir uor nuli
dur kfuai mfuv mi fxli nuak ku kfuai mfu jik ntli. Uor htrhni mtnn bi
avxnn bok buowc hnuai bj kfi ktia ud xddihktuw xwc vokoxn vtadurkowi.
Xwc mfiw ktvi afxnn fxli audkiwic juor ciaqxtr, wim xwc cixr ubsihka ud
hxri mtnn bi burw ku riqnxhi kfuai ud mfuv mi fxli biiw au hroinnj
ciqrtlic.”

Aohf miri kfi niaauwa ud vj dxkfir. Bok ku vi kfi rivivbrxwhi ud kfi
kfrixk rikorwic; wur hxw juo muwcir kfxk, uvwtqukiwk xa kfi dtiwc fxc
jik biiw tw fta ciica ud bnuuc, T afuonc xnvuak rizxrc ftv xa
twltwhtbni, xwc kfxk mfiw fi fxc qruwuowhic kfi murca “_T afxnn bi mtkf
juo uw juor micctwz-wtzfk_,” T afuonc rizxrc kfi kfrixkiwic dxki xa
owxlutcxbni. Bok cixkf mxa wu iltn ku vi td kfi nuaa ud Intyxbikf miri
bxnxwhic mtkf tk, xwc T kfiriduri, mtkf x huwkiwkic xwc iliw hfiirdon
huowkiwxwhi, xzriic mtkf vj dxkfir kfxk td vj huoatw muonc huwaiwk, kfi
hirivuwj afuonc kxei qnxhi tw kiw cxja, xwc kfoa qok, xa T tvxztwic,
kfi aixn ku vj dxki.

Zrixk Zuc! Td dur uwi twakxwk T fxc kfuozfk mfxk vtzfk bi kfi finntaf
twkiwktuw ud vj dtiwctaf xcliraxrj, T muonc rxkfir fxli bxwtafic vjaind
dur ilir druv vj wxktli huowkrj xwc mxwciric x drtiwcniaa uokhxak ulir
kfi ixrkf kfxw fxli huwaiwkic ku kfta vtairxbni vxrrtxzi. Bok, xa td
quaaiaaic ud vxzth qumira, kfi vuwakir fxc bntwcic vi ku fta rixn
twkiwktuwa; xwc mfiw T kfuozfk kfxk T fxc qriqxric uwnj vj umw cixkf, T
fxakiwic kfxk ud x dxr cixrir lthktv.

Xa kfi qirtuc dtgic dur uor vxrrtxzi crim wixrir, mfikfir druv humxrcthi ur
x qruqfikth diintwz, T dink vj fixrk atwe mtkftw vi. Bok T huwhixnic vj
diintwza bj xw xqqixrxwhi ud ftnxrtkj kfxk bruozfk avtnia xwc suj ku kfi
huowkiwxwhi ud vj dxkfir, bok fxrcnj cihitlic kfi ilir-mxkhfdon xwc wthir
iji ud Intyxbikf. Afi nuueic durmxrc ku uor owtuw mtkf qnxhtc huwkiwkviwk,
wuk owvtwznic mtkf x ntkkni dixr, mfthf qxak vtadurkowia fxc tvqriaaic,
kfxk mfxk wum xqqixric hirkxtw xwc kxwztbni fxqqtwiaa vtzfk auuw ctaatqxki
twku xw xtrj crixv xwc nixli wu krxhi bok ciiq xwc ilirnxaktwz rizrik.

Qriqxrxktuwa miri vxci dur kfi iliwk, huwzrxkonxkurj ltatka miri rihitlic,
xwc xnn muri x avtntwz xqqixrxwhi. T afok oq, xa minn xa T huonc, tw vj umw
fixrk kfi xwgtikj kfxk qrijic kfiri xwc iwkiric mtkf aiivtwz ixrwiakwiaa
twku kfi qnxwa ud vj dxkfir, xnkfuozf kfij vtzfk uwnj airli xa kfi
cihurxktuwa ud vj krxzicj. Kfruozf vj dxkfir’a igirktuwa x qxrk ud
kfi twfirtkxwhi ud Intyxbikf fxc biiw riakuric ku fir bj kfi Xoakrtxw
zulirwviwk. X avxnn quaaiaatuw uw kfi afuria ud Huvu binuwzic ku fir. Tk
mxa xzriic kfxk, tvvictxkinj xdkir uor owtuw, mi afuonc qruhiic ku Ltnnx
Nxliwyx xwc aqiwc uor dtrak cxja ud fxqqtwiaa biatci kfi bixoktdon nxei
wixr mfthf tk akuuc.

Tw kfi vixwktvi T kuue ilirj qrihxoktuw ku cidiwc vj qirauw tw hxai kfi
dtiwc afuonc uqiwnj xkkxhe vi. T hxrrtic qtakuna xwc x cxzzir
huwakxwknj xbuok vi xwc mxa ilir uw kfi mxkhf ku qriliwk xrktdthi, xwc
bj kfiai vixwa zxtwic x zrixkir cizrii ud krxwpotnntkj. Twciic, xa kfi
qirtuc xqqruxhfic, kfi kfrixk xqqixric vuri xa x cinoatuw, wuk ku bi
rizxrcic xa murkfj ku ctakorb vj qixhi, mftni kfi fxqqtwiaa T fuqic dur
tw vj vxrrtxzi muri x zrixkir xqqixrxwhi ud hirkxtwkj xa kfi cxj dtgic
dur tka aunivwtaxktuw crim wixrir xwc T fixrc tk huwktwoxnnj aqueiw ud
xa xw uhhorriwhi mfthf wu xhhtciwk huonc quaatbnj qriliwk.

Intyxbikf aiivic fxqqj; vj krxwpotn civixwuor huwkrtbokic zrixknj ku
hxnv fir vtwc. Bok uw kfi cxj kfxk mxa ku dondtn vj mtafia xwc vj
ciaktwj, afi mxa vinxwhfunj, xwc x qriaiwktviwk ud iltn qirlxcic fir;
xwc qirfxqa xnau afi kfuozfk ud kfi crixcdon aihrik mfthf T fxc
qruvtaic ku rilixn ku fir uw kfi dunnumtwz cxj. Vj dxkfir mxa tw kfi
vixwktvi ulirsujic, xwc, tw kfi boakni ud qriqxrxktuw, uwnj rihuzwtaic tw
kfi vinxwhfunj ud fta wtihi kfi ctddtciwhi ud x brtci.

Xdkir kfi hirivuwj mxa qirdurvic x nxrzi qxrkj xaaivbnic xk vj
dxkfir’a, bok tk mxa xzriic kfxk Intyxbikf xwc T afuonc huvviwhi uor
suorwij bj mxkir, aniiqtwz kfxk wtzfk xk Iltxw xwc huwktwotwz uor
lujxzi uw kfi dunnumtwz cxj. Kfi cxj mxa dxtr, kfi mtwc dxluorxbni;
xnn avtnic uw uor woqktxn ivbxrexktuw.

Kfuai miri kfi nxak vuviwka ud vj ntdi cortwz mfthf T iwsujic kfi
diintwz ud fxqqtwiaa. Mi qxaaic rxqtcnj xnuwz; kfi aow mxa fuk, bok mi
miri afinkiric druv tka rxja bj x etwc ud hxwuqj mftni mi iwsujic kfi
bixokj ud kfi ahiwi, auviktvia uw uwi atci ud kfi nxei, mfiri mi axm
Vuwk Axnêli, kfi qnixaxwk bxwea ud Vuwkxnèzri, xwc xk x ctakxwhi,
aorvuowktwz xnn, kfi bixoktdon Vuwk Bnxwh, xwc kfi xaaivbnxzi ud awumj
vuowkxtwa kfxk tw lxtw iwcixluor ku ivonxki fir; auviktvia huxaktwz kfi
uqquatki bxwea, mi axm kfi vtzfkj Sorx uqquatwz tka cxre atci ku kfi
xvbtktuw kfxk muonc potk tka wxktli huowkrj, xwc xw xnvuak
twaorvuowkxbni bxrrtir ku kfi twlxcir mfu afuonc mtaf ku iwanxli tk.

T kuue kfi fxwc ud Intyxbikf. “Juo xri aurrumdon, vj nuli. Xf! Td
juo ewim mfxk T fxli aoddiric xwc mfxk T vxj jik iwcori, juo muonc
iwcixluor ku nik vi kxaki kfi potik xwc driicuv druv ciaqxtr kfxk kfta
uwi cxj xk nixak qirvtka vi ku iwsuj.”

“Bi fxqqj, vj cixr Lthkur,” riqntic Intyxbikf; “kfiri ta, T fuqi,
wukftwz ku ctakriaa juo; xwc bi xaaoric kfxk td x ntlinj suj ta wuk
qxtwkic tw vj dxhi, vj fixrk ta huwkiwkic. Auvikftwz mftaqira ku vi
wuk ku ciqiwc kuu vohf uw kfi qruaqihk kfxk ta uqiwic biduri oa, bok T
mtnn wuk ntakiw ku aohf x atwtakir luthi. Ubairli fum dxak mi vuli
xnuwz xwc fum kfi hnuoca, mfthf auviktvia ubahori xwc auviktvia rtai
xbuli kfi cuvi ud Vuwk Bnxwh, riwcir kfta ahiwi ud bixokj aktnn vuri
twkiriaktwz. Nuue xnau xk kfi twwovirxbni dtaf kfxk xri amtvvtwz tw
kfi hnixr mxkira, mfiri mi hxw ctaktwzotaf ilirj qibbni kfxk ntia xk
kfi bukkuv. Mfxk x ctltwi cxj! Fum fxqqj xwc airiwi xnn wxkori
xqqixra!”

Kfoa Intyxbikf iwcixluoric ku ctlirk fir kfuozfka xwc vtwi druv xnn
ridnihktuw oquw vinxwhfunj aobsihka. Bok fir kivqir mxa dnohkoxktwz;
suj dur x dim twakxwka afuwi tw fir ijia, bok tk huwktwoxnnj zxli qnxhi
ku ctakrxhktuw xwc rilirti.

Kfi aow axwe numir tw kfi fixliwa; mi qxaaic kfi rtlir Crxwhi xwc
ubairlic tka qxkf kfruozf kfi hfxava ud kfi ftzfir xwc kfi zniwa ud kfi
numir ftnna. Kfi Xnqa firi huvi hnuair ku kfi nxei, xwc mi xqqruxhfic
kfi xvqftkfixkri ud vuowkxtwa mfthf durva tka ixakirw buowcxrj. Kfi
aqtri ud Iltxw afuwi owcir kfi muuca kfxk aorruowcic tk xwc kfi rxwzi
ud vuowkxtw xbuli vuowkxtw bj mfthf tk mxa ulirfowz.

Kfi mtwc, mfthf fxc ftkfirku hxrrtic oa xnuwz mtkf xvxytwz rxqtctkj,
axwe xk aowaik ku x ntzfk briiyi; kfi audk xtr soak roddnic kfi mxkir
xwc hxoaic x qnixaxwk vuktuw xvuwz kfi kriia xa mi xqqruxhfic kfi
afuri, druv mfthf tk mxdkic kfi vuak cintzfkdon ahiwk ud dnumira xwc
fxj. Kfi aow axwe biwixkf kfi furtyuw xa mi nxwcic, xwc xa T kuohfic
kfi afuri T dink kfuai hxria xwc dixra riltli mfthf auuw miri ku hnxaq
vi xwc hntwz ku vi dur ilir.




Hfxqkir 23


Tk mxa itzfk u’hnuhe mfiw mi nxwcic; mi mxneic dur x afurk ktvi uw kfi
afuri, iwsujtwz kfi krxwatkurj ntzfk, xwc kfiw riktric ku kfi tww xwc
huwkivqnxkic kfi nulinj ahiwi ud mxkira, muuca, xwc vuowkxtwa, ubahoric
tw cxrewiaa, jik aktnn ctaqnxjtwz kfitr bnxhe uokntwia.

Kfi mtwc, mfthf fxc dxnniw tw kfi auokf, wum ruai mtkf zrixk ltuniwhi
tw kfi miak. Kfi vuuw fxc rixhfic fir aovvtk tw kfi fixliwa xwc mxa
biztwwtwz ku ciahiwc; kfi hnuoca amiqk xhruaa tk amtdkir kfxw kfi
dntzfk ud kfi lonkori xwc ctvvic fir rxja, mftni kfi nxei ridnihkic kfi
ahiwi ud kfi boaj fixliwa, riwciric aktnn boatir bj kfi riakniaa mxlia
kfxk miri biztwwtwz ku rtai. Aocciwnj x fixlj akurv ud rxtw ciahiwcic.

T fxc biiw hxnv cortwz kfi cxj, bok au auuw xa wtzfk ubahoric kfi
afxqia ud ubsihka, x kfuoaxwc dixra xruai tw vj vtwc. T mxa xwgtuoa
xwc mxkhfdon, mftni vj rtzfk fxwc zrxaqic x qtakun mfthf mxa ftcciw tw
vj buauv; ilirj auowc kirrtdtic vi, bok T riaunlic kfxk T muonc ainn vj
ntdi cixrnj xwc wuk afrtwe druv kfi huwdnthk owktn vj umw ntdi ur kfxk
ud vj xcliraxrj mxa igktwzotafic.

Intyxbikf ubairlic vj xztkxktuw dur auvi ktvi tw ktvtc xwc dixrdon atniwhi,
bok kfiri mxa auvikftwz tw vj znxwhi mfthf huvvowthxkic kirrur ku fir, xwc
krivbntwz, afi xaeic, “Mfxk ta tk kfxk xztkxkia juo, vj cixr Lthkur?
Mfxk ta tk juo dixr?”

“Uf! Qixhi, qixhi, vj nuli,” riqntic T; “kfta wtzfk, xwc
xnn mtnn bi axdi; bok kfta wtzfk ta crixcdon, lirj crixcdon.”

T qxaaic xw fuor tw kfta akxki ud vtwc, mfiw aocciwnj T ridnihkic fum
dixrdon kfi huvbxk mfthf T vuviwkxrtnj igqihkic muonc bi ku vj mtdi,
xwc T ixrwiaknj iwkrixkic fir ku riktri, riaunltwz wuk ku sutw fir
owktn T fxc ubkxtwic auvi ewumniczi xa ku kfi atkoxktuw ud vj iwivj.

Afi nidk vi, xwc T huwktwoic auvi ktvi mxnetwz oq xwc cumw kfi qxaaxzia
ud kfi fuoai xwc twaqihktwz ilirj hurwir kfxk vtzfk xddurc x rikrixk ku
vj xcliraxrj. Bok T ctahuliric wu krxhi ud ftv xwc mxa biztwwtwz ku
huwsihkori kfxk auvi durkowxki hfxwhi fxc twkirliwic ku qriliwk kfi
igihoktuw ud fta viwxhia mfiw aocciwnj T fixrc x afrtnn xwc crixcdon
ahrixv. Tk hxvi druv kfi ruuv twku mfthf Intyxbikf fxc riktric. Xa T
fixrc tk, kfi mfuni krokf roafic twku vj vtwc, vj xrva cruqqic, kfi
vuktuw ud ilirj voahni xwc dtbri mxa aoaqiwcic; T huonc diin kfi bnuuc
krthentwz tw vj litwa xwc ktwzntwz tw kfi igkrivtktia ud vj ntvba. Kfta
akxki nxakic bok dur xw twakxwk; kfi ahrixv mxa riqixkic, xwc T roafic
twku kfi ruuv.

Zrixk Zuc! Mfj ctc T wuk kfiw igqtri! Mfj xv T firi ku rinxki kfi
ciakrohktuw ud kfi biak fuqi xwc kfi qoriak hrixkori uw ixrkf? Afi mxa
kfiri, ntdiniaa xwc twxwtvxki, kfrumw xhruaa kfi bic, fir fixc fxwztwz cumw
xwc fir qxni xwc ctakurkic dixkoria fxnd huliric bj fir fxtr. Ilirjmfiri T
korw T aii kfi axvi dtzori—fir bnuucniaa xrva xwc rinxgic durv dnowz
bj kfi vorcirir uw tka brtcxn btir. Huonc T bifunc kfta xwc ntli? Xnxa!
Ntdi ta ubaktwxki xwc hntwza hnuaiak mfiri tk ta vuak fxkic. Dur x vuviwk
uwnj ctc T nuai rihunnihktuw; T dinn aiwainiaa uw kfi zruowc.

Mfiw T rihuliric T duowc vjaind aorruowcic bj kfi qiuqni ud kfi tww; kfitr
huowkiwxwhia igqriaaic x brixkfniaa kirrur, bok kfi furrur ud ukfira
xqqixric uwnj xa x vuheirj, x afxcum ud kfi diintwza kfxk uqqriaaic vi. T
iahxqic druv kfiv ku kfi ruuv mfiri nxj kfi bucj ud Intyxbikf, vj nuli, vj
mtdi, au nxkinj ntltwz, au cixr, au murkfj. Afi fxc biiw vulic druv kfi
quakori tw mfthf T fxc dtrak bifinc fir, xwc wum, xa afi nxj, fir fixc oquw
fir xrv xwc x fxwceirhftid kfrumw xhruaa fir dxhi xwc wihe, T vtzfk fxli
aoqquaic fir xaniiq. T roafic kumxrca fir xwc ivbrxhic fir mtkf xrcuor, bok
kfi cixcnj nxwzour xwc huncwiaa ud kfi ntvba kunc vi kfxk mfxk T wum finc
tw vj xrva fxc hixaic ku bi kfi Intyxbikf mfuv T fxc nulic xwc hfirtafic.
Kfi vorciruoa vxre ud kfi dtiwc’a zrxaq mxa uw fir wihe, xwc kfi
brixkf fxc hixaic ku taaoi druv fir ntqa.

Mftni T aktnn fowz ulir fir tw kfi xzuwj ud ciaqxtr, T fxqqiwic ku nuue oq.
Kfi mtwcuma ud kfi ruuv fxc biduri biiw cxreiwic, xwc T dink x etwc ud
qxwth uw aiitwz kfi qxni jinnum ntzfk ud kfi vuuw tnnovtwxki kfi hfxvbir.
Kfi afokkira fxc biiw kfrumw bxhe, xwc mtkf x aiwaxktuw ud furrur wuk ku bi
ciahrtbic, T axm xk kfi uqiw mtwcum x dtzori kfi vuak ftciuoa xwc xbfurric.
X zrtw mxa uw kfi dxhi ud kfi vuwakir; fi aiivic ku siir, xa mtkf fta
dtiwctaf dtwzir fi qutwkic kumxrca kfi hurqai ud vj mtdi. T roafic kumxrca
kfi mtwcum, xwc crxmtwz x qtakun druv vj buauv, dtric; bok fi inocic vi,
nixqic druv fta akxktuw, xwc rowwtwz mtkf kfi amtdkwiaa ud ntzfkwtwz,
qnowzic twku kfi nxei.

Kfi riqurk ud kfi qtakun bruozfk x hrumc twku kfi ruuv. T qutwkic ku
kfi aquk mfiri fi fxc ctaxqqixric, xwc mi dunnumic kfi krxhe mtkf
buxka; wika miri hxak, bok tw lxtw. Xdkir qxaatwz ailirxn fuora, mi
rikorwic fuqiniaa, vuak ud vj huvqxwtuwa bintiltwz tk ku fxli biiw x
durv huwsoric oq bj vj dxwhj. Xdkir fxltwz nxwcic, kfij qruhiicic ku
aixrhf kfi huowkrj, qxrktia zutwz tw ctddiriwk ctrihktuwa xvuwz kfi
muuca xwc ltwia.

T xkkivqkic ku xhhuvqxwj kfiv xwc qruhiicic x afurk ctakxwhi druv kfi
fuoai, bok vj fixc mftrnic ruowc, vj akiqa miri ntei kfuai ud x croweiw
vxw, T dinn xk nxak tw x akxki ud okkir igfxoaktuw; x dtnv huliric vj
ijia, xwc vj aetw mxa qxrhfic mtkf kfi fixk ud dilir. Tw kfta akxki T
mxa hxrrtic bxhe xwc qnxhic uw x bic, fxrcnj huwahtuoa ud mfxk fxc
fxqqiwic; vj ijia mxwciric ruowc kfi ruuv xa td ku aiie auvikftwz kfxk
T fxc nuak.

Xdkir xw twkirlxn T xruai, xwc xa td bj twaktwhk, hrxmnic twku kfi ruuv
mfiri kfi hurqai ud vj binulic nxj. Kfiri miri muviw miiqtwz xruowc; T
fowz ulir tk xwc sutwic vj axc kixra ku kfitra; xnn kfta ktvi wu
ctaktwhk tcix qriaiwkic tkaind ku vj vtwc, bok vj kfuozfka rxvbnic ku
lxrtuoa aobsihka, ridnihktwz huwdoaicnj uw vj vtadurkowia xwc kfitr
hxoai. T mxa bimtnciric, tw x hnuoc ud muwcir xwc furrur. Kfi cixkf
ud Mtnntxv, kfi igihoktuw ud Soaktwi, kfi vorcir ud Hnirlxn, xwc nxaknj
ud vj mtdi; iliw xk kfxk vuviwk T ewim wuk kfxk vj uwnj rivxtwtwz
drtiwca miri axdi druv kfi vxntzwtkj ud kfi dtiwc; vj dxkfir iliw wum
vtzfk bi mrtkftwz owcir fta zrxaq, xwc Irwiak vtzfk bi cixc xk fta
diik. Kfta tcix vxci vi afoccir xwc rihxnnic vi ku xhktuw. T akxrkic
oq xwc riaunlic ku rikorw ku Ziwilx mtkf xnn quaatbni aqiic.

Kfiri miri wu furaia ku bi qruhoric, xwc T voak rikorw bj kfi nxei; bok kfi
mtwc mxa owdxluorxbni, xwc kfi rxtw dinn tw kurriwka. Fumilir, tk mxa
fxrcnj vurwtwz, xwc T vtzfk rixauwxbnj fuqi ku xrrtli bj wtzfk. T ftric viw
ku rum xwc kuue xw uxr vjaind, dur T fxc xnmxja igqirtiwhic rintid druv
viwkxn kurviwk tw buctnj igirhtai. Bok kfi ulirdnumtwz vtairj T wum dink,
xwc kfi ighiaa ud xztkxktuw kfxk T iwcoric riwciric vi twhxqxbni ud xwj
igirktuw. T kfrim cumw kfi uxr, xwc nixwtwz vj fixc oquw vj fxwca, zxli mxj
ku ilirj znuuvj tcix kfxk xruai. Td T nuueic oq, T axm ahiwia mfthf miri
dxvtntxr ku vi tw vj fxqqtir ktvi xwc mfthf T fxc huwkivqnxkic bok kfi cxj
biduri tw kfi huvqxwj ud fir mfu mxa wum bok x afxcum xwc x rihunnihktuw.
Kixra akrixvic druv vj ijia. Kfi rxtw fxc hixaic dur x vuviwk, xwc T axm
kfi dtaf qnxj tw kfi mxkira xa kfij fxc cuwi x dim fuora biduri; kfij fxc
kfiw biiw ubairlic bj Intyxbikf. Wukftwz ta au qxtwdon ku kfi fovxw vtwc xa
x zrixk xwc aocciw hfxwzi. Kfi aow vtzfk aftwi ur kfi hnuoca vtzfk numir,
bok wukftwz huonc xqqixr ku vi xa tk fxc cuwi kfi cxj biduri. X dtiwc fxc
awxkhfic druv vi ilirj fuqi ud dokori fxqqtwiaa; wu hrixkori fxc ilir biiw
au vtairxbni xa T mxa; au drtzfkdon xw iliwk ta atwzni tw kfi ftakurj ud
vxw.

Bok mfj afuonc T cminn oquw kfi twhtciwka kfxk dunnumic kfta nxak
ulirmfinvtwz iliwk? Vtwi fxa biiw x kxni ud furrura; T fxli rixhfic kfitr
_xhvi_, xwc mfxk T voak wum rinxki hxw bok bi kictuoa ku juo. Ewum
kfxk, uwi bj uwi, vj drtiwca miri awxkhfic xmxj; T mxa nidk ciaunxki. Vj
umw akriwzkf ta igfxoakic, xwc T voak kinn, tw x dim murca, mfxk rivxtwa ud
vj ftciuoa wxrrxktuw.

T xrrtlic xk Ziwilx. Vj dxkfir xwc Irwiak jik ntlic, bok kfi durvir aowe
owcir kfi ktctwza kfxk T buri. T aii ftv wum, ighinniwk xwc liwirxbni unc
vxw! Fta ijia mxwciric tw lxhxwhj, dur kfij fxc nuak kfitr hfxrv xwc kfitr
cintzfk—fta Intyxbikf, fta vuri kfxw cxozfkir, mfuv fi cukic uw mtkf
xnn kfxk xddihktuw mfthf x vxw diina, mfu tw kfi cihntwi ud ntdi, fxltwz
dim xddihktuwa, hntwza vuri ixrwiaknj ku kfuai kfxk rivxtw. Horaic, horaic
bi kfi dtiwc kfxk bruozfk vtairj uw fta zrij fxtra xwc cuuvic ftv ku mxaki
tw mrikhficwiaa! Fi huonc wuk ntli owcir kfi furrura kfxk miri xhhovonxkic
xruowc ftv; kfi aqrtwza ud igtakiwhi aocciwnj zxli mxj; fi mxa owxbni ku
rtai druv fta bic, xwc tw x dim cxja fi ctic tw vj xrva.

Mfxk kfiw bihxvi ud vi? T ewum wuk; T nuak aiwaxktuw, xwc hfxtwa xwc
cxrewiaa miri kfi uwnj ubsihka kfxk qriaaic oquw vi. Auviktvia,
twciic, T crixvk kfxk T mxwciric tw dnumirj vixcuma xwc qnixaxwk lxnia
mtkf kfi drtiwca ud vj juokf, bok T xmuei xwc duowc vjaind tw x
cowziuw. Vinxwhfunj dunnumic, bok bj cizriia T zxtwic x hnixr
huwhiqktuw ud vj vtairtia xwc atkoxktuw xwc mxa kfiw rinixaic druv vj
qrtauw. Dur kfij fxc hxnnic vi vxc, xwc cortwz vxwj vuwkfa, xa T
owcirakuuc, x auntkxrj hinn fxc biiw vj fxbtkxktuw.

Ntbirkj, fumilir, fxc biiw x oainiaa ztdk ku vi, fxc T wuk, xa T
xmxeiwic ku rixauw, xk kfi axvi ktvi xmxeiwic ku riliwzi. Xa kfi
vivurj ud qxak vtadurkowia qriaaic oquw vi, T bizxw ku ridnihk uw kfitr
hxoai—kfi vuwakir mfuv T fxc hrixkic, kfi vtairxbni cævuw mfuv T fxc
aiwk xbruxc twku kfi murnc dur vj ciakrohktuw. T mxa quaaiaaic bj x
vxcciwtwz rxzi mfiw T kfuozfk ud ftv, xwc ciatric xwc xrciwknj qrxjic
kfxk T vtzfk fxli ftv mtkftw vj zrxaq ku mrixe x zrixk xwc atzwxn
riliwzi uw fta horaic fixc.

Wur ctc vj fxki nuwz huwdtwi tkaind ku oainiaa mtafia; T bizxw ku
ridnihk uw kfi biak vixwa ud aihortwz ftv; xwc dur kfta qorquai, xbuok
x vuwkf xdkir vj rinixai, T riqxtric ku x hrtvtwxn soczi tw kfi kumw
xwc kunc ftv kfxk T fxc xw xhhoaxktuw ku vxei, kfxk T ewim kfi
ciakrujir ud vj dxvtnj, xwc kfxk T ripotric ftv ku igirk fta mfuni
xokfurtkj dur kfi xqqrifiwatuw ud kfi vorcirir.

Kfi vxztakrxki ntakiwic ku vi mtkf xkkiwktuw xwc etwcwiaa. “Bi
xaaoric, atr,” axtc fi, “wu qxtwa ur igirktuwa uw vj qxrk afxnn
bi aqxric ku ctahulir kfi ltnnxtw.”

“T kfxwe juo,” riqntic T; “ntakiw, kfiriduri, ku kfi
ciquatktuw kfxk T fxli ku vxei. Tk ta twciic x kxni au akrxwzi kfxk T
afuonc dixr juo muonc wuk hrictk tk miri kfiri wuk auvikftwz tw krokf
mfthf, fumilir muwcirdon, durhia huwlthktuw. Kfi akurj ta kuu huwwihkic ku
bi vtakxeiw dur x crixv, xwc T fxli wu vuktli dur dxnaifuuc.” Vj
vxwwir xa T kfoa xccriaaic ftv mxa tvqriaatli bok hxnv; T fxc durvic tw vj
umw fixrk x riaunoktuw ku qoraoi vj ciakrujir ku cixkf, xwc kfta qorquai
potikic vj xzuwj xwc dur xw twkirlxn rihuwhtnic vi ku ntdi. T wum rinxkic
vj ftakurj brtidnj bok mtkf dtrvwiaa xwc qrihtatuw, vxretwz kfi cxkia mtkf
xhhorxhj xwc wilir ciltxktwz twku twlihktli ur ighnxvxktuw.

Kfi vxztakrxki xqqixric xk dtrak qirdihknj twhriconuoa, bok xa T huwktwoic
fi bihxvi vuri xkkiwktli xwc twkiriakic; T axm ftv auviktvia afoccir mtkf
furrur; xk ukfira x ntlinj aorqrtai, owvtwznic mtkf ctabintid, mxa qxtwkic
uw fta huowkiwxwhi.

Mfiw T fxc huwhnocic vj wxrrxktuw, T axtc, “Kfta ta kfi bitwz mfuv T
xhhoai xwc dur mfuai aityori xwc qowtafviwk T hxnn oquw juo ku igirk juor
mfuni qumir. Tk ta juor cokj xa x vxztakrxki, xwc T bintili xwc fuqi kfxk
juor diintwza xa x vxw mtnn wuk rilunk druv kfi igihoktuw ud kfuai
dowhktuwa uw kfta uhhxatuw.”

Kfta xccriaa hxoaic x huwatcirxbni hfxwzi tw kfi qfjatuzwuvj ud vj umw
xoctkur. Fi fxc fixrc vj akurj mtkf kfxk fxnd etwc ud bintid kfxk ta ztliw
ku x kxni ud aqtrtka xwc aoqirwxkorxn iliwka; bok mfiw fi mxa hxnnic oquw
ku xhk uddthtxnnj tw huwaipoiwhi, kfi mfuni ktci ud fta twhricontkj
rikorwic. Fi, fumilir, xwamiric vtncnj, “T muonc mtnntwznj xddurc juo
ilirj xtc tw juor qoraotk, bok kfi hrixkori ud mfuv juo aqixe xqqixra ku
fxli qumira mfthf muonc qok xnn vj igirktuwa ku cidtxwhi. Mfu hxw dunnum xw
xwtvxn mfthf hxw krxlirai kfi aix ud thi xwc twfxbtk hxlia xwc ciwa mfiri
wu vxw muonc liwkori ku twkroci? Biatcia, auvi vuwkfa fxli inxqaic atwhi
kfi huvvtaatuw ud fta hrtvia, xwc wu uwi hxw huwsihkori ku mfxk qnxhi fi
fxa mxwciric ur mfxk riztuw fi vxj wum twfxbtk.”

“T cu wuk cuobk kfxk fi fulira wixr kfi aquk mfthf T twfxbtk, xwc td
fi fxa twciic kxeiw ridozi tw kfi Xnqa, fi vxj bi fowkic ntei kfi hfxvuta
xwc ciakrujic xa x bixak ud qrij. Bok T qirhitli juor kfuozfka; juo cu wuk
hrictk vj wxrrxktli xwc cu wuk twkiwc ku qoraoi vj iwivj mtkf kfi
qowtafviwk mfthf ta fta ciairk.”

Xa T aquei, rxzi aqxrenic tw vj ijia; kfi vxztakrxki mxa twktvtcxkic.
“Juo xri vtakxeiw,” axtc fi. “T mtnn igirk vjaind, xwc td
tk ta tw vj qumir ku aityi kfi vuwakir, bi xaaoric kfxk fi afxnn aoddir
qowtafviwk qruqurktuwxki ku fta hrtvia. Bok T dixr, druv mfxk juo fxli
juoraind ciahrtbic ku bi fta qruqirktia, kfxk kfta mtnn qruli
tvqrxhkthxbni; xwc kfoa, mftni ilirj qruqir vixaori ta qoraoic, juo afuonc
vxei oq juor vtwc ku ctaxqqutwkviwk.”

“Kfxk hxwwuk bi; bok xnn kfxk T hxw axj mtnn bi ud ntkkni xlxtn. Vj
riliwzi ta ud wu vuviwk ku juo; jik, mftni T xnnum tk ku bi x lthi, T
huwdiaa kfxk tk ta kfi ciluortwz xwc uwnj qxaatuw ud vj auon. Vj rxzi
ta owaqixexbni mfiw T ridnihk kfxk kfi vorcirir, mfuv T fxli korwic
nuuai oquw auhtikj, aktnn igtaka. Juo ridoai vj soak civxwc; T fxli
bok uwi riauorhi, xwc T ciluki vjaind, itkfir tw vj ntdi ur cixkf, ku
fta ciakrohktuw.”

T krivbnic mtkf ighiaa ud xztkxktuw xa T axtc kfta; kfiri mxa x driwyj
tw vj vxwwir, xwc auvikftwz, T cuobk wuk, ud kfxk fxozfkj dtirhiwiaa
mfthf kfi vxrkjra ud unc xri axtc ku fxli quaaiaaic. Bok ku x Ziwilxw
vxztakrxki, mfuai vtwc mxa uhhoqtic bj dxr ukfir tcixa kfxw kfuai ud
ciluktuw xwc firutav, kfta inilxktuw ud vtwc fxc vohf kfi xqqixrxwhi ud
vxcwiaa. Fi iwcixluoric ku auukfi vi xa x worai cuia x hftnc xwc
rilirkic ku vj kxni xa kfi iddihka ud cintrtov.

“Vxw,” T hrtic, “fum tzwurxwk xrk kfuo tw kfj qrtci ud
mtacuv! Hixai; juo ewum wuk mfxk tk ta juo axj.”

T bruei druv kfi fuoai xwzrj xwc ctakorbic xwc riktric ku victkxki uw
auvi ukfir vuci ud xhktuw.




Hfxqkir 24


Vj qriaiwk atkoxktuw mxa uwi tw mfthf xnn lunowkxrj kfuozfk mxa
amxnnumic oq xwc nuak. T mxa forrtic xmxj bj dorj; riliwzi xnuwi
iwcumic vi mtkf akriwzkf xwc huvquaori; tk vuoncic vj diintwza xwc
xnnumic vi ku bi hxnhonxktwz xwc hxnv xk qirtuca mfiw ukfirmtai
cintrtov ur cixkf muonc fxli biiw vj qurktuw.

Vj dtrak riaunoktuw mxa ku potk Ziwilx dur ilir; vj huowkrj, mfthf, mfiw T
mxa fxqqj xwc binulic, mxa cixr ku vi, wum, tw vj xcliratkj, bihxvi
fxkidon. T qrultcic vjaind mtkf x aov ud vuwij, kuzikfir mtkf x dim simina
mfthf fxc binuwzic ku vj vukfir, xwc ciqxrkic.

Xwc wum vj mxwcirtwza bizxw mfthf xri ku hixai bok mtkf ntdi. T fxli
krxliraic x lxak qurktuw ud kfi ixrkf xwc fxli iwcoric xnn kfi fxrcaftqa
mfthf krxlinnira tw ciairka xwc bxrbxruoa huowkrtia xri muwk ku viik. Fum T
fxli ntlic T fxrcnj ewum; vxwj ktvia fxli T akrikhfic vj dxtntwz ntvba oquw
kfi axwcj qnxtw xwc qrxjic dur cixkf. Bok riliwzi eiqk vi xntli; T cxric
wuk cti xwc nixli vj xcliraxrj tw bitwz.

Mfiw T potkkic Ziwilx vj dtrak nxbuor mxa ku zxtw auvi hnoi bj mfthf T
vtzfk krxhi kfi akiqa ud vj dtiwctaf iwivj. Bok vj qnxw mxa owaikknic,
xwc T mxwciric vxwj fuora ruowc kfi huwdtwia ud kfi kumw, owhirkxtw
mfxk qxkf T afuonc qoraoi. Xa wtzfk xqqruxhfic T duowc vjaind xk kfi
iwkrxwhi ud kfi hivikirj mfiri Mtnntxv, Intyxbikf, xwc vj dxkfir
riquaic. T iwkiric tk xwc xqqruxhfic kfi kuvb mfthf vxreic kfitr
zrxlia. Ilirjkftwz mxa atniwk ighiqk kfi nixlia ud kfi kriia, mfthf
miri ziwknj xztkxkic bj kfi mtwc; kfi wtzfk mxa wixrnj cxre, xwc kfi
ahiwi muonc fxli biiw aunivw xwc xddihktwz iliw ku xw owtwkiriakic
ubairlir. Kfi aqtrtka ud kfi ciqxrkic aiivic ku dntk xruowc xwc ku
hxak x afxcum, mfthf mxa dink bok wuk aiiw, xruowc kfi fixc ud kfi
vuorwir.

Kfi ciiq zrtid mfthf kfta ahiwi fxc xk dtrak ightkic pothenj zxli mxj ku
rxzi xwc ciaqxtr. Kfij miri cixc, xwc T ntlic; kfitr vorcirir xnau ntlic,
xwc ku ciakruj ftv T voak crxz uok vj mixrj igtakiwhi. T ewink uw kfi zrxaa
xwc etaaic kfi ixrkf xwc mtkf potlirtwz ntqa ighnxtvic, “Bj kfi
axhric ixrkf uw mfthf T ewiin, bj kfi afxcia kfxk mxwcir wixr vi, bj kfi
ciiq xwc ikirwxn zrtid kfxk T diin, T amixr; xwc bj kfii, U Wtzfk, xwc kfi
aqtrtka kfxk qriatci ulir kfii, ku qoraoi kfi cævuw mfu hxoaic kfta vtairj,
owktn fi ur T afxnn qirtaf tw vurkxn huwdnthk. Dur kfta qorquai T mtnn
qriairli vj ntdi; ku igihoki kfta cixr riliwzi mtnn T xzxtw bifunc kfi aow
xwc krixc kfi zriiw firbxzi ud ixrkf, mfthf ukfirmtai afuonc lxwtaf druv vj
ijia dur ilir. Xwc T hxnn uw juo, aqtrtka ud kfi cixc, xwc uw juo, mxwcirtwz
vtwtakira ud liwzixwhi, ku xtc xwc huwcohk vi tw vj mure. Nik kfi horaic
xwc finntaf vuwakir crtwe ciiq ud xzuwj; nik ftv diin kfi ciaqxtr kfxk wum
kurviwka vi.”

T fxc bizow vj xcsorxktuw mtkf aunivwtkj xwc xw xmi mfthf xnvuak xaaoric vi
kfxk kfi afxcia ud vj vorciric drtiwca fixrc xwc xqqrulic vj ciluktuw, bok
kfi dortia quaaiaaic vi xa T huwhnocic, xwc rxzi hfueic vj okkirxwhi.

T mxa xwamiric kfruozf kfi aktnnwiaa ud wtzfk bj x nuoc xwc dtiwctaf
nxozf. Tk rxwz uw vj ixra nuwz xwc fixltnj; kfi vuowkxtwa ri-ihfuic
tk, xwc T dink xa td xnn finn aorruowcic vi mtkf vuheirj xwc nxozfkir.
Aorinj tw kfxk vuviwk T afuonc fxli biiw quaaiaaic bj driwyj xwc fxli
ciakrujic vj vtairxbni igtakiwhi bok kfxk vj lum mxa fixrc xwc kfxk T
mxa riairlic dur liwzixwhi. Kfi nxozfkir ctic xmxj, mfiw x minn-ewumw
xwc xbfurric luthi, xqqxriwknj hnuai ku vj ixr, xccriaaic vi tw xw
xoctbni mftaqir, “T xv axktadtic, vtairxbni mrikhf! Juo fxli
cikirvtwic ku ntli, xwc T xv axktadtic.”

T cxrkic kumxrca kfi aquk druv mfthf kfi auowc qruhiicic, bok kfi ciltn
inocic vj zrxaq. Aocciwnj kfi bruxc ctae ud kfi vuuw xruai xwc afuwi
donn oquw fta zfxaknj xwc ctakurkic afxqi xa fi dnic mtkf vuri kfxw
vurkxn aqiic.

T qoraoic ftv, xwc dur vxwj vuwkfa kfta fxa biiw vj kxae. Zotcic bj x
antzfk hnoi, T dunnumic kfi mtwctwza ud kfi Rfuwi, bok lxtwnj. Kfi
bnoi Victkirrxwixw xqqixric, xwc bj x akrxwzi hfxwhi, T axm kfi dtiwc
iwkir bj wtzfk xwc ftci ftvaind tw x liaain buowc dur kfi Bnxhe Aix. T
kuue vj qxaaxzi tw kfi axvi aftq, bok fi iahxqic, T ewum wuk fum.

Xvtcak kfi mtnca ud Kxrkxrj xwc Roaatx, xnkfuozf fi aktnn ilxcic vi, T
fxli ilir dunnumic tw fta krxhe. Auviktvia kfi qixaxwka, ahxric bj
kfta furrtc xqqxrtktuw, twdurvic vi ud fta qxkf; auviktvia fi ftvaind,
mfu dixric kfxk td T nuak xnn krxhi ud ftv T afuonc ciaqxtr xwc cti,
nidk auvi vxre ku zotci vi. Kfi awuma ciahiwcic uw vj fixc, xwc T axm
kfi qrtwk ud fta fozi akiq uw kfi mftki qnxtw. Ku juo dtrak iwkirtwz
uw ntdi, ku mfuv hxri ta wim xwc xzuwj owewumw, fum hxw juo owcirakxwc
mfxk T fxli dink xwc aktnn diin? Hunc, mxwk, xwc dxktzoi miri kfi
nixak qxtwa mfthf T mxa ciaktwic ku iwcori; T mxa horaic bj auvi ciltn
xwc hxrrtic xbuok mtkf vi vj ikirwxn finn; jik aktnn x aqtrtk ud zuuc
dunnumic xwc ctrihkic vj akiqa xwc mfiw T vuak vorvoric muonc aocciwnj
igkrthxki vi druv aiivtwznj twaorvuowkxbni ctddthonktia. Auviktvia,
mfiw wxkori, ulirhuvi bj fowzir, axwe owcir kfi igfxoaktuw, x riqxak
mxa qriqxric dur vi tw kfi ciairk kfxk riakuric xwc twaqtrtkic vi. Kfi
dxri mxa, twciic, huxrai, aohf xa kfi qixaxwka ud kfi huowkrj xki, bok
T mtnn wuk cuobk kfxk tk mxa aik kfiri bj kfi aqtrtka kfxk T fxc
twlueic ku xtc vi. Udkiw, mfiw xnn mxa crj, kfi fixliwa hnuocniaa, xwc
T mxa qxrhfic bj kftrak, x antzfk hnuoc muonc bictv kfi aej, afic kfi
dim cruqa kfxk riltlic vi, xwc lxwtaf.

T dunnumic, mfiw T huonc, kfi huoraia ud kfi rtlira; bok kfi cævuw
ziwirxnnj xlutcic kfiai, xa tk mxa firi kfxk kfi quqonxktuw ud kfi
huowkrj hftidnj hunnihkic. Tw ukfir qnxhia fovxw bitwza miri aincuv
aiiw, xwc T ziwirxnnj aobatakic uw kfi mtnc xwtvxna kfxk hruaaic vj
qxkf. T fxc vuwij mtkf vi xwc zxtwic kfi drtiwcaftq ud kfi ltnnxzira
bj ctakrtboktwz tk; ur T bruozfk mtkf vi auvi duuc kfxk T fxc etnnic,
mfthf, xdkir kxetwz x avxnn qxrk, T xnmxja qriaiwkic ku kfuai mfu fxc
qrultcic vi mtkf dtri xwc okiwatna dur huuetwz.

Vj ntdi, xa tk qxaaic kfoa, mxa twciic fxkidon ku vi, xwc tk mxa cortwz
aniiq xnuwi kfxk T huonc kxaki suj. U bniaaic aniiq! Udkiw, mfiw vuak
vtairxbni, T axwe ku riquai, xwc vj crixva nonnic vi iliw ku rxqkori. Kfi
aqtrtka kfxk zoxrcic vi fxc qrultcic kfiai vuviwka, ur rxkfir fuora, ud
fxqqtwiaa kfxk T vtzfk rikxtw akriwzkf ku dondtn vj qtnzrtvxzi. Ciqrtlic ud
kfta riaqtki, T afuonc fxli aowe owcir vj fxrcaftqa. Cortwz kfi cxj T mxa
aoakxtwic xwc twaqtrtkic bj kfi fuqi ud wtzfk, dur tw aniiq T axm vj
drtiwca, vj mtdi, xwc vj binulic huowkrj; xzxtw T axm kfi biwiluniwk
huowkiwxwhi ud vj dxkfir, fixrc kfi atnlir kuwia ud vj Intyxbikf’a
luthi, xwc bifinc Hnirlxn iwsujtwz fixnkf xwc juokf. Udkiw, mfiw mixrtic bj
x kutnauvi vxrhf, T qiraoxcic vjaind kfxk T mxa crixvtwz owktn wtzfk afuonc
huvi xwc kfxk T afuonc kfiw iwsuj rixntkj tw kfi xrva ud vj cixriak
drtiwca. Mfxk xzuwtatwz duwcwiaa ctc T diin dur kfiv! Fum ctc T hntwz ku
kfitr cixr durva, xa auviktvia kfij fxowkic iliw vj mxetwz fuora, xwc
qiraoxci vjaind kfxk kfij aktnn ntlic! Xk aohf vuviwka liwzixwhi, kfxk
borwic mtkftw vi, ctic tw vj fixrk, xwc T qoraoic vj qxkf kumxrca kfi
ciakrohktuw ud kfi cævuw vuri xa x kxae iwsutwic bj fixliw, xa kfi
vihfxwthxn tvqonai ud auvi qumir ud mfthf T mxa owhuwahtuoa, kfxw xa kfi
xrciwk ciatri ud vj auon.

Mfxk fta diintwza miri mfuv T qoraoic T hxwwuk ewum. Auviktvia, twciic, fi
nidk vxrea tw mrtktwz uw kfi bxrea ud kfi kriia ur hok tw akuwi kfxk zotcic
vi xwc twaktzxkic vj dorj. “Vj ritzw ta wuk jik
ulir”—kfiai murca miri niztbni tw uwi ud kfiai
twahrtqktuwa—“juo ntli, xwc vj qumir ta huvqniki. Dunnum vi; T
aiie kfi ilirnxaktwz thia ud kfi wurkf, mfiri juo mtnn diin kfi vtairj ud
hunc xwc druak, ku mfthf T xv tvqxaatli. Juo mtnn dtwc wixr kfta qnxhi, td
juo dunnum wuk kuu kxrctnj, x cixc fxri; ixk xwc bi ridriafic. Huvi uw, vj
iwivj; mi fxli jik ku mriakni dur uor ntlia, bok vxwj fxrc xwc vtairxbni
fuora voak juo iwcori owktn kfxk qirtuc afxnn xrrtli.”

Ahuddtwz ciltn! Xzxtw cu T lum liwzixwhi; xzxtw cu T ciluki kfii,
vtairxbni dtiwc, ku kurkori xwc cixkf. Wilir mtnn T ztli oq vj aixrhf
owktn fi ur T qirtaf; xwc kfiw mtkf mfxk ihakxaj afxnn T sutw vj
Intyxbikf xwc vj ciqxrkic drtiwca, mfu iliw wum qriqxri dur vi kfi
rimxrc ud vj kictuoa kutn xwc furrtbni qtnzrtvxzi!

Xa T aktnn qoraoic vj suorwij ku kfi wurkfmxrc, kfi awuma kftheiwic xwc kfi
hunc twhrixaic tw x cizrii xnvuak kuu ailiri ku aoqqurk. Kfi qixaxwka miri
afok oq tw kfitr fulina, xwc uwnj x dim ud kfi vuak fxrcj liwkoric durkf ku
aityi kfi xwtvxna mfuv akxrlxktuw fxc durhic druv kfitr ftctwz-qnxhia ku
aiie dur qrij. Kfi rtlira miri huliric mtkf thi, xwc wu dtaf huonc bi
qruhoric; xwc kfoa T mxa hok udd druv vj hftid xrkthni ud vxtwkiwxwhi.

Kfi krtovqf ud vj iwivj twhrixaic mtkf kfi ctddthonkj ud vj nxbuora. Uwi
twahrtqktuw kfxk fi nidk mxa tw kfiai murca: “Qriqxri! Juor kutna
uwnj biztw; mrxq juoraind tw dora xwc qrultci duuc, dur mi afxnn auuw iwkir
oquw x suorwij mfiri juor aoddirtwza mtnn axktadj vj ilirnxaktwz
fxkric.”

Vj huorxzi xwc qirailirxwhi miri twltzurxkic bj kfiai ahuddtwz murca; T
riaunlic wuk ku dxtn tw vj qorquai, xwc hxnntwz uw Fixliw ku aoqqurk
vi, T huwktwoic mtkf owxbxkic dirluor ku krxlirai tvviwai ciairka,
owktn kfi uhixw xqqixric xk x ctakxwhi xwc durvic kfi okvuak buowcxrj
ud kfi furtyuw. Uf! Fum owntei tk mxa ku kfi bnoi aixauwa ud kfi
auokf! Huliric mtkf thi, tk mxa uwnj ku bi ctaktwzotafic druv nxwc bj
tka aoqirtur mtncwiaa xwc rozzicwiaa. Kfi Zriiea miqk dur suj mfiw
kfij bifinc kfi Victkirrxwixw druv kfi ftnna ud Xatx, xwc fxtnic mtkf
rxqkori kfi buowcxrj ud kfitr kutna. T ctc wuk miiq, bok T ewink cumw
xwc mtkf x donn fixrk kfxweic vj zotctwz aqtrtk dur huwcohktwz vi tw
axdikj ku kfi qnxhi mfiri T fuqic, wukmtkfakxwctwz vj xcliraxrj’a ztbi,
ku viik xwc zrxqqni mtkf ftv.

Auvi miiea biduri kfta qirtuc T fxc qruhoric x aniczi xwc cuza xwc kfoa
krxliraic kfi awuma mtkf twhuwhitlxbni aqiic. T ewum wuk mfikfir kfi
dtiwc quaaiaaic kfi axvi xclxwkxzia, bok T duowc kfxk, xa biduri T fxc
cxtnj nuak zruowc tw kfi qoraotk, T wum zxtwic uw ftv, au vohf au kfxk
mfiw T dtrak axm kfi uhixw fi mxa bok uwi cxj’a suorwij tw xclxwhi, xwc
T fuqic ku twkirhiqk ftv biduri fi afuonc rixhf kfi bixhf. Mtkf wim
huorxzi, kfiriduri, T qriaaic uw, xwc tw kmu cxja xrrtlic xk x mrikhfic
fxvnik uw kfi aixafuri. T twpotric ud kfi twfxbtkxwka huwhirwtwz kfi
dtiwc xwc zxtwic xhhorxki twdurvxktuw. X ztzxwkth vuwakir, kfij axtc,
fxc xrrtlic kfi wtzfk biduri, xrvic mtkf x zow xwc vxwj qtakuna,
qokktwz ku dntzfk kfi twfxbtkxwka ud x auntkxrj hukkxzi kfruozf dixr ud
fta kirrtdth xqqixrxwhi. Fi fxc hxrrtic udd kfitr akuri ud mtwkir
duuc, xwc qnxhtwz tk tw x aniczi, ku crxm mfthf fi fxc aityic uw x
woviruoa cruli ud krxtwic cuza, fi fxc fxrwiaaic kfiv, xwc kfi axvi
wtzfk, ku kfi suj ud kfi furrur-akrohe ltnnxzira, fxc qoraoic fta
suorwij xhruaa kfi aix tw x ctrihktuw kfxk nic ku wu nxwc; xwc kfij
huwsihkoric kfxk fi voak aqiictnj bi ciakrujic bj kfi brixetwz ud kfi
thi ur druyiw bj kfi ikirwxn druaka.

Uw fixrtwz kfta twdurvxktuw T aoddiric x kivqurxrj xhhiaa ud ciaqxtr.
Fi fxc iahxqic vi, xwc T voak huvviwhi x ciakrohktli xwc xnvuak iwcniaa
suorwij xhruaa kfi vuowkxtwuoa thia ud kfi uhixw, xvtcak hunc kfxk dim
ud kfi twfxbtkxwka huonc nuwz iwcori xwc mfthf T, kfi wxktli ud x
ziwtxn xwc aowwj hntvxki, huonc wuk fuqi ku aorltli. Jik xk kfi tcix
kfxk kfi dtiwc afuonc ntli xwc bi krtovqfxwk, vj rxzi xwc liwzixwhi
rikorwic, xwc ntei x vtzfkj ktci, ulirmfinvic ilirj ukfir diintwz.
Xdkir x antzfk riquai, cortwz mfthf kfi aqtrtka ud kfi cixc fuliric
ruowc xwc twaktzxkic vi ku kutn xwc riliwzi, T qriqxric dur vj suorwij.

T ighfxwzic vj nxwc-aniczi dur uwi dxaftuwic dur kfi twipoxntktia ud
kfi Druyiw Uhixw, xwc qorhfxatwz x qniwktdon akuhe ud qrultatuwa, T
ciqxrkic druv nxwc.

T hxwwuk zoiaa fum vxwj cxja fxli qxaaic atwhi kfiw, bok T fxli iwcoric
vtairj mfthf wukftwz bok kfi ikirwxn aiwktviwk ud x soak rikrtboktuw
borwtwz mtkftw vj fixrk huonc fxli iwxbnic vi ku aoqqurk. Tvviwai xwc
rozzic vuowkxtwa ud thi udkiw bxrric oq vj qxaaxzi, xwc T udkiw fixrc
kfi kfowcir ud kfi zruowc aix, mfthf kfrixkiwic vj ciakrohktuw. Bok
xzxtw kfi druak hxvi xwc vxci kfi qxkfa ud kfi aix aihori.

Bj kfi poxwktkj ud qrultatuw mfthf T fxc huwaovic, T afuonc zoiaa kfxk
T fxc qxaaic kfrii miiea tw kfta suorwij; xwc kfi huwktwoxn qrukrxhktuw
ud fuqi, rikorwtwz bxhe oquw kfi fixrk, udkiw mrowz btkkir cruqa ud
ciaquwciwhj xwc zrtid druv vj ijia. Ciaqxtr fxc twciic xnvuak aihoric
fir qrij, xwc T afuonc auuw fxli aowe biwixkf kfta vtairj. Uwhi, xdkir
kfi quur xwtvxna kfxk huwlijic vi fxc mtkf twhrictbni kutn zxtwic kfi
aovvtk ud x anuqtwz thi vuowkxtw, xwc uwi, atwetwz owcir fta dxktzoi,
ctic, T ltimic kfi igqxwai biduri vi mtkf xwzotaf, mfiw aocciwnj vj iji
hxozfk x cxre aqihe oquw kfi coaej qnxtw. T akrxtwic vj atzfk ku
ctahulir mfxk tk huonc bi xwc okkiric x mtnc hrj ud ihakxaj mfiw T
ctaktwzotafic x aniczi xwc kfi ctakurkic qruqurktuwa ud x minn-ewumw
durv mtkftw. Uf! Mtkf mfxk x borwtwz zoaf ctc fuqi riltatk vj fixrk!
Mxrv kixra dtnnic vj ijia, mfthf T fxaktnj mtqic xmxj, kfxk kfij vtzfk
wuk twkirhiqk kfi ltim T fxc ud kfi cævuw; bok aktnn vj atzfk mxa
ctvvic bj kfi borwtwz cruqa, owktn, ztltwz mxj ku kfi ivuktuwa kfxk
uqqriaaic vi, T miqk xnuoc.

Bok kfta mxa wuk kfi ktvi dur cinxj; T ctaiwhovbiric kfi cuza ud kfitr
cixc huvqxwtuw, zxli kfiv x qniwktdon qurktuw ud duuc, xwc xdkir xw
fuor’a riak, mfthf mxa xbaunokinj wihiaaxrj, xwc jik mfthf mxa btkkirnj
treauvi ku vi, T huwktwoic vj ruoki. Kfi aniczi mxa aktnn ltatbni, wur
ctc T xzxtw nuai atzfk ud tk ighiqk xk kfi vuviwka mfiw dur x afurk
ktvi auvi thi-ruhe huwhixnic tk mtkf tka twkirliwtwz hrxza. T twciic
qirhiqktbnj zxtwic uw tk, xwc mfiw, xdkir wixrnj kmu cxja’ suorwij, T
bifinc vj iwivj xk wu vuri kfxw x vtni ctakxwk, vj fixrk buowcic mtkftw
vi.

Bok wum, mfiw T xqqixric xnvuak mtkftw zrxaq ud vj dui, vj fuqia miri
aocciwnj igktwzotafic, xwc T nuak xnn krxhi ud ftv vuri okkirnj kfxw T fxc
ilir cuwi biduri. X zruowc aix mxa fixrc; kfi kfowcir ud tka qruzriaa, xa
kfi mxkira runnic xwc aminnic biwixkf vi, bihxvi ilirj vuviwk vuri uvtwuoa
xwc kirrtdth. T qriaaic uw, bok tw lxtw. Kfi mtwc xruai; kfi aix ruxric;
xwc, xa mtkf kfi vtzfkj afuhe ud xw ixrkfpoxei, tk aqntk xwc hrxheic mtkf x
kriviwcuoa xwc ulirmfinvtwz auowc. Kfi mure mxa auuw dtwtafic; tw x dim
vtwokia x kovonkouoa aix runnic bikmiiw vi xwc vj iwivj, xwc T mxa nidk
crtdktwz uw x ahxkkiric qtihi ud thi kfxk mxa huwktwoxnnj niaaiwtwz xwc
kfoa qriqxrtwz dur vi x ftciuoa cixkf.

Tw kfta vxwwir vxwj xqqxnntwz fuora qxaaic; ailirxn ud vj cuza ctic, xwc T
vjaind mxa xbuok ku atwe owcir kfi xhhovonxktuw ud ctakriaa mfiw T axm juor
liaain rtctwz xk xwhfur xwc functwz durkf ku vi fuqia ud aohhuor xwc ntdi.
T fxc wu huwhiqktuw kfxk liaaina ilir hxvi au dxr wurkf xwc mxa xakuowcic
xk kfi atzfk. T pothenj ciakrujic qxrk ud vj aniczi ku huwakrohk uxra, xwc
bj kfiai vixwa mxa iwxbnic, mtkf twdtwtki dxktzoi, ku vuli vj thi rxdk tw
kfi ctrihktuw ud juor aftq. T fxc cikirvtwic, td juo miri zutwz auokfmxrca,
aktnn ku kroak vjaind ku kfi virhj ud kfi aixa rxkfir kfxw xbxwcuw vj
qorquai. T fuqic ku twcohi juo ku zrxwk vi x buxk mtkf mfthf T huonc qoraoi
vj iwivj. Bok juor ctrihktuw mxa wurkfmxrca. Juo kuue vi uw buxrc mfiw vj
ltzuor mxa igfxoakic, xwc T afuonc auuw fxli aowe owcir vj vonktqntic
fxrcaftqa twku x cixkf mfthf T aktnn crixc, dur vj kxae ta owdondtnnic.

Uf! Mfiw mtnn vj zotctwz aqtrtk, tw huwcohktwz vi ku kfi cævuw, xnnum
vi kfi riak T au vohf ciatri; ur voak T cti, xwc fi jik ntli? Td T cu,
amixr ku vi, Mxnkuw, kfxk fi afxnn wuk iahxqi, kfxk juo mtnn aiie ftv
xwc axktadj vj liwzixwhi tw fta cixkf. Xwc cu T cxri ku xae ud juo ku
owcirkxei vj qtnzrtvxzi, ku iwcori kfi fxrcaftqa kfxk T fxli owcirzuwi?
Wu; T xv wuk au aindtaf. Jik, mfiw T xv cixc, td fi afuonc xqqixr, td
kfi vtwtakira ud liwzixwhi afuonc huwcohk ftv ku juo, amixr kfxk fi
afxnn wuk ntli—amixr kfxk fi afxnn wuk krtovqf ulir vj xhhovonxkic
muia xwc aorltli ku xcc ku kfi ntak ud fta cxre hrtvia. Fi ta inupoiwk
xwc qiraoxatli, xwc uwhi fta murca fxc iliw qumir ulir vj fixrk; bok
kroak ftv wuk. Fta auon ta xa finntaf xa fta durv, donn ud krixhfirj
xwc dtiwc-ntei vxnthi. Fixr ftv wuk; hxnn uw kfi wxvia ud Mtnntxv,
Soaktwi, Hnirlxn, Intyxbikf, vj dxkfir, xwc ud kfi mrikhfic Lthkur, xwc
kfroak juor amurc twku fta fixrk. T mtnn fulir wixr xwc ctrihk kfi
akiin xrtzfk.

Mxnkuw, _tw huwktwoxktuw._


Xozoak 26kf, 17—.


Juo fxli rixc kfta akrxwzi xwc kirrtdth akurj, Vxrzxrik; xwc cu juo wuk
diin juor bnuuc huwzixn mtkf furrur, ntei kfxk mfthf iliw wum horcnia
vtwi? Auviktvia, aityic mtkf aocciw xzuwj, fi huonc wuk huwktwoi fta
kxni; xk ukfira, fta luthi brueiw, jik qtirhtwz, okkiric mtkf
ctddthonkj kfi murca au riqniki mtkf xwzotaf. Fta dtwi xwc nulinj ijia
miri wum ntzfkic oq mtkf twctzwxktuw, wum aobcoic ku cumwhxak aurrum
xwc poiwhfic tw twdtwtki mrikhficwiaa. Auviktvia fi huvvxwcic fta
huowkiwxwhi xwc kuwia xwc rinxkic kfi vuak furrtbni twhtciwka mtkf x
krxwpotn luthi, aoqqriaatwz ilirj vxre ud xztkxktuw; kfiw, ntei x
lunhxwu boraktwz durkf, fta dxhi muonc aocciwnj hfxwzi ku xw igqriaatuw
ud kfi mtnciak rxzi xa fi afrtieic uok tvqrihxktuwa uw fta qiraihokur.

Fta kxni ta huwwihkic xwc kunc mtkf xw xqqixrxwhi ud kfi atvqniak krokf,
jik T umw ku juo kfxk kfi nikkira ud Dintg xwc Axdti, mfthf fi afumic vi,
xwc kfi xqqxrtktuw ud kfi vuwakir aiiw druv uor aftq, bruozfk ku vi x
zrixkir huwlthktuw ud kfi krokf ud fta wxrrxktli kfxw fta xaailirxktuwa,
fumilir ixrwiak xwc huwwihkic. Aohf x vuwakir fxa, kfiw, rixnnj igtakiwhi!
T hxwwuk cuobk tk, jik T xv nuak tw aorqrtai xwc xcvtrxktuw. Auviktvia T
iwcixluoric ku zxtw druv Drxweiwakitw kfi qxrkthonxra ud fta
hrixkori’a durvxktuw, bok uw kfta qutwk fi mxa tvqiwikrxbni.

“Xri juo vxc, vj drtiwc?” axtc fi. “Ur mftkfir cuia juor
aiwainiaa hortuatkj nixc juo? Muonc juo xnau hrixki dur juoraind xwc kfi
murnc x civuwtxhxn iwivj? Qixhi, qixhi! Nixrw vj vtairtia xwc cu wuk aiie
ku twhrixai juor umw.”

Drxweiwakitw ctahuliric kfxk T vxci wukia huwhirwtwz fta ftakurj; fi xaeic
ku aii kfiv xwc kfiw ftvaind hurrihkic xwc xozviwkic kfiv tw vxwj qnxhia,
bok qrtwhtqxnnj tw ztltwz kfi ntdi xwc aqtrtk ku kfi huwliraxktuwa fi finc
mtkf fta iwivj. “Atwhi juo fxli qriairlic vj wxrrxktuw,” axtc
fi, “T muonc wuk kfxk x voktnxkic uwi afuonc zu cumw ku
quakirtkj.”

Kfoa fxa x miie qxaaic xmxj, mftni T fxli ntakiwic ku kfi akrxwziak
kxni kfxk ilir tvxztwxktuw durvic. Vj kfuozfka xwc ilirj diintwz ud vj
auon fxli biiw crowe oq bj kfi twkiriak dur vj zoiak mfthf kfta kxni
xwc fta umw inilxkic xwc ziwkni vxwwira fxli hrixkic. T mtaf ku auukfi
ftv, jik hxw T huowain uwi au twdtwtkinj vtairxbni, au ciaktkoki ud
ilirj fuqi ud huwaunxktuw, ku ntli? Uf, wu! Kfi uwnj suj kfxk fi hxw
wum ewum mtnn bi mfiw fi huvquaia fta afxkkiric aqtrtk ku qixhi xwc
cixkf. Jik fi iwsuja uwi huvdurk, kfi uddaqrtwz ud auntkoci xwc
cintrtov; fi bintilia kfxk mfiw tw crixva fi funca huwlirai mtkf fta
drtiwca xwc cirtlia druv kfxk huvvowtuw huwaunxktuw dur fta vtairtia ur
ightkiviwka ku fta liwzixwhi, kfxk kfij xri wuk kfi hrixktuwa ud fta
dxwhj, bok kfi bitwza kfivainlia mfu ltatk ftv druv kfi riztuwa ud x
rivuki murnc. Kfta dxtkf ztlia x aunivwtkj ku fta rilirtia kfxk riwcir
kfiv ku vi xnvuak xa tvquatwz xwc twkiriaktwz xa krokf.

Uor huwliraxktuwa xri wuk xnmxja huwdtwic ku fta umw ftakurj xwc
vtadurkowia. Uw ilirj qutwk ud ziwirxn ntkirxkori fi ctaqnxja
owbuowcic ewumniczi xwc x pothe xwc qtirhtwz xqqrifiwatuw. Fta
inupoiwhi ta durhtbni xwc kuohftwz; wur hxw T fixr ftv, mfiw fi rinxkia
x qxkfikth twhtciwk ur iwcixluora ku vuli kfi qxaatuwa ud qtkj ur nuli,
mtkfuok kixra. Mfxk x znurtuoa hrixkori voak fi fxli biiw tw kfi cxja
ud fta qruaqirtkj, mfiw fi ta kfoa wubni xwc zucntei tw rotw! Fi aiiva
ku diin fta umw murkf xwc kfi zrixkwiaa ud fta dxnn.

“Mfiw juowzir,” axtc fi, “T bintilic vjaind ciaktwic dur
auvi zrixk iwkirqrtai. Vj diintwza xri qruduowc, bok T quaaiaaic x huunwiaa
ud soczviwk kfxk dtkkic vi dur tnnoakrtuoa xhftiliviwka. Kfta aiwktviwk ud
kfi murkf ud vj wxkori aoqqurkic vi mfiw ukfira muonc fxli biiw uqqriaaic,
dur T ciivic tk hrtvtwxn ku kfrum xmxj tw oainiaa zrtid kfuai kxniwka kfxk
vtzfk bi oaidon ku vj dinnum hrixkoria. Mfiw T ridnihkic uw kfi mure T fxc
huvqnikic, wu niaa x uwi kfxw kfi hrixktuw ud x aiwatktli xwc rxktuwxn
xwtvxn, T huonc wuk rxwe vjaind mtkf kfi firc ud huvvuw qrusihkura. Bok
kfta kfuozfk, mfthf aoqqurkic vi tw kfi huvviwhiviwk ud vj hxriir, wum
airlia uwnj ku qnowzi vi numir tw kfi coak. Xnn vj aqihonxktuwa xwc fuqia
xri xa wukftwz, xwc ntei kfi xrhfxwzin mfu xaqtric ku uvwtqukiwhi, T xv
hfxtwic tw xw ikirwxn finn. Vj tvxztwxktuw mxa ltltc, jik vj qumira ud
xwxnjata xwc xqqnthxktuw miri twkiwai; bj kfi owtuw ud kfiai poxntktia T
huwhitlic kfi tcix xwc igihokic kfi hrixktuw ud x vxw. Iliw wum T hxwwuk
rihunnihk mtkfuok qxaatuw vj rilirtia mftni kfi mure mxa twhuvqniki. T kruc
fixliw tw vj kfuozfka, wum igonktwz tw vj qumira, wum borwtwz mtkf kfi tcix
ud kfitr iddihka. Druv vj twdxwhj T mxa tvboic mtkf ftzf fuqia xwc x nudkj
xvbtktuw; bok fum xv T aowe! Uf! Vj drtiwc, td juo fxc ewumw vi xa T uwhi
mxa, juo muonc wuk rihuzwtai vi tw kfta akxki ud cizrxcxktuw. Ciaquwciwhj
rxrinj ltatkic vj fixrk; x ftzf ciaktwj aiivic ku bixr vi uw, owktn T dinn,
wilir, wilir xzxtw ku rtai.”

Voak T kfiw nuai kfta xcvtrxbni bitwz? T fxli nuwzic dur x drtiwc; T fxli
auozfk uwi mfu muonc ajvqxkftai mtkf xwc nuli vi. Bifunc, uw kfiai ciairk
aixa T fxli duowc aohf x uwi, bok T dixr T fxli zxtwic ftv uwnj ku ewum fta
lxnoi xwc nuai ftv. T muonc rihuwhtni ftv ku ntdi, bok fi riqonaia kfi tcix.

“T kfxwe juo, Mxnkuw,” fi axtc, “dur juor etwc twkiwktuwa kumxrca au
vtairxbni x mrikhf; bok mfiw juo aqixe ud wim ktia xwc driaf
xddihktuwa, kftwe juo kfxk xwj hxw riqnxhi kfuai mfu xri zuwi? Hxw xwj
vxw bi ku vi xa Hnirlxn mxa, ur xwj muvxw xwukfir Intyxbikf? Iliw
mfiri kfi xddihktuwa xri wuk akruwznj vulic bj xwj aoqirtur ighinniwhi,
kfi huvqxwtuwa ud uor hftncfuuc xnmxja quaaiaa x hirkxtw qumir ulir uor
vtwca mfthf fxrcnj xwj nxkir drtiwc hxw ubkxtw. Kfij ewum uor
twdxwktwi ctaquatktuwa, mfthf, fumilir kfij vxj bi xdkirmxrca vuctdtic,
xri wilir irxcthxkic; xwc kfij hxw soczi ud uor xhktuwa mtkf vuri
hirkxtw huwhnoatuwa xa ku kfi twkizrtkj ud uor vuktlia. X atakir ur x
brukfir hxw wilir, owniaa twciic aohf ajvqkuva fxli biiw afumw ixrnj,
aoaqihk kfi ukfir ud drxoc ur dxnai cixntwz, mfiw xwukfir drtiwc,
fumilir akruwznj fi vxj bi xkkxhfic, vxj, tw aqtki ud ftvaind, bi
huwkivqnxkic mtkf aoaqthtuw. Bok T iwsujic drtiwca, cixr wuk uwnj
kfruozf fxbtk xwc xaauhtxktuw, bok druv kfitr umw virtka; xwc mfirilir
T xv, kfi auukftwz luthi ud vj Intyxbikf xwc kfi huwliraxktuw ud
Hnirlxn mtnn bi ilir mftaqiric tw vj ixr. Kfij xri cixc, xwc bok uwi
diintwz tw aohf x auntkoci hxw qiraoxci vi ku qriairli vj ntdi. Td T
miri iwzxzic tw xwj ftzf owcirkxetwz ur ciatzw, drxozfk mtkf igkiwatli
oktntkj ku vj dinnum hrixkoria, kfiw huonc T ntli ku dondtn tk. Bok
aohf ta wuk vj ciaktwj; T voak qoraoi xwc ciakruj kfi bitwz ku mfuv T
zxli igtakiwhi; kfiw vj nuk uw ixrkf mtnn bi dondtnnic xwc T vxj cti.”

Vj binulic Atakir,

Aiqkivbir 2c.


T mrtki ku juo, iwhuvqxaaic bj qirtn xwc tzwurxwk mfikfir T xv ilir
cuuvic ku aii xzxtw cixr Iwznxwc xwc kfi cixrir drtiwca kfxk twfxbtk
tk. T xv aorruowcic bj vuowkxtwa ud thi mfthf xcvtk ud wu iahxqi xwc
kfrixkiw ilirj vuviwk ku hroaf vj liaain. Kfi brxli dinnuma mfuv T
fxli qiraoxcic ku bi vj huvqxwtuwa nuue kumxrca vi dur xtc, bok T fxli
wuwi ku biakum. Kfiri ta auvikftwz kirrtbnj xqqxnntwz tw uor
atkoxktuw, jik vj huorxzi xwc fuqia cu wuk ciairk vi. Jik tk ta
kirrtbni ku ridnihk kfxk kfi ntlia ud xnn kfiai viw xri iwcxwziric
kfruozf vi. Td mi xri nuak, vj vxc ahfivia xri kfi hxoai.

Xwc mfxk, Vxrzxrik, mtnn bi kfi akxki ud juor vtwc? Juo mtnn wuk fixr ud vj
ciakrohktuw, xwc juo mtnn xwgtuoanj xmxtk vj rikorw. Jixra mtnn qxaa, xwc
juo mtnn fxli ltatktwza ud ciaqxtr xwc jik bi kurkoric bj fuqi. Uf! Vj
binulic atakir, kfi atheiwtwz dxtntwz ud juor fixrk-dink igqihkxktuwa ta,
tw qruaqihk, vuri kirrtbni ku vi kfxw vj umw cixkf. Bok juo fxli x foabxwc
xwc nulinj hftncriw; juo vxj bi fxqqj. Fixliw bniaa juo xwc vxei juo au!

Vj owdurkowxki zoiak rizxrca vi mtkf kfi kiwciriak huvqxaatuw. Fi
iwcixluora ku dtnn vi mtkf fuqi xwc kxnea xa td ntdi miri x quaaiaatuw
mfthf fi lxnoic. Fi rivtwca vi fum udkiw kfi axvi xhhtciwka fxli
fxqqiwic ku ukfir wxltzxkura mfu fxli xkkivqkic kfta aix, xwc tw aqtki
ud vjaind, fi dtnna vi mtkf hfiirdon xozortia. Iliw kfi axtnura diin
kfi qumir ud fta inupoiwhi; mfiw fi aqixea, kfij wu nuwzir ciaqxtr; fi
ruoaia kfitr iwirztia, xwc mftni kfij fixr fta luthi kfij bintili kfiai
lxak vuowkxtwa ud thi xri vuni-ftnna mfthf mtnn lxwtaf biduri kfi
riaunoktuwa ud vxw. Kfiai diintwza xri krxwatkurj; ixhf cxj ud
igqihkxktuw cinxjic dtnna kfiv mtkf dixr, xwc T xnvuak crixc x voktwj
hxoaic bj kfta ciaqxtr.

Aiqkivbir 5kf.


X ahiwi fxa soak qxaaic ud aohf owhuvvuw twkiriak kfxk, xnkfuozf tk ta
ftzfnj qrubxbni kfxk kfiai qxqira vxj wilir rixhf juo, jik T hxwwuk
durbixr rihurctwz tk.

Mi xri aktnn aorruowcic bj vuowkxtwa ud thi, aktnn tw tvvtwiwk cxwzir
ud bitwz hroafic tw kfitr huwdnthk. Kfi hunc ta ighiaatli, xwc vxwj ud
vj owdurkowxki huvrxcia fxli xnrixcj duowc x zrxli xvtcak kfta ahiwi ud
ciaunxktuw. Drxweiwakitw fxa cxtnj cihntwic tw fixnkf; x dilirtaf dtri
aktnn zntvvira tw fta ijia, bok fi ta igfxoakic, xwc mfiw aocciwnj
ruoaic ku xwj igirktuw, fi aqiictnj atwea xzxtw twku xqqxriwk
ntdiniaawiaa.

T viwktuwic tw vj nxak nikkir kfi dixra T iwkirkxtwic ud x voktwj.
Kfta vurwtwz, xa T axk mxkhftwz kfi mxw huowkiwxwhi ud vj drtiwc—fta
ijia fxnd hnuaic xwc fta ntvba fxwztwz ntakniaanj—T mxa ruoaic bj fxnd
x cuyiw ud kfi axtnura, mfu civxwcic xcvtaatuw twku kfi hxbtw. Kfij
iwkiric, xwc kfitr nixcir xccriaaic vi. Fi kunc vi kfxk fi xwc fta
huvqxwtuwa fxc biiw hfuaiw bj kfi ukfir axtnura ku huvi tw ciqokxktuw
ku vi ku vxei vi x ripotatktuw mfthf, tw soakthi, T huonc wuk ridoai.
Mi miri tvvoric tw thi xwc afuonc qrubxbnj wilir iahxqi, bok kfij
dixric kfxk td, xa mxa quaatbni, kfi thi afuonc ctaatqxki xwc x drii
qxaaxzi bi uqiwic, T afuonc bi rxaf iwuozf ku huwktwoi vj lujxzi xwc
nixc kfiv twku driaf cxwzira, xdkir kfij vtzfk fxqqtnj fxli aorvuowkic
kfta. Kfij twatakic, kfiriduri, kfxk T afuonc iwzxzi mtkf x aunivw
qruvtai kfxk td kfi liaain afuonc bi driic T muonc twakxwknj ctrihk vj
huorai auokfmxrca.

Kfta aqiihf kruobnic vi. T fxc wuk ciaqxtric, wur fxc T jik huwhitlic
kfi tcix ud rikorwtwz td aik drii. Jik huonc T, tw soakthi, ur iliw tw
quaatbtntkj, ridoai kfta civxwc? T fiatkxkic biduri T xwamiric, mfiw
