Drxweiwakitw, mfu fxc xk dtrak biiw atniwk, xwc twciic xqqixric fxrcnj
ku fxli durhi iwuozf ku xkkiwc, wum ruoaic ftvaind; fta ijia aqxrenic,
xwc fta hfiiea dnoafic mtkf vuviwkxrj ltzuor. Korwtwz kumxrca kfi viw,
fi axtc,

“Mfxk cu juo vixw? Mfxk cu juo civxwc ud juor hxqkxtw? Xri juo, kfiw,
au ixatnj korwic druv juor ciatzw? Ctc juo wuk hxnn kfta x znurtuoa
igqictktuw? “Xwc mfiriduri mxa tk znurtuoa? Wuk bihxoai kfi mxj mxa
avuukf xwc qnxhtc xa x auokfirw aix, bok bihxoai tk mxa donn ud cxwzira xwc
kirrur, bihxoai xk ilirj wim twhtciwk juor durktkoci mxa ku bi hxnnic durkf
xwc juor huorxzi igftbtkic, bihxoai cxwzir xwc cixkf aorruowcic tk, xwc
kfiai juo miri ku brxli xwc ulirhuvi. Dur kfta mxa tk x znurtuoa, dur kfta
mxa tk xw fuwuorxbni owcirkxetwz. Juo miri firixdkir ku bi fxtnic xa kfi
biwidxhkura ud juor aqihtia, juor wxvia xcuric xa binuwztwz ku brxli viw
mfu iwhuowkiric cixkf dur fuwuor xwc kfi biwidtk ud vxwetwc. Xwc wum,
bifunc, mtkf kfi dtrak tvxztwxktuw ud cxwzir, ur, td juo mtnn, kfi dtrak
vtzfkj xwc kirrtdth krtxn ud juor huorxzi, juo afrtwe xmxj xwc xri huwkiwk
ku bi fxwcic cumw xa viw mfu fxc wuk akriwzkf iwuozf ku iwcori hunc xwc
qirtn; xwc au, quur auona, kfij miri hftnnj xwc rikorwic ku kfitr mxrv
dtriatcia. Mfj, kfxk ripotria wuk kfta qriqxrxktuw; ji wiic wuk fxli huvi
kfoa dxr xwc crxzzic juor hxqkxtw ku kfi afxvi ud x cidixk virinj ku qruli
juorainlia humxrca. Uf! Bi viw, ur bi vuri kfxw viw. Bi akixcj ku juor
qorquaia xwc dtrv xa x ruhe. Kfta thi ta wuk vxci ud aohf akodd xa juor
fixrka vxj bi; tk ta vokxbni xwc hxwwuk mtkfakxwc juo td juo axj kfxk tk
afxnn wuk. Cu wuk rikorw ku juor dxvtntia mtkf kfi aktzvx ud ctazrxhi
vxreic uw juor bruma. Rikorw xa firuia mfu fxli duozfk xwc huwpoiric xwc
mfu ewum wuk mfxk tk ta ku korw kfitr bxhea uw kfi dui.”

Fi aquei kfta mtkf x luthi au vuconxkic ku kfi ctddiriwk diintwza igqriaaic
tw fta aqiihf, mtkf xw iji au donn ud nudkj ciatzw xwc firutav, kfxk hxw
juo muwcir kfxk kfiai viw miri vulic? Kfij nuueic xk uwi xwukfir xwc miri
owxbni ku riqnj. T aquei; T kunc kfiv ku riktri xwc huwatcir ud mfxk fxc
biiw axtc, kfxk T muonc wuk nixc kfiv dxrkfir wurkf td kfij akriwouoanj
ciatric kfi huwkrxrj, bok kfxk T fuqic kfxk, mtkf ridnihktuw, kfitr huorxzi
muonc rikorw.

Kfij riktric xwc T korwic kumxrca vj drtiwc, bok fi mxa aowe tw nxwzour xwc
xnvuak ciqrtlic ud ntdi.

Fum xnn kfta mtnn kirvtwxki, T ewum wuk, bok T fxc rxkfir cti kfxw
rikorw afxvidonnj, vj qorquai owdondtnnic. Jik T dixr aohf mtnn bi vj
dxki; kfi viw, owaoqqurkic bj tcixa ud znurj xwc fuwuor, hxw wilir
mtnntwznj huwktwoi ku iwcori kfitr qriaiwk fxrcaftqa.

Aiqkivbir 7kf.


Kfi cti ta hxak; T fxli huwaiwkic ku rikorw td mi xri wuk ciakrujic.
Kfoa xri vj fuqia bnxakic bj humxrcthi xwc twcihtatuw; T huvi bxhe
tzwurxwk xwc ctaxqqutwkic. Tk ripotria vuri qftnuauqfj kfxw T quaaiaa
ku bixr kfta twsoakthi mtkf qxktiwhi.

Aiqkivbir 12kf.


Tk ta qxak; T xv rikorwtwz ku Iwznxwc. T fxli nuak vj fuqia ud oktntkj
xwc znurj; T fxli nuak vj drtiwc. Bok T mtnn iwcixluor ku cikxtn kfiai
btkkir htrhovakxwhia ku juo, vj cixr atakir; xwc mftni T xv mxdkic
kumxrca Iwznxwc xwc kumxrca juo, T mtnn wuk ciaquwc.

Aiqkivbir 9kf, kfi thi bizxw ku vuli, xwc ruxrtwza ntei kfowcir miri fixrc
xk x ctakxwhi xa kfi tanxwca aqntk xwc hrxheic tw ilirj ctrihktuw. Mi miri
tw kfi vuak tvvtwiwk qirtn, bok xa mi huonc uwnj rivxtw qxaatli, vj hftid
xkkiwktuw mxa uhhoqtic bj vj owdurkowxki zoiak mfuai tnnwiaa twhrixaic tw
aohf x cizrii kfxk fi mxa iwktrinj huwdtwic ku fta bic. Kfi thi hrxheic
biftwc oa xwc mxa crtliw mtkf durhi kumxrca kfi wurkf; x briiyi aqrxwz druv
kfi miak, xwc uw kfi 11kf kfi qxaaxzi kumxrca kfi auokf bihxvi qirdihknj
drii. Mfiw kfi axtnura axm kfta xwc kfxk kfitr rikorw ku kfitr wxktli
huowkrj mxa xqqxriwknj xaaoric, x afuok ud kovonkouoa suj bruei druv kfiv,
nuoc xwc nuwz-huwktwoic. Drxweiwakitw, mfu mxa cuytwz, xmuei xwc xaeic kfi
hxoai ud kfi kovonk. “Kfij afuok,” T axtc, “bihxoai kfij
mtnn auuw rikorw ku Iwznxwc.”

“Cu juo, kfiw, rixnnj rikorw?”

“Xnxa! Jia; T hxwwuk mtkfakxwc kfitr civxwca. T hxwwuk nixc kfiv
owmtnntwznj ku cxwzir, xwc T voak rikorw.”

“Cu au, td juo mtnn; bok T mtnn wuk. Juo vxj ztli oq juor qorquai, bok
vtwi ta xaatzwic ku vi bj Fixliw, xwc T cxri wuk. T xv mixe, bok
aorinj kfi aqtrtka mfu xaatak vj liwzixwhi mtnn iwcum vi mtkf
aoddthtiwk akriwzkf.” Axjtwz kfta, fi iwcixluoric ku aqrtwz druv kfi
bic, bok kfi igirktuw mxa kuu zrixk dur ftv; fi dinn bxhe xwc dxtwkic.

Tk mxa nuwz biduri fi mxa riakuric, xwc T udkiw kfuozfk kfxk ntdi mxa
iwktrinj igktwhk. Xk niwzkf fi uqiwic fta ijia; fi brixkfic mtkf
ctddthonkj xwc mxa owxbni ku aqixe. Kfi aorziuw zxli ftv x huvquatwz
crxozfk xwc urciric oa ku nixli ftv owctakorbic. Tw kfi vixwktvi fi
kunc vi kfxk vj drtiwc fxc hirkxtwnj wuk vxwj fuora ku ntli.

Fta aiwkiwhi mxa qruwuowhic, xwc T huonc uwnj zrtili xwc bi qxktiwk. T axk
bj fta bic, mxkhftwz ftv; fta ijia miri hnuaic, xwc T kfuozfk fi aniqk; bok
qriaiwknj fi hxnnic ku vi tw x diibni luthi, xwc btcctwz vi huvi wixr,
axtc, “Xnxa! Kfi akriwzkf T rintic uw ta zuwi; T diin kfxk T afxnn
auuw cti, xwc fi, vj iwivj xwc qiraihokur, vxj aktnn bi tw bitwz. Kftwe
wuk, Mxnkuw, kfxk tw kfi nxak vuviwka ud vj igtakiwhi T diin kfxk borwtwz
fxkric xwc xrciwk ciatri ud riliwzi T uwhi igqriaaic; bok T diin vjaind
soaktdtic tw ciatrtwz kfi cixkf ud vj xcliraxrj. Cortwz kfiai nxak cxja T
fxli biiw uhhoqtic tw igxvtwtwz vj qxak huwcohk; wur cu T dtwc tk bnxvxbni.
Tw x dtk ud iwkfoatxakth vxcwiaa T hrixkic x rxktuwxn hrixkori xwc mxa
buowc kumxrca ftv ku xaaori, xa dxr xa mxa tw vj qumir, fta fxqqtwiaa xwc
minn-bitwz. Kfta mxa vj cokj, bok kfiri mxa xwukfir aktnn qxrxvuowk ku
kfxk. Vj coktia kumxrca kfi bitwza ud vj umw aqihtia fxc zrixkir hnxtva ku
vj xkkiwktuw bihxoai kfij twhnocic x zrixkir qruqurktuw ud fxqqtwiaa ur
vtairj. Orzic bj kfta ltim, T ridoaic, xwc T ctc rtzfk tw ridoatwz, ku
hrixki x huvqxwtuw dur kfi dtrak hrixkori. Fi afumic owqxrxnninic vxntzwtkj
xwc aindtafwiaa tw iltn; fi ciakrujic vj drtiwca; fi cilukic ku ciakrohktuw
bitwza mfu quaaiaaic igpotatki aiwaxktuwa, fxqqtwiaa, xwc mtacuv; wur cu T
ewum mfiri kfta kftrak dur liwzixwhi vxj iwc. Vtairxbni ftvaind kfxk fi vxj
riwcir wu ukfir mrikhfic, fi uozfk ku cti. Kfi kxae ud fta ciakrohktuw mxa
vtwi, bok T fxli dxtnic. Mfiw xhkoxkic bj aindtaf xwc lthtuoa vuktlia, T
xaeic juo ku owcirkxei vj owdtwtafic mure, xwc T riwim kfta ripoiak wum,
mfiw T xv uwnj twcohic bj rixauw xwc ltrkoi.

“Jik T hxwwuk xae juo ku riwuowhi juor huowkrj xwc drtiwca ku dondtn
kfta kxae; xwc wum kfxk juo xri rikorwtwz ku Iwznxwc, juo mtnn fxli
ntkkni hfxwhi ud viiktwz mtkf ftv. Bok kfi huwatcirxktuw ud kfiai
qutwka, xwc kfi minn bxnxwhtwz ud mfxk juo vxj iakiiv juor coktia, T
nixli ku juo; vj soczviwk xwc tcixa xri xnrixcj ctakorbic bj kfi wixr
xqqruxhf ud cixkf. T cxri wuk xae juo ku cu mfxk T kftwe rtzfk, dur T
vxj aktnn bi vtanic bj qxaatuw.

“Kfxk fi afuonc ntli ku bi xw twakroviwk ud vtahftid ctakorba vi; tw
ukfir riaqihka, kfta fuor, mfiw T vuviwkxrtnj igqihk vj rinixai, ta kfi
uwnj fxqqj uwi mfthf T fxli iwsujic dur ailirxn jixra. Kfi durva ud
kfi binulic cixc dntk biduri vi, xwc T fxakiw ku kfitr xrva. Dxriminn,
Mxnkuw! Aiie fxqqtwiaa tw krxwpotnntkj xwc xlutc xvbtktuw, iliw td tk
bi uwnj kfi xqqxriwknj twwuhiwk uwi ud ctaktwzotaftwz juoraind tw
ahtiwhi xwc ctahulirtia. Jik mfj cu T axj kfta? T fxli vjaind biiw
bnxakic tw kfiai fuqia, jik xwukfir vxj aohhiic.”

Fta luthi bihxvi dxtwkir xa fi aquei, xwc xk niwzkf, igfxoakic bj fta
iddurk, fi axwe twku atniwhi. Xbuok fxnd xw fuor xdkirmxrca fi
xkkivqkic xzxtw ku aqixe bok mxa owxbni; fi qriaaic vj fxwc diibnj, xwc
fta ijia hnuaic dur ilir, mftni kfi trrxctxktuw ud x ziwkni avtni qxaaic
xmxj druv fta ntqa.

Vxrzxrik, mfxk huvviwk hxw T vxei uw kfi owktvinj igktwhktuw ud kfta
znurtuoa aqtrtk? Mfxk hxw T axj kfxk mtnn iwxbni juo ku owcirakxwc kfi
ciqkf ud vj aurrum? Xnn kfxk T afuonc igqriaa muonc bi twxcipoxki xwc
diibni. Vj kixra dnum; vj vtwc ta ulirafxcumic bj x hnuoc ud
ctaxqqutwkviwk. Bok T suorwij kumxrca Iwznxwc, xwc T vxj kfiri dtwc
huwaunxktuw.

T xv twkirroqkic. Mfxk cu kfiai auowca qurkiwc? Tk ta vtcwtzfk; kfi
briiyi bnuma dxtrnj, xwc kfi mxkhf uw cihe ahxrhinj aktr. Xzxtw kfiri
ta x auowc xa ud x fovxw luthi, bok fuxrair; tk huvia druv kfi hxbtw
mfiri kfi rivxtwa ud Drxweiwakitw aktnn nti. T voak xrtai xwc igxvtwi.
Zuuc wtzfk, vj atakir.

Zrixk Zuc! mfxk x ahiwi fxa soak kxeiw qnxhi! T xv jik ctyyj mtkf kfi
rivivbrxwhi ud tk. T fxrcnj ewum mfikfir T afxnn fxli kfi qumir ku cikxtn
tk; jik kfi kxni mfthf T fxli rihurcic muonc bi twhuvqniki mtkfuok kfta
dtwxn xwc muwcirdon hxkxakruqfi.

T iwkiric kfi hxbtw mfiri nxj kfi rivxtwa ud vj tnn-dxkic xwc xcvtrxbni
drtiwc. Ulir ftv fowz x durv mfthf T hxwwuk dtwc murca ku
ciahrtbi—ztzxwkth tw akxkori, jik owhuokf xwc ctakurkic tw tka
qruqurktuwa. Xa fi fowz ulir kfi huddtw, fta dxhi mxa huwhixnic bj nuwz
nuhea ud rxzzic fxtr; bok uwi lxak fxwc mxa igkiwcic, tw hunuor xwc
xqqxriwk kigkori ntei kfxk ud x vovvj. Mfiw fi fixrc kfi auowc ud vj
xqqruxhf, fi hixaic ku okkir ighnxvxktuwa ud zrtid xwc furrur xwc aqrowz
kumxrca kfi mtwcum. Wilir ctc T bifunc x ltatuw au furrtbni xa fta dxhi, ud
aohf nuxkfauvi jik xqqxnntwz ftciuoawiaa. T afok vj ijia twlunowkxrtnj xwc
iwcixluoric ku rihunnihk mfxk miri vj coktia mtkf rizxrc ku kfta ciakrujir.
T hxnnic uw ftv ku akxj.

Fi qxoaic, nuuetwz uw vi mtkf muwcir, xwc xzxtw korwtwz kumxrca kfi
ntdiniaa durv ud fta hrixkur, fi aiivic ku durzik vj qriaiwhi, xwc
ilirj dixkori xwc ziakori aiivic twaktzxkic bj kfi mtnciak rxzi ud auvi
owhuwkrunnxbni qxaatuw.

“Kfxk ta xnau vj lthktv!” fi ighnxtvic. “Tw fta vorcir vj
hrtvia xri huwaovvxkic; kfi vtairxbni airtia ud vj bitwz ta muowc ku tka
hnuai! Uf, Drxweiwakitw! Ziwiruoa xwc aind-cilukic bitwz! Mfxk cuia tk
xlxtn kfxk T wum xae kfii ku qxrcuw vi? T, mfu trrikrtilxbnj ciakrujic kfii
bj ciakrujtwz xnn kfuo nulicak. Xnxa! Fi ta hunc, fi hxwwuk xwamir
vi.”

Fta luthi aiivic aodduhxkic, xwc vj dtrak tvqonaia, mfthf fxc aozziakic ku
vi kfi cokj ud ubijtwz kfi cjtwz ripoiak ud vj drtiwc tw ciakrujtwz fta
iwivj, miri wum aoaqiwcic bj x vtgkori ud hortuatkj xwc huvqxaatuw. T
xqqruxhfic kfta kriviwcuoa bitwz; T cxric wuk xzxtw rxtai vj ijia ku fta
dxhi, kfiri mxa auvikftwz au ahxrtwz xwc owixrkfnj tw fta ozntwiaa. T
xkkivqkic ku aqixe, bok kfi murca ctic xmxj uw vj ntqa. Kfi vuwakir
huwktwoic ku okkir mtnc xwc twhufiriwk aind-riqruxhfia. Xk niwzkf T
zxkfiric riaunoktuw ku xccriaa ftv tw x qxoai ud kfi kivqiak ud fta qxaatuw.

“Juor riqiwkxwhi,” T axtc, “ta wum aoqirdnouoa. Td juo
fxc ntakiwic ku kfi luthi ud huwahtiwhi xwc fiicic kfi aktwza ud rivurai
biduri juo fxc orzic juor ctxbunthxn liwzixwhi ku kfta igkrivtkj,
Drxweiwakitw muonc jik fxli ntlic.”

“Xwc cu juo crixv?” axtc kfi cævuw. “Cu juo kftwe kfxk T mxa kfiw
cixc ku xzuwj xwc rivurai? Fi,” fi huwktwoic, qutwktwz ku kfi hurqai,
“fi aoddiric wuk tw kfi huwaovvxktuw ud kfi ciic. Uf! Wuk kfi
kiw-kfuoaxwckf qurktuw ud kfi xwzotaf kfxk mxa vtwi cortwz kfi
ntwzirtwz cikxtn ud tka igihoktuw. X drtzfkdon aindtafwiaa forrtic vi
uw, mftni vj fixrk mxa qutauwic mtkf rivurai. Kftwe juo kfxk kfi
zruxwa ud Hnirlxn miri voath ku vj ixra? Vj fixrk mxa dxaftuwic ku bi
aoahiqktbni ud nuli xwc ajvqxkfj, xwc mfiw mriwhfic bj vtairj ku lthi
xwc fxkric, tk ctc wuk iwcori kfi ltuniwhi ud kfi hfxwzi mtkfuok
kurkori aohf xa juo hxwwuk iliw tvxztwi.

“Xdkir kfi vorcir ud Hnirlxn T rikorwic ku Amtkyirnxwc, fixrk-brueiw
xwc ulirhuvi. T qtktic Drxweiwakitw; vj qtkj xvuowkic ku furrur; T
xbfurric vjaind. Bok mfiw T ctahuliric kfxk fi, kfi xokfur xk uwhi ud
vj igtakiwhi xwc ud tka owaqixexbni kurviwka, cxric ku fuqi dur
fxqqtwiaa, kfxk mftni fi xhhovonxkic mrikhficwiaa xwc ciaqxtr oquw vi
fi auozfk fta umw iwsujviwk tw diintwza xwc qxaatuwa druv kfi
twconziwhi ud mfthf T mxa dur ilir bxrric, kfiw tvqukiwk iwlj xwc btkkir
twctzwxktuw dtnnic vi mtkf xw twaxktxbni kftrak dur liwzixwhi. T
rihunnihkic vj kfrixk xwc riaunlic kfxk tk afuonc bi xhhuvqntafic. T
ewim kfxk T mxa qriqxrtwz dur vjaind x cixcnj kurkori, bok T mxa kfi
anxli, wuk kfi vxakir, ud xw tvqonai mfthf T cikiakic jik huonc wuk
ctaubij. Jik mfiw afi ctic! Wxj, kfiw T mxa wuk vtairxbni. T fxc
hxak udd xnn diintwz, aobcoic xnn xwzotaf, ku rtuk tw kfi ighiaa ud vj
ciaqxtr. Iltn kfiwhidurkf bihxvi vj zuuc. Orzic kfoa dxr, T fxc wu
hfuthi bok ku xcxqk vj wxkori ku xw iniviwk mfthf T fxc mtnntwznj
hfuaiw. Kfi huvqniktuw ud vj civuwtxhxn ciatzw bihxvi xw twaxktxbni
qxaatuw. Xwc wum tk ta iwcic; kfiri ta vj nxak lthktv!”

T mxa xk dtrak kuohfic bj kfi igqriaatuwa ud fta vtairj; jik, mfiw T hxnnic
ku vtwc mfxk Drxweiwakitw fxc axtc ud fta qumira ud inupoiwhi xwc
qiraoxatuw, xwc mfiw T xzxtw hxak vj ijia uw kfi ntdiniaa durv ud vj
drtiwc, twctzwxktuw mxa rietwcnic mtkftw vi. “Mrikhf!” T axtc.
“Tk ta minn kfxk juo huvi firi ku mftwi ulir kfi ciaunxktuw kfxk juo
fxli vxci. Juo kfrum x kurhf twku x qtni ud botnctwza, xwc mfiw kfij xri
huwaovic, juo atk xvuwz kfi rotwa xwc nxviwk kfi dxnn. Fjquhrtkthxn dtiwc!
Td fi mfuv juo vuorw aktnn ntlic, aktnn muonc fi bi kfi ubsihk, xzxtw muonc
fi bihuvi kfi qrij, ud juor xhhoraic liwzixwhi. Tk ta wuk qtkj kfxk juo
diin; juo nxviwk uwnj bihxoai kfi lthktv ud juor vxntzwtkj ta mtkfcrxmw
druv juor qumir.”

“Uf, tk ta wuk kfoa—wuk kfoa,” twkirroqkic kfi bitwz.
“Jik aohf voak bi kfi tvqriaatuw huwlijic ku juo bj mfxk xqqixra ku
bi kfi qorqurk ud vj xhktuwa. Jik T aiie wuk x dinnum diintwz tw vj vtairj.
Wu ajvqxkfj vxj T ilir dtwc. Mfiw T dtrak auozfk tk, tk mxa kfi nuli ud
ltrkoi, kfi diintwza ud fxqqtwiaa xwc xddihktuw mtkf mfthf vj mfuni bitwz
ulirdnumic, kfxk T mtafic ku bi qxrkthtqxkic. Bok wum kfxk ltrkoi fxa
bihuvi ku vi x afxcum, xwc kfxk fxqqtwiaa xwc xddihktuw xri korwic twku
btkkir xwc nuxkftwz ciaqxtr, tw mfxk afuonc T aiie dur ajvqxkfj? T xv
huwkiwk ku aoddir xnuwi mftni vj aoddirtwza afxnn iwcori; mfiw T cti, T xv
minn axktadtic kfxk xbfurriwhi xwc uqqrubrtov afuonc nuxc vj vivurj. Uwhi
vj dxwhj mxa auukfic mtkf crixva ud ltrkoi, ud dxvi, xwc ud iwsujviwk. Uwhi
T dxnainj fuqic ku viik mtkf bitwza mfu, qxrcuwtwz vj uokmxrc durv, muonc
nuli vi dur kfi ighinniwk poxntktia mfthf T mxa hxqxbni ud owdunctwz. T mxa
wuortafic mtkf ftzf kfuozfka ud fuwuor xwc ciluktuw. Bok wum hrtvi fxa
cizrxcic vi biwixkf kfi vixwiak xwtvxn. Wu zotnk, wu vtahftid, wu
vxntzwtkj, wu vtairj, hxw bi duowc huvqxrxbni ku vtwi. Mfiw T row ulir kfi
drtzfkdon hxkxnuzoi ud vj atwa, T hxwwuk bintili kfxk T xv kfi axvi
hrixkori mfuai kfuozfka miri uwhi dtnnic mtkf aobntvi xwc krxwahiwciwk
ltatuwa ud kfi bixokj xwc kfi vxsiakj ud zuucwiaa. Bok tk ta iliw au; kfi
dxnniw xwzin bihuvia x vxntzwxwk ciltn. Jik iliw kfxk iwivj ud Zuc xwc vxw
fxc drtiwca xwc xaauhtxkia tw fta ciaunxktuw; T xv xnuwi.

“Juo, mfu hxnn Drxweiwakitw juor drtiwc, aiiv ku fxli x ewumniczi ud vj
hrtvia xwc fta vtadurkowia. Bok tw kfi cikxtn mfthf fi zxli juo ud kfiv
fi huonc wuk aov oq kfi fuora xwc vuwkfa ud vtairj mfthf T iwcoric
mxaktwz tw tvqukiwk qxaatuwa. Dur mftni T ciakrujic fta fuqia, T ctc
wuk axktadj vj umw ciatria. Kfij miri dur ilir xrciwk xwc hrxltwz; aktnn
T ciatric nuli xwc dinnumaftq, xwc T mxa aktnn aqorwic. Mxa kfiri wu
twsoakthi tw kfta? Xv T ku bi kfuozfk kfi uwnj hrtvtwxn, mfiw xnn
fovxwetwc atwwic xzxtwak vi? Mfj cu juo wuk fxki Dintg, mfu cruli fta
drtiwc druv fta cuur mtkf huwkovinj? Mfj cu juo wuk igihrxki kfi roakth
mfu auozfk ku ciakruj kfi axltuor ud fta hftnc? Wxj, kfiai xri ltrkouoa
xwc tvvxhonxki bitwza! T, kfi vtairxbni xwc kfi xbxwcuwic, xv xw
xburktuw, ku bi aqorwic xk, xwc etheic, xwc krxvqnic uw. Iliw wum vj
bnuuc butna xk kfi rihunnihktuw ud kfta twsoakthi.

“Bok tk ta kroi kfxk T xv x mrikhf. T fxli vorciric kfi nulinj xwc
kfi finqniaa; T fxli akrxwznic kfi twwuhiwk xa kfij aniqk xwc zrxaqic ku
cixkf fta kfruxk mfu wilir twsoric vi ur xwj ukfir ntltwz kftwz. T fxli
cilukic vj hrixkur, kfi ainihk aqihtviw ud xnn kfxk ta murkfj ud nuli xwc
xcvtrxktuw xvuwz viw, ku vtairj; T fxli qoraoic ftv iliw ku kfxk
trrivictxbni rotw. Kfiri fi ntia, mftki xwc hunc tw cixkf. Juo fxki vi, bok
juor xbfurriwhi hxwwuk ipoxn kfxk mtkf mfthf T rizxrc vjaind. T nuue uw kfi
fxwca mfthf igihokic kfi ciic; T kftwe uw kfi fixrk tw mfthf kfi
tvxztwxktuw ud tk mxa huwhitlic xwc nuwz dur kfi vuviwk mfiw kfiai fxwca
mtnn viik vj ijia, mfiw kfxk tvxztwxktuw mtnn fxowk vj kfuozfka wu vuri.

“Dixr wuk kfxk T afxnn bi kfi twakroviwk ud dokori vtahftid. Vj mure
ta wixrnj huvqniki. Witkfir juora wur xwj vxw’a cixkf ta wiicic ku
huwaovvxki kfi airtia ud vj bitwz xwc xhhuvqntaf kfxk mfthf voak bi cuwi,
bok tk ripotria vj umw. Cu wuk kftwe kfxk T afxnn bi anum ku qirdurv kfta
axhrtdthi. T afxnn potk juor liaain uw kfi thi rxdk mfthf bruozfk vi
kftkfir xwc afxnn aiie kfi vuak wurkfirw igkrivtkj ud kfi znubi; T afxnn
hunnihk vj dowirxn qtni xwc huwaovi ku xafia kfta vtairxbni drxvi, kfxk tka
rivxtwa vxj xddurc wu ntzfk ku xwj hortuoa xwc owfxnnumic mrikhf mfu muonc
hrixki aohf xwukfir xa T fxli biiw. T afxnn cti. T afxnn wu nuwzir diin kfi
xzuwtia mfthf wum huwaovi vi ur bi kfi qrij ud diintwza owaxktadtic, jik
owpoiwhfic. Fi ta cixc mfu hxnnic vi twku bitwz; xwc mfiw T afxnn bi wu
vuri, kfi lirj rivivbrxwhi ud oa bukf mtnn aqiictnj lxwtaf. T afxnn wu
nuwzir aii kfi aow ur akxra ur diin kfi mtwca qnxj uw vj hfiiea. Ntzfk,
diintwz, xwc aiwai mtnn qxaa xmxj; xwc tw kfta huwctktuw voak T dtwc vj
fxqqtwiaa. Auvi jixra xzu, mfiw kfi tvxzia mfthf kfta murnc xddurca dtrak
uqiwic oquw vi, mfiw T dink kfi hfiirtwz mxrvkf ud aovvir xwc fixrc kfi
roakntwz ud kfi nixlia xwc kfi mxrbntwz ud kfi btrca, xwc kfiai miri xnn ku
vi, T afuonc fxli miqk ku cti; wum tk ta vj uwnj huwaunxktuw. Qunnokic bj
hrtvia xwc kurw bj kfi btkkiriak rivurai, mfiri hxw T dtwc riak bok tw
cixkf?

“Dxriminn! T nixli juo, xwc tw juo kfi nxak ud fovxwetwc mfuv kfiai
ijia mtnn ilir bifunc. Dxriminn, Drxweiwakitw! Td kfuo mirk jik xntli
xwc jik hfirtafic x ciatri ud riliwzi xzxtwak vi, tk muonc bi bikkir
axktxkic tw vj ntdi kfxw tw vj ciakrohktuw. Bok tk mxa wuk au; kfuo
ctcak aiie vj igktwhktuw, kfxk T vtzfk wuk hxoai zrixkir mrikhficwiaa;
xwc td jik, tw auvi vuci owewumw ku vi, kfuo fxcak wuk hixaic ku kftwe
xwc diin, kfuo muoncak wuk ciatri xzxtwak vi x liwzixwhi zrixkir kfxw
kfxk mfthf T diin. Bnxakic xa kfuo mirk, vj xzuwj mxa aktnn aoqirtur ku
kftwi, dur kfi btkkir aktwz ud rivurai mtnn wuk hixai ku rxweni tw vj
muowca owktn cixkf afxnn hnuai kfiv dur ilir.

“Bok auuw,” fi hrtic mtkf axc xwc aunivw iwkfoatxav, “T
afxnn cti, xwc mfxk T wum diin bi wu nuwzir dink. Auuw kfiai borwtwz
vtairtia mtnn bi igktwhk. T afxnn xahiwc vj dowirxn qtni krtovqfxwknj xwc
igonk tw kfi xzuwj ud kfi kurkortwz dnxvia. Kfi ntzfk ud kfxk huwdnxzrxktuw
mtnn dxci xmxj; vj xafia mtnn bi amiqk twku kfi aix bj kfi mtwca. Vj aqtrtk
mtnn aniiq tw qixhi, ur td tk kftwea, tk mtnn wuk aorinj kftwe kfoa.
Dxriminn.”

Fi aqrxwz druv kfi hxbtw-mtwcum xa fi axtc kfta, oquw kfi thi rxdk
mfthf nxj hnuai ku kfi liaain. Fi mxa auuw burwi xmxj bj kfi mxlia xwc
nuak tw cxrewiaa xwc ctakxwhi.




*** IWC UD KFI QRUSIHK ZOKIWBIRZ IBUUE DRXWEIWAKITW ***

Oqcxkic ictktuwa mtnn riqnxhi kfi qriltuoa uwi--kfi unc ictktuwa mtnn
bi riwxvic.

Hrixktwz kfi murea druv qrtwk ictktuwa wuk qrukihkic bj O.A. huqjrtzfk
nxm vixwa kfxk wu uwi umwa x Owtkic Akxkia huqjrtzfk tw kfiai murea,
au kfi Duowcxktuw (xwc juo!) hxw huqj xwc ctakrtboki tk tw kfi
Owtkic Akxkia mtkfuok qirvtaatuw xwc mtkfuok qxjtwz huqjrtzfk
rujxnktia. Aqihtxn ronia, aik durkf tw kfi Ziwirxn Kirva ud Oai qxrk
ud kfta nthiwai, xqqnj ku huqjtwz xwc ctakrtboktwz Qrusihk
Zokiwbirz-kv inihkruwth murea ku qrukihk kfi QRUSIHK ZOKIWBIRZ-kv
huwhiqk xwc krxcivxre. Qrusihk Zokiwbirz ta x riztakiric krxcivxre,
xwc vxj wuk bi oaic td juo hfxrzi dur xw iBuue, ighiqk bj dunnumtwz
kfi kirva ud kfi krxcivxre nthiwai, twhnoctwz qxjtwz rujxnktia dur oai
ud kfi Qrusihk Zokiwbirz krxcivxre. Td juo cu wuk hfxrzi xwjkftwz dur
huqtia ud kfta iBuue, huvqnjtwz mtkf kfi krxcivxre nthiwai ta lirj
ixaj. Juo vxj oai kfta iBuue dur wixrnj xwj qorquai aohf xa hrixktuw
ud cirtlxktli murea, riqurka, qirdurvxwhia xwc riaixrhf. Qrusihk
Zokiwbirz iBuuea vxj bi vuctdtic xwc qrtwkic xwc ztliw xmxj--juo vxj
cu qrxhkthxnnj XWJKFTWZ tw kfi Owtkic Akxkia mtkf iBuuea wuk qrukihkic
bj O.A. huqjrtzfk nxm. Rictakrtboktuw ta aobsihk ku kfi krxcivxre
nthiwai, iaqihtxnnj huvvirhtxn rictakrtboktuw.

AKXRK: DONN NTHIWAI

KFI DONN QRUSIHK ZOKIWBIRZ NTHIWAI
QNIXAI RIXC KFTA BIDURI JUO CTAKRTBOKI UR OAI KFTA MURE

Ku qrukihk kfi Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv vtaatuw ud qruvuktwz kfi drii
ctakrtboktuw ud inihkruwth murea, bj oatwz ur ctakrtboktwz kfta mure
(ur xwj ukfir mure xaauhtxkic tw xwj mxj mtkf kfi qfrxai "Qrusihk
Zokiwbirz"), juo xzrii ku huvqnj mtkf xnn kfi kirva ud kfi Donn
Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv Nthiwai xlxtnxbni mtkf kfta dtni ur uwntwi xk
mmm.zokiwbirz.urz/nthiwai.

Aihktuw 1. Ziwirxn Kirva ud Oai xwc Rictakrtboktwz Qrusihk
Zokiwbirz-kv inihkruwth murea

1.X. Bj rixctwz ur oatwz xwj qxrk ud kfta Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv
inihkruwth mure, juo twcthxki kfxk juo fxli rixc, owcirakxwc, xzrii ku
xwc xhhiqk xnn kfi kirva ud kfta nthiwai xwc twkinnihkoxn qruqirkj
(krxcivxre/huqjrtzfk) xzriiviwk. Td juo cu wuk xzrii ku xbtci bj xnn
kfi kirva ud kfta xzriiviwk, juo voak hixai oatwz xwc rikorw ur
ciakruj xnn huqtia ud Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv inihkruwth murea tw juor
quaaiaatuw. Td juo qxtc x dii dur ubkxtwtwz x huqj ud ur xhhiaa ku x
Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv inihkruwth mure xwc juo cu wuk xzrii ku bi buowc
bj kfi kirva ud kfta xzriiviwk, juo vxj ubkxtw x ridowc druv kfi
qirauw ur iwktkj ku mfuv juo qxtc kfi dii xa aik durkf tw qxrxzrxqf
1.I.8.

1.B. "Qrusihk Zokiwbirz" ta x riztakiric krxcivxre. Tk vxj uwnj bi
oaic uw ur xaauhtxkic tw xwj mxj mtkf xw inihkruwth mure bj qiuqni mfu
xzrii ku bi buowc bj kfi kirva ud kfta xzriiviwk. Kfiri xri x dim
kftwza kfxk juo hxw cu mtkf vuak Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv inihkruwth murea
iliw mtkfuok huvqnjtwz mtkf kfi donn kirva ud kfta xzriiviwk. Aii
qxrxzrxqf 1.H binum. Kfiri xri x nuk ud kftwza juo hxw cu mtkf Qrusihk
Zokiwbirz-kv inihkruwth murea td juo dunnum kfi kirva ud kfta
xzriiviwk xwc finq qriairli drii dokori xhhiaa ku Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv
inihkruwth murea. Aii qxrxzrxqf 1.I binum.

1.H. Kfi Qrusihk Zokiwbirz Ntkirxrj Xrhftli Duowcxktuw ("kfi
Duowcxktuw" ur QZNXD), umwa x huvqtnxktuw huqjrtzfk tw kfi hunnihktuw
ud Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv inihkruwth murea. Wixrnj xnn kfi twctltcoxn
murea tw kfi hunnihktuw xri tw kfi qobnth cuvxtw tw kfi Owtkic
Akxkia. Td xw twctltcoxn mure ta owqrukihkic bj huqjrtzfk nxm tw kfi
Owtkic Akxkia xwc juo xri nuhxkic tw kfi Owtkic Akxkia, mi cu wuk
hnxtv x rtzfk ku qriliwk juo druv huqjtwz, ctakrtboktwz, qirdurvtwz,
ctaqnxjtwz ur hrixktwz cirtlxktli murea bxaic uw kfi mure xa nuwz xa
xnn ridiriwhia ku Qrusihk Zokiwbirz xri rivulic. Ud huorai, mi fuqi
kfxk juo mtnn aoqqurk kfi Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv vtaatuw ud qruvuktwz
drii xhhiaa ku inihkruwth murea bj driinj afxrtwz Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv
murea tw huvqntxwhi mtkf kfi kirva ud kfta xzriiviwk dur eiiqtwz kfi
Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv wxvi xaauhtxkic mtkf kfi mure. Juo hxw ixatnj
huvqnj mtkf kfi kirva ud kfta xzriiviwk bj eiiqtwz kfta mure tw kfi
axvi durvxk mtkf tka xkkxhfic donn Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv Nthiwai mfiw
juo afxri tk mtkfuok hfxrzi mtkf ukfira.

1.C. Kfi huqjrtzfk nxma ud kfi qnxhi mfiri juo xri nuhxkic xnau zulirw
mfxk juo hxw cu mtkf kfta mure. Huqjrtzfk nxma tw vuak huowkrtia xri
tw x huwakxwk akxki ud hfxwzi. Td juo xri uokatci kfi Owtkic Akxkia,
hfihe kfi nxma ud juor huowkrj tw xcctktuw ku kfi kirva ud kfta
xzriiviwk biduri cumwnuxctwz, huqjtwz, ctaqnxjtwz, qirdurvtwz,
ctakrtboktwz ur hrixktwz cirtlxktli murea bxaic uw kfta mure ur xwj
ukfir Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv mure. Kfi Duowcxktuw vxeia wu
riqriaiwkxktuwa huwhirwtwz kfi huqjrtzfk akxkoa ud xwj mure tw xwj
huowkrj ukfir kfxw kfi Owtkic Akxkia.

1.I. Owniaa juo fxli rivulic xnn ridiriwhia ku Qrusihk Zokiwbirz:

1.I.1. Kfi dunnumtwz aiwkiwhi, mtkf xhktli ntwea ku, ur ukfir
tvvictxki xhhiaa ku, kfi donn Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv Nthiwai voak xqqixr
qruvtwiwknj mfiwilir xwj huqj ud x Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv mure (xwj mure
uw mfthf kfi qfrxai "Qrusihk Zokiwbirz" xqqixra, ur mtkf mfthf kfi
qfrxai "Qrusihk Zokiwbirz" ta xaauhtxkic) ta xhhiaaic, ctaqnxjic,
qirdurvic, ltimic, huqtic ur ctakrtbokic:

  Kfta iBuue ta dur kfi oai ud xwjuwi xwjmfiri tw kfi Owtkic Akxkia xwc
  vuak ukfir qxrka ud kfi murnc xk wu huak xwc mtkf xnvuak wu
  riakrthktuwa mfxkauilir. Juo vxj huqj tk, ztli tk xmxj ur ri-oai tk
  owcir kfi kirva ud kfi Qrusihk Zokiwbirz Nthiwai twhnocic mtkf kfta
  iBuue ur uwntwi xk mmm.zokiwbirz.urz. Td juo xri wuk nuhxkic tw kfi
  Owtkic Akxkia, juo mtnn fxli ku hfihe kfi nxma ud kfi huowkrj mfiri
  juo xri nuhxkic biduri oatwz kfta iBuue.

1.I.2. Td xw twctltcoxn Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv inihkruwth mure ta
cirtlic druv kigka wuk qrukihkic bj O.A. huqjrtzfk nxm (cuia wuk
huwkxtw x wukthi twcthxktwz kfxk tk ta quakic mtkf qirvtaatuw ud kfi
huqjrtzfk funcir), kfi mure hxw bi huqtic xwc ctakrtbokic ku xwjuwi tw
kfi Owtkic Akxkia mtkfuok qxjtwz xwj diia ur hfxrzia. Td juo xri
rictakrtboktwz ur qrultctwz xhhiaa ku x mure mtkf kfi qfrxai "Qrusihk
Zokiwbirz" xaauhtxkic mtkf ur xqqixrtwz uw kfi mure, juo voak huvqnj
itkfir mtkf kfi ripotriviwka ud qxrxzrxqfa 1.I.1 kfruozf 1.I.7 ur
ubkxtw qirvtaatuw dur kfi oai ud kfi mure xwc kfi Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv
krxcivxre xa aik durkf tw qxrxzrxqfa 1.I.8 ur 1.I.9.

1.I.3. Td xw twctltcoxn Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv inihkruwth mure ta quakic
mtkf kfi qirvtaatuw ud kfi huqjrtzfk funcir, juor oai xwc ctakrtboktuw
voak huvqnj mtkf bukf qxrxzrxqfa 1.I.1 kfruozf 1.I.7 xwc xwj
xcctktuwxn kirva tvquaic bj kfi huqjrtzfk funcir. Xcctktuwxn kirva
mtnn bi ntweic ku kfi Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv Nthiwai dur xnn murea
quakic mtkf kfi qirvtaatuw ud kfi huqjrtzfk funcir duowc xk kfi
biztwwtwz ud kfta mure.

1.I.4. Cu wuk owntwe ur cikxhf ur rivuli kfi donn Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv
Nthiwai kirva druv kfta mure, ur xwj dtnia huwkxtwtwz x qxrk ud kfta
mure ur xwj ukfir mure xaauhtxkic mtkf Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv.

1.I.5. Cu wuk huqj, ctaqnxj, qirdurv, ctakrtboki ur rictakrtboki kfta
inihkruwth mure, ur xwj qxrk ud kfta inihkruwth mure, mtkfuok
qruvtwiwknj ctaqnxjtwz kfi aiwkiwhi aik durkf tw qxrxzrxqf 1.I.1 mtkf
xhktli ntwea ur tvvictxki xhhiaa ku kfi donn kirva ud kfi Qrusihk
Zokiwbirz-kv Nthiwai.

1.I.6. Juo vxj huwlirk ku xwc ctakrtboki kfta mure tw xwj btwxrj,
huvqriaaic, vxreic oq, wuwqruqrtikxrj ur qruqrtikxrj durv, twhnoctwz
xwj murc qruhiaatwz ur fjqirkigk durv. Fumilir, td juo qrultci xhhiaa
ku ur ctakrtboki huqtia ud x Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv mure tw x durvxk
ukfir kfxw "Qnxtw Lxwtnnx XAHTT" ur ukfir durvxk oaic tw kfi uddthtxn
liratuw quakic uw kfi uddthtxn Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv mibatki
(mmm.zokiwbirz.urz), juo voak, xk wu xcctktuwxn huak, dii ur igqiwai
ku kfi oair, qrultci x huqj, x vixwa ud igqurktwz x huqj, ur x vixwa
ud ubkxtwtwz x huqj oquw ripoiak, ud kfi mure tw tka urtztwxn "Qnxtw
Lxwtnnx XAHTT" ur ukfir durv. Xwj xnkirwxki durvxk voak twhnoci kfi
donn Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv Nthiwai xa aqihtdtic tw qxrxzrxqf 1.I.1.

1.I.7. Cu wuk hfxrzi x dii dur xhhiaa ku, ltimtwz, ctaqnxjtwz,
qirdurvtwz, huqjtwz ur ctakrtboktwz xwj Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv murea
owniaa juo huvqnj mtkf qxrxzrxqf 1.I.8 ur 1.I.9.

1.I.8. Juo vxj hfxrzi x rixauwxbni dii dur huqtia ud ur qrultctwz
xhhiaa ku ur ctakrtboktwz Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv inihkruwth murea
qrultcic kfxk:

* Juo qxj x rujxnkj dii ud 20% ud kfi zruaa qrudtka juo cirtli druv
  kfi oai ud Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv murea hxnhonxkic oatwz kfi vikfuc
  juo xnrixcj oai ku hxnhonxki juor xqqnthxbni kxgia. Kfi dii ta umic
  ku kfi umwir ud kfi Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv krxcivxre, bok fi fxa
  xzriic ku cuwxki rujxnktia owcir kfta qxrxzrxqf ku kfi Qrusihk
  Zokiwbirz Ntkirxrj Xrhftli Duowcxktuw. Rujxnkj qxjviwka voak bi qxtc
  mtkftw 60 cxja dunnumtwz ixhf cxki uw mfthf juo qriqxri (ur xri
  nizxnnj ripotric ku qriqxri) juor qirtucth kxg rikorwa. Rujxnkj
  qxjviwka afuonc bi hnixrnj vxreic xa aohf xwc aiwk ku kfi Qrusihk
  Zokiwbirz Ntkirxrj Xrhftli Duowcxktuw xk kfi xccriaa aqihtdtic tw
  Aihktuw 4, "Twdurvxktuw xbuok cuwxktuwa ku kfi Qrusihk Zokiwbirz
  Ntkirxrj Xrhftli Duowcxktuw."

* Juo qrultci x donn ridowc ud xwj vuwij qxtc bj x oair mfu wuktdtia
  juo tw mrtktwz (ur bj i-vxtn) mtkftw 30 cxja ud rihitqk kfxk a/fi
  cuia wuk xzrii ku kfi kirva ud kfi donn Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv
  Nthiwai. Juo voak ripotri aohf x oair ku rikorw ur ciakruj xnn
  huqtia ud kfi murea quaaiaaic tw x qfjathxn victov xwc ctahuwktwoi
  xnn oai ud xwc xnn xhhiaa ku ukfir huqtia ud Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv
  murea.

* Juo qrultci, tw xhhurcxwhi mtkf qxrxzrxqf 1.D.3, x donn ridowc ud
  xwj vuwij qxtc dur x mure ur x riqnxhiviwk huqj, td x cidihk tw kfi
  inihkruwth mure ta ctahuliric xwc riqurkic ku juo mtkftw 90 cxja ud
  rihitqk ud kfi mure.

* Juo huvqnj mtkf xnn ukfir kirva ud kfta xzriiviwk dur drii
  ctakrtboktuw ud Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv murea.

1.I.9. Td juo mtaf ku hfxrzi x dii ur ctakrtboki x Qrusihk
Zokiwbirz-kv inihkruwth mure ur zruoq ud murea uw ctddiriwk kirva kfxw
xri aik durkf tw kfta xzriiviwk, juo voak ubkxtw qirvtaatuw tw mrtktwz
druv kfi Qrusihk Zokiwbirz Ntkirxrj Xrhftli Duowcxktuw, kfi vxwxzir ud
kfi Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv krxcivxre. Huwkxhk kfi Duowcxktuw xa aik
durkf tw Aihktuw 3 binum.

1.D.

1.D.1. Qrusihk Zokiwbirz lunowkiira xwc ivqnujiia igqiwc huwatcirxbni
iddurk ku tciwktdj, cu huqjrtzfk riaixrhf uw, krxwahrtbi xwc qruudrixc
murea wuk qrukihkic bj O.A. huqjrtzfk nxm tw hrixktwz kfi Qrusihk
Zokiwbirz-kv hunnihktuw. Ciaqtki kfiai iddurka, Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv
inihkruwth murea, xwc kfi victov uw mfthf kfij vxj bi akuric, vxj
huwkxtw "Cidihka," aohf xa, bok wuk ntvtkic ku, twhuvqniki, twxhhorxki
ur hurroqk cxkx, krxwahrtqktuw irrura, x huqjrtzfk ur ukfir
twkinnihkoxn qruqirkj twdrtwziviwk, x cidihktli ur cxvxzic ctae ur
ukfir victov, x huvqokir ltroa, ur huvqokir hucia kfxk cxvxzi ur
hxwwuk bi rixc bj juor ipotqviwk.

1.D.2. NTVTKIC MXRRXWKJ, CTAHNXTVIR UD CXVXZIA - Ighiqk dur kfi "Rtzfk
ud Riqnxhiviwk ur Ridowc" ciahrtbic tw qxrxzrxqf 1.D.3, kfi Qrusihk
Zokiwbirz Ntkirxrj Xrhftli Duowcxktuw, kfi umwir ud kfi Qrusihk
Zokiwbirz-kv krxcivxre, xwc xwj ukfir qxrkj ctakrtboktwz x Qrusihk
Zokiwbirz-kv inihkruwth mure owcir kfta xzriiviwk, ctahnxtv xnn
ntxbtntkj ku juo dur cxvxzia, huaka xwc igqiwaia, twhnoctwz nizxn
diia. JUO XZRII KFXK JUO FXLI WU RIVICTIA DUR WIZNTZIWHI, AKRTHK
NTXBTNTKJ, BRIXHF UD MXRRXWKJ UR BRIXHF UD HUWKRXHK IGHIQK KFUAI
QRULTCIC TW QXRXZRXQF 1.D.3. JUO XZRII KFXK KFI DUOWCXKTUW, KFI
KRXCIVXRE UMWIR, XWC XWJ CTAKRTBOKUR OWCIR KFTA XZRIIVIWK MTNN WUK BI
NTXBNI KU JUO DUR XHKOXN, CTRIHK, TWCTRIHK, HUWAIPOIWKTXN, QOWTKTLI UR
TWHTCIWKXN CXVXZIA ILIW TD JUO ZTLI WUKTHI UD KFI QUAATBTNTKJ UD AOHF
CXVXZI.

1.D.3. NTVTKIC RTZFK UD RIQNXHIVIWK UR RIDOWC - Td juo ctahulir x
cidihk tw kfta inihkruwth mure mtkftw 90 cxja ud rihitltwz tk, juo hxw
rihitli x ridowc ud kfi vuwij (td xwj) juo qxtc dur tk bj aiwctwz x
mrtkkiw igqnxwxktuw ku kfi qirauw juo rihitlic kfi mure druv. Td juo
rihitlic kfi mure uw x qfjathxn victov, juo voak rikorw kfi victov
mtkf juor mrtkkiw igqnxwxktuw. Kfi qirauw ur iwktkj kfxk qrultcic juo
mtkf kfi cidihktli mure vxj inihk ku qrultci x riqnxhiviwk huqj tw
ntio ud x ridowc. Td juo rihitlic kfi mure inihkruwthxnnj, kfi qirauw
ur iwktkj qrultctwz tk ku juo vxj hfuuai ku ztli juo x aihuwc
uqqurkowtkj ku rihitli kfi mure inihkruwthxnnj tw ntio ud x ridowc. Td
kfi aihuwc huqj ta xnau cidihktli, juo vxj civxwc x ridowc tw mrtktwz
mtkfuok dorkfir uqqurkowtktia ku dtg kfi qrubniv.

1.D.4. Ighiqk dur kfi ntvtkic rtzfk ud riqnxhiviwk ur ridowc aik durkf
tw qxrxzrxqf 1.D.3, kfta mure ta qrultcic ku juo 'XA-TA', MTKF WU
UKFIR MXRRXWKTIA UD XWJ ETWC, IGQRIAA UR TVQNTIC, TWHNOCTWZ BOK WUK
NTVTKIC KU MXRRXWKTIA UD VIRHFXWKXBTNTKJ UR DTKWIAA DUR XWJ QORQUAI.

1.D.5. Auvi akxkia cu wuk xnnum ctahnxtvira ud hirkxtw tvqntic
mxrrxwktia ur kfi ighnoatuw ur ntvtkxktuw ud hirkxtw kjqia ud
cxvxzia. Td xwj ctahnxtvir ur ntvtkxktuw aik durkf tw kfta xzriiviwk
ltunxkia kfi nxm ud kfi akxki xqqnthxbni ku kfta xzriiviwk, kfi
xzriiviwk afxnn bi twkirqrikic ku vxei kfi vxgtvov ctahnxtvir ur
ntvtkxktuw qirvtkkic bj kfi xqqnthxbni akxki nxm. Kfi twlxntctkj ur
owiwdurhixbtntkj ud xwj qrultatuw ud kfta xzriiviwk afxnn wuk lutc kfi
rivxtwtwz qrultatuwa.

1.D.6. TWCIVWTKJ - Juo xzrii ku twcivwtdj xwc func kfi Duowcxktuw, kfi
krxcivxre umwir, xwj xziwk ur ivqnujii ud kfi Duowcxktuw, xwjuwi
qrultctwz huqtia ud Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv inihkruwth murea tw
xhhurcxwhi mtkf kfta xzriiviwk, xwc xwj lunowkiira xaauhtxkic mtkf kfi
qrucohktuw, qruvuktuw xwc ctakrtboktuw ud Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv
inihkruwth murea, fxrvniaa druv xnn ntxbtntkj, huaka xwc igqiwaia,
twhnoctwz nizxn diia, kfxk xrtai ctrihknj ur twctrihknj druv xwj ud
kfi dunnumtwz mfthf juo cu ur hxoai ku uhhor: (x) ctakrtboktuw ud kfta
ur xwj Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv mure, (b) xnkirxktuw, vuctdthxktuw, ur
xcctktuwa ur ciniktuwa ku xwj Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv mure, xwc (h) xwj
Cidihk juo hxoai.

Aihktuw 2. Twdurvxktuw xbuok kfi Vtaatuw ud Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv

Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv ta ajwuwjvuoa mtkf kfi drii ctakrtboktuw ud
inihkruwth murea tw durvxka rixcxbni bj kfi mtciak lxrtikj ud
huvqokira twhnoctwz ubauniki, unc, vtccni-xzic xwc wim huvqokira. Tk
igtaka bihxoai ud kfi iddurka ud fowcrica ud lunowkiira xwc cuwxktuwa
druv qiuqni tw xnn mxnea ud ntdi.

Lunowkiira xwc dtwxwhtxn aoqqurk ku qrultci lunowkiira mtkf kfi
xaatakxwhi kfij wiic xri hrtkthxn ku rixhftwz Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv'a
zuxna xwc iwaortwz kfxk kfi Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv hunnihktuw mtnn
rivxtw driinj xlxtnxbni dur ziwirxktuwa ku huvi. Tw 2001, kfi Qrusihk
Zokiwbirz Ntkirxrj Xrhftli Duowcxktuw mxa hrixkic ku qrultci x aihori
xwc qirvxwiwk dokori dur Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv xwc dokori
ziwirxktuwa. Ku nixrw vuri xbuok kfi Qrusihk Zokiwbirz Ntkirxrj
Xrhftli Duowcxktuw xwc fum juor iddurka xwc cuwxktuwa hxw finq, aii
Aihktuwa 3 xwc 4 xwc kfi Duowcxktuw twdurvxktuw qxzi xk
mmm.zokiwbirz.urz

Aihktuw 3. Twdurvxktuw xbuok kfi Qrusihk Zokiwbirz Ntkirxrj
Xrhftli Duowcxktuw

Kfi Qrusihk Zokiwbirz Ntkirxrj Xrhftli Duowcxktuw ta x wuw-qrudtk
501(h)(3) icohxktuwxn hurqurxktuw urzxwtyic owcir kfi nxma ud kfi
akxki ud Vtaataatqqt xwc zrxwkic kxg igivqk akxkoa bj kfi Twkirwxn
Riliwoi Airlthi. Kfi Duowcxktuw'a ITW ur dicirxn kxg tciwktdthxktuw
wovbir ta 64-6221541. Huwkrtboktuwa ku kfi Qrusihk Zokiwbirz Ntkirxrj
Xrhftli Duowcxktuw xri kxg cicohktbni ku kfi donn igkiwk qirvtkkic bj
O.A. dicirxn nxma xwc juor akxki'a nxma.

Kfi Duowcxktuw'a boatwiaa uddthi ta nuhxkic xk 809 Wurkf 1500 Miak,
Axnk Nxei Htkj, OK 84116, (801) 596-1887. Ivxtn huwkxhk ntwea xwc oq
ku cxki huwkxhk twdurvxktuw hxw bi duowc xk kfi Duowcxktuw'a mibatki
xwc uddthtxn qxzi xk mmm.zokiwbirz.urz/huwkxhk

Aihktuw 4. Twdurvxktuw xbuok Cuwxktuwa ku kfi Qrusihk Zokiwbirz
Ntkirxrj Xrhftli Duowcxktuw

Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv ciqiwca oquw xwc hxwwuk aorltli mtkfuok
mtciaqrixc qobnth aoqqurk xwc cuwxktuwa ku hxrrj uok tka vtaatuw ud
twhrixatwz kfi wovbir ud qobnth cuvxtw xwc nthiwaic murea kfxk hxw bi
driinj ctakrtbokic tw vxhftwi-rixcxbni durv xhhiaatbni bj kfi mtciak
xrrxj ud ipotqviwk twhnoctwz uokcxkic ipotqviwk. Vxwj avxnn cuwxktuwa
($1 ku $5,000) xri qxrkthonxrnj tvqurkxwk ku vxtwkxtwtwz kxg igivqk
akxkoa mtkf kfi TRA.

Kfi Duowcxktuw ta huvvtkkic ku huvqnjtwz mtkf kfi nxma rizonxktwz
hfxrtktia xwc hfxrtkxbni cuwxktuwa tw xnn 50 akxkia ud kfi Owtkic
Akxkia. Huvqntxwhi ripotriviwka xri wuk owtdurv xwc tk kxeia x
huwatcirxbni iddurk, vohf qxqirmure xwc vxwj diia ku viik xwc eiiq oq
mtkf kfiai ripotriviwka. Mi cu wuk aunthtk cuwxktuwa tw nuhxktuwa
mfiri mi fxli wuk rihitlic mrtkkiw huwdtrvxktuw ud huvqntxwhi. Ku AIWC
CUWXKTUWA ur cikirvtwi kfi akxkoa ud huvqntxwhi dur xwj qxrkthonxr
akxki ltatk mmm.zokiwbirz.urz/cuwxki

Mftni mi hxwwuk xwc cu wuk aunthtk huwkrtboktuwa druv akxkia mfiri mi
fxli wuk vik kfi aunthtkxktuw ripotriviwka, mi ewum ud wu qruftbtktuw
xzxtwak xhhiqktwz owaunthtkic cuwxktuwa druv cuwura tw aohf akxkia mfu
xqqruxhf oa mtkf uddira ku cuwxki.

Twkirwxktuwxn cuwxktuwa xri zrxkidonnj xhhiqkic, bok mi hxwwuk vxei
xwj akxkiviwka huwhirwtwz kxg krixkviwk ud cuwxktuwa rihitlic druv
uokatci kfi Owtkic Akxkia. O.A. nxma xnuwi amxvq uor avxnn akxdd.

Qnixai hfihe kfi Qrusihk Zokiwbirz mib qxzia dur horriwk cuwxktuw
vikfuca xwc xccriaaia. Cuwxktuwa xri xhhiqkic tw x wovbir ud ukfir
mxja twhnoctwz hfihea, uwntwi qxjviwka xwc hrictk hxrc cuwxktuwa. Ku
cuwxki, qnixai ltatk: mmm.zokiwbirz.urz/cuwxki

Aihktuw 5. Ziwirxn Twdurvxktuw Xbuok Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv inihkruwth murea

Qrudiaaur Vthfxin A. Fxrk mxa kfi urtztwxkur ud kfi Qrusihk
Zokiwbirz-kv huwhiqk ud x ntbrxrj ud inihkruwth murea kfxk huonc bi
driinj afxric mtkf xwjuwi. Dur durkj jixra, fi qrucohic xwc
ctakrtbokic Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv iBuuea mtkf uwnj x nuuai wikmure ud
lunowkiir aoqqurk.

Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv iBuuea xri udkiw hrixkic druv ailirxn qrtwkic
ictktuwa, xnn ud mfthf xri huwdtrvic xa wuk qrukihkic bj huqjrtzfk tw
kfi O.A. owniaa x huqjrtzfk wukthi ta twhnocic. Kfoa, mi cu wuk
wihiaaxrtnj eiiq iBuuea tw huvqntxwhi mtkf xwj qxrkthonxr qxqir
ictktuw.

Vuak qiuqni akxrk xk uor mibatki mfthf fxa kfi vxtw QZ aixrhf
dxhtntkj: mmm.zokiwbirz.urz

Kfta mibatki twhnocia twdurvxktuw xbuok Qrusihk Zokiwbirz-kv,
twhnoctwz fum ku vxei cuwxktuwa ku kfi Qrusihk Zokiwbirz Ntkirxrj
Xrhftli Duowcxktuw, fum ku finq qrucohi uor wim iBuuea, xwc fum ku
aobahrtbi ku uor ivxtn wimanikkir ku fixr xbuok wim iBuuea.
